WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA NUHÆN ‘ILA KAWMIHI ‘INNI LEKUM NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
‘EN LA TA’BUDU ‘ILLALLAHE ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘ALEJKUM ‘ADHABE JEWMIN ‘ELIMIN
FEKALEL-MELE’UL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN KAWMIHI MA NERAKE ‘ILLA BESHERÆN MITHLENA WE MA NERAKE ETTEBE’AKE ‘ILLAL-LEDHINE HUM ‘ERADHILUNA BADIJE ER-RE’JI WE MA NERA LEKUM ‘ALEJNA MIN FEDLIN BEL NEDHUNNUKUM KADHIBINE
KALE JA KAWMI ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN KUNTU ‘ALA BEJJINETIN MIN RABBI WE ‘ATANI REHMETEN MIN ‘INDIHI FA’UMMIJET ‘ALEJKUM ‘ENULZIMUKUMUHA WE ‘ENTUM LEHA KARIHUNE
WE JAKAWMI LA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MALÆN ‘IN ‘EXHRIJE ‘ILLA ‘ALA ELLAHI WE MA ‘ENA BITARIDIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘INNEHUM MULAKU RABBIHIM WE LEKINNI ‘ERAKUM KAWMÆN TEXHHELUNE
WE JAKAWMI MEN JENSURUNI MINEL-LAHI ‘IN TEREDTUHUM ‘EFELA TEDHEKKERUNE
WE LA ‘EKULU LEKUM ‘INDI HAZA’INU ELLAHI WE LA ‘A’LEMUL-GAJBE WE LA ‘EKULU ‘INNI MELEKUN WE LA ‘EKULU LILLEDHINE TEZDERI ‘A’JUNUKUM LEN JU’UTIJEHUMU ELLAHU HAJRÆN ELLAHU ‘A’LEMU BIMA FI ‘ENFUSIHIM ‘INNI ‘IDHÆN LEMINE EDH-DHALIMINE
KALU JA NUHU KAD XHADELTENA FE’EKTHERTE XHIDALENA FE’TINA BIMA TA’IDUNA ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
KALE ‘INNEMA JE’TIKUM BIHI ELLAHU ‘IN SHA’E WE MA ‘ENTUM BIMU’XHIZINE
WE LA JENFA’UKUM NUSHI ‘IN ‘EREDTU ‘EN ‘ENSEHE LEKUM ‘IN KANEL-LAHU JURIDU ‘EN JUGWIJEKUM HUWE REBBUKUM WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
‘EM JEKULUNE EFTERAHU KUL ‘INI EFTEREJTUHU FE’ALEJJE ‘IXHRAMI WE ‘ENA BERI’UN MIMMA TUXHRIMUNE
WE ‘UHIJE ‘ILA NUHIN ‘ENNEHU LEN JU’UMINE MIN KAWMIKE ‘ILLA MEN KAD ‘AMENE FELA TEBTE’IS BIMA KANU JEF’ALUNE
WE ESNA’IL-FULKE BI’A’JUNINA WE WEHJINA WE LA TUHATIBNI FIL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ‘INNEHUM MUGREKUNE
WE JESNA’UL-FULKE WE KULLEMA MERRE ‘ALEJHI MELE’UN MIN KAWMIHI SEHIRU MINHU KALE ‘IN TESHARU MINNA FE’INNA NESHARU MINKUM KEMA TESHARUNE
FESEWFE TA’LEMUNE MEN JE’TIHI ‘ADHABUN JUHZIHI WE JEHILLU ‘ALEJHI ‘ADHABUN MUKIMUN
HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’E ‘EMRUNA WE FARET-TENNURU KULNA EHMIL FIHA MIN KULLIN ZEWXHEJNI ETHNEJNI WE ‘EHLEKE ‘ILLA MEN SEBEKA ‘ALEJHIL-KAWLU WE MEN ‘AMENE WE MA ‘AMENE ME’AHU ‘ILLA KALILUN
WE KALE ERKEBU FIHA BISMI ELLAHI MEXHRAHA WE MURSAHA ‘INNE RABBI LEGAFURUN REHIMUN
WE HIJE TEXHRI BIHIM FI MEWXHIN KALXHIBALI WE NADA NUHUN EBNEHU WE KANE FI MA’ZILIN JA BUNEJJE ERKEB ME’ANA WE LA TEKUN ME’AL-KAFIRINE
KALE SE’AWI ‘ILA XHEBELIN JA’SIMUNI MINEL-MA’I KALE LA ‘ASIMEL-JEWME MIN ‘EMRI ELLAHI ‘ILLA MEN REHIME WE HALE BEJNEHUMAL-MEWXHU FEKANE MINEL-MUGREKINE
WE KILE JA ‘ERDU EBLA’I MA’EKI WE JA SEMA’U ‘EKLI’I WE GIDEL-MA’U WE KUDIJEL-’EMRU WE ESTEWET ‘ALEL-XHUDIJI WE KILE BU’DÆN LILKAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
WE NADA NUHUN REBBEHU FEKALE RABBI ‘INNE EBNI MIN ‘EHLI WE ‘INNE WA’DEKEL-HEKKU WE ‘ENTE ‘EHKEMUL-HAKIMINE
KALE JA NUHU ‘INNEHU LEJSE MIN ‘EHLIKE ‘INNEHU ‘AMELUN GAJRU SALIHIN FELA TES’ELNI MA LEJSE LEKE BIHI ‘ILMUN ‘INNI ‘A’IDHUKE ‘EN TEKUNE MINEL-XHAHILINE
KALE RABBI ‘INNI ‘A’UDHU BIKE ‘EN ‘ES’ELEKE MA LEJSE LI BIHI ‘ILMUN WE ‘ILLA TEGFIR LI WE TERHEMNI ‘EKUN MINEL-HASIRINE
KILE JA NUHU EHBIT BISELAMIN MINNA WE BEREKATIN ‘ALEJKE WE ‘ALA ‘UMEMIN MIMMEN ME’AKE WE ‘UMEMUN SENUMETTI’UHUM THUMME JEMESSUHUM MINNA ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
TILKE MIN ‘ENBA’IL-GAJBI NUHIHA ‘ILEJKE MA KUNTE TA’LEMUHA ‘ENTE WE LA KAWMUKE MIN KABLI HADHA FASBIR ‘INNEL-’AKIBETE LILMUTTEKINE
WE ‘ILA ‘ADIN ‘EHAHUM HUDÆN KALE JA KAWMI A’BUDU ELLAHE MA LEKUM MIN ‘ILEHIN GAJRUHU ‘IN ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA MUFTERUNE
JA KAWMI LA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI ‘EXHRÆN ‘IN ‘EXHRIJE ‘ILLA ‘ALEL-LEDHI FETERENI ‘EFELA TA’KILUNE
WE JA KAWMI ESTEGFIRU REBBEKUM THUMME TUBU ‘ILEJHI JURSILI ES-SEMA’E ‘ALEJKUM MIDRARÆN WE JEZIDKUM KUWETEN ‘ILA KUWETIKUM WE LA TETEWELLEW MUXHRIMINE
KALU JA HUDU MA XHI’TENA BIBEJJINETIN WE MA NEHNU BITARIKI ‘ALIHETINA ‘AN KAWLIKE WE MA NEHNU LEKE BIMU’UMININE
‘IN NEKULU ‘ILLA A’TERAKE BA’DU ‘ALIHETINA BISU’IN KALE ‘INNI ‘USH/HIDU ELLAHE WE ESH/HEDU ‘ENNI BERI’UN MIMMA TUSHRIKUNE
MIN DUNIHI FEKIDUNI XHEMI’ÆN THUMME LA TUNDHIRUNI
‘INNI TEWEKKELTU ‘ALA ELLAHI RABBI WE RABBIKUM MA MIN DABBETIN ‘ILLA HUWE ‘AHIDHUN BINASIJETIHA ‘INNE RABBI ‘ALA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
FE’IN TEWELLEW FEKAD ‘EBLEGTUKUM MA ‘URSILTU BIHI ‘ILEJKUM WE JESTEHLIFU RABBI KAWMÆN GAJREKUM WE LA TEDURRUNEHU SHEJ’ÆN ‘INNE RABBI ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN HEFIDHUN
WE LEMMA XHA’E ‘EMRUNA NEXHXHEJNA HUDÆN WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ME’AHU BIREHMETIN MINNA WE NEXHXHEJNAHUM MIN ‘ADHABIN GALIDHIN
WE TILKE ‘ADUN XHEHEDU BI’AJATI RABBIHIM WE ‘ASEW RUSULEHU WE ETTEBA’U ‘EMRE KULLI XHEBBARIN ‘ANIDIN
WE ‘UTBI’U FI HEDHIHI ED-DUNJA LA’NETEN WE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘ELA ‘INNE ‘ADÆN KEFERU REBBEHUM ‘ELA BU’DÆN LI’ADIN KAWMI HUDIN
WE ‘ILA THEMUDE ‘EHAHUM SALIHÆN KALE JA KAWMI A’BUDU ELLAHE MA LEKUM MIN ‘ILEHIN GAJRUHU HUWE ‘ENSHE’EKUM MINEL-’ERDI WE ESTA’MEREKUM FIHA FASTEGFIRUHU THUMME TUBU ‘ILEJHI ‘INNE RABBI KARIBUN MUXHIBUN
KALU JA SALIHU KAD KUNTE FINA MERXHUWÆN KABLE HADHA ‘ETENHANA ‘EN NA’BUDE MA JA’BUDU ‘ABA’UUNA WE ‘INNENA LEFI SHEKKIN MIMMA TED’UNA ‘ILEJHI MURIBIN
KALE JA KAWMI ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN KUNTU ‘ALA BEJJINETIN MIN RABBI WE ‘ATANI MINHU REHMETEN FEMEN JENSURUNI MINEL-LAHI ‘IN ‘ASEJTUHU FEMA TEZIDUNENI GAJRE TEHSIRIN
WE JA KAWMI HEDHIHI NAKATU ELLAHI LEKUM ‘AJETEN FEDHERUHA TE’KUL FI ‘ERDI ELLAHI WE LA TEMESSUHA BISU’IN FEJE’HUDHEKUM ‘ADHABUN KARIBUN
FE’AKARUHA FEKALE TEMETTA’U FI DARIKUM THELATHETE ‘EJJAMIN DHALIKE WA’DUN GAJRU MEKDHUBIN
FELEMMA XHA’E ‘EMRUNA NEXHXHEJNA SALIHÆN WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ME’AHU BIREHMETIN MINNA WE MIN HIZJI JEWMI’IDHIN ‘INNE REBBEKE HUWEL-KAWIJUL-’AZIZU
WE ‘EHADHEL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ES-SEJHETU FE’ESBEHU FI DIJARIHIM XHATHIMINE
KE’EN LEM JEGNEW FIHA ‘ELA ‘INNE THEMUDE KEFERU REBBEHUM ‘ELA BU’DÆN LITHEMUDE
WE LEKAD XHA’ET RUSULUNA ‘IBRAHIME BIL-BUSHRA KALU SELAMÆN KALE SELAMUN FEMA LEBITHE ‘EN XHA’E BI’IXHLIN HENIDHIN
FELEMMA RE’A ‘EJDIJEHUM LA TESILU ‘ILEJHI NEKIREHUM WE ‘EWXHESE MINHUM HIFETEN KALU LA TEHAF ‘INNA ‘URSILNA ‘ILA KAWMI LUTIN
WE EMRE’ETUHU KA’IMETUN FEDEHIKET FEBESHSHERNAHA BI’ISHAKA WE MIN WERA’I ‘ISHAKA JA’KUBE
KALET JA WEJLETA ‘E’ELIDU WE ‘ENA ‘AXHUZUN WE HEDHA BA’LI SHEJHÆN ‘INNE HADHA LESHEJ’UN ‘AXHIBUN
KALU ‘ETA’XHEBINE MIN ‘EMRI ELLAHI REHMETU ELLAHI WE BEREKATUHU ‘ALEJKUM ‘EHLEL-BEJTI ‘INNEHU HEMIDUN MEXHIDUN
FELEMMA DHEHEBE ‘AN ‘IBRAHIME ER-REW’U WE XHA’ET/HUL-BUSHRA JUXHADILUNA FI KAWMI LUTIN
‘INNE ‘IBRAHIME LEHELIMUN ‘EWWAHUN MUNIBUN
JA ‘IBRAHIMU ‘A’RID ‘AN HADHA ‘INNEHU KAD XHA’E ‘EMRU RABBIKE WE ‘INNEHUM ‘ATIHIM ‘ADHABUN GAJRU MERDUDIN
WE LEMMA XHA’ET RUSULUNA LUTÆN SI’E BIHIM WE DAKA BIHIM DHER’ÆN WE KALE HADHA JEWMUN ‘ASIBUN
WE XHA’EHU KAWMUHU JUHRA’UNE ‘ILEJHI WE MIN KABLU KANU JA’MELUNE ES-SEJJI’ATI KALE JA KAWMI HA’UULA’ BENATI HUNNE ‘ETHERU LEKUM FE ETTEKU ELLAHE WE LA TUHZUNI FI DEJFI ‘ELEJSE MINKUM REXHULUN RESHIDUN
KALU LEKAD ‘ALIMTE MA LENA FI BENATIKE MIN HEKKIN WE ‘INNEKE LETA’LEMU MA NURIDU
KALE LEW ‘ENNE LI BIKUM KUWETEN ‘EW ‘AWI ‘ILA RUKNIN SHEDIDIN
KALU JA LUTU ‘INNA RUSULU RABBIKE LEN JESILU ‘ILEJKE FE’ESRI BI’EHLIKE BIKIT’IN MINEL-LEJLI WE LA JELTEFIT MINKUM ‘EHEDUN ‘ILLA EMRE’ETEKE ‘INNEHU MUSIBUHA MA ‘ESABEHUM ‘INNE MEW’IDEHUMU ES-SUBHU ‘ELEJSE ES-SUBHU BIKARIBIN
FELEMMA XHA’E ‘EMRUNA XHE’ALNA ‘ALIJEHA SAFILEHA WE ‘EMTERNA ‘ALEJHA HIXHARETEN MIN SIXHXHILIN MENDUDIN
MUSEWWEMETEN ‘INDE RABBIKE WE MA HIJE MINE EDH-DHALIMINE BIBA’IDIN
WE ‘ILA MEDJENE ‘EHAHUM SHU’AJBÆN KALE JA KAWMI A’BUDU ELLAHE MA LEKUM MIN ‘ILEHIN GAJRUHU WE LA TENKUSUL-MIKJA LE WEL-MIZANE ‘INNI ‘ERAKUM BIHAJRIN WE ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘ALEJKUM ‘ADHABE JEWMIN MUHITIN
WE JA KAWMI ‘EWFUL-MIKJALE WEL-MIZANE BIL-KISTI WE LA TEBHASU EN-NASE ‘ESHJA’EHUM WE LA TA’THEW FIL-’ERDI MUFSIDINE
BEKIJETU ELLAHI HAJRUN LEKUM ‘IN KUNTUM MU’UMININE WE MA ‘ENA ‘ALEJKUM BIHEFIDHIN
KALU JA SHU’AJBU ‘ESELATUKE TE’MURUKE ‘EN NETRUKE MA JA’BUDU ‘ABA’UUNA ‘EW ‘EN NEF’ALE FI ‘EMWALINA MA NESHA’U ‘INNEKE LE’ENTEL-HELIMU ER-RESHIDU
KALE JA KAWMI ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN KUNTU ‘ALA BEJJINETIN MIN RABBI WE REZEKANI MINHU RIZKÆN HESENÆN WE MA ‘URIDU ‘EN ‘UHALIFEKUM ‘ILA MA ‘ENHAKUM ‘ANHU ‘IN ‘URIDU ‘ILLAL-’ISLAHE MA ESTETA’TU WE MA TEWFIKI ‘ILLA BILLAHI ‘ALEJHI TEWEKKELTU WE ‘ILEJHI ‘UNIBU
WE JA KAWMI LA JEXHRIMENNEKUM SHIKAKI ‘EN JUSIBEKUM MITHLU MA ‘ESABE KAWME NUHIN ‘EW KAWME HUDIN ‘EW KAWME SALIHIN WE MA KAWMU LUTIN MINKUM BIBA’IDIN
WE ESTEGFIRU REBBEKUM THUMME TUBU ‘ILEJHI ‘INNE RABBI REHIMUN WEDUDUN
KALU JA SHU’AJBU MA NEFKAHU KETHIRÆN MIMMA TEKULU WE ‘INNA LENERAKE FINA DA’IFÆN WE LEWLA REHTUKE LEREXHEMNAKE WE MA ‘ENTE ‘ALEJNA BI’AZIZIN
KALE JA KAWMI ‘EREHTI ‘E’AZZU ‘ALEJKUM MINEL-LAHI WE ETTEHADHTUMUHU WERA’EKUM DHIHRIJÆN ‘INNE RABBI BIMA TA’MELUNE MUHITUN
WE JA KAWMI A’MELU ‘ALA MEKANETIKUM ‘INNI ‘AMILUN SEWFE TA’LEMUNE MEN JE’TIHI ‘ADHABUN JUHZIHI WE MEN HUWE KADHIBUN WE ERTEKIBU ‘INNI ME’AKUM REKIBUN
WE LEMMA XHA’E ‘EMRUNA NEXHXHEJNA SHU’AJBÆN WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ME’AHU BIREHMETIN MINNA WE ‘EHADHETIL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ES-SEJHETU FE’ESBEHU FI DIJARIHIM XHATHIMINE
KE’EN LEM JEGNEW FIHA ‘ELA BU’DÆN LIMEDJENE KEMA BA’IDET THEMUDU
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA MUSA BI’AJATINA WE SULTANIN MUBININ
‘ILA FIR’AWNE WE MELE’IHI FE ETTEBA’U ‘EMRE FIR’AWNE WE MA ‘EMRU FIR’AWNE BIRESHIDIN
JEKDUMU KAWMEHU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI FE’EWREDEHUMU EN-NARE WE BI’SEL-WIRDUL-MEWRUDU
WE ‘UTBI’U FI HEDHIHI LA’NETEN WE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI BI’SE ER-RIFDUL-MERFUDU
DHALIKE MIN ‘ENBA’IL-KURA NEKUSSUHU ‘ALEJKE MINHA KA’IMUN WE HESIDUN
WE MA DHELEMNAHUM WE LEKIN DHELEMU ‘ENFUSEHUM FEMA ‘EGNET ‘ANHUM ‘ALIHETUHUMU ELLETI JED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI MIN SHEJ’IN LEMMA XHA’E ‘EMRU RABBIKE WE MA ZADUHUM GAJRE TETBIBIN
WE KEDHELIKE ‘EHDHU RABBIKE ‘IDHA ‘EHADHEL-KURA WE HIJE DHALIMETUN ‘INNE ‘EHDHEHU ‘ELIMUN SHEDIDUN
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIMEN HAFE ‘ADHABEL-’AHIRETI DHALIKE JEWMUN MEXHMU’UN LEHU EN-NASU WE DHELIKE JEWMUN MESH/HUDUN
WE MA NU’UEHHIRUHU ‘ILLA LI’XHELIN MA’DUDIN
JEWME JE’TI LA TEKELLEMU NEFSUN ‘ILLA BI’IDHNIHI FEMINHUM SHEKIJUN WE SA’IDUN
FE’EMMAL-LEDHINE SHEKU FEFI EN-NARI LEHUM FIHA ZEFIRUN WE SHEHIKUN
HALIDINE FIHA MA DAMETI ES-SEMAWATU WEL-’ERDU ‘ILLA MA SHA’E REBBUKE ‘INNE REBBEKE FA’’ALUN LIMA JURIDU
WE ‘EMMAL-LEDHINE SU’IDU FEFIL-XHENNETI HALIDINE FIHA MA DAMETI ES-SEMAWATU WEL-’ERDU ‘ILLA MA SHA’E REBBUKE ‘ATA’EN GAJRE MEXHDHUDHIN
FELA TEKU FI MIRJETIN MIMMA JA’BUDU HA’UULA’ MA JA’BUDUNE ‘ILLA KEMA JA’BUDU ‘ABA’UUHUM MIN KABLU WE ‘INNA LEMUWEFFUHUM NESIBEHUM GAJRE MENKUSIN
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE FAHTULIFE FIHI WE LEWLA KELIMETUN SEBEKAT MIN RABBIKE LEKUDIJE BEJNEHUM WE ‘INNEHUM LEFI SHEKKIN MINHU MURIBIN
WE ‘INNE KULLA LEMMA LEJUWEFFIJENNEHUM REBBUKE ‘A’MALEHUM ‘INNEHU BIMA JA’MELUNE HABIRUN
FASTEKIM KEMA ‘UMIRTE WE MEN TABE ME’AKE WE LA TETGAW ‘INNEHU BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRUN
WE LA TERKENU ‘ILAL-LEDHINE DHELEMU FETEMESSEKUMU EN-NARU WE MA LEKUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI MIN ‘EWLIJA’E THUMME LA TUNSERUNE
WE ‘EKIMI ES-SELÆTE TEREFEJI EN-NEHARI WE ZULEFÆN MINEL-LEJLI ‘INNEL-HESENATI JUDH/HIBNE ES-SEJJI’ATI DHALIKE DHIKRA LILDHDHAKIRINE
WE ESBIR FE’INNALL-LLAHE LA JUDI’U ‘EXHREL-MUHSININE
FELEWLA KANE MINEL-KURUNI MIN KABLIKUM ‘ULU BEKIJETIN JENHEWNE ‘ANIL-FESADI FIL-’ERDI ‘ILLA KALILÆN MIMMEN ‘ENXHEJNA MINHUM WE ETTEBE’AL-LEDHINE DHELEMU MA ‘UTRIFU FIHI WE KANU MUXHRIMINE
WE MA KANE REBBUKE LIJUHLIKEL-KURA BIDHULMIN WE ‘EHLUHA MUSLIHUNE
WE LEW SHA’E REBBUKE LEXHE’ALE EN-NASE ‘UMMETEN WAHIDETEN WE LA JEZALUNE MUHTELIFINE
‘ILLA MEN REHIME REBBUKE WE LIDHELIKE HALEKAHUM WE TEMMET KELIMETU RABBIKE LE’EMLE’ENNE XHEHENNEME MINEL-XHINNETI WE EN-NASI ‘EXHMA’INE
WE KULLÆN NEKUSSU ‘ALEJKE MIN ‘ENBA’I ER-RUSULI MA NUTHEBBITU BIHI FU’UADEKE WE XHA’EKE FI HEDHIHIL-HEKKU WE MEW’IDHETUN WE DHIKRA LILMU’UMININE
WE KUL LILLEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE A’MELU ‘ALA MEKANETIKUM ‘INNA ‘AMILUNE
WE ENTEDHIRU ‘INNA MUNTEDHIRUNE
WE LILLEHI GAJBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE ‘ILEJHI JURXHA’UL-’EMRU KULLUHU FA’BUD/HU WE TEWEKKEL ‘ALEJHI WE MA REBBUKE BIGAFILIN ‘AMMA TA’MELUNE
‘ELIF-LAM-RA TILKE ‘AJATUL-KITABIL-MUBINI
‘INNA ‘ENZELNAHU KUR’ANÆN ‘AREBIJÆN LE’ALLEKUM TA’KILUNE
NEHNU NEKUSSU ‘ALEJKE ‘EHSENEL-KASESI BIMA ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE HADHAL-KUR’ANE WE ‘IN KUNTE MIN KABLIHI LEMINEL-GAFILINE
‘IDH KALE JUSUFU LI’EBIHI JA ‘EBETI ‘INNI RE’EJTU ‘EHEDE ‘ASHERE KEWKEBÆN WE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE RE’EJTUHUM LI SAXHIDINE
KALE JA BUNEJJE LA TEKSUS RU’UJA KE ‘ALA ‘IHWETIKE FEJEKIDU LEKE KEJDÆN ‘INNE ESH-SHEJTANE LIL’INSANI ‘ADUWUN MUBINUN
WE KEDHELIKE JEXHTEBIKE REBBUKE WE JU’ALLIMUKE MIN TE’WILIL-’EHADITHI WE JUTIMMU NI’METEHU ‘ALEJKE WE ‘ALA ‘ALI JA’KUBE KEMA ‘ETEMMEHA ‘ALA ‘EBEWEJKE MIN KABLU ‘IBRAHIME WE ‘ISHAKA ‘INNE REBBEKE ‘ALIMUN HEKIMUN
LEKAD KANE FI JUSUFE WE ‘IHWETIHI ‘AJATUN LILSSA’ILINE
‘IDH KALU LEJUSUFU WE ‘EHUHU ‘EHEBBU ‘ILA ‘EBINA MINNA WE NEHNU ‘USBETUN ‘INNE ‘EBANA LEFI DELALIN MUBININ
EKTULU JUSUFE ‘EWI ETREHUHU ‘ERDÆN JEHLU LEKUM WEXHHU ‘EBIKUM WE TEKUNU MIN BA’DIHI KAWMÆN SALIHINE
KALE KA’ILUN MINHUM LA TEKTULU JUSUFE WE ‘ELKUHU FI GAJABETIL-XHUBBI JELTEKITHU BA’DU ES-SEJJARETI ‘IN KUNTUM FA’ILINE
KALU JA ‘EBANA MA LEKE LA TE’MENNA ‘ALA JUSUFE WE ‘INNA LEHU LENASIHUNE
‘ERSILHU ME’ANA GADÆN JERTA’ WE JEL’AB WE ‘INNA LEHU LEHAFIDHUNE
KALE ‘INNI LEJEHZUNUNI ‘EN TEDH/HEBU BIHI WE ‘EHAFU ‘EN JE’KULEHU EDH-DHI’BU WE ‘ENTUM ‘ANHU GAFILUNE
KALU LE’IN ‘EKELEHU EDH-DHI’BU WE NEHNU ‘USBETUN ‘INNA ‘IDHÆN LEHASIRUNE
FELEMMA DHEHEBU BIHI WE ‘EXHMA’U ‘EN JEXH’ALUHU FI GAJABETIL-XHUBBI WE ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJHI LETUNEBBI’ENNEHUM BI’EMRIHIM HADHA WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
WE XHA’U ‘EBAHUM ‘ISHA’EN JEBKUNE
KALU JA ‘EBANA ‘INNA DHEHEBNA NESTEBIKU WE TEREKNA JUSUFE ‘INDE META’INA FE’EKELEHU EDH-DHI’BU WE MA ‘ENTE BIMU’UMININ LENA WE LEW KUNNA SADIKINE
WE XHA’U ‘ALA KAMISIHI BIDEMIN KEDHIBIN KALE BEL SEWWELET LEKUM ‘ENFUSUKUM ‘EMRÆN FESEBRUN XHEMILUN WEL-LAHUL-MUSTA’ANU ‘ALA MA TESIFUNE
WE XHA’ET SEJJARETUN FE’ERSELU WE ERIDEHUM FE’EDLA DELWEHU KALE JA BUSHRA HADHA GULAMUN WE ‘ESERRUHU BIDA’ATEN WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN BIMA JA’MELUNE
WE SHEREWHU BITHEMENIN BEHSIN DERAHIME MA’DUDETIN WE KANU FIHI MINE EZ-ZAHIDINE
WE KALEL-LEDHI ESHTERAHU MIN MISRE LI’IMRE’ETIHI ‘EKRIMI METHWAHU ‘ASA ‘EN JENFE’ANA ‘EW NETTEHIDHEHU WELEDÆN WE KEDHELIKE MEKKENNA LIJUSUFE FIL-’ERDI WE LINU’ALLIMEHU MIN TE’WILIL-’EHADITHI WEL-LAHU GALIBUN ‘ALA ‘EMRIHI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’
WE LEMMA BELEGA ‘ESHUDDEHU ‘ATEJNAHU HUKMÆN WE ‘ILMÆN WE KEDHELIKE NEXHZIL-MUHSININE
WE RAWEDET/HU ELLETI HUWE FI BEJTIHA ‘AN NEFSIHI WE GALLEKATIL-’EBWABE WE KALET HEJTE LEKE KALE MA’ADHEL-LAHI ‘INNEHU RABBI ‘EHSENE METHWAJE ‘INNEHU LA JUFLIHU EDH-DHALIMUNE
WE LEKAD HEMMET BIHI WE HEMME BIHA LEWLA ‘EN RE’A BURHANE RABBIHI KEDHALIKE LINESRIFE ‘ANHU ES-SU’E WEL-FEHSHA’E ‘INNEHU MIN ‘IBADINAL-MUHLESINE
WE ESTEBEKAL-BABE WE KADDET KAMISEHU MIN DUBURIN WE ‘ELFEJA SEJJIDEHA LEDAL-BABI KALET MA XHEZA’U MEN ‘ERADE BI’EHLIKE SU’ÆN ‘ILLA ‘EN JUSXHENE ‘EW ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
KALE HIJE RAWEDETNI ‘AN NEFSI WE SHEHIDE SHAHIDUN MIN ‘EHLIHA ‘IN KANE KAMISUHU KUDDE MIN KUBULIN FESEDEKAT WE HUWE MINEL-KADHIBINE
WE ‘IN KANE KAMISUHU KUDDE MIN DUBURIN FEKEDHEBET WE HUWE MINE ES-SADIKINE
FELEMMA RE’A KAMISEHU KUDDE MIN DUBURIN KALE ‘INNEHU MIN KEJDIKUNNE ‘INNE KEJDEKUNNE ‘ADHIMUN
JUSUFU ‘A’RID ‘AN HADHA WE ESTEGFIRI LIDHENBIKI ‘INNEKI KUNTI MINEL-HATI’INE
WE KALE NISWETUN FIL-MEDINETI EMRE’ETUL-’AZIZI TURAWIDU FETAHA ‘AN NEFSIHI KAD SHEGAFEHA HUBBÆN ‘INNA LENERAHA FI DELALIN MUBININ
FELEMMA SEMI’AT BIMEKRIHINNE ‘ERSELET ‘ILEJHINNE WE ‘A’TEDET LEHUNNE MUTTEKE’EN WE ‘ATET KULLE WAHIDETIN MINHUNNE SIKKINÆN WE KALETI EHRUXH ‘ALEJHINNE FELEMMA RE’EJNEHU ‘EKBERNEHU WE KATTA’NE ‘EJDIJEHUNNE WE KULNE HASHE LILLAHI MA HADHA BESHERÆN ‘IN HADHA
KALET FEDHALIKUNNEL-LEDHI LUMTUNNENI FIHI WE LEKAD RAWEDTTUHU ‘AN NEFSIHI FASTA’SEME WE LE’IN LEM JEF’AL MA ‘AMURUHU LEJUSXHENENNE WE LEJEKUNÆN MINE ES-SAGIRINE
KALE RABBI ES-SIXHNU ‘EHEBBU ‘ILEJJE MIMMA JED’UNENI ‘ILEJHI WE ‘ILLA TESRIF ‘ANNI KEJDEHUNNE ‘ESBU ‘ILEJHINNE WE ‘EKUN MINEL-XHAHILINE
FASTEXHABE LEHU REBBUHU FESEREFE ‘ANHU KEJDEHUNNE ‘INNEHU HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-’ALIMU
THUMME BEDA LEHUM MIN BA’DI MA RE’EWL-’AJATI LEJESXHUNUNNEHU HETTA HININ
WE DEHALE ME’AHU ES-SIXHNE FETEJANI KALE ‘EHEDUHUMA ‘INNI ‘ERANI ‘A’SIRU HAMRÆN WE KALEL-’AHARU ‘INNI ‘ERANI ‘EHMILU FEWKA RE’SI HUBZÆN TE’KULUT-TEJRU MINHU NEBBI’NA BITE’WILIHI ‘INNA NERAKE MINEL-MUHSININE
KALE LA JE’TIKUMA TA’AMUN TURZEKANIHI ‘ILLA NEBBE’TUKUMA BITE’WILIHI KABLE ‘EN JE’TIJEKUMA DHALIKUMA MIMMA ‘ALLEMENI RABBI ‘INNI TEREKTU MILLETE KAWMIN LA JU’UMINUNE BILLAHI WE HUM BIL-’AHIRETI HUM KAFIRUNE
WE ETTEBA’TU MILLETE ‘ABA’I ‘IBRAHIME WE ‘ISHAKA WE JA’KUBE MA KANE LENA ‘EN NUSHRIKE BILLAHI MIN SHEJ’IN DHALIKE MIN FEDLI ELLAHI ‘ALEJNA WE ‘ALA EN-NASI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JESHKURUNE
JA SAHIBEJI ES-SIXHNI ‘E’ERBABUN MUTEFERRIKUNE HAJRUN ‘EMI ELLAHUL-WAHIDUL-KAHHARU
MA TA’BUDUNE MIN DUNIHI ‘ILLA ‘ESMA’EN SEMMEJTUMUHA ‘ENTUM WE ‘ABA’UUKUM MA ‘ENZELEL-LAHU BIHA MIN SULTANIN ‘INIL-HUKMU ‘ILLA LILLAHI ‘EMERE ‘ELLA TA’BUDU ‘ILLA ‘IJAHU DHALIKE ED-DINUL-KAJJIMU WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
JA SAHIBEJI ES-SIXHNI ‘EMMA ‘EHEDUKUMA FEJESKI REBBEHU HAMRÆN WE ‘EMMAL-’AHARU FEJUSLEBU FETE’KULUT-TEJRU MIN RE’SIHI KUDIJEL-’EMRUL-LEDHI FIHI TESTEFTIJANI
WE KALE LILLEDHI DHENNE ‘ENNEHU NAXHIN MINHUMA EDHKURNI ‘INDE RABBIKE FE’ENSAHU ESH-SHEJTANU DHIKRE RABBIHI FELEBITHE FI ES-SIXHNI BID’A SININE
WE KALEL-MELIKU ‘INNI ‘ERA SEB’A BEKARATIN SIMANIN JE’KULUHUNNE SEB’UN ‘IXHAFUN WE SEB’A SUNBULATIN HUDRIN WE ‘UHARE JA BISATIN JA ‘EJJUHAL-MELE’U ‘EFTUNI FI RU’UJA JE ‘IN KUNTUM LILRRU’UJA TA’BURUNE
KALU ‘EDGATHU ‘EHLAMIN WE MA NEHNU BITE’WILIL-’EHLAMI BI’ALIMINE
WE KALEL-LEDHI NEXHA MINHUMA WE EIDDEKERE BA’DE ‘UMMETIN ‘ENA ‘UNEBBI’UKUM BITE’WILIHI FE’ERSILUNI
JUSUFU ‘EJJUHA ES-SIDDIKU ‘EFTINA FI SEB’I BEKARATIN SIMANIN JE’KULUHUNNE SEB’UN ‘IXHAFUN WE SEB’I SUNBULATIN HUDRIN WE ‘UHARE JA BISATIN LE’ALLI ‘ERXHI’U ‘ILA EN-NASI LE’ALLEHUM JA’LEMUNE
KALE TEZRA’UNE SEB’A SININE DE’EBÆN FEMA HESEDTUM FEDHERUHU FI SUNBULIHI ‘ILLA KALILÆN MIMMA TE’KULUNE
THUMME JE’TI MIN BA’DI DHALIKE SEB’UN SHIDADUN JE’KULNE MA KADDEMTUM LEHUNNE ‘ILLA KALILÆN MIMMA TUHSINUNE
THUMME JE’TI MIN BA’DI DHALIKE ‘AMUN FIHI JUGATHU EN-NASU WE FIHI JA’SIRUNE
WE KALEL-MELIKU E’TUNI BIHI FELEMMA XHA’EHU ER-RESULU KALE ERXHI’ ‘ILA RABBIKE FAS’ELHU MA BALU EN-NISWETIL-LATI KATTA’NE ‘EJDIJEHUNNE ‘INNE RABBI BIKEJDIHINNE ‘ALIMUN
KALE MA HATBUKUNNE ‘IDH RAWEDTTUNNE JUSUFE ‘AN NEFSIHI KULNE HASHE LILLAHI MA ‘ALIMNA ‘ALEJHI MIN SU’IN KALETI EMRE’ETUL-’AZIZIL-’ANE HESHESEL-HEKKU ‘ENA RAWEDTTUHU ‘AN NEFSIHI WE ‘INNEHU LEMINE ES-SADIKINE
DHALIKE LIJA’LEME ‘ENNI LEM ‘EHUNHU BIL-GAJBI WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE LA JEHDI KEJDEL-HA’ININE
WE MA ‘UBERRI’U NEFSI ‘INNE EN-NEFSE LE’EMMARETUN BIS-SU’I ‘ILLA MA REHIME RABBI ‘INNE RABBI GAFURUN REHIMUN
WE KALEL-MELIKU E’TUNI BIHI ‘ESTEHLISHU LINEFSI FELEMMA KELLEMEHU KALE ‘INNEKEL-JEWME LEDEJNA MEKINUN ‘EMINUN
KALE EXH’ALNI ‘ALA HAZA’INIL-’ERDI ‘INNI HEFIDHUN ‘ALIMUN
WE KEDHELIKE MEKKENNA LIJUSUFE FIL-’ERDI JETEBEWWE’U MINHA HEJTHU JESHA’U NUSIBU BIREHMETINA MEN NESHA’U WE LA NUDI’U ‘EXHREL-MUHSININE
WE LE’EXHRUL-’AHIRETI HAJRUN LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU WE KANU JETTEKUNE
WE XHA’E ‘IHWETU JUSUFE FEDEHALU ‘ALEJHI FE’AREFEHUM WE HUM LEHU MUNKIRUNE
WE LEMMA XHEHHEZEHUM BIXHEHAZIHIM KALE E’TUNI BI’EHIN LEKUM MIN ‘EBIKUM ‘ELA TEREWNE ‘ENNI ‘UFIL-KEJLE WE ‘ENA HAJRUL-MUNZILINE
FE’IN LEM TE’TUNI BIHI FELA KEJLE LEKUM ‘INDI WE LA TEKREBUNI
KALU SENURAWIDU ‘ANHU ‘EBAHU WE ‘INNA LEFA’ILUNE
WE KALE LIFITJANIHI EXH’ALU BIDA’ATEHUM FI RIHALIHIM LE’ALLEHUM JA’RIFUNEHA ‘IDHA ENKALEBU ‘ILA ‘EHLIHIM LE’ALLEHUM JERXHI’UNE
FELEMMA REXHA’U ‘ILA ‘EBIHIM KALU JA ‘EBANA MUNI’A MINNAL-KEJLU FE’ERSIL ME’ANA ‘EHANA NEKTEL WE ‘INNA LEHU LEHAFIDHUNE
KALE HEL ‘AMENUKUM ‘ALEJHI ‘ILLA KEMA ‘EMINTUKUM ‘ALA ‘EHIHI MIN KABLU FE-ELLAHU HAJRUN HAFIDHÆN WE HUWE ‘ERHEMU ER-RAHIMINE
WE LEMMA FETEHU META’AHUM WE XHEDU BIDA’ATEHUM RUDDET ‘ILEJHIM KALU JA ‘EBANA MA NEBGI HEDHIHI BIDA’ATUNA RUDDET ‘ILEJNA WE NEMIRU ‘EHLENA WE NEHFEDHU ‘EHANA WE NEZDADU KEJLE BA’IRIN DHALIKE KEJLUN JESIRUN
KALE LEN ‘URSILEHU ME’AKUM HETTA TU’UTUNI MEWTHIKÆN MINEL-LAHI LETE’TUNENI BIHI ‘ILLA ‘EN JUHATE BIKUM FELEMMA ‘ATEWHU MEWTHIKAHUM KALEL-LAHU ‘ALA MA NEKULU WE KILUN
WE KALE JA BENIJE LA TEDHULU MIN BABIN WAHIDIN WE EDHULU MIN ‘EBWABIN MUTEFERRIKATIN WE MA ‘UGNI ‘ANKUM MINEL-LAHI MIN SHEJ’IN ‘INIL-HUKMU ‘ILLA LILLAHI ‘ALEJHI TEWEKKELTU WE ‘ALEJHI FELJETEWEKKELIL-MUTEWEKKILUNE
WE LEMMA DEHALU MIN HEJTHU ‘EMEREHUM ‘EBUHUM MMA KANE JUGNI ‘ANHUM MMINEL-LAHI MIN SHEJ’IN ‘ILLA HAXHETEN FI NEFSI JA’KUBE KADAHA WE ‘INNEHU LEDHU ‘ILMIN LIMA ‘ALLEMNAHU WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
WE LEMMA DEHALU ‘ALA JUSUFE ‘AWA ‘ILEJHI ‘EHAHU KALE ‘INNI ‘ENA ‘EHUKE FELA TEBTE’IS BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
FELEMMA XHEHHEZEHUM BIXHEHAZIHIM XHE’ALE ES-SIKAJETE FI REHLI ‘EHIHI THUMME ‘EDHDHENE MU’UEDHDHINUN ‘EJJETUHAL-’IRU ‘INNEKUM LESARIKUNE
KALU WE ‘EKBELU ‘ALEJHIM MADHA TEFKIDUNE
KALU NEFKIDU SUWA’AL-MELIKI WE LIMEN XHA’E BIHI HIMLU BA’IRIN WE ‘ENA BIHI ZA’IMUN
KALU TE-ELLAHI LEKAD ‘ALIMTUM MA XHI’NA LINUFSIDE FIL-’ERDI WE MA KUNNA SARIKINE
KALU FEMA XHEZA’UUHU ‘IN KUNTUM KADHIBINE
KALU XHEZA’UUHU MEN WUXHIDE FI REHLIHI FEHUWE XHEZA’UUHU KEDHALIKE NEXHZI EDH-DHALIMINE
FEBEDE’E BI’EW’IJETIHIM KABLE WI’A’I ‘EHIHI THUMME ESTEHREXHEHA MIN WI’A’I ‘EHIHI KEDHALIKE KIDNA LIJUSUFE MA KANE LIJE’HUDHE ‘EHAHU FI DINIL-MELIKI ‘ILLA ‘EN JESHA’EL-LAHU NERFA’U DEREXHATIN MEN NESHA’U WE FEWKA KULLI DHI ‘ILMIN ‘ALIMUN
KALU ‘IN JESRIK FEKAD SEREKA ‘EHUN LEHU MIN KABLU FE’ESERREHA JUSUFU FI NEFSIHI WE LEM JUBDIHA LEHUM KALE ‘ENTUM SHERRUN MEKANÆN WEL-LAHU ‘A’LEMU BIMA TESIFUNE
KALU JA ‘EJJUHAL-’AZIZU ‘INNE LEHU ‘EBÆN SHEJHÆN KEBIRÆN FEHUDH ‘EHEDENA MEKANEHU ‘INNA NERAKE MINEL-MUHSININE
KALE MA’ADHEL-LAHI ‘EN NE’HUDHE ‘ILLA MEN WEXHEDNA META’ANA ‘INDEHU ‘INNA ‘IDHÆN LEDHALIMUNE
FELEMMA ESTEJ’ESU MINHU HALESU NEXHIJÆN KALE KEBIRUHUM ‘ELEM TA’LEMU ‘ENNE ‘EBAKUM KAD ‘EHADHE ‘ALEJKUM MEWTHIKÆN MINEL-LAHI WE MIN KABLU MA FERRETTUM FI JUSUFE FELEN ‘EBREHEL-’ERDE HETTA JE’DHENE LI ‘EBI ‘EW JEHKUMEL-LAHU LI WE HUWE HAJRUL-HAKIMINE
ERXHI’U ‘ILA ‘EBIKUM FEKULU JA ‘EBANA ‘INNE EBNEKE SEREKA WE MA SHEHIDNA ‘ILLA BIMA ‘ALIMNA WE MA KUNNA LILGAJBI HAFIDHINE
WE ES’ELIL-KARJETEL-LETI KUNNA FIHA WEL-’IREL-LETI ‘EKBELNA FIHA WE ‘INNA LESADIKUNE
KALE BEL SEWWELET LEKUM ‘ENFUSUKUM ‘EMRÆN FESEBRUN XHEMILUN ‘ASALLAHU ‘EN JE’TIJENI BIHIM XHEMI’ÆN ‘INNEHU HUWEL-’ALIMUL-HEKIMU
WE TEWELLA ‘ANHUM WE KALE JA ‘ESEFA ‘ALA JUSUFE WE EBJEDDET ‘AJNAHU MINEL-HUZNI FEHUWE KEDHIMUN
KALU TE-ELLAHI TEFTE’U TEDHKURU JUSUFE HETTA TEKUNE HEREDÆN ‘EW TEKUNE MINEL-HALIKINE
KALE ‘INNEMA ‘ESHKU BETHTHI WE HUZNI ‘ILA ELLAHI WE ‘A’LEMU MINEL-LAHI MA LA TA’LEMUNE
JA BENIJE EDH/HEBU FETEHESSESU MIN JUSUFE WE ‘EHIHI WE LA TEJ’ESU MIN REWHI ELLAHI ‘INNEHU LA JEJ’ESU MIN REWHI ELLAHI ‘ILLAL-KAWMUL-KAFIRUNE
FELEMMA DEHALU ‘ALEJHI KALU JA ‘EJJUHAL-’AZIZU MESSENA WE ‘EHLENA ED-DURRU WE XHI’NA BIBIDA’ATIN MUZXHÆTIN FE’EWFI LENAL-KEJLE WE TESEDDEK ‘ALEJNA ‘INNALL-LLAHE JEXHZIL-MUTESEDDIKINE
KALE HEL ‘ALIMTUM MA FE’ALTUM BIJUSUFE WE ‘EHIHI ‘IDH ‘ENTUM XHAHILUNE
KALU ‘E’INNEKE LE’ENTE JUSUFU KALE ‘ENA JUSUFU WE HEDHA ‘EHI KAD MENNEL-LAHU ‘ALEJNA ‘INNEHU MEN JETTEKI WE JESBIR FE’INNALL-LLAHE LA JUDI’U ‘EXHREL-MUHSININE
KALU TE-ELLAHI LEKAD ‘ATHEREKEL-LAHU ‘ALEJNA WE ‘IN KUNNA LEHATI’INE
KALE LA TETHRIBE ‘ALEJKUMUL-JEWME JEGFIRU ELLAHU LEKUM WE HUWE ‘ERHEMU ER-RAHIMINE
EDH/HEBU BIKAMISI HADHA FE’ELKUHU ‘ALA WEXHHI ‘EBI JE’TI BESIRÆN WE ‘TUNI BI’EHLIKUM ‘EXHMA’INE
WE LEMMA FESELETIL-’IRU KALE ‘EBUHUM ‘INNI LE’EXHIDU RIHE JUSUFE LEWLA ‘EN TUFENNIDUNI
KALU TE-ELLAHI ‘INNEKE LEFI DELALIKEL-KADIMI
FELEMMA ‘EN XHA’EL-BESHIRU ‘ELKAHU ‘ALA WEXHHIHI FARTEDDE BESIRÆN KALE ‘ELEM ‘EKUL LEKUM ‘INNI ‘A’LEMU MINEL-LAHI MA LA TA’LEMUNE
KALU JA ‘EBANA ESTEGFIR LENA DHUNUBENA ‘INNA KUNNA HATI’INE
KALE SEWFE ‘ESTEGFIRU LEKUM RABBI ‘INNEHU HUWEL-GAFURU ER-REHIMU
FELEMMA DEHALU ‘ALA JUSUFE ‘AWA ‘ILEJHI ‘EBEWEJHI WE KALE EDHULU MISRE ‘IN SHA’EL-LAHU ‘AMININE
WE REFE’A ‘EBEWEJHI ‘ALEL-’ARSHI WE HARRU LEHU SUXHXHEDÆN WE KALE JA ‘EBETI HADHA TE’WILU RU’UJA J MIN KABLU KAD XHE’ALEHA RABBI HEKKÆN WE KAD ‘EHSENE BI ‘IDH ‘EHREXHENI MINE ES-SIXHNI WE XHA’E BIKUM MINEL-BEDWI MIN BA’DI ‘EN NEZEGA ESH-SHEJTANU BEJNI WE 
REBBI KAD ‘ATEJTENI MINEL-MULKI WE ‘ALLEMTENI MIN TE’WILIL-’EHADITHI FATIRE ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘ENTE WE LIJI FI ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETI TEWEFFENI MUSLIMÆN WE ‘ELHIKNI BIS-SALIHINE
DHALIKE MIN ‘ENBA’IL-GAJBI NUHIHI ‘ILEJKE WE MA KUNTE LEDEJHIM ‘IDH ‘EXHMA’U ‘EMREHUM WE HUM JEMKURUNE
WE MA ‘EKTHERU EN-NASI WE LEW HERESTE BIMU’UMININE
WE MA TES’ELUHUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN ‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA DHIKRUN LIL’ALEMINE
WE KE’EJJIN MIN ‘AJETIN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI JEMURRUNE ‘ALEJHA WE HUM ‘ANHA MU’RIDUNE
WE MA JU’UMINU ‘EKTHERUHUM BILLAHI ‘ILLA WE HUM MUSHRIKUNE
‘EFE’EMINU ‘EN TE’TIJEHUM GASHIJETUN MIN ‘ADHABI ELLAHI ‘EW TE’TIJEHUMU ES-SA’ATU BEGTETEN WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
KUL HEDHIHI SEBILI ‘ED’U ‘ILA ELLAHI ‘ALA BESIRETIN ‘ENA WE MENI ETTEBE’ANI WE SUBHANEL-LAHI WE MA ‘ENA MINEL-MUSHRIKINE
WE MA ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE ‘ILLA RIXHALÆN NUHI ‘ILEJHIM MIN ‘EHLIL-KURA ‘EFELEM JESIRU FIL-’ERDI FEJENDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM WE LEDARUL-’AHIRETI HAJRUN LILLEDHINE ETTEKAW ‘EFELA TA’KILUNE
HETTA ‘IDHA ESTEJ’ESE ER-RUSULU WE DHENNU ‘ENNEHUM KAD KUDHIBU XHA’EHUM NESRUNA FENUXHXHIJE MEN NESHA’U WE LA JUREDDU BE’SUNA ‘ANIL-KAWMIL-MUXHRIMINE
LEKAD KANE FI KASESIHIM ‘IBRETUN LI’WLIL-’ELBABI MA KANE HEDITHÆN JUFTERA WE LEKIN TESDIKAL-LEDHI BEJNE JEDEJHI WE TEFSILE KULLI SHEJ’IN WE HUDEN WE REHMETEN LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
‘ELIF-LAM-MIM-RA TILKE ‘AJATUL-KITABI WEL-LEDHI ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJKE MIN RABBIKEL-HEKKU WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JU’UMINUNE
ELLAHUL-LEDHI REFE’A ES-SEMAWATI BIGAJRI ‘AMEDIN TEREWNEHA THUMME ESTEWA ‘ALEL-’ARSHI WE SEHHARE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE KULLUN JEXHRI LI’XHELIN MUSEMMEN JUDEBBIRUL-’EMRE JUFESSILUL-’AJATI LE’ALLEKUM BILIKA’I RABBIKUM TUKINUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI MEDDEL-’ERDE WE XHE’ALE FIHA REWASIJE WE ‘ENHARÆN WE MIN KULLI ETH-THEMERATI XHE’ALE FIHA ZEWXHEJNI ETHNEJNI JUGSHIL-LEJLE EN-NEHARE ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JETEFEKKERUNE
WE FIL-’ERDI KITA’UN MUTEXHAWIRATUN WE XHENNATUN MIN ‘A’NABIN WE ZER’UN WE NEHILUN SINWANUN WE GAJRU SINWANIN JUSKA BIMA’IN WAHIDIN WE NUFEDDILU BA’DEHA ‘ALA BA’DIN FIL-’UKULI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JA’KILUNE
WE ‘IN TA’XHEB FE’AXHEBUN KAWLUHUM ‘E’IDHA KUNNA TURABÆN ‘E’INNA LEFI HALKIN XHEDIDIN ‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BIREBBIHIM WE ‘ULA’IKEL-’EGLALU FI ‘A’NAKIHIM WE ‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABU EN-NARI HUM FIHA HALIDUNE
WE JESTA’XHILUNEKE BIS-SEJJI’ETI KABLEL-HESENETI WE KAD HALET MIN KABLIHIMUL-METHULATU WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEDHU MEGFIRETIN LILNNASI ‘ALA DHULMIHIM WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LESHEDIDUL-’IKABI
WE JEKULUL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEWLA ‘UNZILE ‘ALEJHI ‘AJETUN MIN RABBIHI ‘INNEMA ‘ENTE MUNDHIRUN WE LIKULLI KAWMIN HADIN
ELLAHU JA’LEMU MA TEHMILU KULLU ‘UNTHA WE MA TEGIDUL-’ERHAMU WE MA TEZDADU WE KULLU SHEJ’IN ‘INDEHU BIMIKDARIN
‘ALIMUL-GAJBI WE ESH-SHEHADETIL-KEBIRUL-MUTA’ALI
SEWA’UN MINKUM MEN ‘ESERREL-KAWLE WE MEN XHEHERE BIHI WE MEN HUWE MUSTEHFIN BIL-LEJLI WE SARIBUN BIN-NEHARI
LEHU MU’AKKIBATUN MIN BEJNI JEDEJHI WE MIN HALFIHI JEHFEDHUNEHU MIN ‘EMRI ELLAHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JUGAJJIRU MA BIKAWMIN HETTA JUGAJJIRU MA BI’ENFUSIHIM WE ‘IDHA ‘ERADEL-LAHU BIKAWMIN SU’ÆN FELA MEREDDE LEHU WE MA LEHUM MIN DUNIHI MIN WE E-
HUWEL-LEDHI JURIKUMUL-BERKA HAWFÆN WE TEMA’ÆN WE JUNSHI’U ES-SEHABE ETH-THIKALE
WE JUSEBBIHU ER-RA’DU BIHEMDIHI WEL-MELA’IKETU MIN HIFETIHI WE JURSILU ES-SEWA’IKA FEJUSIBU BIHA MEN JESHA’U WE HUM JUXHADILUNE FI ELLAHI WE HUWE SHEDIDUL-MIHALI
LEHU DA’WETUL-HEKKI WEL-LEDHINE JED’UNE MIN DUNIHI LA JESTEXHIBUNE LEHUM BISHEJ’IN ‘ILLA KEBASITI KEFFEJHI ‘ILAL-MA’I LIJEBLUGA FAHU WE MA HUWE BIBALIGIHI WE MA DU’A’UL-KAFIRINE ‘ILLA FI DELALIN
WE LILLEHI JESXHUDU MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI TEW’ÆN WE KERHÆN WE DHILALUHUM BIL-GUDUWI WEL-’ASALI
KUL MEN REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI KULI ELLAHU KUL ‘EFATTEHADHTUM MIN DUNIHI ‘EWLIJA’E LA JEMLIKUNE LI’NFUSIHIM NEF’ÆN WE LA DERRÆN KUL HEL JESTEWIL-’A’MA WEL-BESIRU ‘EM HEL TESTEWI EDH-DHULUMATU WE EN-NUR ‘EM XHE’ALU LILLAHI SHUREKA’E HALEKU KEHALKIHI F
‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FESALET ‘EWDIJETUN BIKADERIHA FAHTEMELE ES-SEJLU ZEBEDÆN RABIÆN WE MIMMA JUKIDUNE ‘ALEJHI FI EN-NARI EBTIGA’E HILJETIN ‘EW META’IN ZEBEDUN MITHLUHU KEDHALIKE JEDRIBU ELLAHUL-HEKKA WEL-BATILE FE’EMMA EZ-ZEBEDU FEJEDH/HEBU XHUFA
LILLEDHINE ESTEXHABU LIREBBIHIMUL-HUSNA WEL-LEDHINE LEM JESTEXHIBU LEHU LEW ‘ENNE LEHUM MA FIL-’ERDI XHEMI’ÆN WE MITHLEHU ME’AHU LAFTEDEW BIHI ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM SU’UL-HISABI WE ME’WAHUM XHEHENNEMU WE BI’SEL-MIHADU
‘EFEMEN JA’LEMU ‘ENNEMA ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJKE MIN RABBIKEL-HEKKU KEMEN HUWE ‘A’MA ‘INNEMA JETEDHEKKERU ‘ULUL-’ELBABI
EL-LEDHINE JUFUNE BI’AHDI ELLAHI WE LA JENKUDUNEL-MITHAKA
WEL-LEDHINE JESILUNE MA ‘EMEREL-LAHU BIHI ‘EN JUSELE WE JEHSHEWNE REBBEHUM WE JEHAFUNE SU’EL-HISABI
WEL-LEDHINE SEBERU EBTIGA’E WEXHHI RABBIHIM WE ‘EKAMU ES-SELÆTE WE ‘ENFEKU MIMMA REZEKNAHUM SIRRÆN WE ‘ALANIJETEN WE JEDRE’UNE BIL-HESENETI ES-SEJJI’ETE ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM ‘UKBA ED-DARI
XHENNATU ‘ADNIN JEDHULUNEHA WE MEN SELEHE MIN ‘ABA’IHIM WE ‘EZWAXHIHIM WE DHURRIJATIHIM WEL-MELA’IKETU JEDHULUNE ‘ALEJHIM MIN KULLI BABIN
SELAMUN ‘ALEJKUM BIMA SEBERTUM FENI’ME ‘UKBA ED-DARI
WEL-LEDHINE JENKUDUNE ‘AHDEL-LAHI MIN BA’DI MITHAKIHI WE JEKTA’UNE MA ‘EMEREL-LAHU BIHI ‘EN JUSELE WE JUFSIDUNE FIL-’ERDI ‘ULA’IKE LEHUMUL-LA’NETU WE LEHUM SU’U ED-DARI
ELLAHU JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U WE JEKDIRU WE FERIHU BIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE MAL-HEJÆTU ED-DUNJA FIL-’AHIRETI ‘ILLA META’UN
WE JEKULUL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEWLA ‘UNZILE ‘ALEJHI ‘AJETUN MIN RABBIHI KUL ‘INNALL-LLAHE JUDILLU MEN JESHA’U WE JEHDI ‘ILEJHI MEN ‘ENABE
EL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE TETME’INNU KULUBUHUM BIDHIKRI ELLAHI ‘ELA BIDHIKRI ELLAHI TETME’INNUL-KULUBU
EL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI TUBA LEHUM WE HUSNU ME’ABIN
KEDHALIKE ‘ERSELNAKE FI ‘UMMETIN KAD HALET MIN KABLIHA ‘UMEMUN LITETLUWE ‘ALEJHIMUL-LEDHI ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE WE HUM JEKFURUNE BIR-REHMENI KUL HUWE RABBI LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE ‘ALEJHI TEWEKKELTU WE ‘ILEJHI METABI
WE LEW ‘ENNE KUR’ANÆN SUJJIRET BIHIL-XHIBALU ‘EW KUTTI’AT BIHIL-’ERDU ‘EW KULLIME BIHIL-MEWTA BEL LILLAHIL-’EMRU XHEMI’ÆN ‘EFELEM JEJ’ESIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘EN LEW JESHA’U ELLAHU LEHEDA EN-NASE XHEMI’ÆN WE LA JEZALUL-LEDHINE KEFERU TUSIBUHUM BIMA SENA’U KAR
WE LEKADI ESTUHZI’E BIRUSULIN MIN KABLIKE FE’EMLEJTU LILLEDHINE KEFERU THUMME ‘EHADHTUHUM FEKEJFE KANE ‘IKABI
‘EFEMEN HUWE KA’IMUN ‘ALA KULLI NEFSIN BIMA KESEBET WE XHE’ALU LILLAHI SHUREKA’E KUL SEMMUHUM ‘EM TUNEBBI’UNEHU BIMA LA JA’LEMU FIL-’ERDI ‘EM BIDHAHIRIN MINEL-KAWLI BEL ZUJJINE LILLEDHINE KEFERU MEKRUHUM WE SUDDU ‘ANI ES-SEBILI WE MEN JUDLILI ELLAHU FEMA 
LEHUM ‘ADHABUN FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE LE’ADHABUL-’AHIRETI ‘ESHEKKU WE MA LEHUM MINEL-LAHI MIN WAKIN
METHELUL-XHENNETI ELLETI WU’IDEL-MUTTEKUNE TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU ‘UKULUHA DA’IMUN WE DHILLUHA TILKE ‘UKBAL-LEDHINE ETTEKAW WE ‘UKBAL-KAFIRINE EN-NARU
WEL-LEDHINE ‘ATEJNAHUMUL-KITABE JEFREHUNE BIMA ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJKE WE MINEL-’EHZABI MEN JUNKIRU BA’DEHU KUL ‘INNEMA ‘UMIRTU ‘EN ‘A’BUDEL-LAHE WE LA ‘USHRIKE BIHI ‘ILEJHI ‘ED’U WE ‘ILEJHI ME’ABI
WE KEDHELIKE ‘ENZELNAHU HUKMÆN ‘AREBIJÆN WE LE’INI ETTEBA’TE ‘EHWA’EHUM BA’DEMA XHA’EKE MINEL-’ILMI MA LEKE MINEL-LAHI MIN WE LIJIN WE LA WAKIN
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA RUSULÆN MIN KABLIKE WE XHE’ALNA LEHUM ‘EZWAXHÆN WE DHURRIJETEN WE MA KANE LIRESULIN ‘EN JE’TIJE BI’AJETIN ‘ILLA BI’IDHNI ELLAHI LIKULLI ‘EXHELIN KITABUN
JEMHU ELLAHU MA JESHA’U WE JUTHBITU WE ‘INDEHU ‘UMMUL-KITABI
WE ‘IN MA NURIJENNEKE BA’DEL-LEDHI NA’IDUHUM ‘EW NETEWEFFEJENNEKE FE’INNEMA ‘ALEJKEL-BELAGU WE ‘ALEJNAL-HISABU
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNA NE’TIL-’ERDE NENKUSUHA MIN ‘ETRAFIHA WEL-LAHU JEHKUMU LA MU’AKKIBE LIHUKMIHI WE HUWE SERI’UL-HISABI
WE KAD MEKEREL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM FELILLAHIL-MEKRU XHEMI’ÆN JA’LEMU MA TEKSIBU KULLU NEFSIN WE SEJA’LEMUL-KUFFARU LIMEN ‘UKBA ED-DARI
WE JEKULUL-LEDHINE KEFERU LESTE MURSELÆN KUL KEFA BILLAHI SHEHIDÆN BEJNI WE BEJNEKUM WE MEN ‘INDEHU ‘ILMUL-KITABI
‘ELIF-LAM-RA KITABUN ‘ENZELNAHU ‘ILEJKE LITUHRIXHE EN-NASE MINE EDH-DHULUMATI ‘ILA EN-NUR BI’IDHNI RABBIHIM ‘ILA SIRATIL-’AZIZIL-HEMIDI
ELLAHIL-LEDHI LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE WEJLUN LILKAFIRINE MIN ‘ADHABIN SHEDIDIN
EL-LEDHINE JESTEHIBBUNEL-HEJÆTE ED-DUNJA ‘ALEL-’AHIRETI WE JESUDDUNE ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI WE JEBGUNEHA ‘IWEXHÆN ‘ULA’IKE FI DELALIN BA’IDIN
WE MA ‘ERSELNA MIN RESULIN ‘ILLA BILISANI KAWMIHI LIJUBEJJINE LEHUM FEJUDILLU ELLAHU MEN JESHA’U WE JEHDI MEN JESHA’U WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA MUSA BI’AJATINA ‘EN ‘EHRIXH KAWMEKE MINE EDH-DHULUMATI ‘ILA EN-NURI WE DHEKKIRHUM BI’EJJAMI ELLAHI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKULLI SEBBARIN SHEKURIN
WE ‘IDH KALE MUSA LIKAWMIHI EDHKURU NI’METEL-LAHI ‘ALEJKUM ‘IDH ‘ENXHAKUM MIN ‘ALI FIR’AWNE JESUMUNEKUM SU’EL-’ADHABI WE JUDHEBBIHUNE ‘EBNA’EKUM WE JESTEHJUNE NISA’EKUM WE FI DHALIKUM BELA’UN MIN RABBIKUM ‘ADHIMUN
WE ‘IDH TE’EDHDHENE REBBUKUM LE’IN SHEKERTUM LE’EZIDENNEKUM WE LE’IN KEFERTUM ‘INNE ‘ADHABI LESHEDIDUN
WE KALE MUSA ‘IN TEKFURU ‘ENTUM WE MEN FIL-’ERDI XHEMI’ÆN FE’INNALL-LLAHE LEGANIJUN HEMIDUN
‘ELEM JE’TIKUM NEBE’UL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIKUM KAWMI NUHIN WE ‘ADIN WE THEMUDE WEL-LEDHINE MIN BA’DIHIM LA JA’LEMUHUM ‘ILLALLAHU XHA’ET/HUM RUSULUHUM BIL-BEJJINATI FEREDDU ‘EJDIJEHUM FI ‘EFWAHIHIM WE KALU ‘INNA KEFERNA BIMA ‘URSILTUM BIHI WE ‘INNA LEFI SHEKK
KALET RUSULUHUM ‘EFI ELLAHI SHEKKUN FATIRI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI JED’UKUM LIJEGFIRE LEKUM MIN DHUNUBIKUM WE JU’UEHHIREKUM ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN KALU ‘IN ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUNA TURIDUNE ‘EN TESUDDUNA ‘AMMA KANE JA’BUDU ‘ABA’UUNA FE’TUNA BISULTANIN
KALET LEHUM RUSULUHUM ‘IN NEHNU ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUKUM WE LEKINNALL-LLAHE JEMUNNU ‘ALA MEN JESHA’U MIN ‘IBADIHI WE MA KANE LENA ‘EN NE’TIJEKUM BISULTANIN ‘ILLA BI’IDHNI ELLAHI WE ‘ALA ELLAHI FELJETEWEKKELIL-MU’UMINUNE
WE MA LENA ‘ELLA NETEWEKKELE ‘ALA ELLAHI WE KAD HEDANA SUBULENA WE LENESBIRENNE ‘ALA MA ‘ADHEJTUMUNA WE ‘ALA ELLAHI FELJETEWEKKELIL-MUTEWEKKILUNE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LIRUSULIHIM LENUHRIXHENNEKUM MIN ‘ERDINA ‘EW LETA’UDUNNE FI MILLETINA FE’EWHA ‘ILEJHIM REBBUHUM LENUHLIKENNE EDH-DHALIMINE
WE LENUSKINENNEKUMUL-’ERDE MIN BA’DIHIM DHALIKE LIMEN HAFE MEKAMI WE HAFE WA’IDI
WE ESTEFTEHU WE HABE KULLU XHEBBARIN ‘ANIDIN
MIN WERA’IHI XHEHENNEMU WE JUSKA MIN MA’IN SEDIDIN
JETEXHERRA’UHU WE LA JEKADU JUSIGUHU WE JE’TIHIL-MEWTU MIN KULLI MEKANIN WE MA HUWE BIMEJJITIN WE MIN WERA’IHI ‘ADHABUN GALIDHUN
METHELUL-LEDHINE KEFERU BIREBBIHIM ‘A’MALUHUM KEREMADIN ESHTEDDET BIHI ER-RIHU FI JEWMIN ‘ASIFIN LA JEKDIRUNE MIMMA KESEBU ‘ALA SHEJ’IN DHALIKE HUWE ED-DELALUL-BA’IDU
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BIL-HEKKI ‘IN JESHE’ JUDH/HIBKUM WE JE’TI BIHALKIN XHEDIDIN
WE MA DHALIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI BI’AZIZIN
WE BEREZU LILLAHI XHEMI’ÆN FEKALE ED-DU’AFA’U LILLEDHINE ESTEKBERU ‘INNA KUNNA LEKUM TEBA’ÆN FEHEL ‘ENTUM MUGNUNE ‘ANNA MIN ‘ADHABI ELLAHI MIN SHEJ’IN KALU LEW HEDANALLAHU LEHEDEJNAKUM SEWA’UN ‘ALEJNA ‘EXHEZI’NA ‘EM SEBERNA MA LENA MIN MEHISIN
WE KALE ESH-SHEJTANU LEMMA KUDIJEL-’EMRU ‘INNALL-LLAHE WE’ADEKUM WA’DEL-HEKKI WE WE’ADTUKUM FE’EHLEFTUKUM WE MA KANE LI ‘ALEJKUM MIN SULTANIN ‘ILLA ‘EN DE’AWTUKUM FASTEXHEBTUM LI FELA TELUMUNI WE LUMU ‘ENFUSEKUM MA ‘ENA BIMUSRIHIKUM WE MA ‘ENTUM BIMUSRIHI
WE ‘UDHILEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA BI’IDHNI RABBIHIM TEHIJETUHUM FIHA SELAMUN
‘ELEM TERA KEJFE DEREBEL-LAHU METHELÆN KELIMETEN TEJJIBETEN KESHEXHERETIN TEJJIBETIN ‘ESLUHA THABITUN WE FER’UHA FI ES-SEMA’I
TU’UTI ‘UKULEHA KULLE HININ BI’IDHNI RABBIHA WE JEDRIBU ELLAHUL-’EMTHALE LILNNASI LE’ALLEHUM JETEDHEKKERUNE
WE METHELU KELIMETIN HABITHETIN KESHEXHERETIN HABITHETIN EXHTUTHTHET MIN FEWKIL-’ERDI MA LEHA MIN KARARIN
JUTHEBBITU ELLAHUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU BIL-KAWLI ETH-THABITI FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE FIL-’AHIRETI WE JUDILLU ELLAHU EDH-DHALIMINE WE JEF’ALU ELLAHU MA JESHA’U
‘ELEM TERA ‘ILAL-LEDHINE BEDDELU NI’METEL-LAHI KUFRÆN WE ‘EHELLU KAWMEHUM DAREL-BEWARI
XHEHENNEME JESLEWNEHA WE BI’SEL-KARARU
WE XHE’ALU LILLAHI ‘ENDADÆN LIJUDILLU ‘AN SEBILIHI KUL TEMETTA’U FE’INNE MESIREKUM ‘ILA EN-NARI
KUL LI’IBADIJEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU JUKIMU ES-SELÆTE WE JUNFIKU MIMMA REZEKNAHUM SIRRÆN WE ‘ALANIJETEN MIN KABLI ‘EN JE’TIJE JEWMUN LA BEJ’UN FIHI WE LA HILALUN
ELLAHUL-LEDHI HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE ‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’EHREXHE BIHI MINE ETH-THEMERATI RIZKÆN LEKUM WE SEHHARE LEKUMUL-FULKE LITEXHRIJE FIL-BEHRI BI’EMRIHI WE SEHHARE LEKUMUL-’ENHARE
WE SEHHARE LEKUMU ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE DA’IBEJNI WE SEHHARE LEKUMUL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHAR
WE ‘ATAKUM MIN KULLI MA SE’ELTUMUHU WE ‘IN TA’UDDU NI’METEL-LAHI LA TUHSUHA ‘INNEL-’INSANE LEDHELUMUN KEFFARUN
WE ‘IDH KALE ‘IBRAHIMU RABBI EXH’AL HADHAL-BELEDE ‘AMINÆN WE EXHNUBNI WE BENIJE ‘EN NA’BUDEL-’ESNAME
REBBI ‘INNEHUNNE ‘EDLELNE KETHIRÆN MINE EN-NASI FEMEN TEBI’ANI FE’INNEHU MINNI WE MEN ‘ASANI FE’INNEKE GAFURUN REHIMUN
REBBENA ‘INNI ‘ESKENTU MIN DHURRIJETI BIWADIN GAJRI DHI ZER’IN ‘INDE BEJTIKEL-MUHERREMI REBBENA LIJUKIMU ES-SELÆTE FAXH’AL ‘EF’IDETEN MINE EN-NASI TEHWI ‘ILEJHIM WE ERZUKHUM MINE ETH-THEMERATI LE’ALLEHUM JESHKURUNE
REBBENA ‘INNEKE TA’LEMU MA NUHFI WE MA NU’LINU WE MA JEHFA ‘ALA ELLAHI MIN SHEJ’IN FIL-’ERDI WE LA FI ES-SEMA’I
EL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI WEHEBE LI ‘ALEL-KIBERI ‘ISMA’ILE WE ‘ISHAKA ‘INNE RABBI LESEMI’U ED-DU’A’I
REBBI EXH’ALNI MUKIME ES-SELÆTI WE MIN DHURRIJETI REBBENA WE TEKABBEL DU’A’I
REBBENA EGFIR LI WE LIWALIDEJJE WE LILMU’UMININE JEWME JEKUMUL-HISABU
WE LA TEHSEBENNEL-LAHE GAFILÆN ‘AMMA JA’MELU EDH-DHALIMUNE ‘INNEMA JU’UEHHIRUHUM LIJEWMIN TESHHASU FIHIL-’EBSARU
MUHTI’INE MUKNI’I RU’USIHIM LA JERTEDDU ‘ILEJHIM TERFUHUM WE ‘EF’IDETUHUM HEWA’UN
WE ‘ENDHIRI EN-NASE JEWME JE’TIHIMUL-’ADHABU FEJEKULUL-LEDHINE DHELEMU REBBENA ‘EHHIRNA ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN KARIBIN NUXHIB DA’WETEKE WE NETTEBI’I ER-RUSULE ‘EWELEM TEKUNU ‘EKSEMTUM MIN KABLU MA LEKUM MIN ZEWALIN
WE SEKENTUM FI MESAKINIL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ‘ENFUSEHUM WE TEBEJJENE LEKUM KEJFE FE’ALNA BIHIM WE DEREBNA LEKUMUL-’EMTHALE
WE KAD MEKERU MEKREHUM WE ‘INDEL-LAHI MEKRUHUM WE ‘IN KANE MEKRUHUM LITEZULE MINHUL-XHIBALU
FELA TEHSEBENNEL-LAHE MUHLIFE WA’DIHI RUSULEHU ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘AZIZUN DHU ENTIKAMIN
JEWME TUBEDDELUL-’ERDU GAJREL-’ERDI WE ES-SEMAWATU WE BEREZU LILLAHIL-WAHIDIL-KAHHARI
WE TERAL-MUXHRIMINE JEWME’IDHIN MUKARRENINE FIL-’ESFADI
SERABILUHUM MIN KATIRANIN WE TEGSHA WUXHUHEHUMU EN-NARU
LIJEXHZIJEL-LAHU KULLE NEFSIN MA KESEBET ‘INNALL-LLAHE SERI’UL-HISABI
HADHA BELAGUN LILNNASI WE LIJUNDHERU BIHI WE LIJA’LEMU ‘ENNEMA HUWE ‘ILEHUN WAHIDUN WE LIJEDHDHEKKERE ‘ULUL-’ELBABI
‘ELIF-LAM-RA TILKE ‘AJATUL-KITABI WE KUR’ANIN MUBININ
RUBEMA JEWEDDUL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEW KANU MUSLIMINE
DHERHUM JE’KULU WE JETEMETTA’U WE JULHIHIMUL-’EMELU FESEWFE JA’LEMUNE
WE MA ‘EHLEKNA MIN KARJETIN ‘ILLA WE LEHA KITABUN MA’LUMUN
MA TESBIKU MIN ‘UMMETIN ‘EXHELEHA WE MA JESTE’HIRUNE
WE KALU JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHI NUZZILE ‘ALEJHI EDH-DHIKRU ‘INNEKE LEMEXHNUNUN
LEW MA TE’TINA BIL-MELA’IKETI ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
MA NUNEZZILUL-MELA’IKETE ‘ILLA BIL-HEKKI WE MA KANU ‘IDHÆN MUNDHERINE
‘INNA NEHNU NEZZELNA EDH-DHIKRE WE ‘INNA LEHU LEHAFIDHUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE FI SHIJA’IL-’EWWELINE
WE MA JE’TIHIM MIN RESULIN ‘ILLA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UNE
KEDHALIKE NESLUKUHU FI KULUBIL-MUXHRIMINE
LA JU’UMINUNE BIHI WE KAD HALET SUNNETUL-’EWWELINE
WE LEW FETEHNA ‘ALEJHIM BABÆN MINE ES-SEMA’I FEDHELLU FIHI JA’RUXHUNE
LEKALU ‘INNEMA SUKKIRET ‘EBSARUNA BEL NEHNU KAWMUN MESHURUNE
WE LEKAD XHE’ALNA FI ES-SEMA’I BURUXHÆN WE ZEJJENNAHA LILNNADHIRINE
WE HEFIDHNAHA MIN KULLI SHEJTANIN REXHIMIN
‘ILLA MENI ESTEREKA ES-SEM’A FE’ETBE’AHU SHIHABUN MUBINUN
WEL-’ERDE MEDEDNAHA WE ‘ELKAJNA FIHA REWASIJE WE ‘ENBETNA FIHA MIN KULLI SHEJ’IN MEWZUNIN
WE XHE’ALNA LEKUM FIHA MA’AJISHE WE MEN LESTUM LEHU BIRAZIKINE
WE ‘IN MIN SHEJ’IN ‘ILLA ‘INDENA HAZA’INUHU WE MA NUNEZZILUHU ‘ILLA BIKADERIN MA’LUMIN
WE ‘ERSELNA ER-RIJAHE LEWAKIHE FE’ENZELNA MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’ESKAJNAKUMUHU WE MA ‘ENTUM LEHU BIHAZININE
WE ‘INNA LENEHNU NUHJI WE NUMITU WE NEHNUL-WARITHUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ALIMNAL-MUSTEKDIMINE MINKUM WE LEKAD ‘ALIMNAL-MUSTE’HIRINE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE HUWE JEHSHURUHUM ‘INNEHU HEKIMUN ‘ALIMUN
WE LEKAD HALEKNAL-’INSANE MIN SELSALIN MIN HEME’IIN MESNUNIN
WEL-XHANNE HALEKNAHU MIN KABLU MIN NARI ES-SEMUMI
WE ‘IDH KALE REBBUKE LILMELA’IKETI ‘INNI HALIKUN BESHERÆN MIN SELSALIN MIN HEME’IIN MESNUNIN
FE’IDHA SEWWEJTUHU WE NEFEHTU FIHI MIN RUHI FEKA’U LEHU SAXHIDINE
FESEXHEDEL-MELA’IKETU KULLUHUM ‘EXHMA’UNE
‘ILLA ‘IBLISE ‘EBA ‘EN JEKUNE ME’A ES-SAXHIDINE
KALE JA ‘IBLISU MA LEKE ‘ELLA TEKUNE ME’A ES-SAXHIDINE
KALE LEM ‘EKUN LI’SXHUDE LIBESHERIN HALEKTEHU MIN SELSALIN MIN HEME’IIN MESNUNIN
KALE FAHRUXH MINHA FE’INNEKE REXHIMUN
WE ‘INNE ‘ALEJKEL-LA’NETE ‘ILA JEWMI ED-DINI
KALE RABBI FE’ENDHIRNI ‘ILA JEWMI JUB’ATHUNE
KALE FE’INNEKE MINEL-MUNDHERINE
‘ILA JEWMIL-WEKTIL-MA’LUMI
KALE RABBI BIMA ‘EGWEJTENI LE’UZEJJINENNE LEHUM FIL-’ERDI WE LE’UGWIJENNEHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
‘ILLA ‘IBADEKE MINHUMUL-MUHLESINE
KALE HADHA SIRATUN ‘ALEJJE MUSTEKIMUN
‘INNE ‘IBADI LEJSE LEKE ‘ALEJHIM SULTANUN ‘ILLA MENI ETTEBE’AKE MINEL-GAWINE
WE ‘INNE XHEHENNEME LEMEW’IDUHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
LEHA SEB’ATU ‘EBWABIN LIKULLI BABIN MINHUM XHUZ’UN MEKSUMUN
‘INNEL-MUTTEKINE FI XHENNATIN WE ‘UJUNIN
EDHULUHA BISELAMIN ‘AMININE
WE NEZA’NA MA FI SUDURIHIM MIN GILLIN ‘IHWANÆN ‘ALA SURURIN MUTEKABILINE
LA JEMESSUHUM FIHA NESEBUN WE MA HUM MINHA BIMUHREXHINE
NEBBI’ ‘IBADI ‘ENNI ‘ENAL-GAFURU ER-REHIMU
WE ‘ENNE ‘ADHABI HUWEL-’ADHABUL-’ELIMU
WE NEBBI’HUM ‘AN DEJFI ‘IBRAHIME
‘IDH DEHALU ‘ALEJHI FEKALU SELAMÆN KALE ‘INNA MINKUM WEXHILUNE
KALU LA TEWXHEL ‘INNA NUBESHSHIRUKE BIGULAMIN ‘ALIMIN
KALE ‘EBESHSHERTUMUNI ‘ALA ‘EN MESSENIJEL-KIBERU FEBIME TUBESHSHIRUNE
KALU BESHSHERNAKE BIL-HEKKI FELA TEKUN MINEL-KANITINE
KALE WE MEN JEKNETU MIN REHMETI RABBIHI ‘ILLA ED-DALLUNE
KALE FEMA HATBUKUM ‘EJJUHAL-MURSELUNE
KALU ‘INNA ‘URSILNA ‘ILA KAWMIN MUXHRIMINE
‘ILLA ‘ALE LUTIN ‘INNA LEMUNEXHXHUHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
‘ILLA EMRE’ETEHU KADDERNA ‘INNEHA LEMINEL-GABIRINE
FELEMMA XHA’E ‘ALE LUTINL-MURSELUNE
KALE ‘INNEKUM KAWMUN MUNKERUNE
KALU BEL XHI’NAKE BIMA KANU FIHI JEMTERUNE
WE ‘ETEJNAKE BIL-HEKKI WE ‘INNA LESADIKUNE
FE’ESRI BI’EHLIKE BIKIT’IN MINEL-LEJLI WE ETTEBI’ ‘EDBAREHUM WE LA JELTEFIT MINKUM ‘EHEDUN WE EMDU HEJTHU TU’UMERUNE
WE KADEJNA ‘ILEJHI DHALIKEL-’EMRE ‘ENNE DABIRE HA’UULA’ MEKTU’UN MUSBIHINE
WE XHA’E ‘EHLUL-MEDINETI JESTEBSHIRUNE
KALE ‘INNE HA’UULA’ DEJFI FELA TEFDEHUNI
WE ETTEKU ELLAHE WE LA TUHZUNI
KALU ‘EWELEM NENHEKE ‘ANIL-’ALEMINE
KALE HA’UULA’ BENATI ‘IN KUNTUM FA’ILINE
LE’AMRUKE ‘INNEHUM LEFI SEKRETIHIM JA’MEHUNE
FE’EHADHET/HUMU ES-SEJHETU MUSHRIKINE
FEXHE’ALNA ‘ALIJEHA SAFILEHA WE ‘EMTERNA ‘ALEJHIM HIXHARETEN MIN SIXHXHILIN
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LILMUTEWESSIMINE
WE ‘INNEHA LEBISEBILIN MUKIMIN
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LILMU’UMININE
WE ‘IN KANE ‘ESHABUL-’EJKETI LEDHALIMINE
FANTEKAMNA MINHUM WE ‘INNEHUMA LEBI’IMAMIN MUBININ
WE LEKAD KEDHDHEBE ‘ESHABUL-HIXHRIL-MURSELINE
WE ‘ATEJNAHUM ‘AJATINA FEKANU ‘ANHA MU’RIDINE
WE KANU JENHITUNE MINEL-XHIBALI BUJUTÆN ‘AMININE
FE’EHADHET/HUMU ES-SEJHETU MUSBIHINE
FEMA ‘EGNA ‘ANHUM MA KANU JEKSIBUNE
WE MA HALEKNA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA ‘ILLA BIL-HEKKI WE ‘INNE ES-SA’ATE LE’ATIJETUN FASFEHI ES-SEFHEL-XHEMILE
‘INNE REBBEKE HUWEL-HALLAKUL-’ALIMU
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNAKE SEB’ÆN MINEL-METHANI WEL-KUR’ANEL-’ADHIME
LA TEMUDDENNE ‘AJNEJKE ‘ILA MA METTA’NA BIHI ‘EZWAXHÆN MINHUM WE LA TEHZEN ‘ALEJHIM WE EHFID XHENAHEKE LILMU’UMININE
WE KUL ‘INNI ‘ENA EN-NEDHIRUL-MUBINU
KEMA ‘ENZELNA ‘ALEL-MUKTESIMINE
EL-LEDHINE XHE’ALUL-KUR’ANE ‘IDINE
FEWEREBBIKE LENES’ELENNEHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
‘AMMA KANU JA’MELUNE
FASDA’ BIMA TU’UMERU WE ‘A’RID ‘ANIL-MUSHRIKINE
‘INNA KEFEJNAKEL-MUSTEHZI’INE
EL-LEDHINE JEXH’ALUNE ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE FESEWFE JA’LEMUNE
WE LEKAD NA’LEMU ‘ENNEKE JEDIKU SEDRUKE BIMA JEKULUNE
FESEBBIH BIHEMDI RABBIKE WE KUN MINE ES-SAXHIDINE
WE A’BUD REBBEKE HETTA JE’TIJEKEL-JEKINU
‘ETA ‘EMRU ELLAHI FELA TESTA’XHILUHU SUBHANEHU WE TA’ALA ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
JUNEZZILUL-MELA’IKETE BIR-RUHI MIN ‘EMRIHI ‘ALA MEN JESHA’U MIN ‘IBADIHI ‘EN ‘ENDHIRU ‘ENNEHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA ‘ENA FE ETTEKUNI
HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BIL-HEKKI TA’ALA ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
HALEKAL-’INSANE MIN NUTFETIN FE’IDHA HUWE HASIMUN MUBINUN
WEL-’EN’AME HALEKAHA LEKUM FIHA DIF’UN WE MENAFI’U WE MINHA TE’KULUNE
WE LEKUM FIHA XHEMALUN HINE TURIHUNE WE HINE TESREHUNE
WE TEHMILU ‘ETHKALEKUM ‘ILA BELEDIN LEM TEKUNU BALIGIHI ‘ILLA BISHIKKIL-’ENFUSI ‘INNE REBBEKUM LERE’UFUN REHIMUN
WEL-HAJLE WEL-BIGALE WEL-HEMIRE LITERKEBUHA WE ZINETEN WE JEHLUKU MA LA TA’LEMUNE
WE ‘ALA ELLAHI KASDU ES-SEBILI WE MINHA XHA’IRUN WE LEW SHA’E LEHEDAKUM ‘EXHMA’INE
HUWEL-LEDHI ‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN LEKUM MINHU SHERABUN WE MINHU SHEXHERUN FIHI TUSIMUNE
JUNBITU LEKUM BIHI EZ-ZER’A WE EZ-ZEJTUNE WE EN-NEHILE WEL-’A’NABE WE MIN KULLI ETH-THEMERATI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKAWMIN JETEFEKKERUNE
WE SEHHARE LEKUMUL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE WE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE WE EN-NUXHUMU MUSEHHARATUN BI’EMRIHI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JA’KILUNE
WE MA DHERE’E LEKUM FIL-’ERDI MUHTELIFÆN ‘ELWANUHU ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKAWMIN JEDHDHEKKERUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI SEHHAREL-BEHRE LITE’KULU MINHU LEHMÆN TERIJÆN WE TESTEHRIXHU MINHU HILJETEN TELBESUNEHA WE TERAL-FULKE MEWAHIRE FIHI WE LITEBTEGU MIN FEDLIHI WE LE’ALLEKUM TESHKURUNE
WE ‘ELKA FIL-’ERDI REWASIJE ‘EN TEMIDE BIKUM WE ‘ENHARÆN WE SUBULÆN LLE’ALLEKUM TEHTEDUNE
WE ‘ALAMATIN WE BIN-NEXHMI HUM JEHTEDUNE
‘EFEMEN JEHLUKU KEMEN LA JEHLUKU ‘EFELA TEDHEKKERUNE
WE ‘IN TA’UDDU NI’METEL-LAHI LA TUHSUHA ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEGAFURUN REHIMUN
WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU MA TUSIRRUNE WE MA TU’LINUNE
WEL-LEDHINE JED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI LA JEHLUKUNE SHEJ’ÆN WE HUM JUHLEKUNE
‘EMWATUN GAJRU ‘EHJA’IN WE MA JESH’URUNE ‘EJJANE JUB’ATHUNE
‘ILEHUKUM ‘ILEHUN WAHIDUN FE-EL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI KULUBUHUM MUNKIRETUN WE HUM MUSTEKBIRUNE
LA XHEREME ‘ENNEL-LAHE JA’LEMU MA JUSIRRUNE WE MA JU’LINUNE ‘INNEHU LA JUHIBBUL-MUSTEKBIRINE
WE ‘IDHA KILE LEHUM MADHA ‘ENZELE REBBUKUM KALU ‘ESATIRUL-’EWWELINE
LIJEHMILU ‘EWZAREHUM KAMILETEN JEWMEL-KIJAMETI WE MIN ‘EWZARIL-LEDHINE JUDILLUNEHUM BIGAJRI ‘ILMIN ‘ELA SA’E MA JEZIRUNE
KAD MEKEREL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM FE’ETALLAHU BUNJANEHUM MINEL-KAWA’IDI FEHARRE ‘ALEJHIMU ES-SEKFU MIN FEWKIHIM WE ‘ETAHUMUL-’ADHABU MIN HEJTHU LA JESH’URUNE
THUMME JEWMEL-KIJAMETI JUHZIHIM WE JEKULU ‘EJNE SHUREKA’IJEL-LEDHINE KUNTUM TUSHAKKUNE FIHIM KALEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME ‘INNEL-HIZJEL-JEWME WE ES-SU’E ‘ALEL-KAFIRINE
EL-LEDHINE TETEWEFFAHUMUL-MELA’IKETU DHALIMI ‘ENFUSIHIM FE’ELKAW ES-SELEME MA KUNNA NA’MELU MIN SU’IN BELA ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALIMUN BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
FADHULU ‘EBWABE XHEHENNEME HALIDINE FIHA FELEBI’SE METHWAL-MUTEKEBBIRINE
WE KILE LILLEDHINE ETTEKAW MADHA ‘ENZELE REBBUKUM KALU HAJRÆN LILLEDHINE ‘EHSENU FI HEDHIHI ED-DUNJA HESENETUN WE LEDARUL-’AHIRETI HAJRUN WE LENI’ME DARUL-MUTTEKINE
XHENNATU ‘ADNIN JEDHULUNEHA TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU LEHUM FIHA MA JESHA’UNE KEDHALIKE JEXHZI ELLAHUL-MUTTEKINE
EL-LEDHINE TETEWEFFAHUMUL-MELA’IKETU TEJJIBINE JEKULUNE SELAMUN ‘ALEJKUMU EDHULUL-XHENNETE BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
HEL JENDHURUNE ‘ILLA ‘EN TE’TIJEHUMUL-MELA’IKETU ‘EW JE’TIJE ‘EMRU RABBIKE KEDHALIKE FE’ALEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM WE MA DHELEMEHUMU ELLAHU WE LEKIN KANU ‘ENFUSEHUM JEDHLIMUNE
FE’ESABEHUM SEJJI’ATU MA ‘AMILU WE HAKA BIHIM MA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
WE KALEL-LEDHINE ‘ESHREKU LEW SHA’EL-LAHU MA ‘ABEDNA MIN DUNIHI MIN SHEJ’IN NEHNU WE LA ‘ABA’UUNA WE LA HERREMNA MIN DUNIHI MIN SHEJ’IN KEDHALIKE FE’ALEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM FEHEL ‘ALA ER-RUSULI ‘ILLAL-BELAGUL-MUBINU
WE LEKAD BE’ATHNA FI KULLI ‘UMMETIN RESULÆN ‘ENI EU’BUDU ELLAHE WE EXHTENIBUT-TAGUTE FEMINHUM MEN HEDALLAHU WE MINHUM MEN HEKKAT ‘ALEJHI ED-DELALETU FESIRU FIL-’ERDI FANDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-MUKEDHDHIBINE
‘IN TEHRIS ‘ALA HUDAHUM FE’INNALL-LLAHE LA JEHDI MEN JUDILLU WE MA LEHUM MIN NASIRINE
WE ‘EKSEMU BILLAHI XHEHDE ‘EJMANIHIM LA JEB’ATHU ELLAHU MEN JEMUTU BELA WA’DÆN ‘ALEJHI HEKKÆN WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
LIJUBEJJINE LEHUMUL-LEDHI JEHTELIFUNE FIHI WE LIJA’LEMEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘ENNEHUM KANU KADHIBINE
‘INNEMA KAWLUNA LISHEJ’IN ‘IDHA ‘EREDNAHU ‘EN NEKULE LEHU KUN FEJEKUNU
WEL-LEDHINE HAXHERU FI ELLAHI MIN BA’DI MA DHULIMU LENUBEWWI’ENNEHUM FI ED-DUNJA HESENETEN WE LE’EXHRUL-’AHIRETI ‘EKBERU LEW KANU JA’LEMUNE
EL-LEDHINE SEBERU WE ‘ALA RABBIHIM JETEWEKKELUNE
WE MA ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE ‘ILLA RIXHALÆN NUHI ‘ILEJHIM FAS’ELU ‘EHLE EDH-DHIKRI ‘IN KUNTUM LA TA’LEMUNE
BIL-BEJJINATI WE EZ-ZUBURI WE ‘ENZELNA ‘ILEJKE EDH-DHIKRE LITUBEJJINE LILNNASI MA NUZZILE ‘ILEJHIM WE LE’ALLEHUM JETEFEKKERUNE
‘EFE’EMINEL-LEDHINE MEKERU ES-SEJJI’ATI ‘EN JEHSIFEL-LAHU BIHIMUL-’ERDE ‘EW JE’TIJEHUMUL-’ADHABU MIN HEJTHU LA JESH’URUNE
‘EW JE’HUDHEHUM FI TEKALLUBIHIM FEMA HUM BIMU’XHIZINE
‘EW JE’HUDHEHUM ‘ALA TEHAWWUFIN FE’INNE REBBEKUM LERE’UFUN REHIMUN
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ILA MA HALEKAL-LAHU MIN SHEJ’IN JETEFEJJE’U DHILALUHU ‘ANIL-JEMINI WE ESH-SHEMA’ILI SUXHXHEDÆN LILLAHI WE HUM DAHIRUNE
WE LILLEHI JESXHUDU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI MIN DABBETIN WEL-MELA’IKETU WE HUM LA JESTEKBIRUNE
JEHAFUNE REBBEHUM MIN FEWKIHIM WE JEF’ALUNE MA JU’UMERUNE
WE KALEL-LAHU LA TETTEHIDHU ‘ILEHEJNI ETHNEJNI ‘INNEMA HUWE ‘ILEHUN WAHIDUN FE’IJAJE FARHEBUNI
WE LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE LEHU ED-DINU WE ESIBÆN ‘EFEGAJREL-LAHI TETTEKUNE
WE MA BIKUM MIN NI’METIN FEMINEL-LAHI THUMME ‘IDHA MESSEKUMU ED-DURRU FE’ILEJHI TEXH’ERUNE
THUMME ‘IDHA KESHEFE ED-DURRE ‘ANKUM ‘IDHA FERIKUN MINKUM BIREBBIHIM JUSHRIKUNE
LIJEKFURU BIMA ‘ATEJNAHUM FETEMETTA’U FESEWFE TA’LEMUNE
WE JEXH’ALUNE LIMA LA JA’LEMUNE NESIBÆN MIMMA REZEKNAHUM TE-ELLAHI LETUS’ELUNNE ‘AMMA KUNTUM TEFTERUNE
WE JEXH’ALUNE LILLAHIL-BENATI SUBHANEHU WE LEHUM MA JESHTEHUNE
WE ‘IDHA BUSHSHIRE ‘EHEDUHUM BIL-’UNTHA DHELLE WEXHHUHU MUSWEDDÆN WE HUWE KEDHIMUN
JETEWARA MINEL-KAWMI MIN SU’I MA BUSHSHIRE BIHI ‘EJUMSIKUHU ‘ALA HUNIN ‘EM JEDUSSUHU FIT-TURABI ‘ELA SA’E MA JEHKUMUNE
LILLEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI METHELU ES-SEW’I WE LILLEHIL-METHELUL-’A’LA WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
WE LEW JU’UAHIDHU ELLAHU EN-NASE BIDHULMIHIM MA TEREKE ‘ALEJHA MIN DABBETIN WE LEKIN JU’UEHHIRUHUM ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN FE’IDHA XHA’E ‘EXHELUHUM LA JESTE’HIRUNE SA’ATEN WE LA JESTEKDIMUNE
WE JEXH’ALUNE LILLAHI MA JEKREHUNE WE TESIFU ‘ELSINETUHUMUL-KEDHIBE ‘ENNE LEHUMUL-HUSNA LA XHEREME ‘ENNE LEHUMU EN-NARE WE ‘ENNEHUM MUFRETUNE
TE-ELLAHI LEKAD ‘ERSELNA ‘ILA ‘UMEMIN MIN KABLIKE FEZEJJENE LEHUMU ESH-SHEJTANU ‘A’MALEHUM FEHUWE WELIJUHUMUL-JEWME WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
WE MA ‘ENZELNA ‘ALEJKEL-KITABE ‘ILLA LITUBEJJINE LEHUMUL-LEDHI EHTELEFU FIHI WE HUDEN WE REHMETEN LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
WEL-LAHU ‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’EHJA BIHIL-’ERDE BA’DE MEWTIHA ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKAWMIN JESMA’UNE
WE ‘INNE LEKUM FIL-’EN’AM LA’IBRETEN NUSKIKUM MIMMA FI BUTUNIHI MIN BEJNI FERTHIN WE DEMIN LEBENÆN HALISÆN SA’IGÆN LILSHSHARIBINE
WE MIN THEMERATI EN-NEHILI WEL-’A’NABI TETTEHIDHUNE MINHU SEKERÆN WE RIZKÆN HESENÆN ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKAWMIN JA’KILUNE
WE ‘EWHA REBBUKE ‘ILA EN-NEHLI ‘ENI ETTEHIDHI MINEL-XHIBALI BUJUTÆN WE MINE ESH-SHEXHERI WE MIMMA JA’RISHUNE
THUMME KULI MIN KULLI ETH-THEMERATI FASLUKI SUBULE RABBIKI DHULULÆN JEHRUXHU MIN BUTUNIHA SHERABUN MUHTELIFUN ‘ELWANUHU FIHI SHIFA’UN LILNNASI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKAWMIN JETEFEKKERUNE
WEL-LAHU HALEKAKUM THUMME JETEWEFFAKUM WE MINKUM MEN JUREDDU ‘ILA ‘ERDHELIL-’UMURI LIKEJ LA JA’LEME BA’DE ‘ILMIN SHEJ’ÆN ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALIMUN KADIRUN
WEL-LAHU FEDDELE BA’DEKUM ‘ALA BA’DIN FI ER-RIZKI FEMAL-LEDHINE FUDDILU BIRADDI RIZKIHIM ‘ALA MA MELEKET ‘EJMANUHUM FEHUM FIHI SEWA’UN ‘EFEBINI’METI ELLAHI JEXHHEDUNE
WEL-LAHU XHE’ALE LEKUM MIN ‘ENFUSIKUM ‘EZWAXHÆN WE XHE’ALE LEKUM MIN ‘EZWAXHIKUM BENINE WE HEFEDETEN WE REZEKAKUM MINET-TEJJIBATI ‘EFEBIALBATILI JU’UMINUNE WE BINI’METI ELLAHI HUM JEKFURUNE
WE JA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI MA LA JEMLIKU LEHUM RIZKÆN MINE ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI SHEJ’ÆN WE LA JESTETI’UNE
FELA TEDRIBU LILLAHIL-’EMTHALE ‘INNALL-LLAHE JA’LEMU WE ‘ENTUM LA TA’LEMUNE
DEREBEL-LAHU METHELÆN ‘ABDÆN MEMLUKÆN LA JEKDIRU ‘ALA SHEJ’IN WE MEN REZEKNAHU MINNA RIZKÆN HESENÆN FEHUWE JUNFIKU MINHU SIRRÆN WE XHEHRÆN HEL JESTEWUNEL-HEMDU LILLAHI BEL ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
WE DEREBEL-LAHU METHELÆN REXHULEJNI ‘EHEDUHUMA ‘EBKEMU LA JEKDIRU ‘ALA SHEJ’IN WE HUWE KELLUN ‘ALA MEWLAHU ‘EJNEMA JUWEXHXHHHHU LA JE’TI BIHAJRIN HEL JESTEWI HUWE WE MEN JE’MURU BIL-’ADLI WE HUWE ‘ALA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
WE LILLEHI GAJBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA ‘EMRU ES-SA’ATI ‘ILLA KELEMHIL-BESERI ‘EW HUWE ‘EKREBU ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
WEL-LAHU ‘EHREXHEKUM MIN BUTUNI ‘UMMEHATIKUM LA TA’LEMUNE SHEJ’ÆN WE XHE’ALE LEKUMU ES-SEM’A WEL-’EBSARE WEL-’EF’IDETE LE’ALLEKUM TESHKURUNE
‘ELEM JEREW ‘ILAT-TEJRI MUSEHHARATIN FI XHEWWI ES-SEMA’I MA JUMSIKUHUNNE ‘ILLALLAHU ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
WEL-LAHU XHE’ALE LEKUM MIN BUJUTIKUM SEKENÆN WE XHE’ALE LEKUM MIN XHULUDIL-’EN’AMI BUJUTÆN TESTEHIFFUNEHA JEWME DHA’NIKUM WE JEWME ‘IKAMETIKUM WE MIN ‘ESWAFIHA WE ‘EWBARIHA WE ‘ESH’ARIHA ‘ETHATHÆN WE META’ÆN ‘ILA HININ
WEL-LAHU XHE’ALE LEKUM MIMMA HALEKA DHILALÆN WE XHE’ALE LEKUM MINEL-XHIBALI ‘EKNANÆN WE XHE’ALE LEKUM SERABILE TEKIKUMUL-HERRE WE SERABILE TEKIKUM BE’SEKUM KEDHALIKE JUTIMMU NI’METEHU ‘ALEJKUM LE’ALLEKUM TUSLIMUNE
FE’IN TEWELLEW FE’INNEMA ‘ALEJKEL-BELAGUL-MUBINU
JA’RIFUNE NI’METEL-LAHI THUMME JUNKIRUNEHA WE ‘EKTHERUHUMUL-KAFIRUNE
WE JEWME NEB’ATHU MIN KULLI ‘UMMETIN SHEHIDÆN THUMME LA JU’UDHENU LILLEDHINE KEFERU WE LA HUM JUSTA’TEBUNE
WE ‘IDHA RE’AL-LEDHINE DHELEMUL-’ADHABE FELA JUHAFFEFU ‘ANHUM WE LA HUM JUNDHERUNE
WE ‘IDHA RE’AL-LEDHINE ‘ESHREKU SHUREKA’EHUM KALU REBBENA HA’UULA’ SHUREKA’UUNAL-LEDHINE KUNNA NED’U MIN DUNIKE FE’ELKAW ‘ILEJHIMUL-KAWLE ‘INNEKUM LEKADHIBUNE
WE ‘ELKAW ‘ILA ELLAHI JEWME’IDHIN ES-SELEME WE DELLE ‘ANHUM MA KANU JEFTERUNE
EL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE SEDDU ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI ZIDNAHUM ‘ADHABÆN FEWKAL-’ADHABI BIMA KANU JUFSIDUNE
WE JEWME NEB’ATHU FI KULLI ‘UMMETIN SHEHIDÆN ‘ALEJHIM MIN ‘ENFUSIHIM WE XHI’NA BIKE SHEHIDÆN ‘ALA HA’UULA’ WE NEZZELNA ‘ALEJKEL-KITABE TIBJANÆN LIKULLI SHEJ’IN WE HUDEN WE REHMETEN WE BUSHRA LILMUSLIMINE
‘INNALL-LLAHE JE’MURU BIL-’ADLI WEL-’IHSANI WE ‘ITA’I DHIL-KURBA WE JENHA ‘ANIL-FEHSHA’I WEL-MUNKERI WEL-BEGJI JA’IDHUKUM LE’ALLEKUM TEDHEKKERUNE
WE ‘EWFU BI’AHDI ELLAHI ‘IDHA ‘AHEDTUM WE LA TENKUDUL-’EJMANE BA’DE TEWKIDIHA WE KAD XHE’ALTUMU ELLAHE ‘ALEJKUM KEFILÆN ‘INNALL-LLAHE JA’LEMU MA TEF’ALUNE
WE LA TEKUNU KALLETI NEKADET GAZLEHA MIN BA’DI KUWETIN ‘ENKATHÆN TETTEHIDHUNE ‘EJMANEKUM DEHALÆN BEJNEKUM ‘EN TEKUNE ‘UMMETUN HIJE ‘ERBA MIN ‘UMMETIN ‘INNEMA JEBLUKUMU ELLAHU BIHI WE LEJUBEJJINENNE LEKUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI MA KUNTUM FIHI TEHTELIFUNE
WE LEW SHA’EL-LAHU LEXHE’ALEKUM ‘UMMETEN WAHIDETEN WE LEKIN JUDILLU MEN JESHA’U WE JEHDI MEN JESHA’U WE LETUS’ELUNNE ‘AMMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
WE LA TETTEHIDHU ‘EJMANEKUM DEHALÆN BEJNEKUM FETEZILLE KADEMUN BA’DE THUBUTIHA WE TEDHUKU ES-SU’E BIMA SEDEDTUM ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI WE LEKUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ADHIMUN
WE LA TESHTERU BI’AHDI ELLAHI THEMENÆN KALILÆN ‘INNEMA ‘INDEL-LAHI HUWE HAJRUN LEKUM ‘IN KUNTUM TA’LEMUNE
MA ‘INDEKUM JENFEDU WE MA ‘INDEL-LAHI BAKIN WE LENEXHZIJENNEL-LEDHINE SEBERU ‘EXHREHUM BI’EHSENI MA KANU JA’MELUNE
MEN ‘AMILE SALIHÆN MIN DHEKERIN ‘EW ‘UNTHA WE HUWE MU’UMINUN FELENUHJIJENNEHU HEJÆTEN TEJJIBETEN WE LENEXHZIJENNEHUM ‘EXHREHUM BI’EHSENI MA KANU JA’MELUNE
FE’IDHA KARE’TEL-KUR’ANE FASTA’IDH BILLAHI MINE ESH-SHEJTANI ER-REXHIMI
‘INNEHU LEJSE LEHU SULTANUN ‘ALEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘ALA RABBIHIM JETEWEKKELUNE
‘INNEMA SULTANUHU ‘ALEL-LEDHINE JETEWELLEWNEHU WEL-LEDHINE HUM BIHI MUSHRIKUNE
WE ‘IDHA BEDDELNA ‘AJETEN MEKANE ‘AJETIN WEL-LAHU ‘A’LEMU BIMA JUNEZZILU KALU ‘INNEMA ‘ENTE MUFTERIN BEL ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
KUL NEZZELEHU RUHUL-KUDUSI MIN RABBIKE BIL-HEKKI LIJUTHEBBITEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE HUDEN WE BUSHRA LILMUSLIMINE
WE LEKAD NA’LEMU ‘ENNEHUM JEKULUNE ‘INNEMA JU’ALLIMUHU BESHERUN LISANUL-LEDHI JULHIDUNE ‘ILEJHI ‘A’XHEMIJUN WE HEDHA LISANUN ‘AREBIJUN MUBINUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BI’AJATI ELLAHI LA JEHDIHIMU ELLAHU WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
‘INNEMA JEFTERIL-KEDHIBEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BI’AJATI ELLAHI WE ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-KADHIBUNE
MEN KEFERE BILLAHI MIN BA’DI ‘IMANIHI ‘ILLA MEN ‘UKRIHE WE KALBUHU MUTME’INNUN BIL-’IMANI WE LEKIN MEN SHEREHE BIL-KUFRI SEDRÆN FE’ALEJHIM GADEBUN MINEL-LAHI WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ADHIMUN
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUMU ESTEHEBBUL-HEJÆTE ED-DUNJA ‘ALEL-’AHIRETI WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE LA JEHDIL-KAWMEL-KAFIRINE
‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE TEBE’ALLAHU ‘ALA KULUBIHIM WE SEM’IHIM WE ‘EBSARIHIM WE ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-GAFILUNE
LA XHEREME ‘ENNEHUM FIL-’AHIRETI HUMUL-HASIRUNE
THUMME ‘INNE REBBEKE LILLEDHINE HAXHERU MIN BA’DI MA FUTINU THUMME XHAHEDU WE SEBERU ‘INNE REBBEKE MIN BA’DIHA LEGAFURUN REHIMUN
JEWME TE’TI KULLU NEFSIN TUXHADILU ‘AN NEFSIHA WE TUWEFFA KULLU NEFSIN MA ‘AMILET WE HUM LA JUDHLEMUNE
WE DEREBEL-LAHU METHELÆN KARJETEN KANET ‘AMINETEN MUTME’INNETEN JE’TIHA RIZKUHA REGADÆN MIN KULLI MEKANIN FEKEFERET BI’EN’UMI ELLAHI FE’EDHAKAHALLAHU LIBASEL-XHU’I WEL-HAWFI BIMA KANU JESNA’UNE
WE LEKAD XHA’EHUM RESULUN MINHUM FEKEDHDHEBUHU FE’EHADHEHUMUL-’ADHABU WE HUM DHALIMUNE
FEKULU MIMMA REZEKAKUMU ELLAHU HELALÆN TEJJIBÆN WE ESHKURU NI’METEL-LAHI ‘IN KUNTUM ‘IJAHU TA’BUDUNE
‘INNEMA HERREME ‘ALEJKUMUL-MEJTETE WE ED-DEME WE LEHMEL-HINZIRI WE MA ‘UHILLE LIGAJRI ELLAHI BIHI FEMENI EDTURRE GAJRE BAGIN WE LA ‘ADIN FE’INNALL-LLAHE GAFURUN REHIMUN
WE LA TEKULU LIMA TESIFU ‘ELSINETUKUMUL-KEDHIBE HADHA HELALUN WE HEDHA HERAMUN LITEFTERU ‘ALA ELLAHIL-KEDHIBE ‘INNEL-LEDHINE JEFTERUNE ‘ALA ELLAHIL-KEDHIBE LA JUFLIHUNE
META’UN KALILUN WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
WE ‘ALEL-LEDHINE HADU HERREMNA MA KASESNA ‘ALEJKE MIN KABLU WE MA DHELEMNAHUM WE LEKIN KANU ‘ENFUSEHUM JEDHLIMUNE
THUMME ‘INNE REBBEKE LILLEDHINE ‘AMILU ES-SU’E BIXHEHALETIN THUMME TABU MIN BA’DI DHALIKE WE ‘ESLEHU ‘INNE REBBEKE MIN BA’DIHA LEGAFURUN REHIMUN
‘INNE ‘IBRAHIME KANE ‘UMMETEN KANITÆN LILLAHI HENIFÆN WE LEM JEKU MINEL-MUSHRIKINE
SHAKIRÆN LI’N’UMIHI EXHTEBAHU WE HEDAHU ‘ILA SIRATIN MUSTEKIM
WE ‘ATEJNAHU FI ED-DUNJA HESENETEN WE ‘INNEHU FIL-’AHIRETI LEMINE ES-SALIHINE
THUMME ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE ‘ENI ETTEBI’ MILLETE ‘IBRAHIME HENIFÆN WE MA KANE MINEL-MUSHRIKINE
‘INNEMA XHU’ILE ES-SEBTU ‘ALEL-LEDHINE EHTELEFU FIHI WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEJEHKUMU BEJNEHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI FIMA KANU FIHI JEHTELIFUNE
ED’U ‘ILA SEBILI RABBIKE BIL-HIKMETI WEL-MEW’IDHETIL-HESENETI WE XHADILHUM BI-ETI HIJE ‘EHSENU ‘INNE REBBEKE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMEN DELLE ‘AN SEBILIHI WE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIL-MUHTEDINE
WE ‘IN ‘AKABTUM FA’AKIBU BIMITHLI MA ‘UKIBTUM BIHI WE LE’IN SEBERTUM LEHUWE HAJRUN LILSSABIRINE
WE ESBIR WE MA SEBRUKE ‘ILLA BILLAHI WE LA TEHZEN ‘ALEJHIM WE LA TEKU FI DEJKIN MIMMA JEMKURUNE
‘INNALL-LLAHE ME’AL-LEDHINE ETTEKAW WEL-LEDHINE HUM MUHSINUNE
SUBHANEL-LEDHI ‘ESRA BI’ABDIHI LEJLÆN MINEL-MESXHIDIL-HERAMI ‘ILAL-MESXHIDIL-’EKSAL-LEDHI BAREKNA HEWLEHU LINURIJEHU MIN ‘AJATINA ‘INNEHU HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-BESIRU
WE ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE WE XHE’ALNAHU HUDEN LIBENI ‘ISRA’ILE ‘ELLA TETTEHIDHU MIN DUNI WE KILÆN
DHURRIJETE MEN HEMELNA ME’A NUHIN ‘INNEHU KANE ‘ABDÆN SHEKURÆN
WE KADEJNA ‘ILA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE FIL-KITABI LETUFSIDUNNE FIL-’ERDI MERRETEJNI WE LETA’LUNNE ‘ULUWÆN KEBIRÆN
FE’IDHA XHA’E WA’DU ‘ULAHUMA BE’ATHNA ‘ALEJKUM ‘IBADÆN LENA ‘ULI BE’SIN SHEDIDIN FEXHASU HILALE ED-DIJARI WE KANE WA’DÆN MEF’ULÆN
THUMME REDEDNA LEKUMUL-KERRETE ‘ALEJHIM WE ‘EMDEDNAKUM BI’EMWALIN WE BENINE WE XHE’ALNAKUM ‘EKTHERE NEFIRÆN
‘IN ‘EHSENTUM ‘EHSENTUM LI’NFUSIKUM WE ‘IN ‘ESE’TUM FELEHA FE’IDHA XHA’E WA’DUL-’AHIRETI LIJESU’U WUXHUHEKUM WE LIJEDHULUL-MESXHIDE KEMA DEHALUHU ‘EWWELE MERRETIN WE LIJUTEBBIRU MA ‘ALEW TETBIRÆN
‘ASA REBBUKUM ‘EN JERHEMEKUM WE ‘IN ‘UDTUM ‘UDNA WE XHE’ALNA XHEHENNEME LILKAFIRINE HESIRÆN
‘INNE HADHAL-KUR’ANE JEHDI LILLETI HIJE ‘EKWEMU WE JUBESHSHIRUL-MU’UMININEL-LEDHINE JA’MELUNE ES-SALIHATI ‘ENNE LEHUM ‘EXHRÆN KEBIRÆN
WE ‘ENNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI ‘A’TEDNA LEHUM ‘ADHABÆN ‘ELIMÆN
WE JED’UL-’INSANU BISH-SHERRI DU’A’EHU BIL-HAJRI WE KANEL-’INSANU ‘AXHULÆN
WE XHE’ALNAL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE ‘AJETEJNI FEMEHEWNA ‘AJETEL-LEJLI WE XHE’ALNA ‘AJETE EN-NEHARI MUBSIRETEN LITEBTEGU FEDLÆN MIN RABBIKUM WE LITA’LEMU ‘ADEDE ES-SININE WEL-HISABE WE KULLE SHEJ’IN FESSELNAHU TEFSILÆN
WE KULLE ‘INSANIN ‘ELZEMNAHU TA’IREHU FI ‘UNUKIHI WE NUHRIXHU LEHU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI KITABÆN JELKAHU MENSHURÆN
EKRE’ KITABEKE KEFA BINEFSIKEL-JEWME ‘ALEJKE HESIBÆN
MENI EHTEDA FE’INNEMA JEHTEDI LINEFSIHI WE MEN DELLE FE’INNEMA JEDILLU ‘ALEJHA WE LA TEZIRU WAZIRETUN WIZRE ‘UHRA WE MA KUNNA MU’ADHDHIBINE HETTA NEB’ATHE RESULÆN
WE ‘IDHA ‘EREDNA ‘EN NUHLIKE KARJETEN ‘EMERNA MUTREFIHA FEFESEKU FIHA FEHEKKA ‘ALEJHAL-KAWLU FEDEMMERNAHA TEDMIRÆN
WE KEM ‘EHLEKNA MINEL-KURUNI MIN BA’DI NUHIN WE KEFA BIREBBIKE BIDHUNUBI ‘IBADIHI HABIRÆN BESIRÆN
MEN KANE JURIDUL-’AXHILETE ‘AXHXHELNA LEHU FIHA MA NESHA’U LIMEN NURIDU THUMME XHE’ALNA LEHU XHEHENNEME JESLAHA MEDHMUMÆN MEDHURÆN
WE MEN ‘ERADEL-’AHIRETE WE SA’A LEHA SA’JEHA WE HUWE MU’UMINUN FE’ULA’IKE KANE SA’JUHUM MESHKURÆN
KULLÆN NUMIDDU HA’UULA’ WE HA’UULA’ MIN ‘ATA’I RABBIKE WE MA KANE ‘ATA’U RABBIKE MEHDHURÆN
ENDHUR KEJFE FEDDELNA BA’DEHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN WE LEL’AHIRETU ‘EKBERU DEREXHATIN WE ‘EKBERU TEFDILÆN
LA TEXH’AL ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE FETEK’UDE MEDHMUMÆN MEHDHULÆN
WE KADA REBBUKE ‘ELLA TA’BUDU ‘ILLA ‘IJAHU WE BIL-WALIDEJNI ‘IHSANÆN ‘IMMA JEBLUGANNE ‘INDEKEL-KIBERE ‘EHEDUHUMA ‘EW KILAHUMA FELA TEKUL LEHUMA ‘UFFIN WE LA TENHERHUMA WE KUL LEHUMA KAWLÆN KERIMÆN
WE EHFID LEHUMA XHENAHE EDH-DHULLI MINE ER-REHMETI WE KUL RREBBI ERHEMHUMA KEMA REBBEJANI SEGIRÆN
REBBUKUM ‘A’LEMU BIMA FI NUFUSIKUM ‘IN TEKUNU SALIHINE FE’INNEHU KANE LIL’EWWABINE GAFURÆN
WE ‘ATI DHAL-KURBA HEKKAHU WEL-MISKINE WE EBNE ES-SEBILI WE LA TUBEDHDHIR TEBDHIRÆN
‘INNEL-MUBEDHDHIRINE KANU ‘IHWANE ESH-SHEJATINI WE KANE ESH-SHEJTANU LIREBBIHI KEFURÆN
WE ‘IMMA TU’RIDENNE ‘ANHUMU EBTIGA’E REHMETIN MIN RABBIKE TERXHUHA FEKUL LEHUM KAWLÆN MEJSURÆN
WE LA TEXH’AL JEDEKE MEGLULETEN ‘ILA ‘UNUKIKE WE LA TEBSUTHA KULLEL-BESTI FETEK’UDE MELUMÆN MEHSURÆN
‘INNE REBBEKE JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U WE JEKDIRU ‘INNEHU KANE BI’IBADIHI HABIRÆN BESIRÆN
WE LA TEKTULU ‘EWLADEKUM HASHJETE ‘IMLAKIN NEHNU NERZUKUHUM WE ‘IJAKUM ‘INNE KATLEHUM KANE HIT’ÆN KEBIRÆN
WE LA TEKREBU EZ-ZINA ‘INNEHU KANE FAHISHETEN WE SA’E SEBILÆN
WE LA TEKTULU EN-NEFSEL-LETI HERREMEL-LAHU ‘ILLA BIL-HEKKI WE MEN KUTILE MEDHLUMÆN FEKAD XHE’ALNA LIWELIJIHI SULTANÆN FELA JUSRIF FIL-KATLI ‘INNEHU KANE MENSURÆN
WE LA TEKREBU MALEL-JETIMI ‘ILLA BI-ETI HIJE ‘EHSENU HETTA JEBLUGA ‘ESHUDDEHU WE ‘EWFU BIL-’AHDI ‘INNEL-’AHDE KANE MES’ULÆN
WE ‘EWFUL-KEJLE ‘IDHA KILTUM WE ZINU BIL-KISTASIL-MUSTEKIMI DHALIKE HAJRUN WE ‘EHSENU TE’WILÆN
WE LA TEKFU MA LEJSE LEKE BIHI ‘ILMUN ‘INNE ES-SEM’A WEL-BESERE WEL-FU’UADE KULLU ‘ULA’IKE KANE ‘ANHU MES’ULÆN
WE LA TEMSHI FIL-’ERDI MEREHÆN ‘INNEKE LEN TEHRIKAL-’ERDE WE LEN TEBLUGAL-XHIBALE TULÆN
KULLU DHALIKE KANE SEJJI’UHU ‘INDE RABBIKE MEKRUHÆN
DHALIKE MIMMA ‘EWHA ‘ILEJKE REBBUKE MINEL-HIKMETI WE LA TEXH’AL ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE FETULKA FI XHEHENNEME MELUMÆN MEDHURÆN
‘EFE’ESFAKUM REBBUKUM BIL-BENINE WE ETTEHADHE MINEL-MELA’IKETI ‘INATHÆN ‘INNEKUM LETEKULUNE KAWLÆN ‘ADHIMÆN
WE LEKAD SERREFNA FI HADHAL-KUR’ANI LIJEDHDHEKKERU WE MA JEZIDUHUM ‘ILLA NUFURÆN
KUL LEW KANE ME’AHU ‘ALIHETUN KEMA JEKULUNE ‘IDHÆN LABTEGAW ‘ILA DHIL-’ARSHI SEBILÆN
SUBHANEHU WE TA’ALA ‘AMMA JEKULUNE ‘ULUWÆN KEBIRÆN
TUSEBBIHU LEHU ES-SEMAWATU ES-SEB’U WEL-’ERDU WE MEN FIHINNE WE ‘IN MIN SHEJ’IN ‘ILLA JUSEBBIHU BIHEMDIHI WE LEKIN LA TEFKAHUNE TESBIHEHUM ‘INNEHU KANE HELIMÆN GAFURÆN
WE ‘IDHA KARE’TEL-KUR’ANE XHE’ALNA BEJNEKE WE BEJNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI HIXHABÆN MESTURÆN
WE XHE’ALNA ‘ALA KULUBIHIM ‘EKINNETEN ‘EN JEFKAHUHU WE FI ‘ADHANIHIM WEKRÆN WE ‘IDHA DHEKERTE REBBEKE FIL-KUR’ANI WEHDEHU WE LLEW ‘ALA ‘EDBARIHIM NUFURÆN
NEHNU ‘A’LEMU BIMA JESTEMI’UNE BIHI ‘IDH JESTEMI’UNE ‘ILEJKE WE ‘IDH HUM NEXHWA ‘IDH JEKULU EDH-DHALIMUNE ‘IN TETTEBI’UNE ‘ILLA REXHULÆN MESHURÆN
ENDHUR KEJFE DEREBU LEKEL-’EMTHALE FEDELLU FELA JESTETI’UNE SEBILÆN
WE KALU ‘E’IDHA KUNNA ‘IDHAMÆN WE RUFATÆN ‘E’INNA LEMEB’UTHUNE HALKÆN XHEDIDÆN
KUL KUNU HIXHARETEN ‘EW HEDIDÆN
‘EW HALKÆN MIMMA JEKBURU FI SUDURIKUM FESEJEKULUNE MEN JU’IDUNA KULIL-LEDHI FETEREKUM ‘EWWELE MERRETIN FESEJUNGIDUNE ‘ILEJKE RU’USEHUM WE JEKULUNE META HUWE KUL ‘ASA ‘EN JEKUNE KARIBÆN
JEWME JED’UKUM FETESTEXHIBUNE BIHEMDIHI WE TEDHUNNUNE ‘IN LEBITHTUM ‘ILLA KALILÆN
WE KUL LI’IBADI JEKULU ELLETI HIJE ‘EHSENU ‘INNE ESH-SHEJTANE JENZEGU BEJNEHUM ‘INNE ESH-SHEJTANE KANE LIL’INSANI ‘ADUWÆN MUBINÆN
REBBUKUM ‘A’LEMU BIKUM ‘IN JESHE’ JERHEMKUM ‘EW ‘IN JESHE’ JU’ADHDHIBKUM WE MA ‘ERSELNAKE ‘ALEJHIM WE KILÆN
WE REBBUKE ‘A’LEMU BIMEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE LEKAD FEDDELNA BA’DE EN-NEBIJINE ‘ALA BA’DIN WE ‘ATEJNA DAWUDE ZEBURÆN
KULI ED’UL-LEDHINE ZE’AMTUM MIN DUNIHI FELA JEMLIKUNE KESHFE ED-DURRI ‘ANKUM WE LA TEHWILÆN
‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE JED’UNE JEBTEGUNE ‘ILA RABBIHIMUL-WESILETE ‘EJJUHUM ‘EKREBU WE JERXHUNE REHMETEHU WE JEHAFUNE ‘ADHABEHU ‘INNE ‘ADHABE RABBIKE KANE MEHDHURÆN
WE ‘IN MIN KARJETIN ‘ILLA NEHNU MUHLIKUHA KABLE JEWMIL-KIJAMETI ‘EW MU’ADHDHIBUHA ‘ADHABÆN SHEDIDÆN KANE DHALIKE FIL-KITABI MESTURÆN
WE MA MENE’ANA ‘EN NURSILE BIL-’AJATI ‘ILLA ‘EN KEDHDHEBE BIHAL-’EWWELUNE WE ‘ATEJNA THEMUDE EN-NAKATE MUBSIRETEN FEDHELEMU BIHA WE MA NURSILU BIL-’AJATI ‘ILLA TEHWIFÆN
WE ‘IDH KULNA LEKE ‘INNE REBBEKE ‘EHATE BIN-NASI WE MA XHE’ALNA ER-RU’UJA ELLETI ‘EREJNAKE ‘ILLA FITNETEN LILNNASI WE ESH-SHEXHERETEL-MEL’UNETE FIL-KUR’ANI WE NUHAWWIFUHUM FEMA JEZIDUHUM ‘ILLA TUGJANÆN KEBIRÆN
WE ‘IDH KULNA LILMELA’IKETI ESXHUDU LI’DEME FESEXHEDU ‘ILLA ‘IBLISE KALE ‘E’ESXHUDU LIMEN HALEKTE TINÆN
KALE ‘ERE’EJTEKE HADHAL-LEDHI KERREMTE ‘ALEJJE LE’IN ‘EHHARTENI ‘ILA JEWMIL-KIJAMETI LE’EHTENIKENNE DHURRIJETEHU ‘ILLA KALILÆN
KALE EDH/HEB FEMEN TEBI’AKE MINHUM FE’INNE XHEHENNEME XHEZA’UUKUM XHEZA’EN MEWFURÆN
WE ESTEFZIZ MENI ESTETA’TE MINHUM BISEWTIKE WE ‘EXHLIB ‘ALEJHIM BIHAJLIKE WE REXHILIKE WE SHARIK/HUM FIL-’EMWLI WEL-’EWLADI WE ‘ID/HUM WE MA JA’IDUHUMU ESH-SHEJTANU ‘ILLA GURURÆN
‘INNE ‘IBADI LEJSE LEKE ‘ALEJHIM SULTANUN WE KEFA BIREBBIKE WE KILÆN
REBBUKUMUL-LEDHI JUZXHI LEKUMUL-FULKE FIL-BEHRI LITEBTEGU MIN FEDLIHI ‘INNEHU KANE BIKUM REHIMÆN
WE ‘IDHA MESSEKUMU ED-DURRU FIL-BEHRI DELLE MEN TED’UNE ‘ILLA ‘IJAHU FELEMMA NEXHXHAKUM ‘ILAL-BERRI ‘A’REDTUM WE KANEL-’INSANU KEFURÆN
‘EFE’EMINTUM ‘EN JEHSIFE BIKUM XHANIBEL-BERRI ‘EW JURSILE ‘ALEJKUM HASIBÆN THUMME LA TEXHIDU LEKUM WE KILÆN
‘EM ‘EMINTUM ‘EN JU’IDEKUM FIHI TARETEN ‘UHRA FEJURSILE ‘ALEJKUM KASIFÆN MINE ER-RIHI FEJUGRIKAKUM BIMA KEFERTUM THUMME LA TEXHIDU LEKUM ‘ALEJNA BIHI TEBI’ÆN
WE LEKAD KERREMNA BENI ‘ADEME WE HEMELNAHUM FIL-BERRI WEL-BEHRI WE REZEKNAHUM MINET-TEJJIBATI WE FEDDELNAHUM ‘ALA KETHIRIN MIMMEN HALEKNA TEFDILÆN
JEWME NED’U KULLE ‘UNASIN BI’IMAMIHIM FEMEN ‘UTIJE KITABEHU BIJEMINIHI FE’ULA’IKE JEKRE’UNE KITABEHUM WE LA JUDHLEMUNE FETILÆN
WE MEN KANE FI HEDHIHI ‘A’MA FEHUWE FIL-’AHIRETI ‘A’MA WE ‘EDELLU SEBILÆN
WE ‘IN KADU LEJEFTINUNEKE ‘ANIL-LEDHI ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE LITEFTERIJE ‘ALEJNA GAJREHU WE ‘IDHÆN LATTEHADHUKE HALILÆN
WE LEWLA ‘EN THEBBETNAKE LEKAD KIDTTE TERKENU ‘ILEJHIM SHEJ’ÆN KALILÆN
‘IDHÆN LE’EDHEKNAKE DI’FEL-HEJÆTI WE DI’FEL-MEMATI THUMME LA TEXHIDU LEKE ‘ALEJNA NESIRÆN
WE ‘IN KADU LEJESTEFIZZUNEKE MINEL-’ERDI LIJUHRIXHUKE MINHA WE ‘IDHÆN LA JELBETHUNE HILAFEKE ‘ILLA KALILÆN
SUNNETE MEN KAD ‘ERSELNA KABLEKE MIN RUSULINA WE LA TEXHIDU LISUNNETINA TEHWILÆN
‘EKIMI ES-SELÆTE LIDULUKI ESH-SHEMSI ‘ILA GASEKIL-LEJLI WE KUR’ANEL-FEXHRI ‘INNE KUR’ANEL-FEXHRI KANE MESH/HUDÆN
WE MINEL-LEJLI FETEHEXHXHED BIHI NAFILETEN LEKE ‘ASA ‘EN JEB’ATHEKE REBBUKE MEKAMÆN MEHMUDÆN
WE KUL RABBI ‘EDHILNI MUDHALE SIDKIN WE ‘EHRIXHNI MUHREXHE SIDKIN WE EXH’AL LI MIN LEDUNKE SULTANÆN NESIRÆN
WE KUL XHA’EL-HEKKU WE ZEHEKAL-BATILU ‘INNEL-BATILE KANE ZEHUKÆN
WE NUNEZZILU MINEL-KUR’ANI MA HUWE SHIFA’UN WE REHMETUN LILMU’UMININE WE LA JEZIDU EDH-DHALIMINE ‘ILLA HASARÆN
WE ‘IDHA ‘EN’AMNA ‘ALEL-’INSANI ‘A’REDE WE NE’A BIXHANIBIHI WE ‘IDHA MESSEHU ESH-SHERRU KANE JE’USÆN
KUL KULLUN JA’MELU ‘ALA SHAKILETIHI FEREBBUKUM ‘A’LEMU BIMEN HUWE ‘EHDA SEBILÆN
WE JES’ELUNEKE ‘ANI ER-RUHI KULI ER-RUHU MIN ‘EMRI RABBI WE MA ‘UTITUM MINEL-’ILMI ‘ILLA KALILÆN
WE LE’IN SHI’NA LENEDH/HEBENNE BIEL-LEDHI ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE THUMME LA TEXHIDU LEKE BIHI ‘ALEJNA WE KILÆN
‘ILLA REHMETEN MIN RABBIKE ‘INNE FEDLEHU KANE ‘ALEJKE KEBIRÆN
KUL LE’INI EXHTEME’ATIL-’INSU WEL-XHINNU ‘ALA ‘EN JE’TU BIMITHLI HADHAL-KUR’ANI LA JE’TUNE BIMITHLIHI WE LEW KANE BA’DUHUM LIBA’DIN DHEHIRÆN
WE LEKAD SERREFNA LILNNASI FI HADHAL-KUR’ANI MIN KULLI METHELIN FE’EBA ‘EKTHERU EN-NASI ‘ILLA KUFURÆN
WE KALU LEN NU’UMINE LEKE HETTA TEFXHURE LENA MINEL-’ERDI JENBU’ÆN
‘EW TEKUNE LEKE XHENNETUN MIN NEHILIN WE ‘INEBIN FETUFEXHXHIREL-’ENHARE HILALEHA TEFXHIRÆN
‘EW TUSKITE ES-SEMA’E KEMA ZE’AMTE ‘ALEJNA KISEFÆN ‘EW TE’TIJE BILLAHI WEL-MELA’IKETI KABILÆN
‘EW JEKUNE LEKE BEJTUN MIN ZUHRUFIN ‘EW TERKA FI ES-SEMA’I WE LEN NU’UMINE LIRUKIJIKE HETTA TUNEZZILE ‘ALEJNA KITABÆN NEKRE’UUHU KUL SUBHANE RABBI HEL KUNTU ‘ILLA BESHERÆN RESULÆN
WE MA MENE’A EN-NASE ‘EN JU’UMINU ‘IDH XHA’EHUMUL-HUDA ‘ILLA ‘EN KALU ‘EBE’ATHEL-LAHU BESHERÆN RESULÆN
KUL LEW KANE FIL-’ERDI MELA’IKETUN JEMSHUNE MUTME’INNINE LENEZZELNA ‘ALEJHIM MINE ES-SEMA’I MELEKÆN RESULÆN
KUL KEFA BILLAHI SHEHIDÆN BEJNI WE BEJNEKUM ‘INNEHU KANE BI’IBADIHI HABIRÆN BESIRÆN
WE MEN JEHDI ELLAHU FEHUWEL-MUHTEDI WE MEN JUDLIL FELEN TEXHIDE LEHUM ‘EWLIJA’E MIN DUNIHI WE NEHSHURUHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘ALA WEXHUHIHIM ‘UMJÆN WE BUKMÆN WE SUMMÆN ME’WAHUM XHEHENNEMU KULLEMA HABET ZIDNAHUM SA’IRÆN
DHALIKE XHEZA’UUHUM BI’ENNEHUM KEFERU BI’AJATINA WE KALU ‘E’IDHA KUNNA ‘IDHAMÆN WE RUFATÆN ‘E’INNA LEMEB’UTHUNE HALKÆN XHEDIDÆN
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNEL-LAHEL-LEDHI HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE KADIRUN ‘ALA ‘EN JEHLUKA MITHLEHUM WE XHE’ALE LEHUM ‘EXHELÆN LA REJBE FIHI FE’EBA EDH-DHALIMUNE ‘ILLA KUFURÆN
KUL LEW ‘ENTUM TEMLIKUNE HAZA’INE REHMETI RABBI ‘IDHÆN LE’EMSEKTUM HASHJETEL-’INFAKI WE KANEL-’INSANU KATURÆN
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSA TIS’A ‘AJATIN BEJJINATIN FAS’L BENI ‘ISRA’ILE ‘IDH XHA’EHUM FEKALE LEHU FIR’AWNU ‘INNI LE’EDHUNNUKE JAMUSA MESHURÆN
KALE LEKAD ‘ALIMTE MA ‘ENZELE HA’UULA’ ‘ILLA REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI BESA’IRE WE ‘INNI LE’EDHUNNUKE JA FIR’AWNU METHBURÆN
FE’ERADE ‘EN JESTEFIZZEHUM MINEL-’ERDI FE’EGREKNAHU WE MEN ME’AHU XHEMI’ÆN
WE KULNA MIN BA’DIHI LIBENI ‘ISRA’ILE ESKUNUL-’ERDE FE’IDHA XHA’E WA’DUL-’AHIRETI XHI’NA BIKUM LEFIFÆN
WE BIL-HEKKI ‘ENZELNAHU WE BIL-HEKKI NEZELE WE MA ‘ERSELNAKE ‘ILLA MUBESHSHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN
WE KUR’ANÆN FEREKNAHU LITEKRE’EHU ‘ALA EN-NASI ‘ALA MUKTHIN WE NEZZELNAHU TENZILÆN
KUL ‘AMINU BIHI ‘EW LA TU’UMINU ‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME MIN KABLIHI ‘IDHA JUTLA ‘ALEJHIM JEHIRRUNE LIL’EDHKANI SUXHXHEDÆN
WE JEKULUNE SUBHANE RABBINA ‘IN KANE WA’DU RABBINA LEMEF’ULÆN
WE JEHIRRUNE LIL’EDHKANI JEBKUNE WE JEZIDUHUM HUSHU’ÆN
KUL ED’U ELLAHE ‘EW ED’U ER-REHMENE ‘EJJENEN MMA TED’U FELEHUL-’ESMA’UL-HUSNA WE LA TEXHHER BISELATIKE WE LA TUHAFIT BIHA WE EBTEGI BEJNE DHALIKE SEBILÆN
WE KULIL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI LEM JETTEHIDH WELEDÆN WE LEM JEKUN LEHU SHERIKUN FIL-MULKI WE LEM JEKUN LEHU WE LIJUN MINE EDH-DHULLI WE KEBBIRHU TEKBIRÆN
EL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI ‘ENZELE ‘ALA ‘ABDIHIL-KITABE WE LEM JEXH’AL LLEHU ‘IWEXHA
KAJJIMÆN LIJUNDHIRE BE’SÆN SHEDIDÆN MIN LEDUNHU WE JUBESHSHIREL-MU’UMININEL-LEDHINE JA’MELUNE ES-SALIHATI ‘ENNE LEHUM ‘EXHRÆN HESENÆN
MAKITHINE FIHI ‘EBEDÆN
WE JUNDHIREL-LEDHINE KALU ETTEHADHEL-LAHU WELEDÆN
MMA LEHUM BIHI MIN ‘ILMIN WE LA LI’ABA’IHIM KEBURET KELIMETEN TEHRUXHU MIN ‘EFWAHIHIM ‘IN JEKULUNE ‘ILLA KEDHIBÆN
FELE’ALLEKE BAHI’UN NEFSEKE ‘ALA ‘ATHARIHIM ‘IN LEM JU’UMINU BIHEDHAL-HEDITHI ‘ESEFÆN
‘INNA XHE’ALNA MA ‘ALEL-’ERDI ZINETEN LEHA LINEBLUWEHUM ‘EJJUHUM ‘EHSENU ‘AMELÆN
WE ‘INNA LEXHA’ILUNE MA ‘ALEJHA SA’IDÆN XHURUZÆN
‘EM HESIBTE ‘ENNE ‘ESHABEL-KEHFI WE ER-REKIMI KANU MIN ‘AJATINA ‘AXHEBÆN
‘IDH ‘EWAL-FITJETU ‘ILAL-KEHFI FEKALU REBBENA ‘ATINA MIN LEDUNKE REHMETEN WE HEJJI’ LENA MIN ‘EMRINA RESHEDÆN
FEDEREBNA ‘ALA ‘ADHANIHIM FIL-KEHFI SININE ‘ADEDÆN
THUMME BE’ATHNAHUM LINA’LEME ‘EJJUL-HIZBEJNI ‘EHSA LIMA LEBITHU ‘EMEDÆN
NEHNU NEKUSSU ‘ALEJKE NEBE’EHUM BIL-HEKKI ‘INNEHUM FITJETUN ‘AMENU BIREBBIHIM WE ZIDNAHUM HUDEN
WE REBETNA ‘ALA KULUBIHIM ‘IDH KAMU FEKALU REBBUNA REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI LEN NED’UWE MIN DUNIHI ‘ILEHÆN LEKAD KULNA ‘IDHÆN SHETETÆN
HA’UULA’ KAWMUNA ETTEHADHU MIN DUNIHI ‘ALIHETEN LEWLA JE’TUNE ‘ALEJHIM BISULTANIN BEJJININ FEMEN ‘EDHLEMU MIMMENI EFTERA ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN
WE ‘IDH A’TEZELTUMUHUM WE MA JA’BUDUNE ‘ILLALLAHE FE’WU ‘ILAL-KEHFI JENSHUR LEKUM REBBUKUM MIN REHMETIHI WE JUHEJJI’ LEKUM MIN ‘EMRIKUM MIRFEKÆN
WE TERA ESH-SHEMSE ‘IDHA TELE’AT TEZAWERU ‘AN KEHFIHIM DHATEL-JEMINI WE ‘IDHA GAREBET TEKRIDUHUM DHATE ESH-SHIMALI WE HUM FI FEXHWETIN MINHU DHALIKE MIN ‘AJATI ELLAHI MEN JEHDI ELLAHU FEHUWEL-MUHTEDI WE MEN JUDLIL FELEN TEXHIDE LEHU WELIJÆN MURSHIDÆN
WE TEHSEBUHUM ‘EJKADHÆN WE HUM RUKUDUN WE NUKALLIBUHUM DHATEL-JEMINI WE DHATE ESH-SHIMALI WE KELBUHUM BASITUN DHIRA’AJHI BIL-WESIDI LEWI ETTELA’TE ‘ALEJHIM LEWELLEJTE MINHUM FIRARÆN WE LEMULI’TE MINHUM RU’BÆN
WE KEDHELIKE BE’ATHNAHUM LIJETESA’ELU BEJNEHUM KALE KA’ILUN MINHUM KEM LEBITHTUM KALU LEBITHNA JEWMÆN ‘EW BA’DE JEWMIN KALU REBBUKUM ‘A’LEMU BIMA LEBITHTUM FAB’ATHU ‘EHEDEKUM BIWERIKIKUM HEDHIHI ‘ILAL-MEDINETI FELJENDHUR ‘EJJUHA ‘EZKA TA’AMÆN FELJE’TIKUM 
‘INNEHUM ‘IN JEDHHERU ‘ALEJKUM JERXHUMUKUM ‘EW JU’IDUKUM FI MILLETIHIM WE LEN TUFLIHU ‘IDHÆN ‘EBEDÆN
WE KEDHELIKE ‘A’THERNA ‘ALEJHIM LIJA’LEMU ‘ENNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN WE ‘ENNE ES-SA’ATE LA REJBE FIHA ‘IDH JETENAZA’UNE BEJNEHUM ‘EMREHUM FEKALU EBNU ‘ALEJHIM BUNJANÆN REBBUHUM ‘A’LEMU BIHIM KALEL-LEDHINE GALEBU ‘ALA ‘EMRIHIM LENETTEHIDHENNE ‘ALEJHIM MESXHI
SEJEKULUNE THELATHETUN RABI’UHUM KELBUHUM WE JEKULUNE HAMSETUN SADISUHUM KELBUHUM REXHMÆN BIL-GAJBI WE JEKULUNE SEB’ATUN WE THAMINUHUM KELBUHUM KUL RABBI ‘A’LEMU BI’IDDETIHIM MA JA’LEMUHUM ‘ILLA KALILUN FELA TUMARI FIHIM ‘ILLA MIRA’EN DHAHIRÆN WE LA TESTE
WE LA TEKULENNE LISHEJ’IN ‘INNI FA’ILUN DHALIKE GADÆN
‘ILLA ‘EN JESHA’EL-LAHU WE EDHKUR REBBEKE ‘IDHA NESITE WE KUL ‘ASA ‘EN JEHDIJENI RABBI LI’KREBE MIN HADHA RESHEDÆN
WE LEBITHU FI KEHFIHIM THELATHE MIA’ETIN SININE WE EZDADU TIS’ÆN
KULI ELLAHU ‘A’LEMU BIMA LEBITHU LEHU GAJBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘EBSIR BIHI WE ‘ESMI’ MA LEHUM MIN DUNIHI MIN WE LIJIN WE LA JUSHRIKU FI HUKMIHI ‘EHEDÆN
WE ETLU MA ‘UHIJE ‘ILEJKE MIN KITABI RABBIKE LA MUBEDDILE LIKELIMATIHI WE LEN TEXHIDE MIN DUNIHI MULTEHEDÆN
WE ESBIR NEFSEKE ME’AL-LEDHINE JED’UNE REBBEHUM BIL-GADÆTI WEL-’ASHIJI JURIDUNE WEXHHEHU WE LA TA’DU ‘AJNAKE ‘ANHUM TURIDU ZINETEL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE LA TUTI’ MEN ‘EGFELNA KALBEHU ‘AN DHIKRINA WE ETTEBE’A HEWAHU WE KANE ‘EMRUHU FURUTÆN
WE KULIL-HEKKU MIN RABBIKUM FEMEN SHA’E FELJU’UMIN WE MEN SHA’E FELJEKFUR ‘INNA ‘A’TEDNA LILDHDHALIMINE NARÆN ‘EHATE BIHIM SURADIKUHA WE ‘IN JESTEGITHU JUGATHU BIMA’IN KALMUHLI JESHWIL-WUXHUHE BI’SE ESH-SHERABU WE SA’ET MURTEFEKÆN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI ‘INNA LA NUDI’U ‘EXHRE MEN ‘EHSENE ‘AMELÆN
‘ULA’IKE LEHUM XHENNATU ‘ADNIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHIMUL-’ENHARU JUHELLEWNE FIHA MIN ‘ESAWIRE MIN DHEHEBIN WE JELBESUNE THIJABÆN HUDRÆN MIN SUNDUSIN WE ‘ISTEBREKIN MUTTEKI’INE FIHA ‘ALEL-’ERA’IKI NI’ME ETH-THEWABU WE HESUNET MURTEFEKÆN
WE EDRIB LEHUM METHELÆN REXHULEJNI XHE’ALNA LI’HEDIHIMA XHENNETEJNI MIN ‘A’NABIN WE HEFEFNAHUMA BINEHLIN WE XHE’ALNA BEJNEHUMA ZER’ÆN
KILTAL-XHENNETEJNI ‘ATET ‘UKULEHA WE LEM TEDHLIM MINHU SHEJ’ÆN WE FEXHXHERNA HILALEHUMA NEHERÆN
WE KANE LEHU THEMERUN FEKALE LISAHIBIHI WE HUWE JUHAWIRUHU ‘ENA ‘EKTHERU MINKE MALÆN WE ‘E’AZZU NEFERÆN
WE DEHALE XHENNETEHU WE HUWE DHALIMUN LINEFSIHI KALE MA ‘EDHUNNU ‘EN TEBIDE HEDHIHI ‘EBEDÆN
WE MA ‘EDHUNNU ES-SA’ATE KA’IMETEN WE LE’IN RUDIDTU ‘ILA RABBI LE’EXHIDENNE HAJRÆN MINHA MUNKALEBÆN
KALE LEHU SAHIBUHU WE HUWE JUHAWIRUHU ‘EKEFERTE BIEL-LEDHI HALEKAKE MIN TURABIN THUMME MIN NUTFETIN THUMME SEWWAKE REXHULÆN
LEKINNA HUWEL-LAHU RABBI WE LA ‘USHRIKU BIREBBI ‘EHEDÆN
WE LEWLA ‘IDH DEHALTE XHENNETEKE KULTE MA SHA’EL-LAHU LA KUWETE ‘ILLA BILLAHI ‘IN TERENI ‘ENA ‘EKALLE MINKE MALÆN WE WELEDÆN
FE’ASA RABBI ‘EN JU’UTIJENI HAJRÆN MIN XHENNETIKE WE JURSILE ‘ALEJHA HUSBANÆN MINE ES-SEMA’I FETUSBIHE SA’IDÆN ZELEKÆN
‘EW JUSBIHE MA’UUHA GAWRÆN FELEN TESTETI’A LEHU TELEBÆN
WE ‘UHITE BITHEMERIHI FE’ESBEHE JUKALLIBU KEFFEJHI ‘ALA MA ‘ENFEKA FIHA WE HIJE HAWIJETUN ‘ALA ‘URUSHIHA WE JEKULU JA LEJTENI LEM ‘USHRIK BIREBBI ‘EHEDÆN
WE LEM TEKUN LEHU FI’ETUN JENSURUNEHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI WE MA KANE MUNTESIRÆN
HUNALIKEL-WELAJETU LILLAHIL-HEKKI HUWE HAJRUN THEWABÆN WE HAJRUN ‘UKBÆN
WE EDRIB LEHUM METHELEL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA KEMA’IN ‘ENZELNAHU MINE ES-SEMA’I FAHTELETE BIHI NEBATUL-’ERDI FE’ESBEHE HESHIMÆN TEDHRUHU ER-RIJAHU WE KANEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN MUKTEDIRÆN
EL-MALU WEL-BENUNE ZINETUL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WEL-BAKIJATU ES-SALIHATU HAJRUN ‘INDE RABBIKE THEWABÆN WE HAJRUN ‘EMELÆN
WE JEWME NUSEJJIRUL-XHIBALE WE TERAL-’ERDE BARIZETEN WE HESHERNAHUM FELEM NUGADIR MINHUM ‘EHEDÆN
WE ‘URIDU ‘ALA RABBIKE SEFFÆN LEKAD XHI’TUMUNA KEMA HALEKNAKUM ‘EWWELE MERRETIN BEL ZE’AMTUM ‘ELLEN NEXH’ALE LEKUM MEW’IDÆN
WE WUDI’AL-KITABU FETERAL-MUXHRIMINE MUSHFIKINE MIMMA FIHI WE JEKULUNE JA WEJLETENA MALI HADHAL-KITABI LA JUGADIRU SEGIRETEN WE LA KEBIRETEN ‘ILLA ‘EHSAHA WE WEXHEDU MA ‘AMILU HADIRÆN WE LA JEDHLIMU REBBUKE ‘EHEDÆN
WE ‘IDH KULNA LILMELA’IKETI ESXHUDU LI’DEME FESEXHEDU ‘ILLA ‘IBLISE KANE MINEL-XHINNI FEFESEKA ‘AN ‘EMRI RABBIHI ‘EFETETTEHIDHUNEHU WE DHURRIJETEHU ‘EWLIJA’E MIN DUNI WE HUM LEKUM ‘ADUWUN BI’SE LILDHDHALIMINE BEDELÆN
MA ‘ESH/HEDTUHUM HALKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE LA HALKA ‘ENFUSIHIM WE MA KUNTU MUTTEHIDHEL-MUDILLINE ‘ADUDÆN
WE JEWME JEKULU NADU SHUREKA’IJEL-LEDHINE ZE’AMTUM FEDE’AWHUM FELEM JESTEXHIBU LEHUM WE XHE’ALNA BEJNEHUM MEWBIKÆN
WE RE’AL-MUXHRIMUNE EN-NARE FEDHENNU ‘ENNEHUM MUWAKI’UHA WE LEM JEXHIDU ‘ANHA MESRIFÆN
WE LEKAD SERREFNA FI HADHAL-KUR’ANI LILNNASI MIN KULLI METHELIN WE KANEL-’INSANU ‘EKTHERE SHEJ’IN XHEDELÆN
WE MA MENE’A EN-NASE ‘EN JU’UMINU ‘IDH XHA’EHUMUL-HUDA WE JESTEGFIRU REBBEHUM ‘ILLA ‘EN TE’TIJEHUM SUNNETUL-’EWWELINE ‘EW JE’TIJEHUMUL-’ADHABU KUBULÆN
WE MA NURSILUL-MURSELINE ‘ILLA MUBESHSHIRINE WE MUNDHIRINE WE JUXHADILUL-LEDHINE KEFERU BIL-BATILI LIJUDHIDU BIHIL-HEKKA WE ETTEHADHU ‘AJATI WE MA ‘UNDHIRU HUZUEN
WE MEN ‘EDHLEMU MIMMEN DHUKKIRE BI’AJATI RABBIHI FE’A’REDE ‘ANHA WE NESIJE MA KADDEMET JEDAHU ‘INNA XHE’ALNA ‘ALA KULUBIHIM ‘EKINNETEN ‘EN JEFKAHUHU WE FI ‘ADHANIHIM WEKRÆN WE ‘IN TED’UHUM ‘ILAL-HUDA FELEN JEHTEDU ‘IDHÆN ‘EBEDÆN
WE REBBUKEL-GAFURU DHU ER-REHMETI LEW JU’UAHIDHUHUM BIMA KESEBU LE’AXHXHELE LEHUMUL-’ADHABE BEL LEHUM MEW’IDUN LEN JEXHIDU MIN DUNIHI MEW’ILÆN
WE TILKEL-KURA ‘EHLEKNAHUM LEMMA DHELEMU WE XHE’ALNA LIMEHLIKIHIM MEW’IDÆN
WE ‘IDH KALE MUSA LIFETAHU LA ‘EBREHU HETTA ‘EBLUGA MEXHME’AL-BEHREJNI ‘EW ‘EMDIJE HUKUBÆN
FELEMMA BELEGA MEXHME’A BEJNIHIMA NESIJA HUTEHUMA FE ETTEHADHE SEBILEHU FIL-BEHRI SEREBÆN
FELEMMA XHAWEZA KALE LIFETAHU ‘ATINA GADA’ENA LEKAD LEKINA MIN SEFERINA HADHA NESEBÆN
KALE ‘ERE’EJTE ‘IDH ‘EWEJNA ‘ILA ES-SEHRETI FE’INNI NESITUL-HUTE WE MA ‘ENSANIHU ‘ILLA ESH-SHEJTANU ‘EN ‘EDHKUREHU WE ETTEHADHE SEBILEHU FIL-BEHRI ‘AXHEBÆN
KALE DHALIKE MA KUNNA NEBGI FARTEDDA ‘ALA ‘ATHARIHIMA KASESÆN
FEWEXHEDA ‘ABDÆN MIN ‘IBADINA ‘ATEJNAHU REHMETEN MIN ‘INDINA WE ‘ALLEMNAHU MIN LEDUNNA ‘ILMÆN
KALE LEHU MUSA HEL ‘ETTEBI’UKE ‘ALA ‘EN TU’ALLIMENI MIMMA ‘ULLIMTE RUSHDÆN
KALE ‘INNEKE LEN TESTETI’A MA’IJE SEBRÆN
WE KEJFE TESBIRU ‘ALA MA LEM TUHIT BIHI HUBRÆN
KALE SETEXHIDUNI ‘IN SHA’EL-LAHU SABIRÆN WE LA ‘A’SI LEKE ‘EMRÆN
KALE FE’INI ETTEBA’TENI FELA TES’ELNI ‘AN SHEJ’IN HETTA ‘UHDITHE LEKE MINHU DHIKRÆN
FANTELEKA HETTA ‘IDHA REKIBA FI ES-SEFINETI HAREKAHA KALE ‘EHAREKTEHA LITUGRIKA ‘EHLEHA LEKAD XHI’TE SHEJ’ÆN ‘IMRÆN
KALE ‘ELEM ‘EKUL ‘INNEKE LEN TESTETI’A MA’IJE SEBRÆN
KALE LA TU’UAHIDHNI BIMA NESITU WE LA TURHIKNI MIN ‘EMRI ‘USRÆN
FANTELEKA HETTA ‘IDHA LEKIJA GULAMÆN FEKATELEHU KALE ‘EKATELTE NEFSÆN ZEKIJETEN BIGAJRI NEFSIN LEKAD XHI’TE SHEJ’ÆN NUKRÆN
KALE ‘ELEM ‘EKUL LEKE ‘INNEKE LEN TESTETI’A MA’IJE SEBRÆN
KALE ‘IN SE’ELTUKE ‘AN SHEJ’IN BA’DEHA FELA TUSAHIBNI KAD BELEGTE MIN LEDUNNI ‘UDHRÆN
FANTELEKA HETTA ‘IDHA ‘ETEJA ‘EHLE KARJETIN ESTET’AMA ‘EHLEHA FE’EBEW ‘EN JUDEJJIFUHUMA FEWEXHEDA FIHA XHIDARÆN JURIDU ‘EN JENKADDE FE’EKAMEHU KALE LEW SHI’TE LATTEHADHTE ‘ALEJHI ‘EXHRÆN
KALE HADHA FIRAKU BEJNI WE BEJNIKE SE’UNEBBI’UKE BITE’WILI MA LEM TESTETI’ ‘ALEJHI SEBRÆN
‘EMMA ES-SEFINETU FEKANET LIMESAKINE JA’MELUNE FIL-BEHRI FE’EREDTU ‘EN ‘A’IBEHA WE KANE WERA’EHUM MELIKUN JE’HUDHU KULLE SEFINETIN GASBÆN
WE ‘EMMAL-GULAMU FEKANE ‘EBEWAHU MU’UMINEJNI FEHASHINA ‘EN JURHIKAHUMA TUGJANÆN WE KUFRÆN
FE’EREDNA ‘EN JUBDILEHUMA REBBUHUMA HAJRÆN MINHU ZEKÆTEN WE ‘EKREBE RUHMÆN
WE ‘EMMAL-XHIDARU FEKANE LIGULAMEJNI JETIMEJNI FIL-MEDINETI WE KANE TEHTEHU KENZUN LEHUMA WE KANE ‘EBUHUMA SALIHÆN FE’ERADE REBBUKE ‘EN JEBLUGA ‘ESHUDDEHUMA WE JESTEHRIXHA KENZEHUMA REHMETEN MIN RABBIKE WE MA FE’ALTUHU ‘AN ‘EMRI DHALIKE TE’WILU MA LEM TES
