WE JES’ELUNEKE ‘AN DHIL-KARNEJNI KUL SE’ETLU ‘ALEJKUM MINHU DHIKRÆN
‘INNA MEKKENNA LEHU FIL-’ERDI WE ‘ATEJNAHU MIN KULLI SHEJ’IN SEBEBÆN
FE’ETBE’A SEBEBÆN
HETTA ‘IDHA BELEGA MEGRIBE ESH-SHEMSI WEXHEDEHA TEGRUBU FI ‘AJNIN HEMI’ETIN WE WEXHEDE ‘INDEHA KAWMÆN KULNA JA DHAL-KARNEJNI ‘IMMA ‘EN TU’ADHDHIBE WE ‘IMMA ‘EN TETTEHIDHE FIHIM HUSNÆN
KALE ‘EMMA MEN DHELEME FESEWFE NU’ADHDHIBUHU THUMME JUREDDU ‘ILA RABBIHI FEJU’ADHDHIBUHU ‘ADHABÆN NUKRÆN
WE ‘EMMA MEN ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FELEHU XHEZA’ENL-HUSNA WE SENEKULU LEHU MIN ‘EMRINA JUSRÆN
THUMME ‘ETBE’A SEBEBÆN
HETTA ‘IDHA BELEGA METLI’A ESH-SHEMSI WEXHEDEHA TETLU’U ‘ALA KAWMIN LEM NEXH’AL LEHUM MIN DUNIHA SITRÆN
KEDHALIKE WE KAD ‘EHETNA BIMA LEDEJHI HUBRÆN
THUMME ‘ETBE’A SEBEBÆN
HETTA ‘IDHA BELEGA BEJNE ES-SEDDEJNI WEXHEDE MIN DUNIHIMA KAWMÆN LA JEKADUNE JEFKAHUNE KAWLÆN
KALU JA DHAL-KARNEJNI ‘INNE JE’XHUXHE WE ME’XHUXHE MUFSIDUNE FIL-’ERDI FEHEL NEXH’ALU LEKE HARXHÆN ‘ALA ‘EN TEXH’ALE BEJNENA WE BEJNEHUM SEDDÆN
KALE MA MEKKENENI FIHI RABBI HAJRUN FE’A’INUNI BIKUWETIN ‘EXH’AL BEJNEKUM WE BEJNEHUM REDMÆN
‘ATUNI ZUBEREL-HEDIDI HETTA ‘IDHA SAWA BEJNE ES-SEDEFEJNI KALE ENFUHU HETTA ‘IDHA XHE’ALEHU NARÆN KALE ‘ATUNI ‘UFRIG ‘ALEJHI KITRÆN
FEMA ESTA’U ‘EN JEDHHERUHU WE MA ESTETA’U LEHU NEKBÆN
KALE HADHA REHMETUN MIN RABBI FE’IDHA XHA’E WA’DU RABBI XHE’ALEHU DEKKA’E WE KANE WA’DU RABBI HEKKÆN
WE TEREKNA BA’DEHUM JEWME’IDHIN JEMUXHU FI BA’DIN WE NUFIHA FI ES-SURI FEXHEMA’NAHUM XHEM’ÆN
WE ‘AREDNA XHEHENNEME JEWME’IDHIN LILKAFIRINE ‘ARDÆN
EL-LEDHINE KANET ‘A’JUNUHUM FI GITA’IN ‘AN DHIKRI WE KANU LA JESTETI’UNE SEM’ÆN
‘EFEHESIBEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘EN JETTEHIDHU ‘IBADI MIN DUNI ‘EWLIJA’E ‘INNA ‘A’TEDNA XHEHENNEME LILKAFIRINE NUZULÆN
KUL HEL NUNEBBI’UKUM BIL-’EHSERINE ‘A’MALÆN
EL-LEDHINE DELLE SA’JUHUM FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE HUM JEHSEBUNE ‘ENNEHUM JUHSINUNE SUN’ÆN
‘ULE’IKEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BI’AJATI RABBIHIM WE LIKA’IHI FEHEBITET ‘A’MALUHUM FELA NUKIMU LEHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI WEZNÆN
DHALIKE XHEZA’UUHUM XHEHENNEMU BIMA KEFERU WE ETTEHADHU ‘AJATI WE RUSULI HUZUEN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI KANET LEHUM XHENNATUL-FIRDEWSI NUZULÆN
HALIDINE FIHA LA JEBGUNE ‘ANHA HIWELÆN
KUL LEW KANEL-BEHRU MIDADÆN LIKELIMATI RABBI LENEFIDEL-BEHRU KABLE ‘EN TENFEDE KELIMATU RABBI WE LEW XHI’NA BIMITHLIHI MEDEDÆN
KUL ‘INNEMA ‘ENA BESHERUN MITHLUKUM JUHA ‘ILEJJE ‘ENNEMA ‘ILEHUKUM ‘ILEHUN WAHIDUN FEMEN KANE JERXHU LIKA’E RABBIHI FELJA’MEL ‘AMELÆN SALIHÆN WE LA JUSHRIK BI’IBADETI RABBIHI ‘EHEDÆN
KAF-HA-JA-’AJN-SAD
DHIKRU REHMETI RABBIKE ‘ABDEHU ZEKERIJA
‘IDH NADA REBBEHU NIDA’EN HAFIJÆN
KALE RABBI ‘INNI WEHENEL-’ADHMU MINNI WE ESHTE’ALE ER-RE’SU SHEJBÆN WE LEM ‘EKUN BIDU’A’IKE RABBI SHEKIJÆN
WE ‘INNI HIFTUL-MEWALIJE MIN WERA’I WE KANETI EMRE’ETI ‘AKIRÆN FEHEB LI MIN LEDUNKE WELIJÆN
JERITHUNI WE JERITHU MIN ‘ALI JA’KUBE WE EXH’ALHU RABBI REDIJÆN
JA ZEKERIJA ‘INNA NUBESHSHIRUKE BIGULAMIN ESMUHU JEHJA LEM NEXH’AL LEHU MIN KABLU SEMIJÆN
KALE RABBI ‘ENNA JEKUNU LI GULAMUN WE KANET EMRE’ETI ‘AKIRÆN WE KAD BELEGTU MINEL-KIBERI ‘ITIJÆN
KALE KEDHALIKE KALE REBBUKE HUWE ‘ALEJJE HEJJINUN WE KAD HALEKTUKE MIN KABLU WE LEM TEKU SHEJ’ÆN
KALE RABBI EXH’AL LI ‘AJETEN KALE ‘AJETUKE ‘ELLA TUKELLIME EN-NASE THELATHE LEJALIN SEWIJÆN
FEHAREXHE ‘ALA KAWMIHI MINEL-MIHRABI FE’EWHA ‘ILEJHIM ‘EN SEBBIHU BUKRETEN WE ‘ASHIJÆN
JA JEHJA HUDHIL-KITABE BIKUWETIN WE ‘ATEJNAHUL-HUKME SEBIJÆN
WE HENANÆN MIN LEDUNNA WE ZEKÆTEN WE KANE TEKIJÆN
WE BERRÆN BIWALIDEJHI WE LEM JEKUN XHEBBARÆN ‘ASIJÆN
WE SELAMUN ‘ALEJHI JEWME WULIDE WE JEWME JEMUTU WE JEWME JUB’ATHU HEJJÆN
WE EDHKUR FIL-KITABI MERJEME ‘IDH ENTEBEDHET MIN ‘EHLIHA MEKANÆN SHERKIJÆN
FATTEHADHET MIN DUNIHIM HIXHABÆN FE’ERSELNA ‘ILEJHA RUHENA FETEMETHTHELE LEHA BESHERÆN SEWIJÆN
KALET ‘INNI ‘A’UDHU BIR-REHMENI MINKE ‘IN KUNTE TEKIJÆN
KALE ‘INNEMA ‘ENA RESULU RABBIKI LI’HEBE LEKI GULAMÆN ZEKIJÆN
KALET ‘ENNA JEKUNU LI GULAMUN WE LEM JEMSESNI BESHERUN WE LEM ‘EKU BEGIJÆN
KALE KEDHALIKI KALE REBBUKI HUWE ‘ALEJJE HEJJINUN WE LINEXH’ALEHU ‘AJETEN LILNNASI WE REHMETEN MINNA WE KANE ‘EMRÆN MEKDIJÆN
FEHEMELET/HU FANTEBEDHET BIHI MEKANÆN KASIJÆN
FE’EXHA’EHAL-MEHADU ‘ILA XHIDH’I EN-NEHLETI KALET JA LEJTENI MITTU KABLE HADHA WE KUNTU NESJÆN MENSIJÆN
FENADAHA MIN TEHTIHA ‘ELLA TEHZENI KAD XHE’ALE REBBUKI TEHTEKI SERIJÆN
WE HUZZI ‘ILEJKI BIXHIDH’I EN-NEHLETI TUSAKIT ‘ALEJKI RUTEBÆN XHENIJÆN
FEKULI WE ESHREBI WE KARRI ‘AJNÆN FE’IMMA TEREJNNE MINEL-BESHERI ‘EHEDÆN FEKULI ‘INNI NEDHERTU LILRREHMENI SEWMÆN FELEN ‘UKELLIMEL-JEWME ‘INSIJÆN
FE’ETET BIHI KAWMEHA TEHMILUHU KALU JA MERJEMU LEKAD XHI’TI SHEJ’ÆN FERIJÆN
JA ‘UHTE HARUNE MA KANE ‘EBUKI EMRE’E SEW’IN WE MA KANET ‘UMMUKI BEGIJÆN
FE’ESHARET ‘ILEJHI KALU KEJFE NUKELLIMU MEN KANE FIL-MEHDI SEBIJÆN
KALE ‘INNI ‘ABDU ELLAHI ‘ATANIJEL-KITABE WE XHE’ALENI NEBIJÆN
WE XHE’ALENI MUBAREKÆN ‘EJNE MA KUNTU WE ‘EWSANI BIS-SELÆTI WE EZ-ZEKÆTI MA DUMTU HEJJÆN
WE BERRÆN BIWALIDETI WE LEM JEXH’ALNI XHEBBARÆN SHEKIJÆN
WE ES-SELAMU ‘ALEJJE JEWME WULIDTU WE JEWME ‘EMUTU WE JEWME ‘UB’ATHU HEJJÆN
DHALIKE ‘ISA EBNU MERJEME KAWLEL-HEKKIL-LEDHI FIHI JEMTERUNE
MA KANE LILLAHI ‘EN JETTEHIDHE MIN WELEDIN SUBHANEHU ‘IDHA KADA ‘EMRÆN FE’INNEMA JEKULU LEHU KUN FEJEKUNU
WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE RABBI WE REBBUKUM FA’BUDUHU HADHA SIRATUN MUSTEKIMUN
FAHTELEFEL-’EHZABU MIN BEJNIHIM FEWEJLUN LILLEDHINE KEFERU MIN MESH/HEDI JEWMIN ‘ADHIMIN
‘ESMI’ BIHIM WE ‘EBSIR JEWME JE’TUNENA LEKINI EDH-DHALIMUNEL-JEWME FI DELALIN MUBININ
WE ‘ENDHIRHUM JEWMEL-HESRETI ‘IDH KUDIJEL-’EMRU WE HUM FI GAFLETIN WE HUM LA JU’UMINUNE
‘INNA NEHNU NERITHUL-’ERDE WE MEN ‘ALEJHA WE ‘ILEJNA JURXHA’UNE
WE EDHKUR FIL-KITABI ‘IBRAHIME ‘INNEHU KANE SIDDIKÆN NEBIJÆN
‘IDH KALE LI’EBIHI JA ‘EBETI LIME TA’BUDU MA LA JESMA’U WE LA JUBSIRU WE LA JUGNI ‘ANKE SHEJ’ÆN
JA ‘EBETI ‘INNI KAD XHA’ENI MINEL-’ILMI MA LEM JE’TIKE FE ETTEBI’NI ‘EHDIKE SIRATÆN SEWIJÆN
JA ‘EBETI LA TA’BUDI ESH-SHEJTANE ‘INNE ESH-SHEJTANE KANE LILRREHMENI ‘ASIJÆN
JA ‘EBETI ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘EN JEMESSEKE ‘ADHABUN MINE ER-REHMANI FETEKUNE LILSHSHEJTANI WELIJÆN
KALE ‘ERAGIBUN ‘ENTE ‘AN ‘ALIHETI JA ‘IBRAHIMU LE’IN LEM TENTEHI LE’ERXHUMENNEKE WE EHXHURNI MELIJÆN
KALE SELAMUN ‘ALEJKE SE’ESTEGFIRU LEKE RABBI ‘INNEHU KANE BI HEFIJÆN
WE ‘A’TEZILUKUM WE MA TED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI WE ‘ED’U RABBI ‘ASA ‘ELLA ‘EKUNE BIDU’A’I RABBI SHEKIJÆN
FELEMMA A’TEZELEHUM WE MA JA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI WEHEBNA LEHU ‘ISHAKA WE JA’KUBE WE KULLA XHE’ALNA NEBIJÆN
WE WEHEBNA LEHUM MIN REHMETINA WE XHE’ALNA LEHUM LISANE SIDKIN ‘ALIJÆN
WE EDHKUR FIL-KITABI MUSA ‘INNEHU KANE MUHLESÆN WE KANE RESULÆN NEBIJÆN
WE NADEJNAHU MIN XHANIBIT-TURIL-’EJMENI WE KARREBNAHU NEXHIJÆN
WE WEHEBNA LEHU MIN REHMETINA ‘EHAHU HARUNE NEBIJÆN
WE EDHKUR FIL-KITABI ‘ISMA’ILE ‘INNEHU KANE SADIKAL-WA’DI WE KANE RESULÆN NEBIJÆN
WE KANE JE’MURU ‘EHLEHU BIS-SELÆTI WE EZ-ZEKÆTI WE KANE ‘INDE RABBIHI MERDIJÆN
WE EDHKUR FIL-KITABI ‘IDRISE ‘INNEHU KANE SIDDIKÆN NEBIJÆN
WE REFA’NAHU MEKANÆN ‘ALIJÆN
‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE ‘EN’AMEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHIM MINE EN-NEBIJINE MIN DHURRIJETI ‘ADEME WE MIMMEN HEMELNA ME’A NUHIN WE MIN DHURRIJETI ‘IBRAHIME WE ‘ISRA’ILE WE MIMMEN HEDEJNA WE EXHTEBEJNA ‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATU ER-REHMANI HARRU SUXHXHEDÆN WE BUKIJÆN
FEHALEFE MIN BA’DIHIM HALFUN ‘EDA’U ES-SELÆTE WE ETTEBA’U ESH-SHEHEWATI FESEWFE JELKAWNE GAJJÆN
‘ILLA MEN TABE WE ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FE’ULA’IKE JEDHULUNEL-XHENNETE WE LA JUDHLEMUNE SHEJ’ÆN
XHENNATI ‘ADNIN ELLETI WE’ADE ER-REHMANU ‘IBADEHU BIL-GAJBI ‘INNEHU KANE WA’DUHU ME’TIJÆN
LA JESMA’UNE FIHA LEGWEN ‘ILLA SELAMÆN WE LEHUM RIZKUHUM FIHA BUKRETEN WE ‘ASHIJÆN
TILKEL-XHENNETU ELLETI NURITHU MIN ‘IBADINA MEN KANE TEKIJÆN
WE MA NETENEZZELU ‘ILLA BI’EMRI RABBIKE LEHU MA BEJNE ‘EJDINA WE MA HALFENA WE MA BEJNE DHALIKE WE MA KANE REBBUKE NESIJÆN
REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMA FA’BUD/HU WE ESTEBIR LI’IBADETIHI HEL TA’LEMU LEHU SEMIJÆN
WE JEKULUL-’INSANU ‘E’IDHA MA MITTU LESEWFE ‘UHREXHU HEJJÆN
‘EWELA JEDHKURUL-’INSANU ‘ENNA HALEKNAHU MIN KABLU WE LEM JEKU SHEJ’ÆN
FEWEREBBIKE LENEHSHURENNEHUM WE ESH-SHEJATINE THUMME LENUHDIRENNEHUM HEWLE XHEHENNEME XHITHIJÆN
THUMME LENENZI’ANNE MIN KULLI SHI’ATIN ‘EJJUHUM ‘ESHEDDU ‘ALA ER-REHMANI ‘ITIJÆN
THUMME LENEHNU ‘A’LEMU BIEL-LEDHINE HUM ‘EWLA BIHA SILIJÆN
WE ‘IN MINKUM ‘ILLA WE ERIDUHA KANE ‘ALA RABBIKE HETMÆN MEKDIJÆN
THUMME NUNEXHXHIL-LEDHINE ETTEKAW WE NEDHERU EDH-DHALIMINE FIHA XHITHIJÆN
WE ‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATUNA BEJJINATIN KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘EJJUL-FERIKAJNI HAJRUN MEKAMÆN WE ‘EHSENU NEDIJÆN
WE KEM ‘EHLEKNA KABLEHUM MIN KARNIN HUM ‘EHSENU ‘ETHATHÆN WE RI’JÆN
KUL MEN KANE FI ED-DELALETI FELJEMDUD LEHU ER-REHMANU MEDDÆN HETTA ‘IDHA RE’EW MA JU’ADUNE ‘IMMAL-’ADHABE WE ‘IMMA ES-SA’ATE FESEJA’LEMUNE MEN HUWE SHERRUN MEKANÆN WE ‘ED’AFU XHUNDÆN
WE JEZIDU ELLAHUL-LEDHINE EHTEDEW HUDEN WEL-BAKIJATU ES-SALIHATU HAJRUN ‘INDE RABBIKE THEWABÆN WE HAJRUN MEREDDÆN
‘EFERE’EJTEL-LEDHI KEFERE BI’AJATINA WE KALE LE’UTEJENNE MALÆN WE WELEDÆN
‘ATTELE’AL-GAJBE ‘EM ETTEHADHE ‘INDE ER-REHMANI ‘AHDÆN
KELLA SENEKTUBU MA JEKULU WE NEMUDDU LEHU MINEL-’ADHABI MEDDÆN
WE NERITHUHU MA JEKULU WE JE’TINA FERDÆN
WE ETTEHADHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘ALIHETEN LIJEKUNU LEHUM ‘IZZÆN
KELLA SEJEKFURUNE BI’IBADETIHIM WE JEKUNUNE ‘ALEJHIM DIDDÆN
‘ELEM TERE ‘ENNA ‘ERSELNA ESH-SHEJATINE ‘ALEL-KAFIRINE TE’UUZZUHUM ‘EZZÆN
FELA TA’XHEL ‘ALEJHIM ‘INNEMA NA’UDDU LEHUM ‘ADDÆN
JEWME NEHSHURUL-MUTTEKINE ‘ILA ER-REHMANI WEFDÆN
WE NESUKUL-MUXHRIMINE ‘ILA XHEHENNEME WIRDÆN
LA JEMLIKUNE ESH-SHEFA’ATE ‘ILLA MENI ETTEHADHE ‘INDE ER-REHMANI ‘AHDÆN
WE KALU ETTEHADHE ER-REHMANU WELEDÆN
LEKAD XHI’TUM SHEJ’ÆN ‘IDDÆN
TEKADU ES-SEMAWATU JETEFETTERNE MINHU WE TENSHEKKUL-’ERDU WE TEHIRRUL-XHIBALU HEDDÆN
‘EN DE’AW LILRREHMENI WELEDÆN
WE MA JENBEGI LILRREHMENI ‘EN JETTEHIDHE WELEDÆN
‘IN KULLU MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘ILLA ‘ATI ER-REHMANI ‘ABDÆN
LEKAD ‘EHSAHUM WE ‘ADDEHUM ‘ADDÆN
WE KULLUHUM ‘ATIHI JEWMEL-KIJAMETI FERDÆN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI SEJEXH’ALU LEHUMU ER-REHMANU WUDDÆN
FE’INNEMA JESSERNAHU BILISANIKE LITUBESHSHIRE BIHIL-MUTTEKINE WE TUNDHIRE BIHI KAWMÆN LUDDÆN
WE KEM ‘EHLEKNA KABLEHUM MIN KARNIN HEL TUHISSU MINHUM MIN ‘EHEDIN ‘EW TESMA’U LEHUM RIKZÆN
TAHA
MA ‘ENZELNA ‘ALEJKEL-KUR’ANE LITESHKA
‘ILLA TEDHKIRETEN LIMEN JEHSHA
TENZILÆN MIMMEN HALEKAL-’ERDE WE ES-SEMAWATIL-’ULA
ER-REHMANU ‘ALEL-’ARSHI ESTEWA
LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMA WE MA TEHTE ETH-THERA
WE ‘IN TEXHHER BIL-KAWLI FE’INNEHU JA’LEMU ES-SIRRE WE ‘EHFA
ELLAHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE LEHUL-’ESMA’UL-HUSNA
WE HEL ‘ETAKE HEDITHU MUSA
‘IDH RE’A NARÆN FEKALE LI’HLIHI EMKUTHU ‘INNI ‘ANESTU NARÆN LE’ALLI ‘ATIKUM MINHA BIKABESIN ‘EW ‘EXHIDU ‘ALA EN-NARI HUDEN
FELEMMA ‘ETAHA NUDI JA MUSA
‘INNI ‘ENA REBBUKE FAHLA’ NA’LEJKE ‘INNEKE BIL-WADIL-MUKADDESI TUWEN
WE ‘ENA EHTERTUKE FASTEMI’ LIMA JUHA
‘INNENI ‘ENALLAHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA ‘ENA FA’BUDNI WE ‘EKIMI ES-SELÆTE LIDHIKRI
‘INNE ES-SA’ATE ‘ATIJETUN ‘EKADU ‘UHFIHA LITUXHZA KULLU NEFSIN BIMA TES’A
FELA JESUDDENNEKE ‘ANHA MEN LA JU’UMINU BIHA WE ETTEBE’A HEWAHU FETERDA
WE MA TILKE BIJEMINIKE JA MUSA
KALE HIJE ‘ASAJE ‘ETEWEKKE’U ‘ALEJHA WE ‘EHUSHSHU BIHA ‘ALA GANEMI WE LIJE FIHA ME’ARIBU ‘UHRA
KALE ‘ELKIHA JA MUSA
FE’ELKAHA FE’IDHA HIJE HEJJETUN TES’A
KALE HUDH/HA WE LA TEHAF SENU’IDUHA SIRETEHAL-’ULA
WE EDMUM JEDEKE ‘ILA XHENAHIKE TEHRUXH BEJDA’E MIN GAJRI SU’IN ‘AJETEN ‘UHRA
LINURIJEKE MIN ‘AJATINAL-KUBRA
EDH/HEB ‘ILA FIR’AWNE ‘INNEHU TEGA
KALE RABBI ESHREH LI SEDRI
WE JESSIR LI ‘EMRI
WE EHLUL ‘UKDETEN MIN LISANI
JEFKAHU KAWLI
WE EXH’AL LI WEZIRÆN MIN ‘EHLI
HARUNE ‘EHI
ESHDUD BIHI ‘EZRI
WE ‘ESHRIK/HU FI ‘EMRI
KEJ NUSEBBIHEKE KETHIRÆN
WE NEDHKUREKE KETHIRÆN
‘INNEKE KUNTE BINA BESIRÆN
KALE KAD ‘UTITE SU’ULEKE JA MUSA
WE LEKAD MENENNA ‘ALEJKE MERRETEN ‘UHRA
‘IDH ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILA ‘UMMIKE MA JUHA
‘ENI EKDHIFIHI FIT-TABUTI FAKDHIFIHI FIL-JEMMI FELJULKIHIL-JEMMU BIS-SAHILI JE’HUDH/HU ‘ADUWUN LI WE’ADUWUN LEHU WE ‘ELKAJTU ‘ALEJKE MEHEBBETEN MINNI WE LITUSNE’A ‘ALA ‘AJNI
‘IDH TEMSHI ‘UHTUKE FETEKULU HEL ‘EDULLUKUM ‘ALA MEN JEKFULUHU FEREXHA’NAKE ‘ILA ‘UMMIKE KEJ TEKARRE ‘AJNUHA WE LA TEHZENE WE KATELTE NEFSÆN FENEXHXHEJNAKE MINEL-GAMMI WE FETENNAKE FUTUNÆN FELEBITHTE SININE FI ‘EHLI MEDJENE THUMME XHI’TE ‘ALA KADERIN JA M
WE ESTENA’TUKE LINEFSI
EDH/HEB ‘ENTE WE ‘EHUKE BI’AJATI WE LA TENIJA FI DHIKRI
EDH/HEBA ‘ILA FIR’AWNE ‘INNEHU TEGA
FEKULA LEHU KAWLÆN LEJJINÆN LE’ALLEHU JETEDHEKKERU ‘EW JEHSHA
KALA REBBENA ‘INNENA NEHAFU ‘EN JEFRUTE ‘ALEJNA ‘EW ‘EN JETGA
KALE LA TEHAFA ‘INNENI ME’AKUMA ‘ESMA’U WE ‘ERA
FE’TIJAHU FEKULA ‘INNA RESULA RABBIKE FE’ERSIL ME’ANA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE WE LA TU’ADHDHIBHUM KAD XHI’NAKE BI’AJETIN MIN RABBIKE WE ES-SELAMU ‘ALA MENI ETTEBE’AL-HUDA
‘INNA KAD ‘UHIJE ‘ILEJNA ‘ENNEL-’ADHABE ‘ALA MEN KEDHDHEBE WE TEWELLA
KALE FEMEN REBBUKUMA JA MUSA
KALE REBBUNAL-LEDHI ‘A’TA KULLE SHEJ’IN HALKAHU THUMME HEDA
KALE FEMA BALUL-KURUNIL-’ULA
KALE ‘ILMUHA ‘INDE RABBI FI KITABIN LA JEDILLU RABBI WE LA JENSA
EL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-’ERDE MEHDÆN WE SELEKE LEKUM FIHA SUBULÆN WE ‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’EHREXHNA BIHI ‘EZWAXHÆN MIN NEBATIN SHETTA
KULU WE ER’AW ‘EN’AMEKUM ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LI’WLI EN-NUHA
MINHA HALEKNAKUM WE FIHA NU’IDUKUM WE MINHA NUHRIXHUKUM TARETEN ‘UHRA
WE LEKAD ‘EREJNAHU ‘AJATINA KULLEHA FEKEDHDHEBE WE ‘EBA
KALE ‘EXHI’TENA LITUHRIXHENA MIN ‘ERDINA BISIHRIKE JA MUSA
FELENE’TIJENNEKE BISIHRIN MITHLIHI FAXH’AL BEJNENA WE BEJNEKE MEW’IDÆN LA NUHLIFUHU NEHNU WE LA ‘ENTE MEKANÆN SUWEN
KALE MEW’IDUKUM JEWMU EZ-ZINETI WE ‘EN JUHSHERE EN-NASU DUHEN
FETEWELLA FIR’AWNU FEXHEME’A KEJDEHU THUMME ‘ETA
KALE LEHUM MUSA WEJLEKUM LA TEFTERU ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN FEJUSHITEKUM BI’ADHABIN WE KAD HABE MENI EFTERA
FETENAZA’U ‘EMREHUM BEJNEHUM WE ‘ESERRU EN-NEXHWA
KALU ‘IN HEDHANI LESAHIRANI JURIDANI ‘EN JUHRIXHAKUM MIN ‘ERDIKUM BISIHRIHIMA WE JEDH/HEBA BITERIKATIKUMUL-MUTHLA
FE’EXHMI’U KEJDEKUM THUMME E’TU SEFFÆN WE KAD ‘EFLEHEL-JEWME MENI ESTA’LA
KALU JA MUSA ‘IMMA ‘EN TULKIJE WE ‘IMMA ‘EN NEKUNE ‘EWWELE MEN ‘ELKA
KALE BEL ‘ELKU FE’IDHA HIBALUHUM WE ‘ISIJUHUM JUHAJJELU ‘ILEJHI MIN SIHRIHIM ‘ENNEHA TES’A
FE’EWXHESE FI NEFSIHI HIFETEN MUSA
KULNA LA TEHAF ‘INNEKE ‘ENTEL-’A’LA
WE ‘ELKI MA FI JEMINIKE TELKAF MA SENA’U ‘INNEMA SENA’U KEJDU SAHIRIN WE LA JUFLIHU ES-SAHIRU HEJTHU ‘ETA
FE’ULKIJE ES-SEHERETU SUXHXHEDÆN KALU ‘AMENNA BIREBBI HARUNE WE MUSA
KALE ‘AMENTUM LEHU KABLE ‘EN ‘ADHENE LEKUM ‘INNEHU LEKEBIRUKUMUL-LEDHI ‘ALLEMEKUMU ES-SIHRE FELE’UKATTI’ANNE ‘EJDIJEKUM WE ‘ERXHULEKUM MIN HILAFIN WE LE’USELLIBENNEKUM FI XHUDHU’I EN-NEHLI WE LETA’LEMUNNE ‘EJJUNA ‘ESHEDDU ‘ADHABÆN WE ‘EBKA
KALU LEN NU’UTHIREKE ‘ALA MA XHA’ENA MINEL-BEJJINATI WEL-LEDHI FETERENA FAKDI MA ‘ENTE KADIN ‘INNEMA TEKDI HEDHIHIL-HEJÆTE ED-DUNJA
‘INNA ‘AMENNA BIREBBINA LIJEGFIRE LENA HATAJANA WE MA ‘EKREHTENA ‘ALEJHI MINE ES-SIHRI WEL-LAHU HAJRUN WE ‘EBKA
‘INNEHU MEN JE’TI REBBEHU MUXHRIMÆN FE’INNE LEHU XHEHENNEME LA JEMUTU FIHA WE LA JEHJA
WE MEN JE’TIHI MU’UMINÆN KAD ‘AMILE ES-SALIHATI FE’ULA’IKE LEHUMU ED-DEREXHATUL-’ULA
XHENNATU ‘ADNIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA WE DHELIKE XHEZA’U MEN TEZEKKA
WE LEKAD ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILA MUSA ‘EN ‘ESRI BI’IBADI FADRIB LEHUM TERIKÆN FIL-BEHRI JEBESÆN LA TEHAFU DEREKÆN WE LA TEHSHA
FE’ETBE’AHUM FIR’AWNU BIXHUNUDIHI FEGASHIJEHUM MINEL-JEMMI MA GASHIJEHUM
WE ‘EDELLE FIR’AWNU KAWMEHU WE MA HEDA
JA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE KAD ‘ENXHEJNAKUM MIN ‘ADUWIKUM WE WA’ADNAKUM XHANIBET-TURIL-’EJMENE WE NEZZELNA ‘ALEJKUMUL-MENNE WE ES-SELWA
KULU MIN TEJJIBATI MA REZEKNAKUM WE LA TETGAW FIHI FEJEHILLE ‘ALEJKUM GADEBI WE MEN JEHLIL ‘ALEJHI GADEBI FEKAD HEWA
WE ‘INNI LEGAFFARUN LIMEN TABE WE ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN THUMME EHTEDA
WE MA ‘A’XHELEKE ‘AN KAWMIKE JA MUSA
KALE HUM ‘ULA’I ‘ALA ‘ETHERI WE ‘AXHILTU ‘ILEJKE RABBI LITERDA
KALE FE’INNA KAD FETENNA KAWMEKE MIN BA’DIKE WE ‘EDELLEHUMU ES-SAMIRIJU
FEREXHE’A MUSA ‘ILA KAWMIHI GADBANE ‘ESIFÆN KALE JA KAWMI ‘ELEM JA’IDKUM REBBUKUM WA’DÆN HESENÆN ‘EFETALE ‘ALEJKUMUL-’AHDU ‘EM ‘EREDTUM ‘EN JEHILLE ‘ALEJKUM GADEBUN MIN RABBIKUM FE’EHLEFTUM MEW’IDI
KALU MA ‘EHLEFNA MEW’IDEKE BIMELKINA WE LEKINNA HUMMILNA ‘EWZARÆN MIN ZINETIL-KAWMI FEKADHEFNAHA FEKEDHELIKE ‘ELKA ES-SAMIRIJU
FE’EHREXHE LEHUM ‘IXHLÆN XHESEDÆN LEHU HUWARUN FEKALU HADHA ‘ILEHUKUM WE ‘ILEHU MUSA FENESIJE
‘EFELA JEREWNE ‘ELLA JERXHI’U ‘ILEJHIM KAWLÆN WE LA JEMLIKU LEHUM DERRÆN WE LA NEF’ÆN
WE LEKAD KALE LEHUM HARUNU MIN KABLU JA KAWMI ‘INNEMA FUTINTUM BIHI WE ‘INNE REBBEKUMU ER-REHMANU FE ETTEBI’UNI WE ‘ETI’U ‘EMRI
KALU LEN NEBREHE ‘ALEJHI ‘AKIFINE HETTA JERXHI’A ‘ILEJNA MUSA
KALE JA HARUNU MA MENE’AKE ‘IDH RE’EJTEHUM DELLU
‘ELLA TETTEBI’ANI ‘EFE’ASEJTE ‘EMRI
KALE JEBNE’UUMME LA TE’HUDH BILIHJETI WE LA BIRE’SI ‘INNI HASHITU ‘EN TEKULE FERREKTE BEJNE BENI ‘ISRA’ILE WE LEM TERKUB KAWLI
KALE FEMA HATBUKE JA SAMIRIJU
KALE BESURTU BIMA LEM JEBSURU BIHI FEKABEDTU KABDETEN MIN ‘ETHERI ER-RESULI FENEBEDHTUHA WE KEDHELIKE SEWWELET LI NEFSI
KALE FADH/HEB FE’INNE LEKE FIL-HEJÆTI ‘EN TEKULE LA MISASE WE ‘INNE LEKE MEW’IDÆN LEN TUHLEFEHU WE ENDHUR ‘ILA ‘ILEHIKEL-LEDHI DHELTE ‘ALEJHI ‘AKIFÆN LENUHERRIKANNEHU THUMME LENENSIFENNEHU FIL-JEMMI NESFÆN
‘INNEMA ‘ILEHUKUMU ELLAHUL-LEDHI LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE WESI’A KULLE SHEJ’IN ‘ILMÆN
KEDHALIKE NEKUSSU ‘ALEJKE MIN ‘ENBA’I MA KAD SEBEKA WE KAD ‘ATEJNAKE MIN LEDUNNA DHIKRÆN
MEN ‘A’REDE ‘ANHU FE’INNEHU JEHMILU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI WIZRÆN
HALIDINE FIHI WE SA’E LEHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI HIMLÆN
JEWME JUNFEHU FI ES-SURI WE NEHSHURUL-MUXHRIMINE JEWME’IDHIN ZURKÆN
JETEHAFETUNE BEJNEHUM ‘IN LEBITHTUM ‘ILLA ‘ASHRÆN
NEHNU ‘A’LEMU BIMA JEKULUNE ‘IDH JEKULU ‘EMTHELUHUM TERIKATEN ‘IN LEBITHTUM ‘ILLA JEWMÆN
WE JES’ELUNEKE ‘ANIL-XHIBALI FEKUL JENSIFUHA RABBI NESFÆN
FEJEDHERUHA KA’ÆN SEFSEFÆN
LA TERA FIHA ‘IWEXHÆN WE LA ‘EMTÆN
JEWME’IDHIN JETTEBI’UNE ED-DA’I LA ‘IWEXHE LEHU WE HASHE’ATIL-’ESWATU LILRREHMENI FELA TESMA’U ‘ILLA HEMSÆN
JEWME’IDHIN LA TENFA’U ESH-SHEFA’ATU ‘ILLA MEN ‘EDHINE LEHU ER-REHMANU WE REDIJE LEHU KAWLÆN
JA’LEMU MA BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE MA HALFEHUM WE LA JUHITUNE BIHI ‘ILMÆN
WE ‘ANETIL-WUXHUHU LILHEJJIL-KAJJUMI WE KAD HABE MEN HEMELE DHULMÆN
WE MEN JA’MEL MINE ES-SALIHATI WE HUWE MU’UMINUN FELA JEHAFU DHULMÆN WE LA HEDMÆN
WE KEDHELIKE ‘ENZELNAHU KUR’ANÆN ‘AREBIJÆN WE SERREFNA FIHI MINEL-WA’IDI LE’ALLEHUM JETTEKUNE ‘EW JUHDITHU LEHUM DHIKRÆN
FETA’ALALLAHUL-MELIKUL-HEKKU WE LA TA’XHEL BIL-KUR’ANI MIN KABLI ‘EN JUKDA ‘ILEJKE WEHJUHU WE KUL RABBI ZIDNI ‘ILMÆN
WE LEKAD ‘AHIDNA ‘ILA ‘ADEME MIN KABLU FENESIJE WE LEM NEXHID LEHU ‘AZMÆN
WE ‘IDH KULNA LILMELA’IKETI ESXHUDU LI’DEME FESEXHEDU ‘ILLA ‘IBLISE ‘EBA
FEKULNA JA ‘ADEMU ‘INNE HADHA ‘ADUWUN LEKE WE LIZEWXHIKE FELA JUHRIXHENNEKUMA MINEL-XHENNETI FETESHKA
‘INNE LEKE ‘ELLA TEXHU’A FIHA WE LA TA’RA
WE ‘ENNEKE LA TEDHME’U FIHA WE LA TEDHA
FEWESWESE ‘ILEJHI ESH-SHEJTANU KALE JA ‘ADEMU HEL ‘EDULLUKE ‘ALA SHEXHERETIL-HULDI WE MULKIN LA JEBLA
FE’EKELA MINHA FEBEDET LEHUMA SEW’ATUHUMA WE TEFIKA JEHSIFANI ‘ALEJHIMA MIN WEREKIL-XHENNETI WE ‘ASA ‘ADEMU REBBEHU FEGAWA
THUMME EXHTEBAHU REBBUHU FETABE ‘ALEJHI WE HEDA
KALE EHBITA MINHA XHEMI’ÆN BA’DUKUM LIBA’DIN ‘ADUWUN FE’IMMA JE’TIJENNEKUM MINNI HUDEN FEMENI ETTEBE’A HUDAJE FELA JEDILLU WE LA JESHKA
WE MEN ‘A’REDE ‘AN DHIKRI FE’INNE LEHU MA’ISHETEN DENKÆN WE NEHSHURUHU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘A’MA
KALE RABBI LIME HESHERTENI ‘A’MA WE KAD KUNTU BESIRÆN
KALE KEDHALIKE ‘ETETKE ‘AJATUNA FENESITEHA WE KEDHELIKEL-JEWME TUNSA
WE KEDHELIKE NEXHZI MEN ‘ESREFE WE LEM JU’UMIN BI’AJATI RABBIHI WE LE’ADHABUL-’AHIRETI ‘ESHEDDU WE ‘EBKA
‘EFELEM JEHDI LEHUM KEM ‘EHLEKNA KABLEHUM MINEL-KURUNI JEMSHUNE FI MESAKINIHIM ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LI’WLI EN-NUHA
WE LEWLA KELIMETUN SEBEKAT MIN RABBIKE LEKANE LIZAMÆN WE ‘EXHELUN MUSEMMEN
FASBIR ‘ALA MA JEKULUNE WE SEBBIH BIHEMDI RABBIKE KABLE TULU’I ESH-SHEMSI WE KABLE GURUBIHA WE MIN ‘ANA’IL-LEJLI FESEBBIH WE ‘ETRAFE EN-NEHARI LE’ALLEKE TERDA
WE LA TEMUDDENNE ‘AJNEJKE ‘ILA MA METTA’NA BIHI ‘EZWAXHÆN MINHUM ZEHRETEL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA LINEFTINEHUM FIHI WE RIZKU RABBIKE HAJRUN WE ‘EBKA
WE ‘MUR ‘EHLEKE BIS-SELÆTI WE ESTEBIR ‘ALEJHA LA NES’ELUKE RIZKÆN NEHNU NERZUKUKE WEL-’AKIBETU LILTTEKWA
WE KALU LEWLA JE’TINA BI’AJETIN MIN RABBIHI ‘EWELEM TE’TIHIM BEJJINETU MA FI ES-SUHUFIL-’ULA
WE LEW ‘ENNA ‘EHLEKNAHUM BI’ADHABIN MIN KABLIHI LEKALU REBBENA LEWLA ‘ERSELTE ‘ILEJNA RESULÆN FENETTEBI’A ‘AJATIKE MIN KABLI ‘EN NEDHILLE WE NEHZA
KUL KULLUN MUTEREBBISUN FETEREBBESU FESETA’LEMUNE MEN ‘ESHABU ES-SIRATI ES-SEWIJI WE MENI EHTEDA
EKTEREBE LILNNASI HISABUHUM WE HUM FI GAFLETIN MU’RIDUNE
MA JE’TIHIM MIN DHIKRIN MIN RABBIHIM MUHDETHIN ‘ILLA ESTEMA’UHU WE HUM JEL’ABUNE
LAHIJETEN KULUBUHUM WE ‘ESERRU EN-NEXHWAL-LEDHINE DHELEMU HEL HADHA ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUKUM ‘EFETE’TUNE ES-SIHRE WE ‘ENTUM TUBSIRUNE
KALE RABBI JA’LEMUL-KAWLE FI ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI WE HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-’ALIMU
BEL KALU ‘EDGATHU ‘EHLAMIN BEL EFTERAHU BEL HUWE SHA’IRUN FELJE’TINA BI’AJETIN KEMA ‘URSILEL-’EWWELUNE
MA ‘AMENET KABLEHUM MIN KARJETIN ‘EHLEKNAHA ‘EFEHUM JU’UMINUNE
WE MA ‘ERSELNA KABLEKE ‘ILLA RIXHALÆN NUHI ‘ILEJHIM FAS’ELU ‘EHLE EDH-DHIKRI ‘IN KUNTUM LA TA’LEMUNE
WE MA XHE’ALNAHUM XHESEDÆN LA JE’KULUNET-TA’AME WE MA KANU HALIDINE
THUMME SEDEKNAHUMUL-WA’DE FE’ENXHEJNAHUM WE MEN NESHA’U WE ‘EHLEKNAL-MUSRIFINE
LEKAD ‘ENZELNA ‘ILEJKUM KITABÆN FIHI DHIKRUKUM ‘EFELA TA’KILUNE
WE KEM KASEMNA MIN KARJETIN KANET DHALIMETEN WE ‘ENSHE’NA BA’DEHA KAWMÆN ‘AHARINE
FELEMMA ‘EHESSU BE’SENA ‘IDHA HUM MINHA JERKUDUNE
LA TERKUDU WE ERXHI’U ‘ILA MA ‘UTRIFTUM FIHI WE MESAKINIKUM LE’ALLEKUM TUS’ELUNE
KALU JA WEJLENA ‘INNA KUNNA DHALIMINE
FEMA ZALET TILKE DA’WAHUM HETTA XHE’ALNAHUM HESIDÆN HAMIDINE
WE MA HALEKNA ES-SEMA’E WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA LA’IBINE
LEW ‘EREDNA ‘EN NETTEHIDHE LEHWEN LATTEHADHNAHU MIN LEDUNNA ‘IN KUNNA FA’ILINE
BEL NEKDHIFU BIL-HEKKI ‘ALEL-BATILI FEJEDMEGUHU FE’IDHA HUWE ZAHIKUN WE LEKUMUL-WEJLU MIMMA TESIFUNE
WE LEHU MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MEN ‘INDEHU LA JESTEKBIRUNE ‘AN ‘IBADETIHI WE LA JESTEHSIRUNE
JUSEBBIHUNEL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE LA JEFTURUNE
‘EM ETTEHADHU ‘ALIHETEN MINEL-’ERDI HUM JUNSHIRUNE
LEW KANE FIHIMA ‘ALIHETUN ‘ILLALLAHU LEFESEDETA FESUBHANEL-LAHI RABBIL-’ARSHI ‘AMMA JESIFUNE
LA JUS’ELU ‘AMMA JEF’ALU WE HUM JUS’ELUNE
‘EM ETTEHADHU MIN DUNIHI ‘ALIHETEN KUL HATU BURHANEKUM HADHA DHIKRU MEN MA’IJE WE DHIKRU MEN KABLI BEL ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’LEMUNEL-HEKKA FEHUM MU’RIDUNE
WE MA ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE MIN RESUL IN’ILLA NUHI ‘ILEJHI ‘ENNEHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA ‘ENA FA’BUDUNI
WE KALU ETTEHADHE ER-REHMANU WELEDÆN SUBHANEHU BEL ‘IBADUN MUKREMUNE
LA JESBIKUNEHU BIL-KAWLI WE HUM BI’EMRIHI JA’MELUNE
JA’LEMU MA BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE MA HALFEHUM WE LA JESHFA’UNE ‘ILLA LIMENI ERTEDA WE HUM MIN HASHJETIHI MUSHFIKUNE
WE MEN JEKUL MINHUM ‘INNI ‘ILEHUN MIN DUNIHI FEDHALIKE NEXHZIHI XHEHENNEME KEDHALIKE NEXHZI EDH-DHALIMINE
‘EWELEM JERAL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘ENNE ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE KANETA RETKÆN FEFETEKNAHUMA WE XHE’ALNA MINEL-MA’I KULLE SHEJ’IN HEJJIN ‘EFELA JU’UMINUNE
WE XHE’ALNA FIL-’ERDI REWASIJE ‘EN TEMIDE BIHIM WE XHE’ALNA FIHA FIXHAXHÆN SUBULÆN LE’ALLEHUM JEHTEDUNE
WE XHE’ALNA ES-SEMA’E SEKFÆN MEHFUDHÆN WE HUM ‘AN ‘AJATIHA MU’RIDUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI HALEKAL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE WE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE KULLUN FI FELEKIN JESBEHUNE
WE MA XHE’ALNA LIBESHERIN MIN KABLIKEL-HULDE ‘EFE’IN MITTE FEHUMUL-HALIDUNE
KULLU NEFSIN DHA’IKATUL-MEWTI WE NEBLUKUM BISH-SHERRI WEL-HAJRI FITNETEN WE ‘ILEJNA TURXHA’UNE
WE ‘IDHA RE’AKEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘IN JETTEHIDHUNEKE ‘ILLA HUZUEN ‘EHEDHAL-LEDHI JEDHKURU ‘ALIHETEKUM WE HUM BIDHIKRI ER-REHMANI HUM KAFIRUNE
HULIKAL-’INSANU MIN ‘AXHELIN SE’URIKUM ‘AJATI FELA TESTA’XHILUNI
WE JEKULUNE META HADHAL-WA’DU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
LEW JA’LEMUL-LEDHINE KEFERU HINE LA JEKUFFUNE ‘AN WUXHUHIHIMU EN-NARE WE LA ‘AN DHUHURIHIM WE LA HUM JUNSERUNE
BEL TE’TIHIM BEGTETEN FETEBHETUHUM FELA JESTETI’UNE REDDEHA WE LA HUM JUNDHERUNE
WE LEKADI ESTUHZI’E BIRUSULIN MIN KABLIKE FEHAKA BIEL-LEDHINE SEHIRU MINHUM MA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
KUL MEN JEKLE’UUKUM BIL-LEJLI WE EN-NEHARI MINE ER-REHMANI BEL HUM ‘AN DHIKRI RABBIHIM MU’RIDUNE
‘EM LEHUM ‘ALIHETUN TEMNA’UHUM MIN DUNINA LA JESTETI’UNE NESRE ‘ENFUSIHIM WE LA HUM MINNA JUSHEBUNE
BEL METTA’NA HA’UULA’ WE ‘ABA’EHUM HETTA TALE ‘ALEJHIMUL-’UMURU ‘EFELA JEREWNE ‘ENNA NE’TIL-’ERDE NENKUSUHA MIN ‘ETRAFIHA ‘EFEHUMUL-GALIBUNE
KUL ‘INNEMA ‘UNDHIRUKUM BIL-WEHJI WE LA JESMA’U ES-SUMMU ED-DU’A’E ‘IDHA MA JUNDHERUNE
WE LE’IN MESSET/HUM NEFHETUN MIN ‘ADHABI RABBIKE LEJEKULUNNE JA WEJLENA ‘INNA KUNNA DHALIMINE
WE NEDA’UL-MEWAZINEL-KISTE LIJEWMIL-KIJAMETI FELA TUDHLEMU NEFSUN SHEJ’ÆN WE ‘IN KANE MITHKALE HEBBETIN MIN HARDELIN ‘ETEJNA BIHA WE KEFA BINA HASIBINE
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSA WE HARUNEL-FURKANE WE DIJA’EN WE DHIKRÆN LILMUTTEKINE
EL-LEDHINE JEHSHEWNE REBBEHUM BIL-GAJBI WE HUM MINE ES-SA’ATI MUSHFIKUNE
WE HEDHA DHIKRUN MUBAREKUN ‘ENZELNAHU ‘EFE’ENTUM LEHU MUNKIRUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA ‘IBRAHIME RUSHDEHU MIN KABLU WE KUNNA BIHI ‘ALIMINE
‘IDH KALE LI’EBIHI WE KAWMIHI MA HEDHIHIT-TEMATHILU ELLETI ‘ENTUM LEHA ‘AKIFUNE
KALU WEXHEDNA ‘ABA’ENA LEHA ‘ABIDINE
KALE LEKAD KUNTUM ‘ENTUM WE ‘ABA’UUKUM FI DELALIN MUBININ
KALU ‘EXHI’TENA BIL-HEKKI ‘EM ‘ENTE MINEL-LA’IBINE
KALE BEL REBBUKUM REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDIL-LEDHI FETEREHUNNE WE ‘ENA ‘ALA DHALIKUM MINE ESH-SHAHIDINE
WE TALLLEHI LE’EKIDENNE ‘ESNAMEKUM BA’DE ‘EN TUWELLU MUDBIRINE
FEXHE’ALEHUM XHUDHADHÆN ‘ILLA KEBIRÆN LEHUM LE’ALLEHUM ‘ILEJHI JERXHI’UNE
KALU MEN FE’ALE HADHA BI’ALIHETINA ‘INNEHU LEMINE EDH-DHALIMINE
KALU SEMI’NA FETEN JEDHKURUHUM JUKALU LEHU ‘IBRAHIMU
KALU FE’TU BIHI ‘ALA ‘A’JUNI EN-NASI LE’ALLEHUM JESH/HEDUNE
KALU ‘E’ENTE FE’ALTE HADHA BI’ALIHETINA JA ‘IBRAHIMU
KALE BEL FE’ALEHU KEBIRUHUM HADHA FAS’ELUHUM ‘IN KANU JENTIKUNE
FEREXHA’U ‘ILA ‘ENFUSIHIM FEKALU ‘INNEKUM ‘ENTUMU EDH-DHALIMUNE
THUMME NUKISU ‘ALA RU’USIHIM LEKAD ‘ALIMTE MA HA’UULA’ JENTIKUNE
KALE ‘EFETA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI MA LA JENFA’UKUM SHEJ’ÆN WE LA JEDURRUKUM
‘UFFIN LEKUM WE LIMA TA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘EFELA TA’KILUNE
KALU HERRIKUHU WE ENSURU ‘ALIHETEKUM ‘IN KUNTUM FA’ILINE
KULNA JA NARU KUNI BERDÆN WE SELAMÆN ‘ALA ‘IBRAHIME
WE ‘ERADU BIHI KEJDÆN FEXHE’ALNAHUMUL-’EHSERINE
WE NEXHXHEJNAHU WE LUTÆN ‘ILAL-’ERDI ELLETI BAREKNA FIHA LIL’ALEMINE
WE WEHEBNA LEHU ‘ISHAKA WE JA’KUBE NAFILETEN WE KULLÆN XHE’ALNA SALIHINE
WE XHE’ALNAHUM ‘E’IMMETEN JEHDUNE BI’EMRINA WE ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJHIM FI’LEL-HAJRATI WE ‘IKAME ES-SELÆTI WE ‘ITA’E EZ-ZEKÆTI WE KANU LENA ‘ABIDINE
WE LUTÆN ‘ATEJNAHU HUKMÆN WE ‘ILMÆN WE NEXHXHEJNAHU MINEL-KARJETI ELLETI KANET TA’MELUL-HABA’ITHE ‘INNEHUM KANU KAWME SEW’IN FASIKINE
WE ‘EDHALNAHU FI REHMETINA ‘INNEHU MINE ES-SALIHINE
WE NUHÆN ‘IDH NADA MIN KABLU FASTEXHEBNA LEHU FENEXHXHEJNAHU WE ‘EHLEHU MINEL-KERBIL-’ADHIMI
WE NESERNAHU MINEL-KAWMIL-LEDHINE KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATINA ‘INNEHUM KANU KAWME SEW’IN FE’EGREKNAHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
WE DAWUDE WE SULEJMANE ‘IDH JEHKUMANI FIL-HERTHI ‘IDH NEFESHET FIHI GANEMUL-KAWMI WE KUNNA LIHUKMIHIM SHAHIDINE
FEFEHHEMNAHA SULEJMANE WE KULLÆN ‘ATEJNA HUKMÆN WE ‘ILMÆN WE SEHHARNA ME’A DAWUDEL-XHIBALE JUSEBBIHNE WET-TEJRE WE KUNNA FA’ILINE
WE ‘ALLEMNAHU SEN’ATE LEBUSIN LEKUM LITUHSINEKUM MIN BE’SIKUM FEHEL ‘ENTUM SHAKIRUNE
WE LISULEJMANE ER-RIHE ‘ASIFETEN TEXHRI BI’EMRIHI ‘ILAL-’ERDI ELLETI BAREKNA FIHA WE KUNNA BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMINE
WE MINE ESH-SHEJATINI MEN JEGUSUNE LEHU WE JA’MELUNE ‘AMELÆN DUNE DHALIKE WE KUNNA LEHUM HAFIDHINE
WE ‘EJJUBE ‘IDH NADA REBBEHU ‘ENNI MESSENI ED-DURRU WE ‘ENTE ‘ERHEMU ER-RAHIMINE
FASTEXHEBNA LEHU FEKESHEFNA MA BIHI MIN DURRIN WE ‘ATEJNAHU ‘EHLEHU WE MITHLEHUM ME’AHUM REHMETEN MIN ‘INDINA WE DHIKRA LIL’ABIDINE
WE ‘ISMA’ILE WE ‘IDRISE WE DHAL-KIFLI KULLUN MINE ES-SABIRINE
WE ‘EDHALNAHUM FI REHMETINA ‘INNEHUM MINE ES-SALIHINE
WE DHA EN-NUNI ‘IDH DHEHEBE MUGADIBÆN FEDHENNE ‘EN LEN NEKDIRE ‘ALEJHI FENADA FI EDH-DHULUMATI ‘EN LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA ‘ENTE SUBHANEKE ‘INNI KUNTU MINE EDH-DHALIMINE
FASTEXHEBNA LEHU WE NEXHXHEJNAHU MINEL-GAMMI WE KEDHELIKE NUNXHIL-MU’UMININE
WE ZEKERIJA ‘IDH NADA REBBEHU RABBI LA TEDHERNI FERDÆN WE ‘ENTE HAJRUL-WARITHINE
FASTEXHEBNA LEHU WE WEHEBNA LEHU JEHJA WE ‘ESLEHNA LEHU ZEWXHEHU ‘INNEHUM KANU JUSARI’UNE FIL-HAJRATI WE JED’UNENA REGABÆN WE REHEBÆN WE KANU LENA HASHI’INE
WE E-ETI ‘EHSENET FERXHEHA FENEFEHNA FIHA MIN RUHINA WE XHE’ALNAHA WE EBNEHA ‘AJETEN LIL’ALEMINE
‘INNE HEDHIHI ‘UMMETUKUM ‘UMMETEN WAHIDETEN WE ‘ENA REBBUKUM FA’BUDUNI
WE TEKATTA’U ‘EMREHUM BEJNEHUM KULLUN ‘ILEJNA RAXHI’UNE
FEMEN JA’MEL MINE ES-SALIHATI WE HUWE MU’UMINUN FELA KUFRANE LISA’JIHI WE ‘INNA LEHU KATIBUNE
WE HERAMUN ‘ALA KARJETIN ‘EHLEKNAHA ‘ENNEHUM LA JERXHI’UNE
HETTA ‘IDHA FUTIHET JE’XHUXHU WE ME’XHUXHU WE HUM MIN KULLI HEDEBIN JENSILUNE
WAKTEREBEL-WA’DUL-HEKKU FE’IDHA HIJE SHAHISETUN ‘EBSARUL-LEDHINE KEFERU JA WEJLENA KAD KUNNA FI GAFLETIN MIN HADHA BEL KUNNA DHALIMINE
‘INNEKUM WE MA TA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI HESEBU XHEHENNEME ‘ENTUM LEHA WE ERIDUNE
LEW KANE HA’UULA’ ‘ALIHETEN MA WEREDUHA WE KULLUN FIHA HALIDUNE
LEHUM FIHA ZEFIRUN WE HUM FIHA LA JESMA’UNE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE SEBEKAT LEHUM MINNAL-HUSNA ‘ULA’IKE ‘ANHA MUB’ADUNE
LA JESMA’UNE HESISEHA WE HUM FI MA ESHTEHET ‘ENFUSUHUM HALIDUNE
LA JEHZUNUHUMUL-FEZA’UL-’EKBERU WE TETELEKKAHUMUL-MELA’IKETU HADHA JEWMUKUMUL-LEDHI KUNTUM TU’ADUNE
JEWME NETWI ES-SEMA’E KETEJJI ES-SIXHILLI LILKUTUBI KEMA BEDE’NA ‘EWWELE HALKIN NU’IDUHU WA’DÆN ‘ALEJNA ‘INNA KUNNA FA’ILINE
WE LEKAD KETEBNA FI EZ-ZEBURI MIN BA’DI EDH-DHIKRI ‘ENNEL-’ERDE JERITHUHA ‘IBADIJE ES-SALIHUNE
‘INNE FI HADHA LEBELAGÆN LIKAWMIN ‘ABIDINE
WE MA ‘ERSELNAKE ‘ILLA REHMETEN LIL’ALEMINE
KUL ‘INNEMA JUHA ‘ILEJJE ‘ENNEMA ‘ILEHUKUM ‘ILEHUN WAHIDUN FEHEL ‘ENTUM MUSLIMUNE
FE’IN TEWELLEW FEKUL ‘ADHENTUKUM ‘ALA SEWA’IN WE ‘IN ‘EDRI ‘EKARIBUN ‘EM BA’IDUN MA TU’ADUNE
‘INNEHU JA’LEMUL-XHEHRE MINEL-KAWLI WE JA’LEMU MA TEKTUMUNE
WE ‘IN ‘EDRI LE’ALLEHU FITNETUN LEKUM WE META’UN ‘ILA HININ
KALE RABBI EHKUM BIL-HEKKI WE REBBUNA ER-REHMANUL-MUSTA’ANU ‘ALA MA TESIFUNE
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ETTEKU REBBEKUM ‘INNE ZELZELETE ES-SA’ATI SHEJ’UN ‘ADHIMUN
JEWME TEREWNEHA TEDH/HELU KULLU MURDI’ATIN ‘AMMA ‘ERDE’AT WE TEDA’U KULLU DHATI HEMLIN HEMLEHA WE TERA EN-NASE SUKARA WE MA HUM BISUKARA WE LEKINNE ‘ADHABEL-LAHI SHEDIDUN
WE MINE EN-NASI MEN JUXHADILU FI ELLAHI BIGAJRI ‘ILMIN WE JETTEBI’U KULLE SHEJTANIN MERIDIN
KUTIBE ‘ALEJHI ‘ENNEHU MEN TEWELLAHU FE’ENNEHU JUDILLUHU WE JEHDIHI ‘ILA ‘ADHABI ES-SA’IRI
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ‘IN KUNTUM FI REJBIN MINEL-BA’THI FE’INNA HALEKNAKUM MIN TURABIN THUMME MIN NUTFETIN THUMME MIN ‘ALEKATIN THUMME MIN MUDGATIN MUHALLEKATIN WE GAJRI MUHALLEKATIN LINUBEJJINE LEKUM WE NUKIRRU FIL-’ERHAMI MA NESHA’U ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN 
DHALIKE BI’ENNEL-LAHE HUWEL-HEKKU WE ‘ENNEHU JUHJIL-MEWTA WE ‘ENNEHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
WE ‘ENNE ES-SA’ATE ‘ATIJETUN LA REJBE FIHA WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE JEB’ATHU MEN FIL-KUBURI
WE MINE EN-NASI MEN JUXHADILU FI ELLAHI BIGAJRI ‘ILMIN WE LA HUDEN WE LA KITABIN MUNIRIN
THANIJE ‘ITFIHI LIJUDILLE ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI LEHU FI ED-DUNJA HIZJUN WE NUDHIKUHU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘ADHABEL-HERIKI
DHALIKE BIMA KADDEMET JEDAKE WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE LEJSE BIDHELLAMIN LIL’ABIDI
WE MINE EN-NASI MEN JA’BUDU ELLAHE ‘ALA HERFIN FE’IN ‘ESABEHU HAJRUN ETME’ENNE BIHI WE ‘IN ‘ESABET/HU FITNETUN ENKALEBE ‘ALA WEXHHIHI HASIRE ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETE DHALIKE HUWEL-HUSRANUL-MUBINU
JED’U MIN DUNI ELLAHI MA LA JEDURRUHU WE MA LA JENFA’UHU DHALIKE HUWE ED-DELALUL-BA’IDU
JED’U LEMEN DERRUHU ‘EKREBU MIN NEF’IHI LEBI’SEL-MEWLA WE LEBI’SEL-’ASHIRU
‘INNALL-LLAHE JUDHILUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU ‘INNALL-LLAHE JEF’ALU MA JURIDU
MEN KANE JEDHUNNU ‘EN LEN JENSUREHU ELLAHU FI ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETI FELJEMDUD BISEBEBIN ‘ILA ES-SEMA’I THUMME LIJEKTA’ FELJENDHUR HEL JUDH/HIBENNE KEJDUHU MA JEGIDHU
WE KEDHELIKE ‘ENZELNAHU ‘AJATIN BEJJINATIN WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE JEHDI MEN JURIDU
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WEL-LEDHINE HADU WE ES-SABI’INE WE EN-NESARA WEL-MEXHUSE WEL-LEDHINE ‘ESHREKU ‘INNALL-LLAHE JEFSILU BEJNEHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN SHEHIDUN
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE JESXHUDU LEHU MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MEN FIL-’ERDI WE ESH-SHEMSU WEL-KAMERU WE EN-NUXHUMU WEL-XHIBALU WE ESH-SHEXHERU WE ED-DEWABBU WE KETHIRUN MINE EN-NASI WE KETHIRUN HEKKA ‘ALEJHIL-’ADHABU WE MEN JUHINI ELLAHU FEMA LEHU MIN MUKRIM
HEDHANI HASMANI EHTESEMU FI RABBIHIM FE-EL-LEDHINE KEFERU KUTTI’AT LEHUM THIJABUN MIN NARIN JUSEBBU MIN FEWKI RU’USIHIMUL-HEMIMU
JUSHERU BIHI MA FI BUTUNIHIM WEL-XHULUDU
WE LEHUM MEKAMI’U MIN HEDIDIN
KULLEMA ‘ERADU ‘EN JEHRUXHU MINHA MIN GAMMIN ‘U’IDU FIHA WE DHUKU ‘ADHABEL-HERIKI
‘INNALL-LLAHE JUDHILUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU JUHELLEWNE FIHA MIN ‘ESAWIRE MIN DHEHEBIN WE LU’ULU’UÆN WE LIBASUHUM FIHA HERIRUN
WE HUDU ‘ILAT-TEJJIBI MINEL-KAWLI WE HUDU ‘ILA SIRATIL-HEMIDI
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE JESUDDUNE ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI WEL-MESXHIDIL-HERAMIL-LEDHI XHE’ALNAHU LILNNASI SEWA’ENL-’AKIFU FIHI WEL-BADI WE MEN JURID FIHI BI’ILHADIN BIDHULMIN NUDHIKHU MIN ‘ADHABIN ‘ELIMIN
WE ‘IDH BEWWE’NA LI’IBRAHIME MEKANEL-BEJTI ‘EN LA TUSHRIK BI SHEJ’ÆN WE TEHHIR BEJTIJE LILTTA’IFINE WEL-KA’IMINE WE ER-RUKKA’I ES-SUXHUDI
WE ‘EDHDHIN FI EN-NASI BIL-HEXHXHI JE’TUKE RIXHALÆN WE ‘ALA KULLI DAMIRIN JE’TINE MIN KULLI FEXHXHIN ‘AMIKIN
LIJESH/HEDU MENAFI’A LEHUM WE JEDHKURU ESMEL-LAHI FI ‘EJJAMIN MA’LUMATIN ‘ALA MA REZEKAHUM MIN BEHIMETIL-’EN’AM FEKULU MINHA WE ‘ET’IMUL-BA’ISEL-FEKIRE
THUMME LIJEKDU TEFETHEHUM WE LIUFU NUDHUREHUM WE LIETTEWWEFU BIL-BEJTIL-’ATIKI
DHALIKE WE MEN JU’ADHDHIM HURUMATI ELLAHI FEHUWE HAJRUN LEHU ‘INDE RABBIHI WE ‘UHILLET LEKUMUL-’EN’AM ‘ILLA MA JUTLA ‘ALEJKUM FAXHTENIBU ER-RIXHSE MINEL-’EWTHANI WE EXHTENIBU KAWLE EZ-ZURI
HUNEFA’E LILLAHI GAJRE MUSHRIKINE BIHI WE MEN JUSHRIK BILLAHI FEKE’ENNEMA HARRE MINE ES-SEMA’I FETEHTEFUHUT-TEJRU ‘EW TEHWI BIHI ER-RIHU FI MEKANIN SEHIKIN
DHALIKE WE MEN JU’ADHDHIM SHA’A’IREL-LAHI FE’INNEHA MIN TEKWAL-KULUBI
LEKUM FIHA MENAFI’U ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN THUMME MEHILLUHA ‘ILAL-BEJTIL-’ATIKI
WE LIKULLI ‘UMMETIN XHE’ALNA MENSEKÆN LIJEDHKURU ESMEL-LAHI ‘ALA MA REZEKAHUM MIN BEHIMETIL-’EN’AMI FE’ILEHUKUM ‘ILEHUN WAHIDUN FELEHU ‘ESLIMU WE BESHSHIRIL-MUHBITINE
EL-LEDHINE ‘IDHA DHUKIREL-LAHU WEXHILET KULUBUHUM WE ES-SABIRINE ‘ALA MA ‘ESABEHUM WEL-MUKIMI ES-SELÆTI WE MIMMA REZEKNAHUM JUNFIKUNE
WEL-BUDNE XHE’ALNAHA LEKUM MIN SHA’A’IRI ELLAHI LEKUM FIHA HAJRUN FADHKURU ESMEL-LAHI ‘ALEJHA SEWAFFE FE’IDHA WEXHEBET XHUNUBUHA FEKULU MINHA WE ‘ET’IMUL-KANI’A WEL-MU’TERRE KEDHALIKE SEHHARNAHA LEKUM LE’ALLEKUM TESHKURUNE
LEN JENALEL-LAHE LUHUMUHA WE LA DIMA’UUHA WE LEKIN JENALUHUT-TEKWA MINKUM KEDHALIKE SEHHAREHA LEKUM LITUKEBBIRU ELLAHE ‘ALA MA HEDAKUM WE BESHSHIRIL-MUHSININE
‘INNALL-LLAHE JUDAFI’U ‘ANIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JUHIBBU KULLE HAWWANIN KEFURIN
‘UDHINE LILLEDHINE JUKATELUNE BI’ENNEHUM DHULIMU WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALA NESRIHIM LEKADIRUN
EL-LEDHINE ‘UHRIXHU MIN DIJARIHIM BIGAJRI HEKKIN ‘ILLA ‘EN JEKULU REBBUNALLAHU WE LEWLA DEF’U ELLAHI EN-NASE BA’DEHUM BIBA’DIN LEHUDDIMET SEWAMI’U WE BIJA’UN WE SELEWATUN WE MESAXHIDU JUDHKERU FIHA ESMU ELLAHI KETHIRÆN WE LEJENSURENNEL-LAHU MEN JENSURUHU 
EL-LEDHINE ‘IN MEKKENNAHUM FIL-’ERDI ‘EKAMU ES-SELÆTE WE ‘ATEW EZ-ZEKÆTE WE ‘EMERU BIL-MA’RUFI WE NEHEW ‘ANIL-MUNKERI WE LILLEHI ‘AKIBETUL-’UMURI
WE ‘IN JUKEDHDHIBUKE FEKAD KEDHDHEBET KABLEHUM KAWMU NUHIN WE ‘ADUN WE THEMUDU
WE KAWMU ‘IBRAHIME WE KAWMU LUTIN
WE ‘ESHABU MEDJENE WE KUDHDHIBE MUSA FE’EMLEJTU LILKAFIRINE THUMME ‘EHADHTUHUM FEKEJFE KANE NEKIRI
FEKE’EJJIN MIN KARJETIN ‘EHLEKNAHA WE HIJE DHALIMETUN FEHIJE HAWIJETUN ‘ALA ‘URUSHIHA WE BI’RIN MU’ATTELETIN WE KASRIN MESHIDIN
‘EFELEM JESIRU FIL-’ERDI FETEKUNE LEHUM KULUBUN JA’KILUNE BIHA ‘EW ‘ADHANUN JESMA’UNE BIHA FE’INNEHA LA TA’MAL-’EBSARU WE LEKIN TA’MAL-KULUBU ELLETI FI ES-SUDURI
WE JESTA’XHILUNEKE BIL-’ADHABI WE LEN JUHLIFEL-LAHU WA’DEHU WE ‘INNE JEWMÆN ‘INDE RABBIKE KE’ELFI SENETIN MIMMA TA’UDDUNE
WE KE’EJJIN MIN KARJETIN ‘EMLEJTU LEHA WE HIJE DHALIMETUN THUMME ‘EHADHTUHA WE ‘ILEJJEL-MESIRU
KUL JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ‘INNEMA ‘ENA LEKUM NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
FE-EL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LEHUM MEGFIRETUN WE RIZKUN KERIMUN
WEL-LEDHINE SE’AW FI ‘AJATINA MU’AXHIZINE ‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABUL-XHEHIMI
WE MA ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE MIN RESULIN WE LA NEBIJIN ‘ILLA ‘IDHA TEMENNA ‘ELKA ESH-SHEJTANU FI ‘UMNIJETIHI FEJENSEHU ELLAHU MA JULKI ESH-SHEJTANU THUMME JUHKIMU ELLAHU ‘AJATIHI WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN HEKIMUN
LIJEXH’ALE MA JULKI ESH-SHEJTANU FITNETEN LILLEDHINE FI KULUBIHIM MEREDUN WEL-KASIJETI KULUBUHUM WE ‘INNE EDH-DHALIMINE LEFI SHIKAKIN BA’IDIN
WE LIJA’LEMEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME ‘ENNEHUL-HEKKU MIN RABBIKE FEJU’UMINU BIHI FETUHBITE LEHU KULUBUHUM WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEHADIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘ILA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
WE LA JEZALUL-LEDHINE KEFERU FI MIRJETIN MINHU HETTA TE’TIJEHUMU ES-SA’ATU BEGTETEN ‘EW JE’TIJEHUM ‘ADHABU JEWMIN ‘AKIMIN
EL-MULKU JEWME’IDHIN LILLAHI JEHKUMU BEJNEHUM FE-EL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI FI XHENNATI EN-NA’IMI
WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATINA FE’ULA’IKE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN MUHINUN
WEL-LEDHINE HAXHERU FI SEBILI ELLAHI THUMME KUTILU ‘EW MATU LEJERZUKANNEHUMU ELLAHU RIZKÆN HESENÆN WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEHUWE HAJRU ER-RAZIKINE
LEJUDHILENNEHUM MUDHALÆN JERDEWNEHU WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE LE’ALIMUN HELIMUN
DHALIKE WE MEN ‘AKABE BIMITHLI MA ‘UKIBE BIHI THUMME BUGIJE ‘ALEJHI LEJENSURENNEHU ELLAHU ‘INNALL-LLAHE LE’AFUWUN GAFURUN
DHALIKE BI’ENNEL-LAHE JULIXHUL-LEJLE FI EN-NEHARI WE JULIXHU EN-NEHARE FIL-LEJLI WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE SEMI’UN BESIRUN
DHALIKE BI’ENNEL-LAHE HUWEL-HEKKU WE ‘ENNE MA JED’UNE MIN DUNIHI HUWEL-BATILU WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE HUWEL-’ALIJUL-KEBIRU
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE ‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FETUSBIHUL-’ERDU MUHDERRETEN ‘INNALL-LLAHE LETIFUN HABIRUN
LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEHUWEL-GANIJUL-HEMIDU
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE SEHHARE LEKUM MA FIL-’ERDI WEL-FULKE TEXHRI FIL-BEHRI BI’EMRIHI WE JUMSIKU ES-SEMA’E ‘EN TEKA’A ‘ALEL-’ERDI ‘ILLA BI’IDHNIHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE BIN-NASI LERE’UFUN REHIMUN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI ‘EHJAKUM THUMME JUMITUKUM THUMME JUHJIKUM ‘INNEL-’INSANE LEKEFURUN
LIKULLI ‘UMMETIN XHE’ALNA MENSEKÆN HUM NASIKUHU FELA JUNAZI’UNNEKE FIL-’EMRI WE ED’U ‘ILA RABBIKE ‘INNEKE LE’ALA HUDEN MUSTEKIMIN
WE ‘IN XHADELUKE FEKULI ELLAHU ‘A’LEMU BIMA TA’MELUNE
ELLAHU JEHKUMU BEJNEKUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI FIMA KUNTUM FIHI TEHTELIFUNE
‘ELEM TA’LEM ‘ENNEL-LAHE JA’LEMU MA FI ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI ‘INNE DHALIKE FI KITABIN ‘INNE DHALIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI JESIRUN
WE JA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI MA LEM JUNEZZIL BIHI SULTANÆN WE MA LEJSE LEHUM BIHI ‘ILMUN WE MA LILDHDHALIMINE MIN NESIRIN
WE ‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATUNA BEJJINATIN TA’RIFU FI WUXHUHIL-LEDHINE KEFERUL-MUNKERE JEKADUNE JESTUNE BIEL-LEDHINE JETLUNE ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATINA KUL ‘EFE’UNEBBI’UKUM BISHERRIN MIN DHELIKUMU EN-NARU WE’ADEHALLAHUL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE BI’SEL-MESIRU
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU DURIBE METHELUN FASTEMI’U LEHU ‘INNEL-LEDHINE TED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI LEN JEHLUKU DHUBABÆN WE LEWI EXHTEMA’U LEHU WE ‘IN JESLUBHUMU EDH-DHUBABU SHEJ’ÆN LA JESTENKIDHUHU MINHU DA’UFET-TALIBU WEL-METLUBU
MA KADERU ELLAHE HEKKA KADRIHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEKAWIJUN ‘AZIZUN
ELLAHU JESTEFI MINEL-MELA’IKETI RUSULÆN WE MINE EN-NASI ‘INNALL-LLAHE SEMI’UN BESIRUN
JA’LEMU MA BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE MA HALFEHUM WE ‘ILA ELLAHI TURXHA’UL-’UMURU
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ERKA’U WE ESXHUDU WE A’BUDU REBBEKUM WE EF’ALUL-HAJRE LE’ALLEKUM TUFLIHUNE
WE XHAHIDU FI ELLAHI HEKKA XHIHADIHI HUWE EXHTEBAKUM WE MA XHE’ALE ‘ALEJKUM FI ED-DINI MIN HEREXHIN MILLETE ‘EBIKUM ‘IBRAHIME HUWE SEMMAKUMUL-MUSLIMJNE MIN KABLU WE FI HADHA LIJEKUNE ER-RESULU SHEHIDÆN ‘ALEJKUM WE TEKUNU SHUHEDA’E ‘ALA EN-NASI FE’EKIMU ES
KAD ‘EFLEHEL-MU’UMINUNE
EL-LEDHINE HUM FI SELATIHIM HASHI’UNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM ‘ANIL-LEGWI MU’RIDUNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM LILZZEKÆTI FA’ILUNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM LIFURUXHIHIM HAFIDHUNE
‘ILLA ‘ALA ‘EZWAXHIHIM ‘W MA MELEKET ‘EJMANUHUM FE’INNEHUM GAJRU MELUMINE
FEMENI EBTEGA WERA’E DHALIKE FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-’ADUNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM LI’MANATIHIM WE ‘AHDIHIM RA’UNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM ‘ALA SELEWATIHIM JUHAFIDHUNE
‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-WARITHUNE
EL-LEDHINE JERITHUNEL-FIRDEWSE HUM FIHA HALIDUNE
WE LEKAD HALEKNAL-’INSANE MIN SULALETIN MIN TININ
THUMME XHE’ALNAHU NUTFETEN FI KARARIN MEKININ
THUMME HALEKNA EN-NUTFETE ‘ALEKATEN FEHALEKNAL-’ALEKATE MUDGATEN FEHALEKNAL-MUDGATE ‘IDHAMÆN FEKESEWNAL-’IDHAME LEHMÆN THUMME ‘ENSHE’NAHU HALKÆN ‘AHARE FETEBAREKEL-LAHU ‘EHSENUL-HALIKINE
THUMME ‘INNEKUM BA’DE DHALIKE LEMEJJITUNE
THUMME ‘INNEKUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI TUB’ATHUNE
WE LEKAD HALEKNA FEWKAKUM SEB’A TERA’IKA WE MA KUNNA ‘ANIL-HALKI GAFILINE
WE ‘ENZELNA MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN BIKADERIN FE’ESKENNAHU FIL-’ERDI WE ‘INNA ‘ALA DHEHABIN BIHI LEKADIRUNE
FE’ENSHE’NA LEKUM BIHI XHENNATIN MIN NEHILIN WE ‘A’NABIN LEKUM FIHA FEWAKIHU KETHIRETUN WE MINHA TE’KULUNE
WE SHEXHERETEN TEHRUXHU MIN TURI SEJNA’E TENBUTU BID-DUHNI WE SIBGIN LIL’AKILINE
WE ‘INNE LEKUM FIL-’EN’AMI LA’IBRETEN NUSKIKUM MIMMA FI BUTUNIHA WE LEKUM FIHA MENAFI’U KETHIRETUN WE MINHA TE’KULUNE
WE ‘ALEJHA WE ‘ALEL-FULKI TUHMELUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA NUHÆN ‘ILA KAWMIHI FEKALE JA KAWMI A’BUDU ELLAHE MA LEKUM MIN ‘ILEHIN GAJRUHU ‘EFELA TETTEKUNE
FEKALEL-MELE’UL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN KAWMIHI MA HADHA ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUKUM JURIDU ‘EN JETEFEDDELE ‘ALEJKUM WE LEW SHA’EL-LAHU LE’ENZELE MELA’IKETEN MA SEMI’NA BIHEDHA FI ‘ABA’INAL-’EWWELINE
‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA REXHULUN BIHI XHINNETUN FETEREBBESU BIHI HETTA HININ
KALE RABBI ENSURNI BIMA KEDHDHEBUNI
FE’EWHEJNA ‘ILEJHI ‘ENI ESNA’IL-FULKE BI’A’JUNINA WE WEHJINA FE’IDHA XHA’E ‘EMRUNA WE FARET-TENNURU FASLUK FIHA MIN KULLIN ZEWXHEJNI ETHNEJNI WE ‘EHLEKE ‘ILLA MEN SEBEKA ‘ALEJHIL-KAWLU MINHUM WE LA TUHATIBNI FIL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ‘INNEHUM MUGREKUNE
FE’IDHA ESTEWEJTE ‘ENTE WE MEN ME’AKE ‘ALEL-FULKI FEKULIL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI NEXHXHANA MINEL-KAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
WE KUL RABBI ‘ENZILNI MUNZELÆN MUBAREKÆN WE ‘ENTE HAJRUL-MUNZILINE
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN WE ‘IN KUNNA LEMUBTELINE
THUMME ‘ENSHE’NA MIN BA’DIHIM KARNÆN ‘AHARINE
FE’ERSELNA FIHIM RESULÆN MINHUM ‘ENI A’BUDU ELLAHE MA LEKUM MIN ‘ILEHIN GAJRUHU ‘EFELA TETTEKUNE
WE KALEL-MELE’U MIN KAWMIHIL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE KEDHDHEBU BILIKA’IL-’AHIRETI WE ‘ETREFNAHUM FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA MA HADHA ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUKUM JE’KULU MIMMA TE’KULUNE MINHU WE JESHREBU MIMMA TESHREBUNE
WE LE’IN ‘ETA’TUM BESHERÆN MITHLEKUM ‘INNEKUM ‘IDHÆN LEHASIRUNE
‘EJA’IDUKUM ‘ENNEKUM ‘IDHA MITTUM WE KUNTUM TURABÆN WE ‘IDHAMÆN ‘ENNEKUM MUHREXHUNE
HEJHATE HEJHATE LIMA TU’ADUNE
‘IN HIJE ‘ILLA HEJATUNA ED-DUNJA NEMUTU WE NEHJA WE MA NEHNU BIMEB’UTHINE
‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA REXHULUN EFTERA ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN WE MA NEHNU LEHU BIMU’UMININE
KALE RABBI ENSURNI BIMA KEDHDHEBUNI
KALE ‘AMMA KALILIN LEJUSBIHUNNE NADIMINE
FE’EHADHET/HUMU ES-SEJHETU BIL-HEKKI FEXHE’ALNAHUM GUTHA’EN FEBU’DÆN LILKAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
THUMME ‘ENSHE’NA MIN BA’DIHIM KURUNÆN ‘AHARINE
MA TESBIKU MIN ‘UMMETIN ‘EXHELEHA WE MA JESTE’HIRUNE
THUMME ‘ERSELNA RUSULENA TETRA KULLE MA XHA’E ‘UMMETEN RESULUHA KEDHDHEBUHU FE’ETBA’NA BA’DEHUM BA’DÆN WE XHE’ALNAHUM ‘EHADITHE FEBU’DÆN LIKAWMIN LA JU’UMINUNE
THUMME ‘ERSELNA MUSA WE ‘EHAHU HARUNE BI’AJATINA WE SULTANIN MUBININ
‘ILA FIR’AWNE WE MELE’IHI FASTEKBERU WE KANU KAWMÆN ‘ALINE
FEKALU ‘ENU’UMINU LIBESHEREJNI MITHLINA WE KAWMUHUMA LENA ‘ABIDUNE
FEKEDHDHEBUHUMA FEKANU MINEL-MUHLEKINE
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE LE’ALLEHUM JEHTEDUNE
WE XHE’ALNA EBNE MERJEME WE ‘UMMEHU ‘AJETEN WE ‘AWEJNAHUMA ‘ILA REBWETIN DHATI KARARIN WE MA’ININ
JA ‘EJJUHA ER-RUSULU KULU MINET-TEJJIBATI WE A’MELU SALIHÆN ‘INNI BIMA TA’MELUNE ‘ALIMUN
WE ‘INNE HEDHIHI ‘UMMETUKUM ‘UMMETEN WAHIDETEN WE ‘ENA REBBUKUM FE ETTEKUNI
FETEKATTA’U ‘EMREHUM BEJNEHUM ZUBURÆN KULLU HIZBIN BIMA LEDEJHIM FERIHUNE
FEDHERHUM FI GAMRETIHIM HETTA HININ
‘EJEHSEBUNE ‘ENNEMA NUMIDDUHUM BIHI MIN MALIN WE BENINE
NUSARI’U LEHUM FIL-HAJRATI BEL LA JESH’URUNE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE HUM MIN HASHJETI RABBIHIM MUSHFIKUNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM BI’AJATI RABBIHIM JU’UMINUNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM BIREBBIHIM LA JUSHRIKUNE
WEL-LEDHINE JU’UTUNE MA ‘ATEW WE KULUBUHUM WE XHILETUN ‘ENNEHUM ‘ILA RABBIHIM RAXHI’UNE
‘ULA’IKE JUSARI’UNE FIL-HAJRATI WE HUM LEHA SABIKUNE
WE LA NUKELLIFU NEFSÆN ‘ILLA WUS’AHA WE LEDEJNA KITABUN JENTIKU BIL-HEKKI WE HUM LA JUDHLEMUN
BEL KULUBUHUM FI GAMRETIN MIN HADHA WE LEHUM ‘A’MALUN MIN DUNI DHALIKE HUM LEHA ‘AMILUNE
HETTA ‘IDHA ‘EHADHNA MUTREFIHIM BIL-’ADHABI ‘IDHA HUM JEXH’ERUNE
LA TEXH’ERUL-JEWME ‘INNEKUM MINNA LA TUNSERUNE
KAD KANET ‘AJATI TUTLA ‘ALEJKUM FEKUNTUM ‘ALA ‘A’KABIKUM TENKISUNE
MUSTEKBIRINE BIHI SAMIRÆN TEHXHURUNE
‘EFELEM JEDDEBBERUL-KAWLE ‘EM XHA’EHUM MA LEM JE’TI ‘ABA’EHUMUL-’EWWELINE
‘EM LEM JA’RIFU RESULEHUM FEHUM LEHU MUNKIRUNE
‘EM JEKULUNE BIHI XHINNETUN BEL XHA’EHUM BIL-HEKKI WE ‘EKTHERUHUM LILHEKKI KARIHUNE
WE LEWI ETTEBE’AL-HEKKU ‘EHWA’EHUM LEFESEDETI ES-SEMAWATU WEL-’ERDU WE MEN FIHINNE BEL ‘ETEJNAHUM BIDHIKRIHIM FEHUM ‘AN DHIKRIHIM MU’RIDUNE
‘EM TES’ELUHUM HARXHÆN FEHARAXHU RABBIKE HAJRUN WE HUWE HAJRU ER-RAZIKINE
WE ‘INNEKE LETED’UHUM ‘ILA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
WE ‘INNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI ‘ANI ES-SIRATI LENAKIBUNE
WE LEW REHIMNAHUM WE KESHEFNA MA BIHIM MIN DURRIN LELEXHXHU FI TUGJANIHIM JA’MEHUNE
WE LEKAD ‘EHADHNAHUM BIL-’ADHABI FEMA ESTEKANU LIREBBIHIM WE MA JETEDERRA’UNE
HETTA ‘IDHA FETEHNA ‘ALEJHIM BABÆN DHA ‘ADHABIN SHEDIDIN ‘IDHA HUM FIHI MUBLISUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI ‘ENSHE’E LEKUMU ES-SEM’A WEL-’EBSARE WEL-’EF’IDETE KALILÆN MA TESHKURUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI DHERE’EKUM FIL-’ERDI WE ‘ILEJHI TUHSHERUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI JUHJI WE JUMITU WE LEHU EHTILAFUL-LEJLI WE EN-NEHARI ‘EFELA TA’KILUNE
BEL KALU MITHLE MA KALEL-’EWWELUNE
KALU ‘E’IDHA MITNA WE KUNNA TURABÆN WE ‘IDHAMÆN ‘E’INNA LEMEB’UTHUNE
LEKAD WU’IDNA NEHNU WE ‘ABA’UUNA HADHA MIN KABLU ‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA ‘ESATIRUL-’EWWELINE
KUL LIMENIL-’ERDU WE MEN FIHA ‘IN KUNTUM TA’LEMUNE
SEJEKULUNE LILLAHI KUL ‘EFELA TEDHEKKERUNE
KUL MEN REBBU ES-SEMAWATI ES-SEB’I WE REBBUL-’ARSHIL-’ADHIMI
SEJEKULUNE LILLAHI KUL ‘EFELA TETTEKUNE
KUL MEN BIJEDIHI MELEKUTU KULLI SHEJ’IN WE HUWE JUXHIRU WE LA JUXHARU ‘ALEJHI ‘IN KUNTUM TA’LEMUN
SEJEKULUNE LILLAHI KUL FE’ENNA TUSHERUNE
BEL ‘ETEJNAHUM BIL-HEKKI WE ‘INNEHUM LEKADHIBUNE
MA ETTEHADHEL-LAHU MIN WELEDIN WE MA KANE ME’AHU MIN ‘ILEHIN ‘IDHÆN LEDHEHEBE KULLU ‘ILEHIN BIMA HALEKA WE LE’ALA BA’DUHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN SUBHANEL-LAHI ‘AMMA JESIFUNE
‘ALIMIL-GAJBI WE ESH-SHEHADETI FETA’ALA ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
KUL RABBI ‘IMMA TURIJENNI MA JU’ADUNE
REBBI FELA TEXH’ALNI FIL-KAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
WE ‘INNA ‘ALA ‘EN NURIJEKE MA NA’IDUHUM LEKADIRUNE
EDFA’ BI-ETI HIJE ‘EHSENU ES-SEJJI’ETE NEHNU ‘A’LEMU BIMA JESIFUNE
WE KUL RABBI ‘A’UDHU BIKE MIN HEMEZATI ESH-SHEJATINI
WE ‘A’UDHU BIKE RABBI ‘EN JEHDURUNI
HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’E ‘EHEDEHUMUL-MEWTU KALE RABBI ERXHI’UNI
LE’ALLI ‘A’MELU SALIHÆN FIMA TEREKTU KELLA ‘INNEHA KELIMETUN HUWE KA’ILUHA WE MIN WERA’IHIM BERZEHUN ‘ILA JEWMI JUB’ATHUNE
FE’IDHA NUFIHA FI ES-SURI FELA ‘ENSABE BEJNEHUM JEWME’IDHIN WE LA JETESA’ELUNE
FEMEN THEKULET MEWAZINUHU FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUFLIHUNE
WE MEN HAFFET MEWAZINUHU FE’ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE HASIRU ‘ENFUSEHUM FI XHEHENNEME HALIDUNE
TELFEHU WUXHUHEHUMU EN-NARU WE HUM FIHA KALIHUNE
‘ELEM TEKUN ‘AJATI TUTLA ‘ALEJKUM FEKUNTUM BIHA TUKEDHDHIBUNE
KALU REBBENA GALEBET ‘ALEJNA SHIKWETUNA WE KUNNA KAWMÆN DALLINE
REBBENA ‘EHRIXHNA MINHA FE’IN ‘UDNA FE’INNA DHALIMUNE
KALE EHSE’U FIHA WE LA TUKELLIMUNI
‘INNEHU KANE FERIKUN MIN ‘IBADI JEKULUNE REBBENA ‘AMENNA FAGFIR LENA WE ERHEMNA WE ‘ENTE HAJRU ER-RAHIMINE
FATTEHADHTUMUHUM SIHRIJÆN HETTA ‘ENSEWKUM DHIKRI WE KUNTUM MINHUM TEDHEKUNE
‘INNI XHEZEJTUHUMUL-JEWME BIMA SEBERU ‘ENNEHUM HUMUL-FA’IZUNE
KALE KEM LEBITHTUM FIL-’ERDI ‘ADEDE SININE
KALU LEBITHNA JEWMÆN ‘EW BA’DE JEWMIN FAS’ELIL-’ADDINE
KALE ‘IN LEBITHTUM ‘ILLA KALILÆN LEW ‘ENNEKUM KUNTUM TA’LEMUNE
‘EFEHESIBTUM ‘ENNEMA HALEKNAKUM ‘ABETHÆN WE ‘ENNEKUM ‘ILEJNA LA TURXHA’UNE
FETA’ALALLAHUL-MELIKUL-HEKKU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE REBBUL-’ARSHIL-KERIMI
WE MEN JED’U ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE LA BURHANE LEHU BIHI FE’INNEMA HISABUHU ‘INDE RABBIHI ‘INNEHU LA JUFLIHUL-KAFIRUNE
WE KUL RABBI EGFIR WE ERHEM WE ‘ENTE HAJRU ER-RAHIMINE
SURETUN ‘ENZELNAHA WE FEREDNAHA WE ‘ENZELNA FIHA ‘AJATIN BEJJINATIN LE’ALLEKUM TEDHEKKERUNE
EZ-ZANIJETU WE EZ-ZANI FAXHLIDU KULLE WAHIDIN MINHUMA MIA’ETE XHELDETIN WE LA TE’HUDHKUM BIHIMA RE’FETUN FI DINI ELLAHI ‘IN KUNTUM TU’UMINUNE BILLAHI WEL-JEWMIL-’AHIRI WE LIESH/HED ‘ADHABEHUMA TA’IFETUN MINEL-MU’UMININE
EZ-ZANI LA JENKIHU ‘ILLA ZANIJETEN ‘EW MUSHRIKETEN WE EZ-ZANIJETU LA JENKIHUHA ‘ILLA ZANIN ‘EW MUSHRIKUN WE HURRIME DHALIKE ‘ALEL-MU’UMININE
WEL-LEDHINE JERMUNEL-MUHSENATI THUMME LEM JE’TU BI’ERBE’ATI SHUHEDA’E FAXHLIDUHUM THEMANINE XHELDETEN WE LA TEKBELU LEHUM SHEHADETEN ‘EBEDÆN WE ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-FASIKUNE
‘ILLAL-LEDHINE TABU MIN BA’DI DHALIKE WE ‘ESLEHU FE’INNALL-LLAHE GAFURUN REHIMUN
WEL-LEDHINE JERMUNE ‘EZWAXHEHUM WE LEM JEKUN LEHUM SHUHEDA’U ‘ILLA ‘ENFUSUHUM FESHEHADETU ‘EHEDIHIM ‘ERBA’U SHEHADATIN BILLAHI ‘INNEHU LEMINE ES-SADIKINE
WEL-HAMISETU ‘ENNE LA’NETEL-LAHI ‘ALEJHI ‘IN KANE MINEL-KADHIBINE
WE JEDRE’U ‘ANHAL-’ADHABE ‘EN TESH/HEDE ‘ERBE’A SHEHADATIN BILLAHI ‘INNEHU LEMINEL-KADHIBINE
WEL-HAMISETE ‘ENNE GADEBEL-LAHI ‘ALEJHA ‘IN KANE MINE ES-SADIKINE
WE LEWLA FEDLU ELLAHI ‘ALEJKUM WE REHMETUHU WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE TEWWABUN HEKIMUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE XHA’U BIL-’IFKI ‘USBETUN MINKUM LA TEHSEBUHU SHERRÆN LEKUM BEL HUWE HAJRUN LEKUM LIKULLI EMRI’IN MINHUM MA EKTESEBE MINEL-’ITHMI WEL-LEDHI TEWELLA KIBREHU MINHUM LEHU ‘ADHABUN ‘ADHIMUN
LEWLA ‘IDH SEMI’TUMUHU DHENNEL-MU’UMINUNE WEL-MU’UMINATU BI’ENFUSIHIM HAJRÆN WE KALU HADHA ‘IFKUN MUBINUN
LEWLA XHA’U ‘ALEJHI BI’ERBE’ATI SHUHEDA’E FE’IDH LEM JE’TU BISH-SHUHEDA’I FE’ULA’IKE ‘INDEL-LAHI HUMUL-KADHIBUNE
WE LEWLA FEDLU ELLAHI ‘ALEJKUM WE REHMETUHU FI ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETI LEMESSEKUM FI MA ‘EFEDTUM FIHI ‘ADHABUN ‘ADHIMUN
‘IDH TELEKKAWNEHU BI’ELSINETIKUM WE TEKULUNE BI’EFWAHIKUM MA LEJSE LEKUM BIHI ‘ILMUN WE TEHSEBUNEHU HEJJINÆN WE HUWE ‘INDEL-LAHI ‘ADHIMUN
WE LEWLA ‘IDH SEMI’TUMUHU KULTUM MA JEKUNU LENA ‘EN NETEKELLEME BIHEDHA SUBHANEKE HADHA BUHTANUN ‘ADHIMUN
JA’IDHUKUMU ELLAHU ‘EN TA’UDU LIMITHLIHI ‘EBEDÆN ‘IN KUNTUM MU’UMININE
WE JUBEJJINU ELLAHU LEKUMUL-’AJATI WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN HEKIMUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JUHIBBUNE ‘EN TESHI’AL-FAHISHETU FIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN FI ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETI WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU WE ‘ENTUM LA TA’LEMUNE
WE LEWLA FEDLU ELLAHI ‘ALEJKUM WE REHMETUHU WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE RE’UFUN REHIM
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TETTEBI’U HUTUWATI ESH-SHEJTANI WE MEN JETTEBI’ HUTUWATI ESH-SHEJTANI FE’INNEHU JE’MURU BIL-FEHSHA’I WEL-MUNKERI WE LEWLA FEDLU ELLAHI ‘ALEJKUM WE REHMETUHU MA ZEKA MINKUM MIN ‘EHEDIN ‘EBEDÆN WE LEKINNALL-LLAHE JUZEKKI MEN JE
WE LA JE’TELI ‘ULUL-FEDLI MINKUM WE ES-SE’ATI ‘EN JU’UTU ‘ULIL-KURBA WEL-MESAKINE WEL-MUHAXHIRINE FI SEBILI ELLAHI WE LIA’FU WE LIESFEHU ‘ELA TUHIBBUNE ‘EN JEGFIREL-LAHU LEKUM WEL-LAHU GAFURUN REHIMUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JERMUNEL-MUHSENATIL-GAFILATIL-MU’UMINATI LU’INU FI ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETI WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ADHIMUN
JEWME TESH/HEDU ‘ALEJHIM ‘ELSINETUHUM WE ‘EJDIHIM WE ‘ERXHULUHUM BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
JEWME’IDHIN JUWEFFIHIMU ELLAHU DINEHUMUL-HEKKA WE JA’LEMUNE ‘ENNEL-LAHE HUWEL-HEKKUL-MUBINU
EL-HABITHATU LILHABITHINE WEL-HABITHUNE LILHABITHATI WET-TEJJIBATU LILTTEJJIBINE WET-TEJJIBUNE LILTTEJJIBATI ‘ULA’IKE MUBERRE’UNE MIMMA JEKULUNE LEHUM MEGFIRETUN WE RIZKUN KERIMUN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TEDHULU BUJUTÆN GAJRE BUJUTIKUM HETTA TESTE’NISU WE TUSELLIMU ‘ALA ‘EHLIHA DHALIKUM HAJRUN LEKUM LE’ALLEKUM TEDHEKKERUNE
FE’IN LEM TEXHIDU FIHA ‘EHEDÆN FELA TEDHULUHA HETTA JU’UDHENE LEKUM WE ‘IN KILE LEKUM ERXHI’U FARXHI’U HUWE ‘EZKA LEKUM WEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE ‘ALIMUN
LEJSE ‘ALEJKUM XHUNAHUN ‘EN TEDHULU BUJUTÆN GAJRE MESKUNETIN FIHA META’UN LEKUM WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU MA TUBDUNE WE MA TEKTUMUNE
KUL LILMU’UMININE JEGUDDU MIN ‘EBSARIHIM WE JEHFEDHU FURUXHEHUM DHALIKE ‘EZKA LEHUM ‘INNALL-LLAHE HABIRUN BIMA JESNA’UNE
WE KUL LILMU’UMINATI JEGDUDNE MIN ‘EBSARIHINNE WE JEHFEDHNE FURUXHEHUNNE WE LA JUBDINE ZINETEHUNNE ‘ILLA MA DHEHERE MINHA WE LIEDRIBNE BIHUMURIHINNE ‘ALA XHUJUBIHINNE WE LA JUBDINE ZINETEHUNNE ‘ILLA LIBU’ULETIHINNE ‘EW ‘ABA’IHINNE ‘EW ‘ABA’I BU’ULETIHINNE
WE ‘ENKIHUL-’EJAMA MINKUM WE ES-SALIHINE MIN ‘IBADIKUM WE ‘IMA’IKUM ‘IN JEKUNU FUKARA’E JUGNIHIMU ELLAHU MIN FEDLIHI WEL-LAHU WASI’UN ‘ALIMUN
WE LIESTA’FIFIL-LEDHINE LA JEXHIDUNE NIKAHÆN HETTA JUGNIJEHUMU ELLAHU MIN FEDLIHI WEL-LEDHINE JEBTEGUNEL-KITABE MIMMA MELEKET ‘EJMANUKUM FEKATIBUHUM ‘IN ‘ALIMTUM FIHIM HAJRÆN WE ‘ATUHUM MIN MALI ELLAHIL-LEDHI ‘ATAKUM WE LA TUKRIHU FETEJATIKUM ‘ALEL-BIGA’I
WE LEKAD ‘ENZELNA ‘ILEJKUM ‘AJATIN MUBEJJINATIN WE METHELÆN MINEL-LEDHINE HALEW MIN KABLIKUM WE MEW’IDHETEN LILMUTTEKINE
ELLAHU NURU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI METHELU NURIHI KEMISHKÆTIN FIHA MISBAHUNL-MISBAHU FI ZUXHAXHETIN EZ-ZUXHAXHETU KE’ENNEHA KEWKEBUN DURRIJUN JUKADU MIN SHEXHERETIN MUBAREKETIN ZEJTUNIETIN LA SHERKIJETIN WE LA GARBIJETIN JEKADU ZEJTUHA JUDI’U WE LEW LEM TE
FI BUJUTIN ‘EDHINEL-LAHU ‘EN TURFE’A WE JUDHKERE FIHA ESMUHU JUSEBBIHU LEHU FIHA BIL-GUDUWI WEL-’ASALI
RIXHALUN LA TULHIHIM TIXHARETUN WE LA BEJ’UN ‘AN DHIKRI ELLAHI WE ‘IKAMI ES-SELÆTI WE ‘ITA’I EZ-ZEKÆTI JEHAFUNE JEWMÆN TETEKALLEBU FIHIL-KULUBU WEL-’EBSARU
LIJEXHZIJEHUMU ELLAHU ‘EHSENE MA ‘AMILU WE JEZIDEHUM MIN FEDLIHI WEL-LAHU JERZUKU MEN JESHA’U BIGAJRI HISABIN
WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘A’MALUHUM KESERABIN BIKI’ATIN JEHSEBUHU EDH-DHEM’ANU MA’EN HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’EHU LEM JEXHID/HU SHEJ’ÆN WE WEXHEDEL-LAHE ‘INDEHU FEWEFFAHU HISABEHU WEL-LAHU SERI’UL-HISABI
‘EW KEDHULUMATIN FI BEHRIN LUXHXHIJIN JEGSHAHU MEWXHUN MIN FEWKIHI MEWXHUN MIN FEWKIHI SEHABUN DHULUMATUN BA’DUHA FEWKA BA’DIN ‘IDHA ‘EHREXHE JEDEHU LEM JEKED JERAHA WE MEN LEM JEXH’ALI ELLAHU LEHU NURÆN FEMA LEHU MIN NURIN
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE JUSEBBIHU LEHU MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WET-TEJRU SAFFATIN KULLUN KAD ‘ALIME SELATEHU WE TESBIHEHU WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN BIMA JEF’ALUNE
WE LILLEHI MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE ‘ILA ELLAHIL-MESIRU
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE JUZXHI SEHABÆN THUMME JU’UELLIFU BEJNEHU THUMME JEXH’ALUHU RUKAMÆN FETERAL-WEDKA JEHRUXHU MIN HILALIHI WE JUNEZZILU MINE ES-SEMA’I MIN XHIBALIN FIHA MIN BEREDIN FEJUSIBU BIHI MEN JESHA’U WE JESRIFUHU ‘AN MEN JESHA’U JEKADU SENA BERK
JUKALLIBU ELLAHUL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LA’IBRETEN LI’WLIL-’EBSARI
WEL-LAHU HALEKA KULLE DABBETIN MIN MA’IN FEMINHUM MEN JEMSHI ‘ALA BETNIHI WE MINHUM MEN JEMSHI ‘ALA RIXHLEJNI WE MINHUM MEN JEMSHI ‘ALA ‘ERBA’IN JEHLUKU ELLAHU MA JESHA’U ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
LEKAD ‘ENZELNA ‘AJATIN MUBEJJINATIN WEL-LAHU JEHDI MEN JESHA’U ‘ILA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
WE JEKULUNE ‘AMENNA BILLAHI WE BIR-RESULI WE ‘ETA’NA THUMME JETEWELLA FERIKUN MINHUM MIN BA’DI DHALIKE WE MA ‘ULA’IKE BIL-MU’UMININE
WE ‘IDHA DU’U ‘ILA ELLAHI WE RESULIHI LIJEHKUME BEJNEHUM ‘IDHA FERIKUN MINHUM MU’RIDUNE
WE ‘IN JEKUN LEHUMUL-HEKKU JE’TU ‘ILEJHI MUDH’ININE
‘EFI KULUBIHIM MEREDUN ‘EM ERTABU ‘EM JEHAFUNE ‘EN JEHIFEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHIM WE RESULUHU BEL ‘ULA’IKE HUMU EDH-DHALIMUN
‘INNEMA KANE KAWLEL-MU’UMININE ‘IDHA DU’U ‘ILA ELLAHI WE RESULIHI LIJEHKUME BEJNEHUM ‘EN JEKULU SEMI’NA WE ‘ETA’NA WE ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUFLIHUNE
WE MEN JUTI’I ELLAHE WE RESULEHU WE JEHSHEL-LAHE WE JETTEKHI FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-FA’IZUNE
WE ‘EKSEMU BILLAHI XHEHDE ‘EJMANIHIM LE’IN ‘EMERTEHUM LEJEHRUXHUNNE KUL LA TUKSIMU TA’ATUN MA’RUFETUN ‘INNALL-LLAHE HABIRUN BIMA TA’MELUNE
KUL ‘ETI’U ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’U ER-RESULE FE’IN TEWELLEW FE’INNEMA ‘ALEJHI MA HUMMILE WE ‘ALEJKUM MA HUMMILTUM WE ‘IN TUTI’UHU TEHTEDU WE MA ‘ALA ER-RESULI ‘ILLAL-BELAGUL-MUBINU
WE’ADEL-LAHUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU MINKUM WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LEJESTEHLIFENNEHUM FIL-’ERDI KEMA ESTEHLEFEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM WE LEJUMEKKINENNE LEHUM DINEHUMUL-LEDHI ERTEDA LEHUM WE LEJUBEDDILENNEHUM MIN BA’DI HAWFIHIM ‘EMNÆN JA’BUDUNENI LA JUSHRIKUNE BI SH
WE ‘EKIMU ES-SELÆTE WE ‘ATU EZ-ZEKÆTE WE ‘ETI’U ER-RESULE LE’ALLEKUM TURHEMUNE
LA TEHSEBENNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU MU’XHIZINE FIL-’ERDI WE ME’WAHUMU EN-NARU WE LEBI’SEL-MESIRU
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LIJESTE’DHINKUMUL-LEDHINE MELEKET ‘EJMANUKUM WEL-LEDHINE LEM JEBLUGUL-HULUME MINKUM THELATHE MERRATIN MIN KABLI SELÆTIL-FEXHRI WE HINE TEDA’UNE THIJA BEKUM MINE EDH-DHEHIRETI WE MIN BA’DI SELÆTIL-’ISHA’I THELATHU ‘AWRATIN LEKUM 
WE ‘IDHA BELEGAL-’ETFALU MINKUMUL-HULUME FELJESTE’DHINU KEMA ESTE’DHENEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM KEDHALIKE JUBEJJINU ELLAHU LEKUM ‘AJATIHI WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN HEKIMUN
WEL-KAWA’IDU MINE EN-NISA’L-LATI LA JERXHUNE NIKAHÆN FELEJSE ‘ALEJHINNE XHUNAHUN ‘EN JEDA’NE THIJABEHUNNE GAJRE MUTEBERRIXHATIN BIZINETIN WE ‘EN JESTA’FIFNE HAJRUN LEHUNNE WEL-LAHU SEMI’UN ‘ALIMUN
LEJSE ‘ALEL-’A’MA HEREXHUN WE LA ‘ALEL-’A’REXHI HEREXHUN WE LA ‘ALEL-MERIDI HEREXHUN WE LA ‘ALA ‘ENFUSIKUM ‘EN TE’KULU MIN BUJUTIKUM ‘EW BUJUTI ‘ABA’IKUM ‘EW BUJUTI ‘UMMEHATIKUM ‘EW BUJUTI ‘IHWANIKUM ‘EW BUJUTI ‘EHAWATIKUM ‘EW BUJUTI ‘A’MAMIKUM ‘EW BUJUTI
‘INNEMAL-MU’UMINUNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU BILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE ‘IDHA KANU ME’AHU ‘ALA ‘EMRIN XHAMI’IN LEM JEDH/HEBU HETTA JESTE’DHINUHU ‘INNEL-LEDHINE JESTE’DHINUNEKE ‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE JU’UMINUNE BILLAHI WE RESULIHI FE’IDHA ESTE’DHENUKE LIBA’DI SHE’NIHIM FE’D
LA TEXH’ALU DU’A’E ER-RESULI BEJNEKUM KEDU’A’I BA’DIKUM BA’DÆN KAD JA’LEMU ELLAHUL-LEDHINE JETESELLELUNE MINKUM LIWADHÆN FELJEHDHERIL-LEDHINE JUHALIFUNE ‘AN ‘EMRIHI ‘EN TUSIBEHUM FITNETUN ‘EW JUSIBEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
‘ELA ‘INNE LILLAHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI KAD JA’LEMU MA ‘ENTUM ‘ALEJHI WE JEWME JURXHA’UNE ‘ILEJHI FEJUNEBBI’UHUM BIMA ‘AMILU WEL-LAHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMUN
TEBAREKEL-LEDHI NEZZELEL-FURKANE ‘ALA ‘ABDIHI LIJEKUNE LIL’ALEMINE NEDHIRÆN
EL-LEDHI LEHU MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE LEM JETTEHIDH WELEDÆN WE LEM JEKUN LEHU SHERIKUN FIL-MULKI WE HALEKA KULLE SHEJ’IN FEKADDEREHU TEKDIRÆN
WE ETTEHADHU MIN DUNIHI ‘ALIHETEN LA JEHLUKUNE SHEJ’ÆN WE HUM JUHLEKUNE WE LA JEMLIKUNE LI’NFUSIHIM DERRÆN WE LA NEF’ÆN WE LA JEMLIKUNE MEWTÆN WE LA HEJÆTEN WE LA NUSHURÆN
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA ‘IFKUN EFTERAHU WE ‘A’ANEHU ‘ALEJHI KAWMUN ‘AHARUNE FEKAD XHA’U DHULMÆN WE ZURÆN
WE KALU ‘ESATIRUL-’EWWELINE EKTETEBEHA FEHIJE TUMLA ‘ALEJHI BUKRETEN WE ‘ESILÆN
KUL ‘ENZELEHUL-LEDHI JA’LEMU ES-SIRRE FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘INNEHU KANE GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
WE KALU MALI HADHA ER-RESULI JE’KULUT-TA’AME WE JEMSHI FIL-’ESWAKI LEWLA ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJHI MELEKUN FEJEKUNE ME’AHU NEDHIRÆN
‘EW JULKA ‘ILEJHI KENZUN ‘EW TEKUNU LEHU XHENNETUN JE’KULU MINHA WE KALE EDH-DHALIMUNE ‘IN TETTEBI’UNE ‘ILLA REXHULÆN MESHURÆN
ENDHUR KEJFE DEREBU LEKEL-’EMTHALE FEDELLU FELA JESTETI’UNE SEBILÆN
TEBAREKEL-LEDHI ‘IN SHA’E XHE’ALE LEKE HAJRÆN MIN DHALIKE XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU WE JEXH’AL LEKE KUSURÆN
BEL KEDHDHEBU BIS-SA’ATI WE ‘A’TEDNA LIMEN KEDHDHEBE BIS-SA’ATI SA’IRÆN
‘IDHA RE’ET/HUM MIN MEKANIN BA’IDIN SEMI’U LEHA TEGAJJUDHÆN WE ZEFIRÆN
WE ‘IDHA ‘ULKU MINHA MEKANÆN DEJJIKÆN MUKARRENINE DE’AW HUNALIKE THUBURÆN
LA TED’UL-JEWME THUBURÆN WAHIDÆN WE ED’U THUBURÆN KETHIRÆN
KUL ‘EDHELIKE HAJRUN ‘EM XHENNETUL-HULDI ELLETI WU’IDEL-MUTTEKUNE KANET LEHUM XHEZA’EN WE MESIRÆN
LEHUM FIHA MA JESHA’UNE HALIDINE KANE ‘ALA RABBIKE WA’DÆN MES’ULÆN
WE JEWME JEHSHURUHUM WE MA JA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI FEJEKULU ‘E’ENTUM ‘EDLELTUM ‘IBADI HA’UULA’ ‘EM HUM DELLU ES-SEBILE
KALU SUBHANEKE MA KANE JENBEGI LENA ‘EN NETTEHIDHE MIN DUNIKE MIN ‘EWLIJA’E WE LEKIN METTA’TEHUM WE ‘ABA’EHUM HETTA NESU EDH-DHIKRE WE KANU KAWMÆN BURÆN
FEKAD KEDHDHEBUKUM BIMA TEKULUNE FEMA TESTETI’UNE SERFÆN WE LA NESRÆN WE MEN JEDHLIM MINKUM NUDHIKHU ‘ADHABÆN KEBIRÆN
WE MA ‘ERSELNA KABLEKE MINEL-MURSELINE ‘ILLA ‘INNEHUM LEJE’KULUNET-TA’AME WE JEMSHUNE FIL-’ESWAKI WE XHE’ALNA BA’DEKUM LIBA’DIN FITNETEN ‘ETESBIRUNE WE KANE REBBUKE BESIRÆN
WE KALEL-LEDHINE LA JERXHUNE LIKA’ENA LEWLA ‘UNZILE ‘ALEJNAL-MELA’IKETU ‘EW NERA REBBENA LEKADI ESTEKBERU FI ‘ENFUSIHIM WE ‘ATEW ‘UTUWÆN KEBIRÆN
JEWME JEREWNEL-MELA’IKETE LA BUSHRA JEWME’IDHIN LILMUXHRIMINE WE JEKULUNE HIXHRÆN MEHXHURÆN
WE KADIMNA ‘ILA MA ‘AMILU MIN ‘AMELIN FEXHE’ALNAHU HEBA’EN MENTHURÆN
‘ESHABUL-XHENNETI JEWME’IDHIN HAJRUN MUSTEKARRÆN WE ‘EHSENU MEKILÆN
WE JEWME TESHEKKAKU ES-SEMA’U BIL-GAMAMI WE NUZZILEL-MELA’IKETU TENZILÆN
EL-MULKU JEWME’IDHINL-HEKKU LILRREHMENI WE KANE JEWMÆN ‘ALEL-KAFIRINE ‘ASIRÆN
WE JEWME JE’ADDU EDH-DHALIMU ‘ALA JEDEJHI JEKULU JA LEJTENI ETTEHADHTU ME’A ER-RESULI SEBILÆN
JA WEJLETI LEJTENI LEM ‘ETTEHIDH FULANÆN HALILÆN
LEKAD ‘EDELLENI ‘ANI EDH-DHIKRI BA’DE ‘IDH XHA’ENI WE KANE ESH-SHEJTANU LIL’INSANI HADHULÆN
WE KALE ER-RESULU JA RABBI ‘INNE KAWMI ETTEHADHU HADHAL-KUR’ANE MEHXHURÆN
WE KEDHELIKE XHE’ALNA LIKULLI NEBIJIN ‘ADUWÆN MINEL-MUXHRIMINE WE KEFA BIREBBIKE HADIÆN WE NESIRÆN
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEWLA NUZZILE ‘ALEJHIL-KUR’ANU XHUMLETEN WAHIDETEN KEDHALIKE LINUTHEBBITE BIHI FU’UADEKE WE RETTELNAHU TERTILÆN
WE LA JE’TUNEKE BIMETHELIN ‘ILLA XHI’NAKE BIL-HEKKI WE ‘EHSENE TEFSIRÆN
EL-LEDHINE JUHSHERUNE ‘ALA WUXHUHIHIM ‘ILA XHEHENNEME ‘ULA’IKE SHERRUN MEKANÆN WE ‘EDELLU SEBILÆN
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE WE XHE’ALNA ME’AHU ‘EHAHU HARUNE WEZIRÆN
FEKULNA EDH/HEBA ‘ILAL-KAWMIL-LEDHINE KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATINA FEDEMMERNAHUM TEDMIRÆN
WE KAWME NUHIN LEMMA KEDHDHEBU ER-RUSULE ‘EGREKNAHUM WE XHE’ALNAHUM LILNNASI ‘AJETEN WE ‘A’TEDNA LILDHDHALIMINE ‘ADHABÆN ‘ELIMÆN
WE ‘ADÆN WE THEMUDE WE ‘ESHABE ER-RESSI WE KURUNÆN BEJNE DHALIKE KETHIRÆN
WE KULLÆN DEREBNA LEHUL-’EMTHALE WE KULLÆN TEBBERNA TETBIRÆN
WE LEKAD ‘ETEW ‘ALEL-KARJETI ELLETI ‘UMTIRET METERE ES-SEW’I ‘EFELEM JEKUNU JEREWNEHA BEL KANU LA JERXHUNE NUSHURÆN
WE ‘IDHA R’EWKE ‘IN JETTEHIDHUNEKE ‘ILLA HUZUEN ‘EHEDHAL-LEDHI BE’ATHEL-LAHU RESULÆN
‘IN KADE LEJUDILLUNA ‘AN ‘ALIHETINA LEWLA ‘EN SEBERNA ‘ALEJHA WE SEWFE JA’LEMUNE HINE JEREWNEL-’ADHABE MEN ‘EDELLU SEBILÆN
‘ERE’EJTE MENI ETTEHADHE ‘ILEHEHU HEWAHU ‘EFE’ENTE TEKUNU ‘ALEJHI WE KILÆN
‘EM TEHSEBU ‘ENNE ‘EKTHEREHUM JESMA’UNE ‘EW JA’KILUNE ‘IN HUM ‘ILLA KAL’EN’AM BEL HUM ‘EDELLU SEBILÆN
‘ELEM TERA ‘ILA RABBIKE KEJFE MEDDE EDH-DHILLE WE LEW SHA’E LEXHE’ALEHU SAKINÆN THUMME XHE’ALNA ESH-SHEMSE ‘ALEJHI DELILÆN
THUMME KABEDNAHU ‘ILEJNA KABDÆN JESIRÆN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-LEJLE LIBASÆN WE EN-NEWME SUBATÆN WE XHE’ALE EN-NEHARE NUSHURÆN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI ‘ERSELE ER-RIJAHE BUSHRÆN BEJNE JEDEJ REHMETIHI WE ‘ENZELNA MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN TEHURÆN
LINUHJIJE BIHI BELDETEN MEJTÆN WE NUSKIJEHU MIMMA HALEKNA ‘EN’AMÆN WE ‘ENASIJE KETHIRÆN
WE LEKAD SERREFNAHU BEJNEHUM LIJEDHDHEKKERU FE’EBA ‘EKTHERU EN-NASI ‘ILLA KUFURÆN
WE LEW SHI’NA LEBE’ATHNA FI KULLI KARJETIN NEDHIRÆN
FELA TUTI’IL-KAFIRINE WE XHAHID/HUM BIHI XHIHADÆN KEBIRÆN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI MEREXHEL-BEHREJNI HADHA ‘ADHBUN FURATUN WE HEDHA MILHUN ‘UXHAXHUN WE XHE’ALE BEJNEHUMA BERZEHÆN WE HIXHRÆN MEHXHURÆN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI HALEKA MINEL-MA’I BESHERÆN FEXHE’ALEHU NESEBÆN WE SIHRÆN WE KANE REBBUKE KADIRÆN
WE JA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI MA LA JENFA’UHUM WE LA JEDURRUHUM WE KANEL-KAFIRU ‘ALA RABBIHI DHEHIRÆN
WE MA ‘ERSELNAKE ‘ILLA MUBESHSHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN
KUL MA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN ‘ILLA MEN SHA’E ‘EN JETTEHIDHE ‘ILA RABBIHI SEBILÆN
WE TEWEKKEL ‘ALEL-HEJJIL-LEDHI LA JEMUTU WE SEBBIH BIHEMDIHI WE KEFA BIHI BIDHUNUBI ‘IBADIHI HABIRÆN
EL-LEDHI HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA FI SITTETI ‘EJJAMIN THUMME ESTEWA ‘ALEL-’ARSHI ER-REHMANU FAS’EL BIHI HABIRÆN
WE ‘IDHA KILE LEHUM ESXHUDU LILRREHMENI KALU WE MA ER-REHMANU ‘ENESXHUDU LIMA TE’MURUNA WE ZADEHUM NUFURÆN
TEBAREKEL-LEDHI XHE’ALE FI ES-SEMA’I BURUXHÆN WE XHE’ALE FIHA SIRAXHÆN WE KAMERÆN MUNIRÆN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI XHE’ALEL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE HILFETEN LIMEN ‘ERADE ‘EN JEDHDHEKKERE ‘EW ‘ERADE SHUKURÆN
WE ‘IBADU ER-REHMANIL-LEDHINE JEMSHUNE ‘ALEL-’ERDI HEWNÆN WE ‘IDHA HATEBEHUMUL-XHAHILUNE KALU SELAMÆN
WEL-LEDHINE JEBITUNE LIREBBIHIM SUXHXHEDÆN WE KIJAMÆN
WEL-LEDHINE JEKULUNE REBBENA ESRIF ‘ANNA ‘ADHABE XHEHENNEME ‘INNE ‘ADHABEHA KANE GARAMÆN
‘INNEHA SA’ET MUSTEKARRÆN WE MUKAMÆN
WEL-LEDHINE ‘IDHA ‘ENFEKU LEM JUSRIFU WE LEM JEKTURU WE KANE BEJNE DHALIKE KAWAMÆN
WEL-LEDHINE LA JED’UNE ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE WE LA JEKTULUNE EN-NEFSEL-LETI HERREMEL-LAHU ‘ILLA BIL-HEKKI WE LA JEZNUNE WE MEN JEF’AL DHALIKE JELKA ‘ETHAMÆN
JUDA’AF LEHUL-’ADHABU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI WE JEHLUD FIHI MUHANÆN
‘ILLA MEN TABE WE ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE ‘AMELÆN SALIHÆN FE’ULA’IKE JUBEDDILU ELLAHU SEJJI’ATIHIM HESENATIN WE KANEL-LAHU GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
WE MEN TABE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FE’INNEHU JETUBU ‘ILA ELLAHI METABÆN
WEL-LEDHINE LA JESH/HEDUNE EZ-ZURE WE ‘IDHA MERRU BIL-LEGWI MERRU KIRAMÆN
WEL-LEDHINE ‘IDHA DHUKKIRU BI’AJATI RABBIHIM LEM JEHIRRU ‘ALEJHA SUMMÆN WE ‘UMJANÆN
WEL-LEDHINE JEKULUNE REBBENA HEB LENA MIN ‘EZWAXHINA WE DHURRIJATINA KURRETE ‘A’JUNIN WE EXH’ALNA LILMUTTEKINE ‘IMAMÆN
‘ULA’IKE JUXHZEWNEL-GURFETE BIMA SEBERU WE JULEKKAWNE FIHA TEHIJETEN WE SELAMÆN
HALIDINE FIHA HESUNET MUSTEKARRÆN WE MUKAMÆN
KUL MA JA’BE’U BIKUM RABBI LEWLA DU’A’UUKUM FEKAD KEDHDHEBTUM FESEWFE JEKUNU LIZAMÆN
TA-SIN-MIM
TILKE ‘AJATUL-KITABIL-MUBINI
LE’ALLEKE BAHI’UN NEFSEKE ‘ELLA JEKUNU MU’UMININE
‘IN NESHE’ NUNEZZIL ‘ALEJHIM MINE ES-SEMA’I ‘AJETEN FEDHELLET ‘A’NAKUHUM LEHA HADI’INE
WE MA JE’TIHIM MIN DHIKRIN MINE ER-REHMANI MUHDETHIN ‘ILLA KANU ‘ANHU MU’RIDINE
FEKAD KEDHDHEBU FESEJE’TIHIM ‘ENBA’U MA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ILAL-’ERDI KEM ‘ENBETNA FIHA MIN KULLI ZEWXHIN KERIMIN
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
WE ‘IDH NADA REBBUKE MUSA ‘ENI E’TIL-KAWME EDH-DHALIMINE
KAWME FIR’AWNE ‘ELA JETTEKUNE
KALE RABBI ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘EN JUKEDHDHIBUNI
WE JEDIKU SEDRI WE LA JENTELIKU LISANI FE’ERSIL ‘ILA HARUNE
WE LEHUM ‘ALEJJE DHENBUN FE’EHAFU ‘EN JEKTULUNI
KALE KELLA FADH/HEBA BI’AJATINA ‘INNA ME’AKUM MUSTEMI’UNE
FE’TIJA FIR’AWNE FEKULA ‘INNA RESULU RABBIL-’ALEMINE
‘EN ‘ERSIL ME’ANA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE
KALE ‘ELEM NUREBBIKE FINA WELIDÆN WE LEBITHTE FINA MIN ‘UMURIKE SININE
WE FE’ALTE FA’LETEKEL-LETI FE’ALTE WE ‘ENTE MINEL-KAFIRINE
KALE FE’ALTUHA ‘IDHÆN WE ‘ENA MINE ED-DALLIN
FEFERERTU MINKUM LEMMA HIFTUKUM FEWEHEBE LI RABBI HUKMÆN WE XHE’ALENI MINEL-MURSELINE
WE TILKE NI’METUN TEMUNNUHA ‘ALEJJE ‘EN ‘ABBEDTE BENI ‘ISRA’ILE
KALE FIR’AWNU WE MA REBBUL-’ALEMINE
KALE REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMA ‘IN KUNTUM MUKININE
KALE LIMEN HEWLEHU ‘ELA TESTEMI’UNE
KALE REBBUKUM WE REBBU ‘ABA’IKUMUL-’EWWELINE
KALE ‘INNE RESULEKUMUL-LEDHI ‘URSILE ‘ILEJKUM LEMEXHNUNUN
KALE REBBUL-MESHRIKI WEL-MEGRIBI WE MA BEJNEHUMA ‘IN KUNTUM TA’KILUNE
KALE LE’INI ETTEHADHTE ‘ILEHÆN GAJRI LE’EXH’ALENNEKE MINEL-MESXHUNINE
KALE ‘EWELEW XHI’TUKE BISHEJ’IN MUBININ
KALE FE’TI BIHI ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
FE’ELKA ‘ASAHU FE’IDHA HIJE THU’BANUN MUBINUN
WE NEZE’A JEDEHU FE’IDHA HIJE BEJDA’U LILNNADHIRINE
KALE LILMELE’I HEWLEHU ‘INNE HADHA LESAHIRUN ‘ALIMUN
JURIDU ‘EN JUHRIXHEKUM MIN ‘ERDIKUM BISIHRIHI FEMADHA TE’MURUNE
KALU ‘ERXHIHI WE ‘EHAHU WE EB’ATH FIL-MEDA’INI HASHIRINE
JE’TUKE BIKULLI SEHHARIN ‘ALIMIN
FEXHUMI’A ES-SEHERETU LIMIKATI JEWMIN MA’LUMIN
WE KILE LILNNASI HEL ‘ENTUM MUXHTEMI’UNE
LE’ALLENA NETTEBI’U ES-SEHERETE ‘IN KANU HUMUL-GALIBINE
FELEMMA XHA’E ES-SEHERETU KALU LIFIR’AWNE ‘E’INNE LENA LE’EXHRÆN ‘IN KUNNA NEHNUL-GALIBINE
KALE NE’AM WE ‘INNEKUM ‘IDHÆN LEMINEL-MUKARREBINE
KALE LEHUM MUSA ‘ELKU MA ‘ENTUM MULKUNE
FE’ELKAW HIBALEHUM WE ‘ISIJEHUM WE KALU BI’IZZETI FIR’AWNE ‘INNA LENEHNUL-GALIBUNE
FE’ELKA MUSA ‘ASAHU FE’IDHA HIJE TELKAFU MA JE’FIKUNE
FE’ULKIJE ES-SEHERETU SAXHIDINE
KALU ‘AMENNA BIREBBIL-’ALEMINE
REBBI MUSA WE HARUNE
KALE ‘AMENTUM LEHU KABLE ‘EN ‘ADHENE LEKUM ‘INNEHU LEKEBIRUKUMUL-LEDHI ‘ALLEMEKUMU ES-SIHRE FELESEWFE TA’LEMUNE LE’UKATTI’ANNE ‘EJDIJEKUM WE ‘ERXHULEKUM MIN HILAFIN WE LE’USELLIBENNEKUM ‘EXHMA’INE
KALU LA DEJRE ‘INNA ‘ILA RABBINA MUNKALIBUNE
‘INNA NETMA’U ‘EN JEGFIRE LENA REBBUNA HATAJANA ‘EN KUNNA ‘EWWELEL-MU’UMININE
WE ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILA MUSA ‘EN ‘ESRI BI’IBADI ‘INNEKUM MUTTEBA’UNE
FE’ERSELE FIR’AWNU FIL-MEDA’INI HASHIRINE
‘INNE HA’UULA’ LESHIRDHIMETUN KALILUNE
WE ‘INNEHUM LENA LEGA’IDHUNE
WE ‘INNA LEXHEMI’UN HADHIRUNE
FE’EHREXHNAHUM MIN XHENNATIN WE ‘UJUNIN
WE KUNUZIN WE MEKAMIN KERIMIN
KEDHALIKE WE ‘EWRETHNAHA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE
FE’ETBA’UHUM MUSHRIKINE
FELEMMA TERA’AL-XHEM’ANI KALE ‘ESHABU MUSA ‘INNA LEMUDREKUNE
KALE KELLA ‘INNE MA’IJE RABBI SEJEHDINI
FE’EWHEJNA ‘ILA MUSA ‘ENI EDRIB BI’ASAKEL-BEHRE FANFELEKA FEKANE KULLU FIRKIN KALTTEWDIL-’ADHIMI
WE ‘EZLEFNA THEMMEL-’AHARINE
WE ‘ENXHEJNA MUSA WE MEN ME’AHU ‘EXHMA’INE
THUMME ‘EGREKNAL-’AHARINE
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
WE ETLU ‘ALEJHIM NEBE’E ‘IBRAHIME
‘IDH KALE LI’EBIHI WE KAWMIHI MA TA’BUDUNE
KALU NA’BUDU ‘ESNAMÆN FENEDHELLU LEHA ‘AKIFINE
KALE HEL JESMA’UNEKUM ‘IDH TED’UNE
‘EW JENFA’UNEKUM ‘EW JEDURRUNE
KALU BEL WEXHEDNA ‘ABA’ENA KEDHALIKE JEF’ALUNE
KALE ‘EFERE’EJTUM MA KUNTUM TA’BUDUNE
‘ENTUM WE ‘ABA’UUKUMUL-’EKDEMUNE
FE’INNEHUM ‘ADUWUN LI ‘ILLA REBBEL-’ALEMINE
EL-LEDHI HALEKANI FEHUWE JEHDINI
WEL-LEDHI HUWE JUT’IMUNI WE JESKINI
WE ‘IDHA MERIDTU FEHUWE JESHFINI
WEL-LEDHI JUMITUNI THUMME JUHJINI
WEL-LEDHI ‘ETMA’U ‘EN JEGFIRE LI HATI’ETI JEWME ED-DINI
REBBI HEB LI HUKMÆN WE ‘ELHIKNI BIS-SALIHINE
WE EXH’AL LI LISANE SIDKIN FIL-’AHIRINE
WE EXH’ALNI MIN WERETHETI XHENNETI EN-NA’IMI
WE EGFIR LI’EBI ‘INNEHU KANE MINE ED-DALLINE
WE LA TUHZINI JEWME JUB’ATHUNE
JEWME LA JENFA’U MALUN WE LA BENUNE
‘ILLA MEN ‘ETA ELLAHE BIKALBIN SELIMIN
WE ‘UZLIFETIL-XHENNETU LILMUTTEKINE
WE BURRIZETIL-XHEHIMU LILGAWINE
WE KILE LEHUM ‘EJNE MA KUNTUM TA’BUDUNE
MIN DUNI ELLAHI HEL JENSURUNEKUM ‘EW JENTESIRUNE
FEKUBKIBU FIHA HUM WEL-GAWUNE
WE XHUNUDU ‘IBLISE ‘EXHMA’UNE
KALU WE HUM FIHA JEHTESIMUNE
TE-ELLAHI ‘IN KUNNA LEFI DELALIN MUBININ
‘IDH NUSEWWIKUM BIREBBIL-’ALEMINE
WE MA ‘EDELLENA ‘ILLAL-MUXHRIMUNE
FEMA LENA MIN SHAFI’INE
WE LA SEDIKIN HEMIMIN
FELEW ‘ENNE LENA KERRETEN FENEKUNE MINEL-MU’UMININE
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
KEDHDHEBET KAWMU NUHINL-MURSELINE
‘IDH KALE LEHUM ‘EHUHUM NUHUN ‘ELA TETTEKUNE
‘INNI LEKUM RESULUN ‘EMINUN
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
WE MA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN ‘IN ‘EXHRI ‘ILLA ‘ALA RABBIL-’ALEMINE
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
KALU ‘ENU’UMINU LEKE WE ETTEBE’AKEL-’ERDHELUNE
KALE WE MA ‘ILMI BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
‘IN HISABUHUM ‘ILLA ‘ALA RABBI LEW TESH’URUNE
WE MA ‘ENA BITARIDIL-MU’UMININE
‘IN ‘ENA ‘ILLA NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
KALU LE’IN LEM TENTEHI JA NUHU LETEKUNENNE MINEL-MERXHUMINE
KALE RABBI ‘INNE KAWMI KEDHDHEBUNI
FAFTEH BEJNI WE BEJNEHUM FETHÆN WE NEXHXHINI WE MEN MA’I MINEL-MU’UMININE
FE’ENXHEJNAHU WE MEN ME’AHU FIL-FULKIL-MESHHUNI
THUMME ‘EGREKNA BA’DUL-BAKINE
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
KEDHDHEBET ‘ADUNL-MURSELINE
‘IDH KALE LEHUM ‘EHUHUM HUDUN ‘ELA TETTEKUNE
‘INNI LEKUM RESULUN ‘EMINUN
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
WE MA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN ‘IN ‘EXHRI ‘ILLA ‘ALA RABBIL-’ALEMINE
‘ETEBNUNE BIKULLI RI’IN ‘AJETEN TA’BETHUNE
WE TETTEHIDHUNE MESANI’A LE’ALLEKUM TEHLUDUNE
WE ‘IDHA BETESHTUM BETESHTUM XHEBBARINE
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
WE ETTEKUL-LEDHI ‘EMEDDEKUM BIMA TA’LEMUNE
‘EMEDDEKUM BI’EN’AMIN WE BENINE
WE XHENNATIN WE ‘UJUNIN
‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘ALEJKUM ‘ADHABE JEWMIN ‘ADHIMIN
KALU SEWA’UN ‘ALEJNA ‘EWE’ADHTE ‘EM LEM TEKUN MINEL-WA’IDHINE
‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA HULUKUL-’EWWELINE
WE MA NEHNU BIMU’ADHDHEBINE
FEKEDHDHEBUHU FE’EHLEKNAHUM ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
KEDHDHEBET THEMUDUL-MURSELINE
‘IDH KALE LEHUM ‘EHUHUM SALIHUN ‘ELA TETTEKUNE
‘INNI LEKUM RESULUN ‘EMINUN
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
WE MA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN ‘IN ‘EXHRIJE ‘ILLA ‘ALA RABBIL-’ALEMINE
‘ETUTREKUNE FI MA HAHUNA ‘AMININE
FI XHENNATIN WE ‘UJUNIN
WE ZURU’IN WE NEHLIN TEL’UHA HEDIMUN
WE TENHITUNE MINEL-XHIBALI BUJUTÆN FARIHINE
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
WE LA TUTI’U ‘EMREL-MUSRIFINE
EL-LEDHINE JUFSIDUNE FIL-’ERDI WE LA JUSLIHUNE
KALU ‘INNEMA ‘ENTE MINEL-MUSEHHERINE
MA ‘ENTE ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUNA FE’TI BI’AJETIN ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
KALE HEDHIHI NAKATUN LEHA SHIRBUN WE LEKUM SHIRBU JEWMIN MA’LUMIN
WE LA TEMESSUHA BISU’IN FEJE’HUDHEKUM ‘ADHABU JEWMIN ‘ADHIMIN
FE’AKARUHA FE’ESBEHU NADIMINE
FE’EHADHEHUMUL-’ADHABU ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
KEDHDHEBET KAWMU LUTINL-MURSELINE
‘IDH KALE LEHUM ‘EHUHUM LUTUN ‘ELA TETTEKUNE
‘INNI LEKUM RESULUN ‘EMINUN
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
WE MA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN ‘IN ‘EXHRIJE ‘ILLA ‘ALA RABBIL-’ALEMINE
‘ETE’TUNE EDH-DHUKRANE MINEL-’ALEMINE
WE TEDHERUNE MA HALEKA LEKUM REBBUKUM MIN ‘EZWAXHIKUM BEL ‘ENTUM KAWMUN ‘ADUNE
KALU LE’IN LEM TENTEHI JA LUTU LETEKUNENNE MINEL-MUHREXHINE
KALE ‘INNI LI’AMELIKUM MINEL-KALINE
REBBI NEXHXHINI WE ‘EHLI MIMMA JA’MELUNE
FENEXHXHEJNAHU WE ‘EHLEHU ‘EXHMA’INE
‘ILLA ‘AXHUZÆN FIL-GABIRINE
THUMME DEMMERNAL-’AHARINE
WE ‘EMTERNA ‘ALEJHIM METERÆN FESA’E METERUL-MUNDHERINE
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
KEDHDHEBE ‘ESHABUL-’EJKETIL-MURSELINE
‘IDH KALE LEHUM SHU’AJBUN ‘ELA TETTEKUNE
‘INNI LEKUM RESULUN ‘EMINUN
FATTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
WE MA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN ‘IN ‘EXHRIJE ‘ILLA ‘ALA RABBIL-’ALEMINE
‘EWFUL-KEJLE WE LA TEKUNU MINEL-MUHSIRINE
WE ZINU BIL-KISTASIL-MUSTEKIMI
WE LA TEBHASU EN-NASE ‘ESHJA’EHUM WE LA TA’THEW FIL-’ERDI MUFSIDINE
WE ETTEKUL-LEDHI HALEKAKUM WEL-XHIBILLETEL-’EWWELINE
KALU ‘INNEMA ‘ENTE MINEL-MUSEHHERINE
WE MA ‘ENTE ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUNA WE ‘IN NEDHUNNUKE LEMINEL-KADHIBINE
FE’ESKIT ‘ALEJNA KISEFÆN MINE ES-SEMA’I ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
KALE RABBI ‘A’LEMU BIMA TA’MELUNE
FEKEDHDHEBUHU FE’EHADHEHUM ‘ADHABU JEWMI EDH-DHULLETI ‘INNEHU KANE ‘ADHABE JEWMIN ‘ADHIMIN
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN WE MA KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEHUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
WE ‘INNEHU LETENZILU RABBIL-’ALEMINE
NEZELE BIHI ER-RUHUL-’EMINU
‘ALA KALBIKE LITEKUNE MINEL-MUNDHIRINE
BILISANIN ‘AREBIJIN MUBININ
WE ‘INNEHU LEFI ZUBURIL-’EWWELINE
‘EWELEM JEKUN LEHUM ‘AJETEN ‘EN JA’LEMEHU ‘ULEMA’U BENI ‘ISRA’ILE
WE LEW NEZZELNAHU ‘ALA BA’DIL-’A’XHEMINE
FEKARE’EHU ‘ALEJHIM MA KANU BIHI MU’UMININE
KEDHALIKE SELEKNAHU FI KULUBIL-MUXHRIMINE
LA JU’UMINUNE BIHI HETTA JEREWL-’ADHABEL-’ELIME
FEJE’TIJEHUM BEGTETEN WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
FEJEKULU HEL NEHNU MUNDHERUNE
‘EFEBI’ADHABINA JESTA’XHILUNE
‘EFERE’EJTE ‘IN METTA’NAHUM SININE
THUMME XHA’EHUM MA KANU JU’ADUNE
MA ‘EGNA ‘ANHUM MA KANU JUMETTA’UNE
WE MA ‘EHLEKNA MIN KARJETIN ‘ILLA LEHA MUNDHIRUNE
DHIKRA WE MA KUNNA DHALIMINE
WE MA TENEZZELET BIHI ESH-SHEJATINU
WE MA JENBEGI LEHUM WE MA JESTETI’UNE
‘INNEHUM ‘ANI ES-SEM’I LEMA’ZULUNE
FELA TED’U ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE FETEKUNE MINEL-MU’ADHDHEBINE
WE ‘ENDHIR ‘ASHIRETEKEL-’EKREBINE
WE EHFID XHENAHEKE LIMENI ETTEBE’AKE MINEL-MU’UMININE
FE’IN ‘ASEWKE FEKUL ‘INNI BERI’UN MIMMA TA’MELUNE
WE TEWEKKEL ‘ALEL-’AZIZI ER-REHIMI
EL-LEDHI JERAKE HINE TEKUMU
WE TEKALLUBEKE FI ES-SAXHIDINE
‘INNEHU HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-’ALIMU
HEL ‘UNEBBI’UKUM ‘ALA MEN TENEZZELU ESH-SHEJATINU
TENEZZELU ‘ALA KULLI ‘EFFAKIN ‘ETHIMIN
JULKUNE ES-SEM’A WE ‘EKTHERUHUM KADHIBUNE
WE ESH-SHU’ARA’U JETTEBI’UHUMUL-GAWUNE
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEHUM FI KULLI WADIN JEHIMUNE
WE ‘ENNEHUM JEKULUNE MA LA JEF’ALUNE
‘ILLAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI WE DHEKERU ELLAHE KETHIRÆN WE ENTESERU MIN BA’DI MA DHULIMU WE SEJA’LEMUL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ‘EJJE MUNKALEBIN JENKALIBUNE
TA-SIN TILKE ‘AJATUL-KUR’ANI WE KITABIN MUBININ
HUDEN WE BUSHRA LILMU’UMININE
EL-LEDHINE JUKIMUNE ES-SELÆTE WE JU’UTUNE EZ-ZEKÆTE WE HUM BIL-’AHIRETI HUM JUKINUNE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI ZEJJENNA LEHUM ‘A’MALEHUM FEHUM JA’MEHUNE
‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE LEHUM SU’UL-’ADHABI WE HUM FIL-’AHIRETI HUMUL-’EHSERUNE
WE ‘INNEKE LETULEKKAL-KUR’ANE MIN LEDUN HEKIMIN ‘ALIMIN
‘IDH KALE MUSA LI’HLIHI ‘INNI ‘ANESTU NARÆN SE’ATIKUM MINHA BIHABERIN ‘EW ‘ATIKUM BISHIHABIN KABESIN LE’ALLEKUM TESTELUNE
FELEMMA XHA’EHA NUDIJE ‘EN BURIKE MEN FI EN-NARI WE MEN HEWLEHA WE SUBHANEL-LAHI RABBIL-’ALEMINE
JA MUSA ‘INNEHU ‘ENALLAHUL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
WE ‘ELKI ‘ASAKE FELEMMA RE’AHA TEHTEZZU KE’ENNEHA XHANNUN WELLA MUDBIRÆN WE LEM JU’AKKIB JA MUSA LA TEHAF ‘INNI LA JEHAFU LEDEJJEL-MURSELUNE
‘ILLA MEN DHELEME THUMME BEDDELE HUSNÆN BA’DE SU’IN FE’INNI GAFURUN REHIMUN
WE ‘EDHIL JEDEKE FI XHEJBIKE TEHRUXH BEJDA’E MIN GAJRI SU’IN FI TIS’I ‘AJATIN ‘ILA FIR’AWNE WE KAWMIHI ‘INNEHUM KANU KAWMÆN FASIKINE
FELEMMA XHA’ET/HUM ‘AJATUNA MUBSIRETEN KALU HADHA SIHRUN MUBINUN
WE XHEHEDU BIHA WE ESTEJKANET/HA ‘ENFUSUHUM DHULMÆN WE ‘ULUWÆN FANDHUR KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-MUFSIDINE
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA DAWUDE WE SULEJMANE ‘ILMÆN WE KALAL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI FEDDELENA ‘ALA KETHIRIN MIN ‘IBADIHIL-MU’UMININE
WE WERITHE SULEJMANU DAWUDE WE KALE JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ‘ULLIMNA MENTIKAT-TEJRI WE ‘UTINA MIN KULLI SHEJ’IN ‘INNE HADHA LEHUWEL-FEDLUL-MUBINU
WE HUSHIRE LISULEJMANE XHUNUDUHU MINEL-XHINNI WEL-’INSI WET-TEJRI FEHUM JUZA’UNE
HETTA ‘IDHA ‘ETEW ‘ALA WADI EN-NEMLI KALET NEMLETUN JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEMLU EDHULU MESAKINEKUM LA JEHTIMENNEKUM SULEJMANU WE XHUNUDUHU WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
FETEBESSEME DAHIKÆN MIN KAWLIHA WE KALE RABBI ‘EWZI’NI ‘EN ‘ESHKURE NI’METEKEL-LETI ‘EN’AMTE ‘ALEJJE WE ‘ALA WE E-DEJJE WE ‘EN ‘A’MELE SALIHÆN TERDAHU WE ‘EDHILNI BIREHMETIKE FI ‘IBADIKE ES-SALIHINE
WE TEFEKKADET-TEJRE FEKALE MA LI LA ‘ERAL-HUD/HUDE ‘EM KANE MINEL-GA’IBINE
LE’U’ADHDHIBENNEHU ‘ADHABÆN SHEDIDÆN ‘EW LE’EDHBEHENNEHU ‘EW LEJE’TIJENI BISULTANIN MUBININ
FEMEKETHE GAJRE BA’IDIN FEKALE ‘EHETTU BIMA LEM TUHIT BIHI WE XHI’TUKE MIN SEBE’IIN BINEBE’IIN JEKININ
‘INNI WE XHEDTTU EMRE’ETEN TEMLIKUHUM WE ‘UTIJET MIN KULLI SHEJ’IN WE LEHA ‘ARSHUN ‘ADHIMUN
WE XHEDTUHA WE KAWMEHA JESXHUDUNE LILSHSHEMSI MIN DUNI ELLAHI WE ZEJJENE LEHUMU ESH-SHEJTANU ‘A’MALEHUM FESEDDEHUM ‘ANI ES-SEBILI FEHUM LA JEHTEDUNE
‘ELLA JESXHUDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI JUHRIXHUL-HAB’E FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE JA’LEMU MA TUHFUNE WE MA TU’LINUNE
ELLAHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE REBBUL-’ARSHIL-’ADHIMI
KALE SENENDHURU ‘ESEDEKTE ‘EM KUNTE MINEL-KADHIBINE
EDH/HEB BIKITABI HADHA FE’ELKIH ‘ILEJHIM THUMME TEWELLE ‘ANHUM FANDHUR MADHA JERXHI’UNE
KALET JA ‘EJJUHAL-MELE’U ‘INNI ‘ULKIJE ‘ILEJJE KITABUN KERIMUN
‘INNEHU MIN SULEJMANE WE ‘INNEHU BISMI ELLAHI ER-REHMANI ER-REHIMI
‘ELLA TA’LU ‘ALEJJE WE ‘TUNI MUSLIMINE
KALET JA ‘EJJUHAL-MELE’U ‘EFTUNI FI ‘EMRI MA KUNTU KATI’ATEN ‘EMRÆN HETTA TESH/HEDUNI
KALU NEHNU ‘ULU KUWETIN WE ‘ULU BE’SIN SHEDIDIN WEL-’EMRU ‘ILEJKI FANDHURI MADHA TE’MURINE
KALET ‘INNEL-MULUKE ‘IDHA DEHALU KARJETEN ‘EFSEDUHA WE XHE’ALU ‘A’IZZETE ‘EHLIHA ‘EDHILLETEN WE KEDHELIKE JEF’ALUNE
WE ‘INNI MURSILETUN ‘ILEJHIM BIHEDIJETIN FENADHIRETUN BIME JERXHI’UL-MURSELUNE
FELEMMA XHA’E SULEJMANE KALE ‘ETUMIDDUNENI BIMALIN FEMA ‘ATANIJEL-LAHU HAJRUN MIMMA ‘ATAKUM BEL ‘ENTUM BIHEDIJETIKUM TEFREHUNE
ERXHI’ ‘ILEJHIM FELENE’TIJENNEHUM BIXHUNUDIN LA KIBELE LEHUM BIHA WE LENUHRIXHENNEHUM MINHA ‘EDHILLETEN WE HUM SAGIRUNE
KALE JA ‘EJJUHAL-MELE’U ‘EJJUKUM JE’TINI BI’ARSHIHA KABLE ‘EN JE’TUNI MUSLIMINE
KALE ‘IFRJTUN MINEL-XHINNI ‘ENA ‘ATIKE BIHI KABLE ‘EN TEKUME MIN MEKAMIKE WE ‘INNI ‘ALEJHI LEKAWIJUN ‘EMINUN
KALEL-LEDHI ‘INDEHU ‘ILMUN MINEL-KITABI ‘ENA ‘ATIKE BIHI KABLE ‘EN JERTEDDE ‘ILEJKE TERFUKE FELEMMA RE’AHU MUSTEKIRRÆN ‘INDEHU KALE HADHA MIN FEDLI RABBI LIJEBLUWENI ‘E’ESHKURU ‘EM ‘EKFURU WE MEN SHEKERE FE’INNEMA JESHKURU LINEFSIHI WE MEN KEFERE FE’INNE 
KALE NEKKIRU LEHA ‘ARSHEHA NENDHUR ‘ETEHTEDI ‘EM TEKUNU MINEL-LEDHINE LA JEHTEDUNE
FELEMMA XHA’ET KILE ‘EHEKEDHA ‘ARSHUKI KALET KE’ENNEHU HUWE WE ‘UTINAL-’ILME MIN KABLIHA WE KUNNA MUSLIMINE
WE SEDDEHA MA KANET TA’BUDU MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘INNEHA KANET MIN KAWMIN KAFIRINE
KILE LEHA EDHULI ES-SERHE FELEMMA RE’ET/HU HESIBET/HU LUXHXHETEN WE KESHEFET ‘AN SAKAJHA KALE ‘INNEHU SERHUN MUMERREDUN MIN KAWARIRE KALET RABBI ‘INNI DHELEMTU NEFSI WE ‘ESLEMTU ME’A SULEJMANE LILLAHI RABBIL-’ALEMINE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA ‘ILA THEMUDE ‘EHAHUM SALIHÆN ‘ENI A’BUDU ELLAHE FE’IDHA HUM FERIKANI JEHTESIMUNE
KALE JA KAWMI LIME TESTA’XHILUNE BIS-SEJJI’ETI KABLEL-HESENETI LEWLA TESTEGFIRUNEL-LAHE LE’ALLEKUM TURHEMUNE
KALU ETTEJJERNA BIKE WE BIMEN ME’AKE KALE TA’IRUKUM ‘INDEL-LAHI BEL ‘ENTUM KAWMUN TUFTENUNE
WE KANE FIL-MEDINETI TIS’ATU REHTIN JUFSIDUNE FIL-’ERDI WE LA JUSLIHUNE
KALU TEKASEMU BILLAHI LENUBEJJITENNEHU WE ‘EHLEHU THUMME LENEKULENNE LIWELIJIHI MA SHEHIDNA MEHLIKE ‘EHLIHI WE ‘INNA LESADIKUNE
WE MEKERU MEKRÆN WE MEKERNA MEKRÆN WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
FANDHUR KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETU MEKRIHIM ‘ENNA DEMMERNAHUM WE KAWMEHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
FETILKE BUJUTUHUM HAWIJETEN BIMA DHELEMU ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKAWMIN JA’LEMUNE
WE ‘ENXHEJNAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE KANU JETTEKUNE
WE LUTÆN ‘IDH KALE LIKAWMIHI ‘ETE’TUNEL-FAHISHETE WE ‘ENTUM TUBSIRUNE
‘E’INNEKUM LETE’TUNE ER-RIXHALE SHEHWETEN MIN DUNI EN-NISA’ BEL ‘ENTUM KAWMUN TEXHHELUNE
FEMA KANE XHEWABE KAWMIHI ‘ILLA ‘EN KALU ‘EHRIXHU ‘ALE LUTIN MIN KARJETIKUM ‘INNEHUM ‘UNASUN JETETEHHERUNE
FE’ENXHEJNAHU WE ‘EHLEHU ‘ILLA EMRE’ETEHU KADDERNAHA MINEL-GABIRINE
WE ‘EMTERNA ‘ALEJHIM METERÆN FESA’E METERUL-MUNDHERINE
KULIL-HEMDU LILLAHI WE SELAMUN ‘ALA ‘IBADIHIL-LEDHINE ESTEFA ‘AALLLEHU HAJRUN ‘EMMA JUSHRIKUNE
‘EMMEN HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE ‘ENZELE LEKUM MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’ENBETNA BIHI HEDA’IKA DHATE BEHXHETIN MA KANE LEKUM ‘EN TUNBITU SHEXHEREHA ‘E’ILEHUN ME’A ELLAHI BEL HUM KAWMUN JA’DILUNE
