‘EMMEN XHE’ALEL-’ERDE KARARÆN WE XHE’ALE HILALEHA ‘ENHARÆN WE XHE’ALE LEHA REWASIJE WE XHE’ALE BEJNEL-BEHREJNI HAXHIZÆN ‘E’ILEHUN ME’A ELLAHI BEL ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
‘EMMEN JUXHIBUL-MUDTERRE ‘IDHA DA’AHU WE JEKSHIFU ES-SU’E WE JEXH’ALUKUM HULEFA’EL-’ERDI ‘E’ILEHUN ME’A ELLAHI KALILÆN MA TEDHEKKERUNE
‘EMMEN JEHDIKUM FI DHULUMATIL-BERRI WEL-BEHRI WE MEN JURSILU ER-RIJAHE BUSHRÆN BEJNE JEDEJ REHMETIHI ‘E’ILEHUN ME’A ELLAHI TA’ALALLAHU ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
‘EMMEN JEBDE’UL-HALKA THUMME JU’IDUHU WE MEN JERZUKUKUM MINE ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI ‘E’ILEHUN ME’A ELLAHI KUL HATU BURHANEKUM ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
KUL LA JA’LEMU MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDIL-GAJBE ‘ILLALLAHU WE MA JESH’URUNE ‘EJJANE JUB’ATHUNE
BEL EDDAREKE ‘ILMUHUM FIL-’AHIRETI BEL HUM FI SHEKKIN MINHA BEL HUM MINHA ‘AMUNE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘E’IDHA KUNNA TURABÆN WE ‘ABA’UUNA ‘E’INNA LEMUHREXHUNE
LEKAD WU’IDNA HADHA NEHNU WE ‘ABA’UUNA MIN KABLU ‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA ‘ESATIRUL-’EWWELINE
KUL SIRU FIL-’ERDI FANDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-MUXHRIMINE
WE LA TEHZEN ‘ALEJHIM WE LA TEKUN FI DEJKIN MIMMA JEMKURUNE
WE JEKULUNE META HADHAL-WA’DU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
KUL ‘ASA ‘EN JEKUNE REDIFE LEKUM BA’DUL-LEDHI TESTA’XHILUNE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEDHU FEDLIN ‘ALA EN-NASI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHEREHUM LA JESHKURUNE
WE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEJA’LEMU MA TUKINNU SUDURUHUM WE MA JU’LINUNE
WE MA MIN GA’IBETIN FI ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI ‘ILLA FI KITABIN MUBININ
‘INNE HADHAL-KUR’ANE JEKUSSU ‘ALA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE ‘EKTHEREL-LEDHI HUM FIHI JEHTELIFUNE
WE ‘INNEHU LEHUDEN WE REHMETUN LILMU’UMININE
‘INNE REBBEKE JEKDI BEJNEHUM BIHUKMIHI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-’ALIMU
FETEWEKKEL ‘ALA ELLAHI ‘INNEKE ‘ALEL-HEKKIL-MUBINI
‘INNEKE LA TUSMI’UL-MEWTA WE LA TUSMI’U ES-SUMME ED-DU’A’E ‘IDHA WE LLEW MUDBIRINE
WE MA ‘ENTE BIHADIL-’UMJI ‘AN DELALETIHIM ‘IN TUSMI’U ‘ILLA MEN JU’UMINU BI’AJATINA FEHUM MUSLIMUNE
WE ‘IDHA WEKA’AL-KAWLU ‘ALEJHIM ‘EHREXHNA LEHUM DABBETEN MINEL-’ERDI TUKELLIMUHUM ‘ENNE EN-NASE KANU BI’AJATINA LA JUKINUNE
WE JEWME NEHSHURU MIN KULLI ‘UMMETIN FEWXHÆN MIMMEN JUKEDHDHIBU BI’AJATINA FEHUM JUZA’UNE
HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’U KALE ‘EKEDHDHEBTUM BI’AJATI WE LEM TUHITU BIHA ‘ILMÆN ‘EMMADHA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
WE WEKA’AL-KAWLU ‘ALEJHIM BIMA DHELEMU FEHUM LA JENTIKUNE
‘ELEM JEREW ‘ENNA XHE’ALNAL-LEJLE LIJESKUNU FIHI WE EN-NEHARE MUBSIRÆN ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
WE JEWME JUNFEHU FI ES-SURI FEFEZI’A MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MEN FIL-’ERDI ‘ILLA MEN SHA’EL-LAHU WE KULLUN ‘ETEWHU DAHIRINE
WE TERAL-XHIBALE TEHSEBUHA XHAMIDETEN WE HIJE TEMURRU MERRE ES-SEHABI SUN’A ELLAHIL-LEDHI ‘ETKANE KULLE SHEJ’IN ‘INNEHU HABIRUN BIMA TEF’ALUNE
MEN XHA’E BIL-HESENETI FELEHU HAJRUN MINHA WE HUM MIN FEZA’IN JEWME’IDHIN ‘AMINUNE
WE MEN XHA’E BIS-SEJJI’ETI FEKUBBET WUXHUHUHUM FI EN-NARI HEL TUXHZEWNE ‘ILLA MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
‘INNEMA ‘UMIRTU ‘EN ‘A’BUDE REBBE HEDHIHIL-BELDETIL-LEDHI HERREMEHA WE LEHU KULLU SHEJ’IN WE ‘UMIRTU ‘EN ‘EKUNE MINEL-MUSLIMINE
WE ‘EN ‘ETLUWEL-KUR’ANE FEMENI EHTEDA FE’INNEMA JEHTEDI LINEFSIHI WE MEN DELLE FEKUL ‘INNEMA ‘ENA MINEL-MUNDHIRINE
WE KULIL-HEMDU LILLAHI SEJURIKUM ‘AJATIHI FETA’RIFUNEHA WE MA REBBUKE BIGAFILIN ‘AMMA TA’MELUNE
TA-SIN-MIM
TILKE ‘AJATUL-KITABIL-MUBINI
NETLU ‘ALEJKE MIN NEBE’I MUSA WE FIR’AWNE BIL-HEKKI LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
‘INNE FIR’AWNE ‘ALA FIL-’ERDI WE XHE’ALE ‘EHLEHA SHIJA’ÆN JESTED’IFU TA’IFETEN MINHUM JUDHEBBIHU ‘EBNA’EHUM WE JESTEHJI NISA’EHUM ‘INNEHU KANE MINEL-MUFSIDINE
WE NURIDU ‘EN NEMUNNE ‘ALEL-LEDHINE ESTUD’IFU FIL-’ERDI WE NEXH’ALEHUM ‘E’IMMETEN WE NEXH’ALEHUMUL-WARITHINE
WE NUMEKKINE LEHUM FIL-’ERDI WE NURIJE FIR’AWNE WE HAMANE WE XHUNUDEHUMA MINHUM MA KANU JEHDHERUNE
WE ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILA ‘UMMI MUSA ‘EN ‘ERDI’IHI FE’IDHA HIFTI ‘ALEJHI FE’ELKIHI FIL-JEMMI WE LA TEHAFI WE LA TEHZENI ‘INNA RADDUHU ‘ILEJKI WE XHA’ILUHU MINEL-MURSELINE
FALTEKATEHU ‘ALU FIR’AWNE LIJEKUNE LEHUM ‘ADUWÆN WE HEZENÆN ‘INNE FIR’AWNE WE HAMANE WE XHUNUDEHUMA KANU HATI’INE
WE KALET EMRE’ETU FIR’AWNE KURRETU ‘AJNIN LI WE LEKE LA TEKTULUHU ‘ASA ‘EN JENFE’ANA ‘EW NETTEHIDHEHU WELEDÆN WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
WE ‘ESBEHE FU’UADU ‘UMMI MUSA FARIGÆN ‘IN KADET LETUBDI BIHI LEWLA ‘EN REBETNA ‘ALA KALBIHA LITEKUNE MINEL-MU’UMININE
WE KALET LI’HTIHI KUSSIHI FEBESURET BIHI ‘AN XHUNUBIN WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
WE HERREMNA ‘ALEJHIL-MERADI’A MIN KABLU FEKALET HEL ‘EDULLUKUM ‘ALA ‘EHLI BEJTIN JEKFULUNEHU LEKUM WE HUM LEHU NASIHUNE
FEREDEDNAHU ‘ILA ‘UMMIHI KEJ TEKARRE ‘AJNUHA WE LA TEHZENE WE LITA’LEME ‘ENNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHEREHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
WE LEMMA BELEGA ‘ESHUDDEHU WE ESTEWA ‘ATEJNAHU HUKMÆN WE ‘ILMÆN WE KEDHELIKE NEXHZIL-MUHSININE
WE DEHALEL-MEDINETE ‘ALA HINI GAFLETIN MIN ‘EHLIHA FEWEXHEDE FIHA REXHULEJNI JEKTETILANI HADHA MIN SHI’ATIHI WE HEDHA MIN ‘ADUWIHI FASTEGATHEHUL-LEDHI MIN SHI’ATIHI ‘ALEL-LEDHI MIN ‘ADUWIHI FEWEKEZEHU MUSA FEKADA ‘ALEJHI KALE HADHA MIN ‘AMELI ESH-SHEJTANI
KALE RABBI ‘INNI DHELEMTU NEFSI FAGFIR LI FEGAFERE LEHU ‘INNEHU HUWEL-GAFURU ER-REHIMU
KALE RABBI BIMA ‘EN’AMTE ‘ALEJJE FELEN ‘EKUNE DHEHIRÆN LILMUXHRIMINE
FE’ESBEHE FIL-MEDINETI HA’IFÆN JETEREKKABU FE’IDHAL-LEDHI ESTENSEREHU BIL-’EMSI JESTESRIHUHU KALE LEHU MUSA ‘INNEKE LEGAWIJUN MUBINUN
FELEMMA ‘EN ‘ERADE ‘EN JEBTISHE BIEL-LEDHI HUWE ‘ADUWUN LEHUMA KALE JA MUSA ‘ETURIDU ‘EN TEKTULENI KEMA KATELTE NEFSÆN BIL-’EMSI ‘IN TURIDU ‘ILLA ‘EN TEKUNE XHEBBARÆN FIL-’ERDI WE MA TURIDU ‘EN TEKUNE MINEL-MUSLIHINE
WE XHA’E REXHULUN MIN ‘EKSAL-MEDINETI JES’A KALE JA MUSA ‘INNEL-MELE’E JE’TEMIRUNE BIKE LIJEKTULUKE FAHRUXH ‘INNI LEKE MINE EN-NASIHINE
FEHAREXHE MINHA HA’IFÆN JETEREKKABU KALE RABBI NEXHXHINI MINEL-KAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
WE LEMMA TEWEXHXHEHE TILKA’E MEDJENE KALE ‘ASA RABBI ‘EN JEHDIJENI SEWA’E ES-SEBIL
WE LEMMA WEREDE MA’E MEDJENE WEXHEDE ‘ALEJHI ‘UMMETEN MINE EN-NASI JESKUNE WE WEXHEDE MIN DUNIHIMU EMRE’TEJNI TEDHUDANI KALE MA HATBUKUMA KALETA LA NESKI HETTA JUSDIRE ER-RI’A’U WE ‘EBUNA SHEJHUN KEBIRUN
FESEKA LEHUMA THUMME TEWELLA ‘ILA EDH-DHILLI FEKALE RABBI ‘INNI LIMA ‘ENZELTE ‘ILEJJE MIN HAJRIN FEKIRUN
FEXHA’ET/HU ‘IHDAHUMA TEMSHI ‘ALA ESTIHJA’IN KALET ‘INNE ‘EBI JED’UKE LIJEXHZIJEKE ‘EXHRE MA SEKAJTE LENA FELEMMA XHA’EHU WE KASSE ‘ALEJHIL-KASESE KALE LA TEHAF NEXHEWTE MINEL-KAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
KALET ‘IHDAHUMA JA ‘EBETI ESTE’XHIRHU ‘INNE HAJRE MENI ESTE’XHERTEL-KAWIJUL-’EMINU
KALE ‘INNI ‘URIDU ‘EN ‘UNKIHEKE ‘IHDA EBNETEJJE HATEJNI ‘ALA ‘EN TE’XHURENI THEMANIJETE HIXHEXHIN FE’IN ‘ETMEMTE ‘ASHRÆN FEMIN ‘INDIKE WE MA ‘URIDU ‘EN ‘ESHUKKA ‘ALEJKE SETEXHIDUNI ‘IN SHA’EL-LAHU MINE ES-SALIHINE
KALE DHALIKE BEJNI WE BEJNEKE ‘EJJEMAL-’EXHELEJNI KADEJTU FELA ‘UDWANE ‘ALEJJE WEL-LAHU ‘ALA MA NEKULU WE KILUN
FELEMMA KADA MUSAL-’EXHELE WE SARE BI’EHLIHI ‘ANESE MIN XHANIBIT-TURI NARÆN KALE LI’HLIHI EMKUTHU ‘INNI ‘ANESTU NARÆN LE’ALLI ‘ATIKUM MINHA BIHABERIN ‘EW XHEDHWETIN MINE EN-NARI LE’ALLEKUM TESTELUNE
FELEMMA ‘ETAHA NUDI MIN SHATI’IL-WADIL-’EJMENI FIL-BUK’ATIL-MUBAREKETI MINE ESH-SHEXHERETI ‘EN JA MUSA ‘INNI ‘ENALLAHU REBBUL-’ALEMINE
WE ‘EN ‘ELKI ‘ASAKE FELEMMA RE’AHA TEHTEZZU KE’ENNEHA XHANNUN WELLA MUDBIRÆN WE LEM JU’AKKIB JA MUSA ‘EKBIL WE LA TEHAF ‘INNEKE MINEL-’AMININE
ESLUK JEDEKE FI XHEJBIKE TEHRUXH BEJDA’E MIN GAJRI SU’IN WE EDMUM ‘ILEJKE XHENAHEKE MINE ER-REHBI FEDHANIKE BURHANANI MIN RABBIKE ‘ILA FIR’AWNE WE MELE’IHI ‘INNEHUM KANU KAWMÆN FASIKINE
KALE RABBI ‘INNI KATELTU MINHUM NEFSÆN FE’EHAFU ‘EN JEKTULUNI
WE ‘EHI HARUNU HUWE ‘EFSEHU MINNI LISANÆN FE’ERSILHU MA’IJE RID’ÆN JUSEDDIKUNI ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘EN JUKEDHDHIBUNI
KALE SENESHUDDU ‘ADUDEKE BI’EHIKE WE NEXH’ALU LEKUMA SULTANÆN FELA JESILUNE ‘ILEJKUMA BI’AJATINA ‘ENTUMA WE MENI ETTEBE’AKUMAL-GALIBUNE
FELEMMA XHA’EHUM MUSA BI’AJATINA BEJJINATIN KALU MA HADHA ‘ILLA SIHRUN MUFTEREN WE MA SEMI’NA BIHEDHA FI ‘ABA’INAL-’EWWELINE
WE KALE MUSA RABBI ‘A’LEMU BIMEN XHA’E BIL-HUDA MIN ‘INDIHI WE MEN TEKUNU LEHU ‘AKIBETU ED-DARI ‘INNEHU LA JUFLIHU EDH-DHALIMUNE
WE KALE FIR’AWNU JA ‘EJJUHAL-MELE’U MA ‘ALIMTU LEKUM MIN ‘ILEHIN GAJRI FE’EWKID LI JA HAMANU ‘ALAT-TINI FAXH’AL LI SERHÆN LE’ALLI ‘ETTELI’U ‘ILA ‘ILEHI MUSA WE ‘INNI LE’EDHUNNUHU MINEL-KADHIBINE
WE ESTEKBERE HUWE WE XHUNUDUHU FIL-’ERDI BIGAJRIL-HEKKI WE DHENNU ‘ENNEHUM ‘ILEJNA LA JURXHA’UNE
FE’EHADHNAHU WE XHUNUDEHU FENEBEDHNAHUM FIL-JEMMI FANDHUR KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETU EDH-DHALIMINE
WE XHE’ALNAHUM ‘E’IMMETEN JED’UNE ‘ILA EN-NARI WE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI LA JUNSERUNE
WE ‘ETBA’NAHUM FI HEDHIHI ED-DUNJA LA’NETEN WE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI HUM MINEL-MEKBUHINE
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE MIN BA’DI MA ‘EHLEKNAL-KURUNEL-’ULA BESA’IRE LILNNASI WE HUDEN WE REHMETEN LE’ALLEHUM JETEDHEKKERUNE
WE MA KUNTE BIXHANIBIL-GARBIJI ‘IDH KADEJNA ‘ILA MUSAL-’EMRE WE MA KUNTE MINE ESH-SHAHIDIN
WE LEKINNA ‘ENSHE’NA KURUNÆN FETETAWELE ‘ALEJHIMUL-’UMURU WE MA KUNTE THAWIÆN FI ‘EHLI MEDJENE TETLU ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATINA WE LEKINNA KUNNA MURSILINE
WE MA KUNTE BIXHANIBIT-TURI ‘IDH NADEJNA WE LEKIN REHMETEN MIN RABBIKE LITUNDHIRE KAWMÆN MA ‘ETAHUM MIN NEDHIRIN MIN KABLIKE LE’ALLEHUM JETEDHEKKERUNE
WE LEWLA ‘EN TUSIBEHUM MUSIBETUN BIMA KADDEMET ‘EJDIHIM FEJEKULU REBBENA LEWLA ‘ERSELTE ‘ILEJNA RESULÆN FENETTEBI’A ‘AJATIKE WE NEKUNE MINEL-MU’UMININE
FELEMMA XHA’EHUMUL-HEKKU MIN ‘INDINA KALU LEWLA ‘UTIJE MITHLE MA ‘UTIJE MUSA ‘EWELEM JEKFURU BIMA ‘UTIJE MUSA MIN KABLU KALU SIHRANI TEDHAHERA WE KALU ‘INNA BIKULLIN KAFIRUNE
KUL FE’TU BIKITABIN MIN ‘INDI ELLAHI HUWE ‘EHDA MINHUMA ‘ETTEBI’HU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
FE’IN LEM JESTEXHIBU LEKE FA’LEM ‘ENNEMA JETTEBI’UNE ‘EHWA’EHUM WE MEN ‘EDELLU MIMMENI ETTEBE’A HEWAHU BIGAJRI HUDEN MINEL-LAHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JEHDIL-KAWME EDH-DHALIMINE
WE LEKAD WESSELNA LEHUMUL-KAWLE LE’ALLEHUM JETEDHEKKERUNE
EL-LEDHINE ‘ATEJNAHUMUL-KITABE MIN KABLIHI HUM BIHI JU’UMINUNE
WE ‘IDHA JUTLA ‘ALEJHIM KALU ‘AMENNA BIHI ‘INNEHUL-HEKKU MIN RABBINA ‘INNA KUNNA MIN KABLIHI MUSLIMINE
‘ULA’IKE JU’UTEWNE ‘EXHREHUM MERRETEJNI BIMA SEBERU WE JEDRE’UNE BIL-HESENETI ES-SEJJI’ETE WE MIMMA REZEKNAHUM JUNFIKUNE
WE ‘IDHA SEMI’UL-LEGWE ‘A’REDU ‘ANHU WE KALU LENA ‘A’MALUNA WE LEKUM ‘A’MALUKUM SELAMUN ‘ALEJKUM LA NEBTEGIL-XHAHILINE
‘INNEKE LA TEHDI MEN ‘EHBEBTE WE LEKINNALL-LLAHE JEHDI MEN JESHA’U WE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIL-MUHTEDINE
WE KALU ‘IN NETTEBI’IL-HUDA ME’AKE NUTEHATTEF MIN ‘ERDINA ‘EWELEM NUMEKKIN LEHUM HEREMÆN ‘AMINÆN JUXHBA ‘ILEJHI THEMERATU KULLI SHEJ’IN RIZKÆN MIN LEDUNNA WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHEREHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
WE KEM ‘EHLEKNA MIN KARJETIN BETIRET MA’ISHETEHA FETILKE MESAKINUHUM LEM TUSKEN MIN BA’DIHIM ‘ILLA KALILÆN WE KUNNA NEHNUL-WARITHINE
WE MA KANE REBBUKE MUHLIKEL-KURA HETTA JEB’ATHE FI ‘UMMIHA RESULÆN JETLU ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATINA WE MA KUNNA MUHLIKIL-KURA ‘ILLA WE ‘EHLUHA DHALIMUNE
WE MA ‘UTITUM MIN SHEJ’IN FEMETA’UL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE ZINETUHA WE MA ‘INDEL-LAHI HAJRUN WE ‘EBKA ‘EFELA TA’KILUNE
‘EFEMEN WE’ADNAHU WA’DÆN HESENÆN FEHUWE LAKIHI KEMEN METTA’NAHU META’AL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA THUMME HUWE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI MINEL-MUHDERINE
WE JEWME JUNADIHIM FEJEKULU ‘EJNE SHUREKA’IJEL-LEDHINE KUNTUM TEZ’UMUNE
KALEL-LEDHINE HEKKA ‘ALEJHIMUL-KAWLU REBBENA HA’UULA’L-LEDHINE ‘EGWEJNA ‘EGWEJNAHUM KEMA GAWEJNA TEBERRE’NA ‘ILEJKE MA KANU ‘IJANA JA’BUDUNE
WE KILE ED’U SHUREKA’EKUM FEDE’AWHUM FELEM JESTEXHIBU LEHUM WE RE’EWL-’ADHABE LEW ‘ENNEHUM KANU JEHTEDUNE
WE JEWME JUNADIHIM FEJEKULU MADHA ‘EXHEBTUMUL-MURSELINE
FE’AMIJET ‘ALEJHIMUL-’ENBA’U JEWME’IDHIN FEHUM LA JETESA’ELUNE
FE’EMMA MEN TABE WE ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FE’ASA ‘EN JEKUNE MINEL-MUFLIHINE
WE REBBUKE JEHLUKU MA JESHA’U WE JEHTARU MA KANE LEHUMUL-HIJERETU SUBHANEL-LAHI WE TA’ALA ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
WE REBBUKE JA’LEMU MA TUKINNU SUDURUHUM WE MA JU’LINUNE
WE HUWEL-LAHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE LEHUL-HEMDU FIL-’ULA WEL-’AHIRETI WE LEHUL-HUKMU WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN XHE’ALEL-LAHU ‘ALEJKUMUL-LEJLE SERMEDÆN ‘ILA JEWMIL-KIJAMETI MEN ‘ILEHUN GAJRU ELLAHI JE’TIKUM BIDIJA’IN ‘EFELA TESMA’UNE
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN XHE’ALEL-LAHU ‘ALEJKUMU EN-NEHARE SERMEDÆN ‘ILA JEWMIL-KIJAMETI MEN ‘ILEHUN GAJRU ELLAHI JE’TIKUM BILEJLIN TESKUNUNE FIHI ‘EFELA TUBSIRUNE
WE MIN REHMETIHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE LITESKUNU FIHI WE LITEBTEGU MIN FEDLIHI WE LE’ALLEKUM TESHKURUNE
WE JEWME JUNADIHIM FEJEKULU ‘EJNE SHUREKA’IJEL-LEDHINE KUNTUM TEZ’UMUNE
WE NEZA’NA MIN KULLI ‘UMMETIN SHEHIDÆN FEKULNA HATU BURHANEKUM FE’ALIMU ‘ENNEL-HEKKA LILLAHI WE DELLE ‘ANHUM MA KANU JEFTERUNE
‘INNE KARUNE KANE MIN KAWMI MUSA FEBEGA ‘ALEJHIM WE ‘ATEJNAHU MINEL-KUNUZI MA ‘INNE MEFATIHEHU LETENU’U BIL-’USBETI ‘ULIL-KUWETI ‘IDH KALE LEHU KAWMUHU LA TEFREH ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JUHIBBUL-FERIHINE
WE EBTEGI FIMA ‘ATAKEL-LAHU ED-DAREL-’AHIRETE WE LA TENSE NESIBEKE MINE ED-DUNJA WE ‘EHSIN KEMA ‘EHSENEL-LAHU ‘ILEJKE WE LA TEBGIL-FESADE FIL-’ERDI ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JUHIBBUL-MUFSIDINE
KALE ‘INNEMA ‘UTITUHU ‘ALA ‘ILMIN ‘INDI ‘EWELEM JA’LEM ‘ENNEL-LAHE KAD ‘EHLEKE MIN KABLIHI MINEL-KURUNI MEN HUWE ‘ESHEDDU MINHU KUWETEN WE ‘EKTHERU XHEM’ÆN WE LA JUS’ELU ‘AN DHUNUBIHIMUL-MUXHRIMUNE
FEHAREXHE ‘ALA KAWMIHI FI ZINETIHI KALEL-LEDHINE JURIDUNEL-HEJÆTE ED-DUNJA JALEJTE LENA MITHLE MA ‘UTIJE KARUNU ‘INNEHU LEDHU HEDHDHIN ‘ADHIMIN
WE KALEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME WEJLEKUM THEWABU ELLAHI HAJRUN LIMEN ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN WE LA JULEKKAHA ‘ILLA ES-SABIRUNE
FEHASEFNA BIHI WE BIDARIHIL-’ERDE FEMA KANE LEHU MIN FI’ETIN JENSURUNEHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI WE MA KANE MINEL-MUNTESIRINE
WE ‘ESBEHEL-LEDHINE TEMENNEW MEKANEHU BIL-’EMSI JEKULUNE WEJKE’ENNEL-LAHE JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U MIN ‘IBADIHI WE JEKDIRU LEWLA ‘EN MENNEL-LAHU ‘ALEJNA LEHASEFE BINA WEJKE’ENNEHU LA JUFLIHUL-KAFIRUNE
TILKE ED-DARUL-’AHIRETU NEXH’ALUHA LILLEDHINE LA JURIDUNE ‘ULUWÆN FIL-’ERDI WE LA FESADÆN WEL-’AKIBETU LILMUTTEKINE
MEN XHA’E BIL-HESENETI FELEHU HAJRUN MINHA WE MEN XHA’E BIS-SEJJI’ETI FELA JUXHZAL-LEDHINE ‘AMILU ES-SEJJI’ATI ‘ILLA MA KANU JA’MELUNE
‘INNEL-LEDHI FEREDE ‘ALEJKEL-KUR’ANE LERADDUKE ‘ILA MA’ADIN KUL RABBI ‘A’LEMU MEN XHA’E BIL-HUDA WE MEN HUWE FI DELALIN MUBININ
WE MA KUNTE TERXHU ‘EN JULKA ‘ILEJKEL-KITABU ‘ILLA REHMETEN MIN RABBIKE FELA TEKUNENNE DHEHIRÆN LILKAFIRINE
WE LA JESUDDUNNEKE ‘AN ‘AJATI ELLAHI BA’DE ‘IDH ‘UNZILET ‘ILEJKE WE ED’U ‘ILA RABBIKE WE LA TEKUNENNE MINEL-MUSHRIKINE
WE LA TED’U ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE KULLU SHEJ’IN HALIKUN ‘ILLA WEXHHEHU LEHUL-HUKMU WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
‘ELIF-LAM-MIM
‘EHESIBE EN-NASU ‘EN JUTREKU ‘EN JEKULU ‘AMENNA WE HUM LA JUFTENUNE
WE LEKAD FETENNAL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM FELEJA’LEMENNEL-LAHUL-LEDHINE SEDEKU WE LEJA’LEMENNEL-KADHIBINE
‘EM HESIBEL-LEDHINE JA’MELUNE ES-SEJJI’ATI ‘EN JESBIKUNA SA’E MA JEHKUMUNE
MEN KANE JERXHU LIKA’EL-LAHI FE’INNE ‘EXHELEL-LAHI LE’ATIN WE HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-’ALIMU
WE MEN XHAHEDE FE’INNEMA JUXHAHIDU LINEFSIHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEGANIJUN ‘ANIL-’ALEMINE
WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LENUKEFFIRENNE ‘ANHUM SEJJI’ATIHIM WE LENEXHZIJENNEHUM ‘EHSENEL-LEDHI KANU JA’MELUNE
WE WESSEJNAL-’INSANE BIWALIDEJHI HUSNÆN WE ‘IN XHAHEDAKE LITUSHRIKE BI MA LEJSE LEKE BIHI ‘ILMUN FELA TUTI’HUMA ‘ILEJJE MERXHI’UKUM FE’UNEBBI’UKUM BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LENUDHILENNEHUM FI ES-SALIHINE
WE MINE EN-NASI MEN JEKULU ‘AMENNA BILLAHI FE’IDHA ‘UDHIJE FI ELLAHI XHE’ALE FITNETE EN-NASI KE’ADHABI ELLAHI WE LE’IN XHA’E NESRUN MIN RABBIKE LEJEKULUNNE ‘INNA KUNNA ME’AKUM ‘EWELEJSEL-LAHU BI’A’LEME BIMA FI SUDURIL-’ALEMINE
WE LEJA’LEMENNEL-LAHUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE LEJA’LEMENNEL-MUNAFIKINE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU ETTEBI’U SEBILENA WE LNEHMIL HATAJAKUM WE MA HUM BIHAMILINE MIN HATAJAHUM MIN SHEJ’IN ‘INNEHUM LEKADHIBUNE
WE LEJEHMILUNNE ‘ETHKALEHUM WE ‘ETHKALÆN ME’A ‘ETHKALIHIM WE LEJUS’ELUNNE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘AMMA KANU JEFTERUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA NUHÆN ‘ILA KAWMIHI FELEBITHE FIHIM ‘ELFE SENETIN ‘ILLA HAMSINE ‘AMÆN FE’EHADHEHUMUT-TUFANU WE HUM DHALIMUN
FE’ENXHEJNAHU WE ‘ESHABE ES-SEFINETI WE XHE’ALNAHA ‘AJETEN LIL’ALEMINE
WE ‘IBRAHIME ‘IDH KALE LIKAWMIHI A’BUDU ELLAHE WE ETTEKUHU DHALIKUM HAJRUN LEKUM ‘IN KUNTUM TA’LEMUNE
‘INNEMA TA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘EWTHANÆN WE TEHLUKUNE ‘IFKÆN ‘INNEL-LEDHINE TA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI LA JEMLIKUNE LEKUM RIZKÆN FABTEGU ‘INDEL-LAHI ER-RIZKA WE A’BUDUHU WE ESHKURU LEHU ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
WE ‘IN TUKEDHDHIBU FEKAD KEDHDHEBE ‘UMEMUN MIN KABLIKUM WE MA ‘ALA ER-RESULI ‘ILLAL-BELAGUL-MUBINU
‘EWELEM JEREW KEJFE JUBDI’U ELLAHUL-HALKA THUMME JU’IDUHU ‘INNE DHALIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI JESIRUN
KUL SIRU FIL-’ERDI FANDHURU KEJFE BEDE’EL-HALKA THUMMEL-LAHU JUNSHI’U EN-NESH’ETEL-’AHIRETE ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
JU’ADHDHIBU MEN JESHA’U WE JERHEMU MEN JESHA’U WE ‘ILEJHI TUKLEBUNE
WE MA ‘ENTUM BIMU’XHIZINE FIL-’ERDI WE LA FI ES-SEMA’I WE MA LEKUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI MIN WE LIJIN WE LA NESIRIN
WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BI’AJATI ELLAHI WE LIKA’IHI ‘ULA’IKE JE’ISU MIN REHMETI WE ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
FEMA KANE XHEWABE KAWMIHI ‘ILLA ‘EN KALU EKTULUHU ‘EW HERRIKUHU FE’ENXHAHU ELLAHU MINE EN-NARI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
WE KALE ‘INNEMA ETTEHADHTUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘EWTHANÆN MEWEDDETE BEJNIKUM FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA THUMME JEWMEL-KIJAMETI JEKFURU BA’DUKUM BIBA’DIN WE JEL’ANU BA’DUKUM BA’DÆN WE ME’WAKUMU EN-NARU WE MA LEKUM MIN NASIRINE
FE’AMENE LEHU LUTUN WE KALE ‘INNI MUHAXHIRUN ‘ILA RABBI ‘INNEHU HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
WE WEHEBNA LEHU ‘ISHAKA WE JA’KUBE WE XHE’ALNA FI DHURRIJETIHI EN-NUBUWETE WEL-KITABE WE ‘ATEJNAHU ‘EXHREHU FI ED-DUNJA WE ‘INNEHU FIL-’AHIRETI LEMINE ES-SALIHIN
WE LUTÆN ‘IDH KALE LIKAWMIHI ‘INNEKUM LETE’TUNEL-FAHISHETE MA SEBEKAKUM BIHA MIN ‘EHEDIN MINEL-’ALEMINE
‘E’INNEKUM LETE’TUNE ER-RIXHALE WE TEKTA’UNE ES-SEBILE WE TE’TUNE FI NADIKUMUL-MUNKERE FEMA KANE XHEWABE KAWMIHI ‘ILLA ‘EN KALU E’TINA BI’ADHABI ELLAHI ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
KALE RABBI ENSURNI ‘ALEL-KAWMIL-MUFSIDINE
WE LEMMA XHA’ET RUSULUNA ‘IBRAHIME BIL-BUSHRA KALU ‘INNA MUHLIKU ‘EHLI HEDHIHIL-KARJETI ‘INNE ‘EHLEHA KANU DHALIMINE
KALE ‘INNE FIHA LUTÆN KALU NEHNU ‘A’LEMU BIMEN FIHA LENUNEXHXHIJENNEHU WE ‘EHLEHU ‘ILLA EMRE’ETEHU KANET MINEL-GABIRIN
WE LEMMA ‘EN XHA’ET RUSULUNA LUTÆN SI’E BIHIM WE DAKA BIHIM DHER’ÆN WE KALU LA TEHAF WE LA TEHZEN ‘INNA MUNEXHXHUKE WE ‘EHLEKE ‘ILLA EMRE’ETEKE KANET MINEL-GABIRINE
‘INNA MUNZILUNE ‘ALA ‘EHLI HEDHIHIL-KARJETI RIXHZÆN MINE ES-SEMA’I BIMA KANU JEFSUKUNE
WE LEKAD TEREKNA MINHA ‘AJETEN BEJJINETEN LIKAWMIN JA’KILUNE
WE ‘ILA MEDJENE ‘EHAHUM SHU’AJBÆN FEKALE JA KAWMI A’BUDU ELLAHE WE ERXHUL-JEWMEL-’AHIRE WE LA TA’THEW FIL-’ERDI MUFSIDIN
FEKEDHDHEBUHU FE’EHADHET/HUMU ER-REXHFETU FE’ESBEHU FI DARIHIM XHATHIMINE
WE ‘ADÆN WE THEMUDE WE KAD TEBEJJENE LEKUM MIN MESAKINIHIM WE ZEJJENE LEHUMU ESH-SHEJTANU ‘A’MALEHUM FESEDDEHUM ‘ANI ES-SEBILI WE KANU MUSTEBSIRINE
WE KARUNE WE FIR’AWNE WE HAMANE WE LEKAD XHA’EHUM MUSA BIL-BEJJINATI FASTEKBERU FIL-’ERDI WE MA KANU SABIKINE
FEKULLÆN ‘EHADHNA BIDHENBIHI FEMINHUM MEN ‘ERSELNA ‘ALEJHI HASIBÆN WE MINHUM MEN ‘EHADHET/HU ES-SEJHETU WE MINHUM MEN HASEFNA BIHIL-’ERDE WE MINHUM MEN ‘EGREKNA WE MA KANEL-LAHU LIJEDHLIMEHUM WE LEKIN KANU ‘ENFUSEHUM JEDHLIMUNE
METHELUL-LEDHINE ETTEHADHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘EWLIJA’E KEMETHELIL-’ANKEBUTI ETTEHADHET BEJTÆN WE ‘INNE ‘EWHENEL-BUJUTI LEBEJTUL-’ANKEBUTI LEW KANU JA’LEMUNE
‘INNALL-LLAHE JA’LEMU MA JED’UNE MIN DUNIHI MIN SHEJ’IN WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
WE TILKEL-’EMTHALU NEDRIBUHA LILNNASI WE MA JA’KILUHA ‘ILLAL-’ALIMUNE
HALEKAL-LAHU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BIL-HEKKI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LILMU’UMININE
ETLU MA ‘UHIJE ‘ILEJKE MINEL-KITABI WE ‘EKIMU ES-SELÆTE ‘INNE ES-SELÆTE TENHA ‘ANIL-FEHSHA’I WEL-MUNKERI WE LEDHIKRU ELLAHI ‘EKBERU WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU MA TESNA’UNE
WE LA TUXHADILU ‘EHLEL-KITABI ‘ILLA BI-ETI HIJE ‘EHSENU ‘ILLAL-LEDHINE DHELEMU MINHUM WE KULU ‘AMENNA BIEL-LEDHI ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJNA WE ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJKUM WE ‘ILEHUNA WE ‘ILEHUKUM WAHIDUN WE NEHNU LEHU MUSLIMUNE
WE KEDHELIKE ‘ENZELNA ‘ILEJKEL-KITABE FE-EL-LEDHINE ‘ATEJNAHUMUL-KITABE JU’UMINUNE BIHI WE MIN HA’UULA’ MEN JU’UMINU BIHI WE MA JEXHHEDU BI’AJATINA ‘ILLAL-KAFIRUNE
WE MA KUNTE TETLU MIN KABLIHI MIN KITABIN WE LA TEHUTTUHU BIJEMINIKE ‘IDHÆN LARTABEL-MUBTILUNE
BEL HUWE ‘AJATUN BEJJINATUN FI SUDURIL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME WE MA JEXHHEDU BI’AJATINA ‘ILLA EDH-DHALIMUNE
WE KALU LEWLA ‘UNZILE ‘ALEJHI ‘AJATUN MIN RABBIHI KUL ‘INNEMAL-’AJATU ‘INDEL-LAHI WE ‘INNEMA ‘ENA NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
‘EWELEM JEKFIHIM ‘ENNA ‘ENZELNA ‘ALEJKEL-KITABE JUTLA ‘ALEJHIM ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LEREHMETEN WE DHIKRA LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
KUL KEFA BILLAHI BEJNI WE BEJNEKUM SHEHIDÆN JA’LEMU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU BIL-BATILI WE KEFERU BILLAHI ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-HASIRUNE
WE JESTA’XHILUNEKE BIL-’ADHABI WE LEWLA ‘EXHELUN MUSEMMEN LEXHA’EHUMUL-’ADHABU WE LEJE’TIJENNEHUM BEGTETEN WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
JESTA’XHILUNEKE BIL-’ADHABI WE ‘INNE XHEHENNEME LEMUHITETUN BIL-KAFIRINE
JEWME JEGSHAHUMUL-’ADHABU MIN FEWKIHIM WE MIN TEHTI ‘ERXHULIHIM WE JEKULU DHUKU MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
JA ‘IBADIJEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘INNE ‘ERDI WASI’ATUN FE’IJAJE FA’BUDUNI
KULLU NEFSIN DHA’IKATUL-MEWTI THUMME ‘ILEJNA TURXHA’UNE
WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LENUBEWWI’ENNEHUM MINEL-XHENNETI GUREFÆN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA NI’ME ‘EXHRUL-’AMILINE
EL-LEDHINE SEBERU WE ‘ALA RABBIHIM JETEWEKKELUNE
WE KE’EJJIN MIN DABBETIN LA TEHMILU RIZKAHALLAHU JERZUKUHA WE ‘IJAKUM WE HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-’ALIMU
WE LE’IN SE’ELTEHUM MEN HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE SEHHARE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE LEJEKULUNNEL-LAHU FE’ENNA JU’UFEKUNE
ELLAHU JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U MIN ‘IBADIHI WE JEKDIRU LEHU ‘INNALL-LLAHE BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMUN
WE LE’IN SE’ELTEHUM MEN NEZZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’EHJA BIHIL-’ERDE MIN BA’DI MEWTIHA LEJEKULUNNEL-LAHU KULIL-HEMDU LILLAHI BEL ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’KILUNE
WE MA HEDHIHIL-HEJÆTU ED-DUNJA ‘ILLA LEHWUN WE LA’IBUN WE ‘INNE ED-DAREL-’AHIRETE LEHIJEL-HEJEWANU LEW KANU JA’LEMUNE
FE’IDHA REKIBU FIL-FULKI DE’AW ELLAHE MUHLISINE LEHU ED-DINE FELEMMA NEXHXHAHUM ‘ILAL-BERRI ‘IDHA HUM JUSHRIKUNE
LIJEKFURU BIMA ‘ATEJNAHUM WE LIJETEMETTA’U FESEWFE JA’LEMUNE
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNA XHE’ALNA HEREMÆN ‘AMINÆN WE JUTEHATTEFU EN-NASU MIN HEWLIHIM ‘EFEBIALBATILI JU’UMINUNE WE BINI’METI ELLAHI JEKFURUNE
WE MEN ‘EDHLEMU MIMMENI EFTERA ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN ‘EW KEDHDHEBE BIL-HEKKI LEMMA XHA’EHU ‘ELEJSE FI XHEHENNEME METHWEN LILKAFIRINE
WEL-LEDHINE XHAHEDU FINA LENEHDIJENNEHUM SUBULENA WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEME’AL-MUHSININE
‘ELIF-LAM-MIM
GULIBETI ER-RUMU
FI ‘EDNAL-’ERDI WE HUM MIN BA’DI GALEBIHIM SEJEGLIBUNE
FI BID’I SININE LILLAHIL-’EMRU MIN KABLU WE MIN BA’DU WE JEWME’IDHIN JEFREHUL-MU’UMINUNE
BINESRI ELLAHI JENSURU MEN JESHA’U WE HUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
WA’DEL-LAHI LA JUHLIFU ELLAHU WA’DEHU WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
JA’LEMUNE DHAHIRÆN MINEL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE HUM ‘ANIL-’AHIRETI HUM GAFILUNE
‘EWELEM JETEFEKKERU FI ‘ENFUSIHIM MA HALEKAL-LAHU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA ‘ILLA BIL-HEKKI WE ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN WE ‘INNE KETHIRÆN MINE EN-NASI BILIKA’I RABBIHIM LEKAFIRUNE
‘EWELEM JESIRU FIL-’ERDI FEJENDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM KANU ‘ESHEDDE MINHUM KUWETEN WE ‘ETHARUL-’ERDE WE ‘AMERUHA ‘EKTHERE MIMMA ‘AMERUHA WE XHA’ET/HUM RUSULUHUM BIL-BEJJINATI FEMA KANEL-LAHU LIJEDHLIMEHUM WE LEKIN KANU ‘ENFUSEHUM J
THUMME KANE ‘AKIBETEL-LEDHINE ‘ESA’U ES-SU’A ‘EN KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATI ELLAHI WE KANU BIHA JESTEHZI’UN
ELLAHU JEBDE’UL-HALKA THUMME JU’IDUHU THUMME ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
WE JEWME TEKUMU ES-SA’ATU JUBLISUL-MUXHRIMUNE
WE LEM JEKUN LEHUM MIN SHUREKA’IHIM SHUFA’A’U WE KANU BISHUREKA’IHIM KAFIRINE
WE JEWME TEKUMU ES-SA’ATU JEWME’IDHIN JETEFERREKUNE
FE’EMMAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI FEHUM FI REWDETIN JUHBERUNE
WE ‘EMMAL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATINA WE LIKA’IL-’AHIRETI FE’ULA’IKE FIL-’ADHABI MUHDERUNE
FESUBHANEL-LAHI HINE TUMSUNE WE HINE TUSBIHUNE
WE LEHUL-HEMDU FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE ‘ASHIJÆN WE HINE TUDHHIRUNE
JUHRIXHUL-HEJJE MINEL-MEJJITI WE JUHRIXHUL-MEJJITE MINEL-HEJJI WE JUHJIL-’ERDE BA’DE MEWTIHA WE KEDHELIKE TUHREXHUNE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI ‘EN HALEKAKUM MIN TURABIN THUMME ‘IDHA ‘ENTUM BESHERUN TENTESHIRUNE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI ‘EN HALEKA LEKUM MIN ‘ENFUSIKUM ‘EZWAXHÆN LITESKUNU ‘ILEJHA WE XHE’ALE BEJNEKUM MEWEDDETEN WE REHMETEN ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JETEFEKKERUNE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI HALKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE EHTILAFU ‘ELSINETIKUM WE ‘ELWANIKUM ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIL’ALIMINE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI MENAMUKUM BIL-LEJLI WE EN-NEHARI WE EBTIGA’UUKUM MIN FEDLIHI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JESMA’UNE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI JURIKUMUL-BERKA HAWFÆN WE TEMA’ÆN WE JUNEZZILU MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FEJUHJI BIHIL-’ERDE BA’DE MEWTIHA ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JA’KILUNE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI ‘EN TEKUME ES-SEMA’U WEL-’ERDU BI’EMRIHI THUMME ‘IDHA DA’AKUM DA’WETEN MINEL-’ERDI ‘IDHA ‘ENTUM TEHRUXHUNE
WE LEHU MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI KULLUN LEHU KANITUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI JEBDE’UL-HALKA THUMME JU’IDUHU WE HUWE ‘EHWENU ‘ALEJHI WE LEHUL-METHELUL-’A’LA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
DEREBE LEKUM METHELÆN MIN ‘ENFUSIKUM HEL LEKUM MIN MA MELEKET ‘EJMANUKUM MIN SHUREKA’E FI MA REZEKNAKUM FE’ENTUM FIHI SEWA’UN TEHAFUNEHUM KEHIFETIKUM ‘ENFUSEKUM KEDHALIKE NUFESSILUL-’AJATI LIKAWMIN JA’KILUNE
BEL ETTEBE’AL-LEDHINE DHELEMU ‘EHWA’EHUM BIGAJRI ‘ILMIN FEMEN JEHDI MEN ‘EDELLEL-LAHU WE MA LEHUM MIN NASIRINE
FE’EKIM WEXHHEKE LILDDINI HENIFÆN FITRETEL-LAHI ELLETI FETERE EN-NASE ‘ALEJHA LA TEBDILE LIHALKI ELLAHI DHALIKE ED-DINUL-KAJJIMU WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
MUNIBINE ‘ILEJHI WE ETTEKUHU WE ‘EKIMU ES-SELÆTE WE LA TEKUNU MINEL-MUSHRIKINE
MINEL-LEDHINE FERREKU DINEHUM WE KANU SHIJA’ÆN KULLU HIZBIN BIMA LEDEJHIM FERIHUNE
WE ‘IDHA MESSE EN-NASE DURRUN DE’AW REBBEHUM MUNIBINE ‘ILEJHI THUMME ‘IDHA ‘EDHAKAHUM MINHU REHMETEN ‘IDHA FERIKUN MINHUM BIREBBIHIM JUSHRIKUNE
LIJEKFURU BIMA ‘ATEJNAHUM FETEMETTA’U FESEWFE TA’LEMUNE
‘EM ‘ENZELNA ‘ALEJHIM SULTANÆN FEHUWE JETEKELLEMU BIMA KANU BIHI JUSHRIKUNE
WE ‘IDHA ‘EDHEKNA EN-NASE REHMETEN FERIHU BIHA WE ‘IN TUSIBHUM SEJJI’ETUN BIMA KADDEMET ‘EJDIHIM ‘IDHA HUM JEKNETUNE
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNEL-LAHE JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U WE JEKDIRU ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
FE’ATI DHAL-KURBA HEKKAHU WEL-MISKINE WE EBNE ES-SEBILI DHALIKE HAJRUN LILLEDHINE JURIDUNE WEXHHEL-LAHI WE ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUFLIHUNE
WE MA ‘ATEJTUM MIN RIBÆN LIJERBUWA FI ‘EMWALI EN-NASI FELA JERBU ‘INDEL-LAHI WE MA ‘ATEJTUM MIN ZEKÆTIN TURIDUNE WEXHHEL-LAHI FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUD’IFUNE
ELLAHUL-LEDHI HALEKAKUM THUMME REZEKAKUM THUMME JUMITUKUM THUMME JUHJIKUM HEL MIN SHUREKA’IKUM MEN JEF’ALU MIN DHALIKUM MIN SHEJ’IN SUBHANEHU WE TA’ALA ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
DHEHEREL-FESADU FIL-BERRI WEL-BEHRI BIMA KESEBET ‘EJDI EN-NASI LIJUDHIKAHUM BA’DEL-LEDHI ‘AMILU LE’ALLEHUM JERXHI’UNE
KUL SIRU FIL-’ERDI FANDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-LEDHINE MIN KABLU KANE ‘EKTHERUHUM MUSHRIKINE
FE’EKIM WEXHHEKE LILDDINIL-KAJJIMI MIN KABLI ‘EN JE’TIJE JEWMUN LA MEREDDE LEHU MINEL-LAHI JEWME’IDHIN JESSEDDA’UNE
MEN KEFERE FE’ALEJHI KUFRUHU WE MEN ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FELI’ENFUSIHIM JEMHEDUNE
LIJEXHZIJEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI MIN FEDLIHI ‘INNEHU LA JUHIBBUL-KAFIRINE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI ‘EN JURSILE ER-RIJAHE MUBESHSHIRATIN WE LIJUDHIKAKUM MIN REHMETIHI WE LITEXHRIJEL-FULKU BI’EMRIHI WE LITEBTEGU MIN FEDLIHI WE LE’ALLEKUM TESHKURUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE RUSULÆN ‘ILA KAWMIHIM FEXHA’UHUM BIL-BEJJINATI FANTEKAMNA MINEL-LEDHINE ‘EXHREMU WE KANE HEKKÆN ‘ALEJNA NESRUL-MU’UMININE
ELLAHUL-LEDHI JURSILU ER-RIJAHE FETUTHIRU SEHABÆN FEJEBSUTUHU FI ES-SEMA’I KEJFE JESHA’U WE JEXH’ALUHU KISEFÆN FETERAL-WEDKA JEHRUXHU MIN HILALIHI FE’IDHA ‘ESABE BIHI MEN JESHA’U MIN ‘IBADIHI ‘IDHA HUM JESTEBSHIRUNE
WE ‘IN KANU MIN KABLI ‘EN JUNEZZELE ‘ALEJHIM MIN KABLIHI LEMUBLISINE
FANDHUR ‘ILA ‘ATHARI REHMETI ELLAHI KEJFE JUHJIL-’ERDE BA’DE MEWTIHA ‘INNE DHALIKE LEMUHJIL-MEWTA WE HUWE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
WE LE’IN ‘ERSELNA RIHÆN FERE’EWHU MUSFERRÆN LEDHELLU MIN BA’DIHI JEKFURUNE
FE’INNEKE LA TUSMI’UL-MEWTA WE LA TUSMI’U ES-SUMME ED-DU’A’E ‘IDHA WE LLEW MUDBIRINE
WE MA ‘ENTE BIHADIL-’UMJI ‘AN DELALETIHIM ‘IN TUSMI’U ‘ILLA MEN JU’UMINU BI’AJATINA FEHUM MUSLIMUN
ELLAHUL-LEDHI HALEKAKUM MIN DA’FIN THUMME XHE’ALE MIN BA’DI DA’FIN KUWETEN THUMME XHE’ALE MIN BA’DI KUWETIN DA’FÆN WE SHEJBETEN JEHLUKU MA JESHA’U WE HUWEL-’ALIMUL-KADIRU
WE JEWME TEKUMU ES-SA’ATU JUKSIMUL-MUXHRIMUNE MA LEBITHU GAJRE SA’ATIN KEDHALIKE KANU JU’UFEKUNE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME WEL-’IMANE LEKAD LEBITHTUM FI KITABI ELLAHI ‘ILA JEWMIL-BA’THI FEHEDHA JEWMUL-BA’THI WE LEKINNEKUM KUNTUM LA TA’LEMUNE
FEJEWME’IDHIN LA JENFA’UL-LEDHINE DHELEMU MA’DHIRETUHUM WE LA HUM JUSTA’TEBUNE
WE LEKAD DEREBNA LILNNASI FI HADHAL-KUR’ANI MIN KULLI METHELIN WE LE’IN XHI’TEHUM BI’AJETIN LEJEKULENNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘IN ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA MUBTILUNE
KEDHALIKE JETBA’U ELLAHU ‘ALA KULUBIL-LEDHINE LA JA’LEMUNE
FASBIR ‘INNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN WE LA JESTEHIFFENNEKEL-LEDHINE LA JUKINUNE
‘ELIF-LAM-MIM
TILKE ‘AJATUL-KITABIL-HEKIMI
HUDEN WE REHMETEN LILMUHSININE
EL-LEDHINE JUKIMUNE ES-SELÆTE WE JU’UTUNE EZ-ZEKÆTE WE HUM BIL-’AHIRETI HUM JUKINUNE
‘ULA’IKE ‘ALA HUDEN MIN RABBIHIM WE ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUFLIHUNE
WE MINE EN-NASI MEN JESHTERI LEHWEL-HEDITHI LIJUDILLE ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI BIGAJRI ‘ILMIN WE JETTEHIDHEHA HUZUEN ‘ULE’IKE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN MUHINUN
WE ‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHI ‘AJATUNA WELLA MUSTEKBIRÆN KE’EN LEM JESMA’HA KE’ENNE FI ‘UDHUNEJHI WEKRÆN FEBESHSHIRHU BI’ADHABIN ‘ELIMIN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LEHUM XHENNATU EN-NA’IMI
HALIDINE FIHA WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKÆN WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI BIGAJRI ‘AMEDIN TEREWNEHA WE ‘ELKA FIL-’ERDI REWASIJE ‘EN TEMIDE BIKUM WE BETHTHE FIHA MIN KULLI DABBETIN WE ‘ENZELNA MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’ENBETNA FIHA MIN KULLI ZEWXHIN KERIMIN
HADHA HALKU ELLAHI FE’ERUNI MADHA HALEKAL-LEDHINE MIN DUNIHI BELI EDH-DHALIMUNE FI DELALIN MUBININ
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA LUKMANEL-HIKMETE ‘ENI ESHKUR LILLAHI WE MEN JESHKUR FE’INNEMA JESHKURU LINEFSIHI WE MEN KEFERE FE’INNALL-LLAHE GANIJUN HEMIDUN
WE ‘IDH KALE LUKMANU LIABNIHI WE HUWE JA’IDHUHU JA BUNEJJE LA TUSHRIK BILLAHI ‘INNE ESH-SHIRKE LEDHULMUN ‘ADHIMUN
WE WESSEJNAL-’INSANE BIWALIDEJHI HEMELET/HU ‘UMMUHU WEHNÆN ‘ALA WEHNIN WE FISALUHU FI ‘AMEJNI ‘ENI ESHKUR LI WE LIWALIDEJKE ‘ILEJJEL-MESIRU
WE ‘IN XHAHEDAKE ‘ALA ‘EN TUSHRIKE BI MA LEJSE LEKE BIHI ‘ILMUN FELA TUTI’HUMA WE SAHIBHUMA FI ED-DUNJA MA’RUFÆN WE ETTEBI’ SEBILE MEN ‘ENABE ‘ILEJJE THUMME ‘ILEJJE MERXHI’UKUM FE’UNEBBI’UKUM BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
JA BUNEJJE ‘INNEHA ‘IN TEKUN MITHKALE HEBBETIN MIN HARDELIN FETEKUN FI SEHRETIN ‘EW FI ES-SEMAWATI ‘EW FIL-’ERDI JE’TI BIHALLAHU ‘INNALL-LLAHE LETIFUN HABIRUN
JA BUNEJJE ‘EKIMI ES-SELÆTE WE ‘MUR BIL-MA’RUFI WE ENHE ‘ANIL-MUNKERI WE ESBIR ‘ALA MA ‘ESABEKE ‘INNE DHALIKE MIN ‘AZMIL-’UMURI
WE LA TUSA’’IR HADDEKE LILNNASI WE LA TEMSHI FIL-’ERDI MEREHÆN ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JUHIBBU KULLE MUHTALIN FEHURIN
WAKSID FI MESHJIKE WE EGDUD MIN SEWTIKE ‘INNE ‘ENKEREL-’ESWATI LESEWTUL-HEMIRI
‘ELEM TEREW ‘ENNEL-LAHE SEHHARE LEKUM MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE ‘ESBEGA ‘ALEJKUM NI’AMEHU DHAHIRETEN WE BATINETEN WE MINE EN-NASI MEN JUXHADILU FI ELLAHI BIGAJRI ‘ILMIN WE LA HUDEN WE LA KITABIN MUNIRIN
WE ‘IDHA KILE LEHUMU ETTEBI’U MA ‘ENZELEL-LAHU KALU BEL NETTEBI’U MA WEXHEDNA ‘ALEJHI ‘ABA’ENA ‘EWELEW KANE ESH-SHEJTANU JED’UHUM ‘ILA ‘ADHABI ES-SA’IRI
WE MEN JUSLIM WEXHHEHU ‘ILA ELLAHI WE HUWE MUHSINUN FEKADI ESTEMSEKE BIL-’URWETIL-WUTHKA WE ‘ILA ELLAHI ‘AKIBETUL-’UMURI
WE MEN KEFERE FELA JEHZUNKE KUFRUHU ‘ILEJNA MERXHI’UHUM FENUNEBBI’UHUM BIMA ‘AMILU ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALIMUN BIDHATI ES-SUDURI
NUMETTI’UHUM KALILÆN THUMME NEDTERRUHUM ‘ILA ‘ADHABIN GALIDHIN
WE LE’IN SE’ELTEHUM MEN HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE LEJEKULUNNEL-LAHU KULIL-HEMDU LILLAHI BEL ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
LILLAHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘INNALL-LLAHE HUWEL-GANIJUL-HEMIDU
WE LEW ‘ENNEMA FIL-’ERDI MIN SHEXHERETIN ‘EKLAMUN WEL-BEHRU JEMUDDUHU MIN BA’DIHI SEB’ATU ‘EBHURIN MA NEFIDET KELIMATU ELLAHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘AZIZUN HEKIMUN
MA HALKUKUM WE LA BA’THUKUM ‘ILLA KENEFSIN WAHIDETIN ‘INNALL-LLAHE SEMI’UN BESIRUN
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE JULIXHUL-LEJLE FI EN-NEHARI WE JULIXHU EN-NEHARE FIL-LEJLI WE SEHHARE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE KULLUN JEXHRI ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE BIMA TA’MELUNE HABIRUN
DHALIKE BI’ENNEL-LAHE HUWEL-HEKKU WE ‘ENNE MA JED’UNE MIN DUNIHIL-BATILU WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE HUWEL-’ALIJUL-KEBIRU
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-FULKE TEXHRI FIL-BEHRI BINI’METI ELLAHI LIJURIJEKUM MIN ‘AJATIHI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKULLI SEBBARIN SHEKURIN
WE ‘IDHA GASHIJEHUM MEWXHUN KALDHDHULELI DE’AW ELLAHE MUHLISINE LEHU ED-DINE FELEMMA NEXHXHAHUM ‘ILAL-BERRI FEMINHUM MUKTESIDUN WE MA JEXHHEDU BI’AJATINA ‘ILLA KULLU HATTARIN KEFURIN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ETTEKU REBBEKUM WE EHSHEW JEWMÆN LA JEXHZI WE E-DUN ‘AN WELEDIHI WE LA MEWLUDUN HUWE XHAZIN ‘AN WE E-DIHI SHEJ’ÆN ‘INNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN FELA TEGURRENNEKUMUL-HEJA ETU ED-DUNJA WE LA JEGURRENNEKUM BILLAHIL-GARURU
‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘INDEHU ‘ILMU ES-SA’ATI WE JUNEZZILUL-GAJTHE WE JA’LEMU MA FIL-’ERHAMI WE MA TEDRI NEFSUN MADHA TEKSIBU GADÆN WE MA TEDRI NEFSUN BI’EJJI ‘ERDIN TEMUTU ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALIMUN HABIRUN
‘ELIF-LAM-MIM
TENZILUL-KITABI LA REJBE FIHI MIN RABBIL-’ALEMINE
‘EM JEKULUNE EFTERAHU BEL HUWEL-HEKKU MIN RABBIKE LITUNDHIRE KAWMÆN MA ‘ETAHUM MIN NEDHIRIN MIN KABLIKE LE’ALLEHUM JEHTEDUNE
ELLAHUL-LEDHI HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA FI SITTETI ‘EJJAMIN THUMME ESTEWA ‘ALEL-’ARSHI MA LEKUM MIN DUNIHI MIN WE LIJIN WE LA SHEFI’IN ‘EFELA TETEDHEKKERUNE
JUDEBBIRUL-’EMRE MINE ES-SEMA’I ‘ILAL-’ERDI THUMME JA’RUXHU ‘ILEJHI FI JEWMIN KANE MIKDARUHU ‘ELFE SENETIN MIMMA TA’UDDUNE
DHALIKE ‘ALIMUL-GAJBI WE ESH-SHEHADETIL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
EL-LEDHI ‘EHSENE KULLE SHEJ’IN HALEKAHU WE BEDE’E HALKAL-’INSANI MIN TININ
THUMME XHE’ALE NESLEHU MIN SULALETIN MIN MA’IN MEHININ
THUMME SEWWAHU WE NEFEHA FIHI MIN RUHIHI WE XHE’ALE LEKUMU ES-SEM’A WEL-’EBSARE WEL-’EF’IDETE KALILÆN MA TESHKURUNE
WE KALU ‘E’IDHA DELELNA FIL-’ERDI ‘E’INNA LEFI HALKIN XHEDIDIN BEL HUM BILIKA’I RABBIHIM KAFIRUNE
KUL JETEWEFFAKUM MELEKUL-MEWTIL-LEDHI WUKKILE BIKUM THUMME ‘ILA RABBIKUM TURXHA’UNE
WE LEW TERA ‘IDHIL-MUXHRIMUNE NAKISU RU’USIHIM ‘INDE RABBIHIM REBBENA ‘EBSERNA WE SEMI’NA FARXHI’NA NA’MEL SALIHÆN ‘INNA MUKINUNE
WE LEW SHI’NA LE’ATEJNA KULLE NEFSIN HUDAHA WE LEKIN HEKKAL-KAWLU MINNI LE’EMLE’ENNE XHEHENNEME MINEL-XHINNETI WE EN-NASI ‘EXHMA’INE
FEDHUKU BIMA NESITUM LIKA’E JEWMIKUM HADHA ‘INNA NESINAKUM WE DHUKU ‘ADHABEL-HULDI BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
‘INNEMA JU’UMINU BI’AJATINAL-LEDHINE ‘IDHA DHUKKIRU BIHA HARRU SUXHXHEDÆN WE SEBBEHU BIHEMDI RABBIHIM WE HUM LA JESTEKBIRUNE
TETEXHAFA XHUNUBUHUM ‘ANIL-MEDAXHI’I JED’UNE REBBEHUM HAWFÆN WE TEMA’ÆN WE MIMMA REZEKNAHUM JUNFIKUNE
FELA TA’LEMU NEFSUN MA ‘UHFIJE LEHUM MIN KURRETI ‘A’JUNIN XHEZA’EN BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
‘EFEMEN KANE MU’UMINÆN KEMEN KANE FASIKÆN LA JESTEWUNE
‘EMMAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI FELEHUM XHENNATUL-ME’WA NUZULÆN BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
WE ‘EMMAL-LEDHINE FESEKU FEME’WAHUMU EN-NARU KULLEMA ‘ERADU ‘EN JEHRUXHU MINHA ‘U’IDU FIHA WE KILE LEHUM DHUKU ‘ADHABE EN-NARIL-LEDHI KUNTUM BIHI TUKEDHDHIBUNE
WE LENUDHIKANNEHUM MINEL-’ADHABIL-’EDNA DUNEL-’ADHABIL-’EKBERI LE’ALLEHUM JERXHI’UNE
WE MEN ‘EDHLEMU MIMMEN DHUKKIRE BI’AJATI RABBIHI THUMME ‘A’REDE ‘ANHA ‘INNA MINEL-MUXHRIMINE MUNTEKIMUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE FELA TEKUN FI MIRJETIN MIN LIKA’IHI WE XHE’ALNAHU HUDEN LIBENI ‘ISRA’ILE
WE XHE’ALNA MINHUM ‘E’IMMETEN JEHDUNE BI’EMRINA LEMMA SEBERU WE KANU BI’AJATINA JUKINUNE
‘INNE REBBEKE HUWE JEFSILU BEJNEHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI FIMA KANU FIHI JEHTELIFUNE
‘EWELEM JEHDI LEHUM KEM ‘EHLEKNA MIN KABLIHIM MINEL-KURUNI JEMSHUNE FI MESAKINIHIM ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN ‘EFELA JESMA’UNE
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNA NESUKUL-MA’E ‘ILAL-’ERDIL-XHURUZI FENUHRIXHU BIHI ZER’ÆN TE’KULU MINHU ‘EN’AMUHUM WE ‘ENFUSUHUM ‘EFELA JUBSIRUNE
WE JEKULUNE META HADHAL-FETHU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
KUL JEWMEL-FETHI LA JENFA’UL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘IMANUHUM WE LA HUM JUNDHERUNE
FE’A’RID ‘ANHUM WE ENTEDHIR ‘INNEHUM MUNTEDHIRUNE
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU ETTEKI ELLAHE WE LA TUTI’IL-KAFIRINE WEL-MUNAFIKINE ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE ‘ALIMÆN HEKIMÆN
WE ETTEBI’ MA JUHA ‘ILEJKE MIN RABBIKE ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE BIMA TA’MELUNE HABIRÆN
WE TEWEKKEL ‘ALA ELLAHI WE KEFA BILLAHI WE KILÆN
MA XHE’ALEL-LAHU LIREXHULIN MIN KALBEJNI FI XHEWFIHI WE MA XHE’ALE ‘EZWAXHEKUMUL-LA’I TUDHAHIRUNE MINHUNNE ‘UMMEHATIKUM WE MA XHE’ALE ‘ED’IJA’EKUM ‘EBNA’EKUM DHALIKUM KAWLUKUM BI’EFWAHIKUM WEL-LAHU JEKULUL-HEKKA WE HUWE JEHDI ES-SEBILE
ED’UHUM LI’EBA’IHIM HUWE ‘EKSETU ‘INDEL-LAHI FE’IN LEM TA’LEMU ‘ABA’EHUM FE’IHWANUKUM FI ED-DINI WE MEWALIKUM WE LEJSE ‘ALEJKUM XHUNAHUN FIMA ‘EHTE’TUM BIHI WE LEKIN MA TE’AMMEDET KULUBUKUM WE KANEL-LAHU GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
EN-NEBIJU ‘EWLA BIL-MU’UMININE MIN ‘ENFUSIHIM WE ‘EZWAXHUHU ‘UMMEHATUHUM WE ‘ULUL-’ERHAMI BA’DUHUM ‘EWLA BIBA’DIN FI KITABI ELLAHI MINEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MUHAXHIRINE ‘ILLA ‘EN TEF’ALU ‘ILA ‘EWLIJA’IKUM MA’RUFÆN KANE DHALIKE FIL-KITABI MESTURÆN
WE ‘IDH ‘EHADHNA MINE EN-NEBIJINE MITHAKAHUM WE MINKE WE MIN NUHIN WE ‘IBRAHIME WE MUSA WE ‘ISA EBNI MERJEME WE ‘EHADHNA MINHUM MITHAKÆN GALIDHÆN
LIJES’ELE ES-SADIKINE ‘AN SIDKIHIM WE ‘E’ADDE LILKAFIRINE ‘ADHABÆN ‘ELIMÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU EDHKURU NI’METEL-LAHI ‘ALEJKUM ‘IDH XHA’ETKUM XHUNUDUN FE’ERSELNA ‘ALEJHIM RIHÆN WE XHUNUDÆN LEM TEREWHA WE KANEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRÆN
‘IDH XHA’UKUM MIN FEWKIKUM WE MIN ‘ESFELE MINKUM WE ‘IDH ZAGATIL-’EBSARU WE BELEGATIL-KULUBUL-HENAXHIRE WE TEDHUNNUNE BILLAHI EDH-DHUNUNE
HUNALIKE EBTULIJEL-MU’UMINUNE WE ZULZILU ZILZALÆN SHEDIDÆN
WE ‘IDH JEKULUL-MUNAFIKUNE WEL-LEDHINE FI KULUBIHIM MEREDUN MA WE’ADENALLAHU WE RESULUHU ‘ILLA GURURÆN
WE ‘IDH KALET TA’IFETUN MINHUM JA ‘EHLE JETHRIBE LA MUKAME LEKUM FARXHI’U WE JESTE’DHINU FERIKUN MINHUMU EN-NEBIJE JEKULUNE ‘INNE BUJUTENA ‘AWRETUN WE MA HIJE BI’AWRETIN ‘IN JURIDUNE ‘ILLA FIRARÆN
WE LEW DUHILET ‘ALEJHIM MIN ‘EKTARIHA THUMME SU’ILUL-FITNETE LE’ATEWHA WE MA TELEBBETHU BIHA ‘ILLA JESIRÆN
WE LEKAD KANU ‘AHEDU ELLAHE MIN KABLU LA JUWELLUNEL-’EDBARE WE KANE ‘AHDU ELLAHI MES’ULÆN
KUL LEN JENFE’AKUMUL-FIRARU ‘IN FERERTUM MINEL-MEWTI ‘EWIL-KATLI WE ‘IDHÆN LA TUMETTA’UNE ‘ILLA KALILÆN
KUL MEN DHAL-LEDHI JA’SIMUKUM MINEL-LAHI ‘IN ‘ERADE BIKUM SU’ÆN ‘EW ‘ERADE BIKUM REHMETEN WE LA JEXHIDUNE LEHUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI WELIJÆN WE LA NESIRÆN
KAD JA’LEMU ELLAHUL-MU’AWWIKINE MINKUM WEL-KA’ILINE LI’IHWANIHIM HELUMME ‘ILEJNA WE LA JE’TUNEL-BE’SE ‘ILLA KALILÆN
‘ESHIHHETEN ‘ALEJKUM FE’IDHA XHA’EL-HAWFU RE’EJTEHUM JENDHURUNE ‘ILEJKE TEDURU ‘A’JUNUHUM KALLEDHI JUGSHA ‘ALEJHI MINEL-MEWTI FE’IDHA DHEHEBEL-HAWFU SELEKUKUM BI’ELSINETIN HIDADIN ‘ESHIHHETEN ‘ALEL-HAJRI ‘ULA’IKE LEM JU’UMINU FE’EHBETEL-LAHU ‘A’MALEHUM WE
JEHSEBUNEL-’EHZABE LEM JEDH/HEBU WE ‘IN JE’TIL-’EHZABU JEWEDDU LEW ‘ENNEHUM BADUNE FIL-’A’RABI JES’ELUNE ‘AN ‘ENBA’IKUM WE LEW KANU FIKUM MA KATELU ‘ILLA KALILÆN
LEKAD KANE LEKUM FI RESULI ELLAHI ‘USWETUN HESENETUN LIMEN KANE JERXHU ELLAHE WEL-JEWMEL-’AHIRE WE DHEKEREL-LAHE KETHIRÆN
WE LEMMA RE’AL-MU’UMINUNEL-’EHZABE KALU HADHA MA WE’ADENALLAHU WE RESULUHU WE SEDEKAL-LAHU WE RESULUHU WE MA ZADEHUM ‘ILLA ‘IMANÆN WE TESLIMÆN
MINEL-MU’UMININE RIXHALUN SEDEKU MA ‘AHEDU ELLAHE ‘ALEJHI FEMINHUM MEN KADA NEHBEHU WE MINHUM MEN JENTEDHIRU WE MA BEDDELU TEBDILÆN
LIJEXHZIJEL-LAHU ES-SADIKINE BISIDKIHIM WE JU’ADHDHIBEL-MUNAFIKINE ‘IN SHA’E ‘EW JETUBE ‘ALEJHIM ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
WEREDDEL-LAHUL-LEDHINE KEFERU BIGAJDHIHIM LEM JENALU HAJRÆN WE KEFALLAHUL-MU’UMININEL-KITALE WE KANEL-LAHU KAWIJÆN ‘AZIZÆN
WE ‘ENZELEL-LEDHINE DHAHERUHUM MIN ‘EHLIL-KITABI MIN SEJASIHIM WE KADHEFE FI KULUBIHIMU ER-RU’BE FERIKÆN TEKTULUNE WE TE’SIRUNE FERIKÆN
WE ‘EWRETHEKUM ‘ERDEHUM WE DIJAREHUM WE ‘EMWALEHUM WE ‘ERDÆN LEM TETE’UHA WE KANEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRÆN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU KUL LI’ZWAXHIKE ‘IN KUNTUNNE TURIDNEL-HEJA ETE ED-DUNJA WE ZINETEHA FETA’ALEJNE ‘UMETTI’KUNNE WE ‘USERRIHKUNNE SERAHÆN XHEMILÆN
WE ‘IN KUNTUNNE TURIDNEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU WE ED-DAREL-’AHIRETE FE’INNALL-LLAHE ‘E’ADDE LILMUHSINATI MINKUNNE ‘EXHRÆN ‘ADHIMÆN
JA NISA’E EN-NEBIJI MEN JE’TI MINKUNNE BIFAHISHETIN MUBEJJINETIN JUDA’AF LEHAL-’ADHABU DI’FEJNI WE KANE DHALIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI JESIRÆN
WE MEN JEKNUT MINKUNNE LILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE TA’MEL SALIHÆN NU’UTIHA ‘EXHREHA MERRETEJNI WE ‘A’TEDNA LEHA RIZKÆN KERIMÆN
JA NISA’E EN-NEBIJI LESTUNNE KE’EHEDIN MINE EN-NISA’ ‘INI ETTEKAJTUNNE FELA TEHDA’NE BIL-KAWLI FEJETME’AL-LEDHI FI KALBIHI MEREDUN WE KULNE KAWLÆN MA’RUFÆN
WE KARNE FI BUJUTIKUNNE WE LA TEBERREXHNE TEBERRUXHEL-XHAHILIJETIL-’ULA WE ‘EKIMNE ES-SELÆTE WE ‘ATINE EZ-ZEKÆTE WE ‘ETI’NEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU ‘INNEMA JURIDU ELLAHU LIJUDH/HIBE ‘ANKUMU ER-RIXHSE ‘EHLEL-BEJTI WE JUTEHHIREKUM TETHIRÆN
WE EDHKURNE MA JUTLA FI BUJUTIKUNNE MIN ‘AJATI ELLAHI WEL-HIKMETI ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE LETIFÆN HABIRÆN
‘INNEL-MUSLIMINE WEL-MUSLIMATI WEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI WEL-KANITINE WEL-KANITATI WE ES-SADIKINE WE ES-SADIKATI WE ES-SABIRINE WE ES-SABIRATI WEL-HASHI’INE WEL-HASHI’ATI WEL-MUTESEDDIKINE WEL-MUTESEDDIKATI WE ES-SA’IMINE WE ES-SA’IMATI WEL-HAFIDHINE 
WE MA KANE LIMU’UMININ WE LA MU’UMINETIN ‘IDHA KADALLAHU WE RESULUHU ‘EMRÆN ‘EN JEKUNE LEHUMUL-HIJERETU MIN ‘EMRIHIM WE MEN JA’SI ELLAHE WE RESULEHU FEKAD DELLE DELALÆN MUBINÆN
WE ‘IDH TEKULU LILLEDHI ‘EN’AMEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHI WE ‘EN’AMTE ‘ALEJHI ‘EMSIK ‘ALEJKE ZEWXHEKE WE ETTEKI ELLAHE WE TUHFI FI NEFSIKE MALLAHU MUBDIHI WE TEHSHA EN-NASE WEL-LAHU ‘EHEKKU ‘EN TEHSHAHU FELEMMA KADA ZEJDUN MINHA WETERÆN ZEWWEXHNAKEHA LIKEJ LA JEKUNE 
MA KANE ‘ALA EN-NEBIJI MIN HEREXHIN FIMA FEREDEL-LAHU LEHU SUNNETEL-LAHI FIL-LEDHINE HALEW MIN KABLU WE KANE ‘EMRU ELLAHI KADERÆN MEKDURÆN
EL-LEDHINE JUBELLIGUNE RISALATI ELLAHI WE JEHSHEWNEHU WE LA JEHSHEWNE ‘EHEDÆN ‘ILLALLAHE WE KEFA BILLAHI HESIBÆN
MA KANE MUHEMMEDUN ‘EBA ‘EHEDIN MIN RIXHALIKUM WE LEKIN RESULEL-LAHI WE HATEME EN-NEBIJINE WE KANEL-LAHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU EDHKURU ELLAHE DHIKRÆN KETHIRÆN
WE SEBBIHUHU BUKRETEN WE ‘ESILÆN
HUWEL-LEDHI JUSELLI ‘ALEJKUM WE MELA’IKETUHU LIJUHRIXHEKUM MINE EDH-DHULUMATI ‘ILA EN-NURI WE KANE BIL-MU’UMININE REHIMÆN
TEHIJETUHUM JEWME JELKAWNEHU SELAMUN WE ‘E’ADDE LEHUM ‘EXHRÆN KERIMÆN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU ‘INNA ‘ERSELNAKE SHAHIDÆN WE MUBESHSHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN
WE DA’IÆN ‘ILA ELLAHI BI’IDHNIHI WE SIRAXHÆN MUNIRÆN
WE BESHSHIRIL-MU’UMININE BI’ENNE LEHUM MINEL-LAHI FEDLÆN KEBIRÆN
WE LA TUTI’IL-KAFIRINE WEL-MUNAFIKINE WE DA’ ‘EDHAHUM WE TEWEKKEL ‘ALA ELLAHI WE KEFA BILLAHI WE KILÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IDHA NEKEHTUMUL-MU’UMINATI THUMME TELLEKTUMUHUNNE MIN KABLI ‘EN TEMESSUHUNNE FEMA LEKUM ‘ALEJHINNE MIN ‘IDDETIN TA’TEDDUNEHA FEMETTI’UHUNNE WE SERRIHUHUNNE SERAHÆN XHEMILÆN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU ‘INNA ‘EHLELNA LEKE ‘EZWAXHEKEL-LATI ‘ATEJTE ‘UXHUREHUNNE WE MA MELEKET JEMINUKE MIMMA ‘EFA’EL-LAHU ‘ALEJKE WE BENATI ‘AMMIKE WE BENATI ‘AMMATIKE WE BENATI HALIKE WE BENATI HALATIKEL-LATI HAXHERNE ME’AKE WE EMRE’ETEN MU’UMINETEN ‘IN W
TURXHI MEN TESHA’U MINHUNNE WE TU’UWI ‘ILEJKE MEN TESHA’U WE MENI EBTEGAJTE MIMMEN ‘AZELTE FELA XHUNAHE ‘ALEJKE DHALIKE ‘EDNA ‘EN TEKARRE ‘A’JUNUHUNNE WE LA JEHZENNE WE JERDEJNE BIMA ‘ATEJTEHUNNE KULLUHUNNE WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU MA FI KULUBIKUM WE KANEL-LAHU ‘
LA JEHILLU LEKE EN-NISA’ MIN BA’DU WE LA ‘EN TEBEDDELE BIHINNE MIN ‘EZWAXHIN WE LEW ‘A’XHEBEKE HUSNUHUNNE ‘ILLA MA MELEKET JEMINUKE WE KANEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN REKIBÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TEDHULU BUJUTE EN-NEBIJI ‘ILLA ‘EN JU’UDHENE LEKUM ‘ILA TA’AMIN GAJRE NADHIRINE ‘INAHU WE LEKIN ‘IDHA DU’ITUM FADHULU FE’IDHA TA’IMTUM FANTESHIRU WE LA MUSTE’NISINE LIHEDITHIN ‘INNE DHALIKUM KANE JU’UDHI EN-NEBIJE FEJESTEHJI 
‘IN TUBDU SHEJ’ÆN ‘EW TUHFUHU FE’INNALL-LLAHE KANE BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMÆN
LA XHUNAHE ‘ALEJHINNE FI ‘ABA’IHINNE WE LA ‘EBNA’IHINNE WE LA ‘IHWANIHINNE WE LA ‘EBNA’I ‘IHWANIHINNE WE LA ‘EBNA’I ‘EHAWATIHINNE WE LA NISA’IHINNE WE LA MA MELEKET ‘EJMANUHUNNE WE ETTEKINEL-LAHE ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN SHEHIDÆN
‘INNALL-LLAHE WE MELA’IKETEHU JUSELLUNE ‘ALA EN-NEBIJI JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU SELLU ‘ALEJHI WE SELLIMU TESLIMÆN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JU’UDHUNEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU LE’ANEHUMU ELLAHU FI ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETI WE ‘E’ADDE LEHUM ‘ADHABÆN MUHINÆN
WEL-LEDHINE JU’UDHUNEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI BIGAJRI MA EKTESEBU FEKADI EHTEMELU BUHTANÆN WE ‘ITHMÆN MUBINÆN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU KUL LI’ZWAXHIKE WE BENATIKE WE NISA’IL-MU’UMININE JUDNINE ‘ALEJHINNE MIN XHELABIBIHINNE DHALIKE ‘EDNA ‘EN JU’REFNE FELA JU’UDHEJNE WE KANEL-LAHU GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
LE’IN LEM JENTEHIL-MUNAFIKUNE WEL-LEDHINE FI KULUBIHIM MEREDUN WEL-MURXHIFUNE FIL-MEDINETI LENUGRIJENNEKE BIHIM THUMME LA JUXHAWIRUNEKE FIHA ‘ILLA KALILÆN
MEL’UNINE ‘EJNEMA THUKIFU ‘UHIDHU WE KUTTILU TEKTILÆN
SUNNETEL-LAHI FIL-LEDHINE HALEW MIN KABLU WE LEN TEXHIDE LISUNNETI ELLAHI TEBDILÆN
JES’ELUKE EN-NASU ‘ANI ES-SA’ATI KUL ‘INNEMA ‘ILMUHA ‘INDEL-LAHI WE MA JUDRIKE LE’ALLE ES-SA’ATE TEKUNU KARIBÆN
‘INNALL-LLAHE LE’ANEL-KAFIRINE WE ‘E’ADDE LEHUM SA’IRÆN
HALIDINE FIHA ‘EBEDÆN LA JEXHIDUNE WELIJÆN WE LA NESIRÆN
JEWME TUKALLEBU WUXHUHUHUM FI EN-NARI JEKULUNE JA LEJTENA ‘ETA’NA ELLAHE WE ‘ETA’NA ER-RESULA
WE KALU REBBENA ‘INNA ‘ETA’NA SADETENA WE KUBERA’ENA FE’EDELLUNA ES-SEBILA
REBBENA ‘ATIHIM DI’FEJNI MINEL-’ADHABI WEL-’ANHUM LA’NÆN KEBIRÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TEKUNU KALLEDHINE ‘ADHEW MUSA FEBERRE’EHU ELLAHU MIMMA KALU WE KANE ‘INDEL-LAHI WEXHIHÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ETTEKU ELLAHE WE KULU KAWLÆN SEDIDÆN
JUSLIH LEKUM ‘A’MALEKUM WE JEGFIR LEKUM DHUNUBEKUM WE MEN JUTI’I ELLAHE WE RESULEHU FEKAD FAZE FEWZÆN ‘ADHIMÆN
‘INNA ‘AREDNAL-’EMANETE ‘ALA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WEL-XHIBALI FE’EBEJNE ‘EN JEHMILNEHA WE ‘ESHFEKNE MINHA WE HEMELEHAL-’INSANU ‘INNEHU KANE DHELUMÆN XHEHULÆN
LIJU’ADHDHIBEL-LAHUL-MUNAFIKINE WEL-MUNAFIKATI WEL-MUSHRIKINE WEL-MUSHRIKATI WE JETUBEL-LAHU ‘ALEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI WE KANEL-LAHU GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
EL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE LEHUL-HEMDU FIL-’AHIRETI WE HUWEL-HEKIMUL-HABIRU
JA’LEMU MA JELIXHU FIL-’ERDI WE MA JEHRUXHU MINHA WE MA JENZILU MINE ES-SEMA’I WE MA JA’RUXHU FIHA WE HUWE ER-REHIMUL-GAFURU
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LA TE’TINA ES-SA’ATU KUL BELA WE RABBI LETE’TIJENNEKUM ‘ALIMIL-GAJBI LA JA’ZUBU ‘ANHU MITHKALU DHERRETIN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE LA FIL-’ERDI WE LA ‘ESGARU MIN DHALIKE WE LA ‘EKBERU ‘ILLA FI KITABIN MUBININ
LIJEXHZIJEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM MEGFIRETUN WE RIZKUN KERIMUN
WEL-LEDHINE SE’AW FI ‘AJATINA MU’AXHIZINE ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN MIN RIXHZIN ‘ELIMUN
WE JERAL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILMEL-LEDHI ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJKE MIN RABBIKE HUWEL-HEKKA WE JEHDI ‘ILA SIRATIL-’AZIZIL-HEMIDI
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU HEL NEDULLUKUM ‘ALA REXHULIN JUNEBBI’UKUM ‘IDHA MUZZIKTUM KULLE MUMEZZEKIN ‘INNEKUM LEFI HALKIN XHEDIDIN
‘AFTERA ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN ‘EM BIHI XHINNETUN BELIL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI FIL-’ADHABI WE ED-DELALIL-BA’IDI
‘EFELEM JEREW ‘ILA MA BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE MA HALFEHUM MINE ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI ‘IN NESHE’ NEHSIF BIHIMUL-’ERDE ‘EW NUSKIT ‘ALEJHIM KISEFÆN MINE ES-SEMA’I ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJETEN LIKULLI ‘ABDIN MUNIBIN
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA DAWUDE MINNA FEDLÆN JA XHIBALU ‘EWWIBI ME’AHU WET-TEJRE WE ‘ELENNA LEHUL-HEDIDE
‘ENI A’MEL SABIGATIN WE KADDIR FI ES-SERDI WE A’MELU SALIHÆN ‘INNI BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRUN
WE LISULEJMANE ER-RIHE GUDUWUHA SHEHRUN WE REWAHUHA SHEHRUN WE ‘ESELNA LEHU ‘AJNEL-KITRI WE MINEL-XHINNI MEN JA’MELU BEJNE JEDEJHI BI’IDHNI RABBIHI WE MEN JEZIG MINHUM ‘AN ‘EMRINA NUDHIKHU MIN ‘ADHABI ES-SA’IRI
JA’MELUNE LEHU MA JESHA’U MIN MEHARIBE WE TEMATHILE WE XHIFANIN KALXHEWABI WE KUDURIN RASIJATIN A’MELU ‘ALE DAWUDE SHUKRÆN WE KALILUN MIN ‘IBADIJE ESH-SHEKURU
FELEMMA KADEJNA ‘ALEJHIL-MEWTE MA DELLEHUM ‘ALA MEWTIHI ‘ILLA DABBETUL-’ERDI TE’KULU MINSE’ETEHU FELEMMA HARRE TEBEJJENETIL-XHINNU ‘EN LEW KANU JA’LEMUNEL-GAJBE MA LEBITHU FIL-’ADHABIL-MUHINI
LEKAD KANE LISEBE’IIN FI MESKENIHIM ‘AJETUN XHENNETANI ‘AN JEMININ WE SHIMALIN KULU MIN RIZKI RABBIKUM WE ESHKURU LEHU BELDETUN TEJJIBETUN WE REBBUN GAFURUN
FE’A’REDU FE’ERSELNA ‘ALEJHIM SEJLEL-’ARIMI WE BEDDELNAHUM BIXHENNETEJHIM XHENNETEJNI DHEWATA ‘UKULIN HAMTIN WE ‘ETHLIN WE SHEJ’IN MIN SIDRIN KALILIN
DHALIKE XHEZEJNAHUM BIMA KEFERU WE HEL NUXHAZI ‘ILLAL-KEFURE
WE XHE’ALNA BEJNEHUM WE BEJNEL-KURA ELLETI BAREKNA FIHA KUREN DHAHIRETEN WE KADDERNA FIHA ES-SEJRE SIRU FIHA LEJALIJE WE ‘EJJAMÆN ‘AMININE
FEKALU REBBENA BA’ID BEJNE ‘ESFARINA WE DHELEMU ‘ENFUSEHUM FEXHE’ALNAHUM ‘EHADITHE WE MEZZEKNAHUM KULLE MUMEZZEKIN ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKULLI SEBBARIN SHEKURIN
WE LEKAD SEDDEKA ‘ALEJHIM ‘IBLISU DHENNEHU FE ETTEBA’UHU ‘ILLA FERIKÆN MINEL-MU’UMININE
WE MA KANE LEHU ‘ALEJHIM MIN SULTANIN ‘ILLA LINA’LEME MEN JU’UMINU BIL-’AHIRETI MIMMEN HUWE MINHA FI SHEKKIN WE REBBUKE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN HEFIDHUN
KUL ED’UL-LEDHINE ZE’AMTUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI LA JEMLIKUNE MITHKALE DHERRETIN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE LA FIL-’ERDI WE MA LEHUM FIHIMA MIN SHIRKIN WE MA LEHU MINHUM MIN DHEHIRIN
WE LA TENFA’U ESH-SHEFA’ATU ‘INDEHU ‘ILLA LIMEN ‘EDHINE LEHU HETTA ‘IDHA FUZZI’A ‘AN KULUBIHIM KALU MADHA KALE REBBUKUM KALUL-HEKKA WE HUWEL-’ALIJUL-KEBIRU
KUL MEN JERZUKUKUM MINE ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI KULI ELLAHU WE ‘INNA ‘EW ‘IJAKUM LE’ALA HUDEN ‘EW FI DELALIN MUBININ
KUL LA TUS’ELUNE ‘AMMA ‘EXHREMNA WE LA NUS’ELU ‘AMMA TA’MELUNE
KUL JEXHMA’U BEJNENA REBBUNA THUMME JEFTEHU BEJNENA BIL-HEKKI WE HUWEL-FETTAHUL-’ALIMU
KUL ‘ERUNIJEL-LEDHINE ‘ELHEKTUM BIHI SHUREKA’E KELLA BEL HUWEL-LAHUL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
WE MA ‘ERSELNAKE ‘ILLA KAFFETEN LILNNASI BESHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
WE JEKULUNE META HADHAL-WA’DU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
KUL LEKUM MI’ADU JEWMIN LA TESTE’HIRUNE ‘ANHU SA’ATEN WE LA TESTEKDIMUNE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEN NU’UMINE BIHEDHAL-KUR’ANI WE LA BIEL-LEDHI BEJNE JEDEJHI WE LEW TERA ‘IDHI EDH-DHALIMUNE MEWKUFUNE ‘INDE RABBIHIM JERXHI’U BA’DUHUM ‘ILA BA’DINL-KAWLE JEKULUL-LEDHINE ESTUD’IFU LILLEDHINE ESTEKBERU LEWLA ‘ENTUM LEKUNNA MU’UMINI
KALEL-LEDHINE ESTEKBERU LILLEDHINE ESTUD’IFU ‘ENEHNU SEDEDNAKUM ‘ANIL-HUDA BA’DE ‘IDH XHA’EKUM BEL KUNTUM MUXHRIMINE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE ESTUD’IFU LILLEDHINE ESTEKBERU BEL MEKRUL-LEJLI WE EN-NEHARI ‘IDH TE’MURUNENA ‘EN NEKFURE BILLAHI WE NEXH’ALE LEHU ‘ENDADÆN WE ‘ESERRU EN-NEDAMETE LEMMA RE’EWL-’ADHABE WE XHE’ALNAL-’EGLALE FI ‘A’NAKIL-LEDHINE KEFERU HEL JUXHZEWNE ‘ILLA MA
WE MA ‘ERSELNA FI KARJETIN MIN NEDHIRIN ‘ILLA KALE MUTREFUHA ‘INNA BIMA ‘URSILTUM BIHI KAFIRUNE
WE KALU NEHNU ‘EKTHERU ‘EMWALÆN WE ‘EWLADÆN WE MA NEHNU BIMU’ADHDHEBINE
KUL ‘INNE RABBI JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U WE JEKDIRU WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
WE MA ‘EMWALUKUM WE LA ‘EWLADUKUM BI-ETI TUKARRIBUKUM ‘INDENA ZULFA ‘ILLA MEN ‘AMENE WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FE’ULA’IKE LEHUM XHEZA’U ED-DI’FI BIMA ‘AMILU WE HUM FIL-GURUFATI ‘AMINUNE
WEL-LEDHINE JES’AWNE FI ‘AJATINA MU’AXHIZINE ‘ULA’IKE FIL-’ADHABI MUHDERUNE
KUL ‘INNE RABBI JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U MIN ‘IBADIHI WE JEKDIRU LEHU WE MA ‘ENFEKTUM MIN SHEJ’IN FEHUWE JUHLIFUHU WE HUWE HAJRU ER-RAZIKINE
WE JEWME JEHSHURUHUM XHEMI’ÆN THUMME JEKULU LILMELA’IKETI ‘EHA’UULA’ ‘IJAKUM KANU JA’BUDUNE
KALU SUBHANEKE ‘ENTE WELIJUNA MIN DUNIHIM BEL KANU JA’BUDUNEL-XHINNE ‘EKTHERUHUM BIHIM MU’UMINUNE
FALJEWME LA JEMLIKU BA’DUKUM LIBA’DIN NEF’ÆN WE LA DERRÆN WE NEKULU LILLEDHINE DHELEMU DHUKU ‘ADHABE EN-NARI ELLETI KUNTUM BIHA TUKEDHDHIBUN
WE ‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATUNA BEJJINATIN KALU MA HADHA ‘ILLA REXHULUN JURIDU ‘EN JESUDDEKUM ‘AMMA KANE JA’BUDU ‘ABA’UUKUM WE KALU MA HADHA ‘ILLA ‘IFKUN MUFTEREN WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LILHEKKI LEMMA XHA’EHUM ‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA SIHRUN MUBINUN
WE MA ‘ATEJNAHUM MIN KUTUBIN JEDRUSUNEHA WE MA ‘ERSELNA ‘ILEJHIM KABLEKE MIN NEDHIRIN
WE KEDHDHEBEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM WE MA BELEGU MI’SHARE MA ‘ATEJNAHUM FEKEDHDHEBU RUSULI FEKEJFE KANE NEKIRI
KUL ‘INNEMA ‘A’IDHUKUM BIWAHIDETIN ‘EN TEKUMU LILLAHI METHNA WE FURADA THUMME TETEFEKKERU MA BISAHIBIKUM MIN XHINNETIN ‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA NEDHIRUN LEKUM BEJNE JEDEJ ‘ADHABIN SHEDIDIN
KUL MA SE’ELTUKUM MIN ‘EXHRIN FEHUWE LEKUM ‘IN ‘EXHRIJE ‘ILLA ‘ALA ELLAHI WE HUWE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN SHEHIDUN
KUL ‘INNE RABBI JEKDHIFU BIL-HEKKI ‘ALLAMUL-GUJUBI
KUL XHA’EL-HEKKU WE MA JUBDI’UL-BATILU WE MA JU’IDU
KUL ‘IN DELELTU FE’INNEMA ‘EDILLU ‘ALA NEFSI WE ‘INI EHTEDEJTU FEBIMA JUHI ‘ILEJJE RABBI ‘INNEHU SEMI’UN KARIBUN
WE LEW TERA ‘IDH FEZI’U FELA FEWTE WE ‘UHIDHU MIN MEKANIN KARIBIN
WE KALU ‘AMENNA BIHI WE ‘ENNA LEHUMUT-TENAWUSHU MIN MEKANIN BA’IDIN
WE KAD KEFERU BIHI MIN KABLU WE JEKDHIFUNE BIL-GAJBI MIN MEKANIN BA’IDIN
WE HILE BEJNEHUM WE BEJNE MA JESHTEHUNE KEMA FU’ILE BI’ESHJA’IHIM MIN KABLU ‘INNEHUM KANU FI SHEKKIN MURIBIN
EL-HEMDU LILLAHI FATIRI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI XHA’ILIL-MELA’IKETI RUSULÆN ‘ULI ‘EXHNIHETIN METHNA WE THULATHE WE RUBA’A JEZIDU FIL-HALKI MA JESHA’U ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
MA JEFTEHI ELLAHU LILNNASI MIN REHMETIN FELA MUMSIKE LEHA WE MA JUMSIK FELA MURSILE LEHU MIN BA’DIHI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU EDHKURU NI’METEL-LAHI ‘ALEJKUM HEL MIN HALIKIN GAJRU ELLAHI JERZUKUKUM MINE ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE FE’ENNA TU’UFEKUNE
WE ‘IN JUKEDHDHIBUKE FEKAD KUDHDHIBET RUSULUN MIN KABLIKE WE ‘ILA ELLAHI TURXHA’UL-’UMURU
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ‘INNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN FELA TEGURRENNEKUMUL-HEJA ETU ED-DUNJA WE LA JEGURRENNEKUM BILLAHIL-GARURU
‘INNE ESH-SHEJTANE LEKUM ‘ADUWUN FE ETTEHIDHUHU ‘ADUWÆN ‘INNEMA JED’U HIZBEHU LIJEKUNU MIN ‘ESHABI ES-SA’IRI
EL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEHUM ‘ADHABUN SHEDIDUN WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LEHUM MEGFIRETUN WE ‘EXHRUN KEBIRUN
‘EFEMEN ZUJJINE LEHU SU’U ‘AMELIHI FERE’AHU HESENÆN FE’INNALL-LLAHE JUDILLU MEN JESHA’U WE JEHDI MEN JESHA’U FELA TEDH/HEB NEFSUKE ‘ALEJHIM HESERATIN ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALIMUN BIMA JESNA’UNE
WEL-LAHUL-LEDHI ‘ERSELE ER-RIJAHE FETUTHIRU SEHABÆN FESUKNAHU ‘ILA BELEDIN MEJJITIN FE’EHJEJNA BIHIL-’ERDE BA’DE MEWTIHA KEDHALIKE EN-NUSHURU
MEN KANE JURIDUL-’IZZETE FELILLAHIL-’IZZETU XHEMI’ÆN ‘ILEJHI JES’ADUL-KELIMUT-TEJJIBU WEL-’AMELU ES-SALIHU JERFA’UHU WEL-LEDHINE JEMKURUNE ES-SEJJI’ATI LEHUM ‘ADHABUN SHEDIDUN WE MEKRU ‘ULA’IKE HUWE JEBURU
WEL-LAHU HALEKAKUM MIN TURABIN THUMME MIN NUTFETIN THUMME XHE’ALEKUM ‘EZWAXHÆN WE MA TEHMILU MIN ‘UNTHA WE LA TEDA’U ‘ILLA BI’ILMIHI WE MA JU’AMMERU MIN MU’AMMERIN WE LA JUNKASU MIN ‘UMURIHI ‘ILLA FI KITABIN ‘INNE DHALIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI JESIRUN
WE MA JESTEWIL-BEHRANI HADHA ‘ADHBUN FURATUN SA’IGUN SHERABUHU WE HEDHA MILHUN ‘UXHAXHUN WE MIN KULLIN TE’KULUNE LEHMÆN TERIJÆN WE TESTEHRIXHUNE HILJETEN TELBESUNEHA WE TERAL-FULKE FIHI MEWAHIRE LITEBTEGU MIN FEDLIHI WE LE’ALLEKUM TESHKURUNE
JULIXHUL-LEJLE FI EN-NEHARI WE JULIXHU EN-NEHARE FIL-LEJLI WE SEHHARE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE KULLUN JEXHRI LI’XHELIN MUSEMMEN DHELIKUMU ELLAHU REBBUKUM LEHUL-MULKU WEL-LEDHINE TED’UNE MIN DUNIHI MA JEMLIKUNE MIN KITMIRIN
‘IN TED’UHUM LA JESMA’U DU’A’EKUM WE LEW SEMI’U MA ESTEXHABU LEKUM WE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI JEKFURUNE BISHIRKIKUM WE LA JUNEBBI’UKE MITHLU HABIRIN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ‘ENTUMUL-FUKARA’U ‘ILA ELLAHI WEL-LAHU HUWEL-GANIJUL-HEMIDU
‘IN JESHE’ JUDH/HIBKUM WE JE’TI BIHALKIN XHEDIDIN
WE MA DHALIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI BI’AZIZIN
WE LA TEZIRU WAZIRETUN WIZRE ‘UHRA WE ‘IN TED’U MUTHKALETUN ‘ILA HIMLIHA LA JUHMEL MINHU SHEJ’UN WE LEW KANE DHA KURBA ‘INNEMA TUNDHIRUL-LEDHINE JEHSHEWNE REBBEHUM BIL-GAJBI WE ‘EKAMU ES-SELÆTE WE MEN TEZEKKA FE’INNEMA JETEZEKKA LINEFSIHI WE ‘ILA ELLAHIL-
WE MA JESTEWIL-’A’MA WEL-BESIRU
WE LA EDH-DHULUMATU WE LA EN-NUR
WE LA EDH-DHILLU WE LAL-HERURU
WE MA JESTEWIL-’EHJA’U WE LAL-’EMWATU ‘INNALL-LLAHE JUSMI’U MEN JESHA’U WE MA ‘ENTE BIMUSMI’IN MEN FIL-KUBURI
‘IN ‘ENTE ‘ILLA NEDHIRUN
‘INNA ‘ERSELNAKE BIL-HEKKI BESHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN WE ‘IN MIN ‘UMMETIN ‘ILLA HALA FIHA NEDHIRUN
WE ‘IN JUKEDHDHIBUKE FEKAD KEDHDHEBEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM XHA’ET/HUM RUSULUHUM BIL-BEJJINATI WE BIZ-ZUBURI WE BIL-KITABIL-MUNIRI
THUMME ‘EHADHTUL-LEDHINE KEFERU FEKEJFE KANE NEKIRI
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE ‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FE’EHREXHNA BIHI THEMERATIN MUHTELIFÆN ‘ELWANUHA WE MINEL-XHIBALI XHUDEDUN BIDUN WE HUMRUN MUHTELIFUN ‘ELWANUHA WE GARABIBU SUDUN
WE MINE EN-NASI WE ED-DEWABBI WEL-’EN’AM MUHTELIFUN ‘ELWANUHU KEDHALIKE ‘INNEMA JEHSHA ELLAHE MIN ‘IBADIHIL-’ULEMA’U ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘AZIZUN GAFURUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JETLUNE KITABEL-LAHI WE ‘EKAMU ES-SELÆTE WE ‘ENFEKU MIMMA REZEKNAHUM SIRRÆN WE ‘ALANIJETEN JERXHUNE TIXHARETEN LEN TEBURE
LIJUWEFFIJEHUM ‘UXHUREHUM WE JEZIDEHUM MIN FEDLIHI ‘INNEHU GAFURUN SHEKURUN
WEL-LEDHI ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE MINEL-KITABI HUWEL-HEKKU MUSEDDIKÆN LIMA BEJNE JEDEJHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE BI’IBADIHI LEHABIRUN BESIRUN
THUMME ‘EWRETHNAL-KITABEL-LEDHINE ESTEFEJNA MIN ‘IBADINA FEMINHUM DHALIMUN LINEFSIHI WE MINHUM MUKTESIDUN WE MINHUM SABIKUN BIL-HAJRATI BI’IDHNI ELLAHI DHALIKE HUWEL-FEDLUL-KEBIRU
XHENNATU ‘ADNIN JEDHULUNEHA JUHELLEWNE FIHA MIN ‘ESAWIRE MIN DHEHEBIN WE LU’ULU’UÆN WE LIBASUHUM FIHA HERIRUN
WE KALUL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI ‘EDH/HEBE ‘ANNAL-HEZENE ‘INNE REBBENA LEGAFURUN SHEKURUN
EL-LEDHI ‘EHELLENA DAREL-MUKAMETI MIN FEDLIHI LA JEMESSUNA FIHA NESEBUN WE LA JEMESSUNA FIHA LUGUBUN
WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEHUM NARU XHEHENNEME LA JUKDA ‘ALEJHIM FEJEMUTU WE LA JUHAFFEFU ‘ANHUM MIN ‘ADHABIHA KEDHALIKE NEXHZI KULLE KEFURIN
WE HUM JESTERIHUNE FIHA REBBENA ‘EHRIXHNA NA’MEL SALIHÆN GAJREL-LEDHI KUNNA NA’MELU ‘EWELEM NU’AMMIRKUM MA JETEDHEKKERU FIHI MEN TEDHEKKERE WE XHA’EKUMU EN-NEDHIRU FEDHUKU FEMA LILDHDHALIMINE MIN NESIR
‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALIMU GAJBI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘INNEHU ‘ALIMUN BIDHATI ES-SUDURI
HUWEL-LEDHI XHE’ALEKUM HALA’IFE FIL-’ERDI FEMEN KEFERE FE’ALEJHI KUFRUHU WE LA JEZIDUL-KAFIRINE KUFRUHUM ‘INDE RABBIHIM ‘ILLA MEKTÆN WE LA JEZIDUL-KAFIRINE KUFRUHUM ‘ILLA HASARÆN
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM SHUREKA’EKUMUL-LEDHINE TED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘ERUNI MADHA HALEKU MINEL-’ERDI ‘EM LEHUM SHIRKUN FI ES-SEMAWATI ‘EM ‘ATEJNAHUM KITABÆN FEHUM ‘ALA BEJJINETIN MINHU BEL ‘IN JA’IDU EDH-DHALIMUNE BA’DUHUM BA’DÆN ‘ILLA GURURÆN
‘INNALL-LLAHE JUMSIKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE ‘EN TEZULA WE LE’IN ZALETA ‘IN ‘EMSEKEHUMA MIN ‘EHEDIN MIN BA’DIHI ‘INNEHU KANE HELIMÆN GAFURÆN
WE ‘EKSEMU BILLAHI XHEHDE ‘EJMANIHIM LE’IN XHA’EHUM NEDHIRUN LEJEKUNUNNE ‘EHDA MIN ‘IHDAL-’UMEMI FELEMMA XHA’EHUM NEDHIRUN MA ZADEHUM ‘ILLA NUFURÆN
ESTIKBARÆN FIL-’ERDI WE MEKRE ES-SEJJI’I WE LA JEHIKUL-MEKRU ES-SEJJI’U ‘ILLA BI’EHLIHI FEHEL JENDHURUNE ‘ILLA SUNNETEL-’EWWELINE FELEN TEXHIDE LISUNNETI ELLAHI TEBDILÆN WE LEN TEXHIDE LISUNNETI ELLAHI TEHWILÆN
‘EWELEM JESIRU FIL-’ERDI FEJENDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM WE KANU ‘ESHEDDE MINHUM KUWETEN WE MA KANEL-LAHU LIJU’XHIZEHU MIN SHEJ’IN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE LA FIL-’ERDI ‘INNEHU KANE ‘ALIMÆN KADIRÆN
WE LEW JU’UAHIDHU ELLAHU EN-NASE BIMA KESEBU MA TEREKE ‘ALA DHEHRIHA MIN DABBETIN WE LEKIN JU’UEHHIRUHUM ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN FE’IDHA XHA’E ‘EXHELUHUM FE’INNALL-LLAHE KANE BI’IBADIHI BESIRÆN
JA -SIN
WEL-KUR’ANIL-HEKIMI
‘INNEKE LEMINEL-MURSELINE
‘ALA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
TENZILEL-’AZIZI ER-REHIMI
LITUNDHIRE KAWMÆN MA ‘UNDHIRE ‘ABA’UUHUM FEHUM GAFILUNE
LEKAD HEKKAL-KAWLU ‘ALA ‘EKTHERIHIM FEHUM LA JU’UMINUNE
‘INNA XHE’ALNA FI ‘A’NAKIHIM ‘EGLALÆN FEHIJE ‘ILAL-’EDHKANI FEHUM MUKMEHUNE
WE XHE’ALNA MIN BEJNI ‘EJDIHIM SEDDÆN WE MIN HALFIHIM SEDDÆN FE’EGSHEJNAHUM FEHUM LA JUBSIRUNE
WE SEWA’UN ‘ALEJHIM ‘E’ENDHERTEHUM ‘EM LEM TUNDHIRHUM LA JU’UMINUNE
‘INNEMA TUNDHIRU MENI ETTEBE’A EDH-DHIKRE WE HASHIJE ER-REHMENE BIL-GAJBI FEBESHSHIRHU BIMEGFIRETIN WE ‘EXHRIN KERIMIN
‘INNA NEHNU NUHJIL-MEWTA WE NEKTUBU MA KADDEMU WE ‘ATHAREHUM WE KULLE SHEJ’IN ‘HSEJNAHU FI ‘IMAMIN MUBININ
WE EDRIB LEHUM METHELÆN ‘ESHABEL-KARJETI ‘IDH XHA’EHAL-MURSELUNE
‘IDH ‘ERSELNA ‘ILEJHIMU ETHNEJNI FEKEDHDHEBUHUMA FE’AZZEZNA BITHALITHIN FEKALU ‘INNA ‘ILEJKUM MURSELUNE
KALU MA ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA BESHERUN MITHLUNA WE MA ‘ENZELE ER-REHMANU MIN SHEJ’IN ‘IN ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA TEKDHIBUNE
KALU REBBUNA JA’LEMU ‘INNA ‘ILEJKUM LEMURSELUNE
WE MA ‘ALEJNA ‘ILLAL-BELAGUL-MUBINU
KALU ‘INNA TETEJJERNA BIKUM LE’IN LEM TENTEHU LENERXHUMENNEKUM WE LEJEMESSENNEKUM MINNA ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
KALU TA’IRUKUM ME’AKUM ‘E’IN DHUKKIRTUM BEL ‘ENTUM KAWMUN MUSRIFUNE
WE XHA’E MIN ‘EKSAL-MEDINETI REXHULUN JES’A KALE JA KAWMI ETTEBI’UL-MURSELINE
ETTEBI’U MEN LA JES’ELUKUM ‘EXHRÆN WE HUM MUHTEDUNE
WE MA LIJE LA ‘A’BUDUL-LEDHI FETERENI WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
‘E’ETTEHIDHU MIN DUNIHI ‘ALIHETEN ‘IN JURIDNI ER-REHMANU BIDURRIN LA TUGNI ‘ANNI SHEFA’ATUHUM SHEJ’ÆN WE LA JUNKIDHUNI
‘INNI ‘IDHÆN LEFI DELALIN MUBININ
‘INNI ‘AMENTU BIREBBIKUM FASMA’UNI
KILE EDHULIL-XHENNETE KALE JA LEJTE KAWMI JA’LEMUNE
BIMA GAFERE LI RABBI WE XHE’ALENI MINEL-MUKREMINE
WE MA ‘ENZELNA ‘ALA KAWMIHI MIN BA’DIHI MIN XHUNDIN MINE ES-SEMA’I WE MA KUNNA MUNZILINE
‘IN KANET ‘ILLA SEJHETEN WAHIDETEN FE’IDHA HUM HAMIDUNE
JA HESRETEN ‘ALEL-’IBADI MA JE’TIHIM MIN RESULIN ‘ILLA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
‘ELEM JEREW KEM ‘EHLEKNA KABLEHUM MINEL-KURUNI ‘ENNEHUM ‘ILEJHIM LA JERXHI’UNE
WE ‘IN KULLUN LEMMA XHEMI’UN LEDEJNA MUHDERUNE
WE ‘AJETUN LEHUMUL-’ERDUL-MEJTETU ‘EHJEJNAHA WE ‘EHREXHNA MINHA HEBBÆN FEMINHU JE’KULUNE
WE XHE’ALNA FIHA XHENNATIN MIN NEHILIN WE ‘A’NABIN WE FEXHXHERNA FIHA MINEL-’UJUNI
LIJE’KULU MIN THEMERIHI WE MA ‘AMILET/HU ‘EJDIHIM ‘EFELA JESHKURUNE
SUBHANEL-LEDHI HALEKAL-’EZWAXHE KULLEHA MIMMA TUNBITUL-’ERDU WE MIN ‘ENFUSIHIM WE MIMMA LA JA’LEMUNE
WE ‘AJETUN LEHUMUL-LEJLU NESLEHU MINHU EN-NEHARE FE’IDHA HUM MUDHLIMUNE
WE ESH-SHEMSU TEXHRI LIMUSTEKARRIN LEHA DHALIKE TEKDIRUL-’AZIZIL-’ALIMI
WEL-KAMERE KADDERNAHU MENAZILE HETTA ‘ADE KAL’URXHUNIL-KADIMI
LA ESH-SHEMSU JENBEGI LEHA ‘EN TUDRIKEL-KAMERE WE LAL-LEJLU SABIKU EN-NEHARI WE KULLUN FI FELEKIN JESBEHUNE
WE ‘AJETUN LEHUM ‘ENNA HEMELNA DHURRIJETEHUM FIL-FULKIL-MESHHUNI
WE HALEKNA LEHUM MIN MITHLIHI MA JERKEBUNE
WE ‘IN NESHE’ NUGRIKHUM FELA SERIHA LEHUM WE LA HUM JUNKADHUNE
‘ILLA REHMETEN MINNA WE META’ÆN ‘ILA HININ
WE ‘IDHA KILE LEHUMU ETTEKU MA BEJNE ‘EJDIKUM WE MA HALFEKUM LE’ALLEKUM TURHEMUNE
WE MA TE’TIHIM MIN ‘AJETIN MIN ‘AJATI RABBIHIM ‘ILLA KANU ‘ANHA MU’RIDINE
WE ‘IDHA KILE LEHUM ‘ENFIKU MIMMA REZEKAKUMU ELLAHU KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘ENUT’IMU MEN LEW JESHA’U ELLAHU ‘ET’AMEHU ‘IN ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA FI DELALIN MUBININ
WE JEKULUNE META HADHAL-WA’DU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
MA JENDHURUNE ‘ILLA SEJHETEN WAHIDETEN TE’HUDHUHUM WE HUM JEHISSIMUNE
FELA JESTETI’UNE TEWSIJETEN WE LA ‘ILA ‘EHLIHIM JERXHI’UNE
WE NUFIHA FI ES-SURI FE’IDHA HUM MINEL-’EXHDATHI ‘ILA RABBIHIM JENSILUNE
KALU JA WEJLENA MEN BE’ATHENA MIN MERKADINA HADHA MA WE’ADE ER-REHMANU WE SEDEKAL-MURSELUNE
‘IN KANET ‘ILLA SEJHETEN WAHIDETEN FE’IDHA HUM XHEMI’UN LEDEJNA MUHDERUNE
FALJEWME LA TUDHLEMU NEFSUN SHEJ’ÆN WE LA TUXHZEWNE ‘ILLA MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
‘INNE ‘ESHABEL-XHENNETIL-JEWME FI SHUGULIN FAKIHUNE
HUM WE ‘EZWAXHUHUM FI DHILALIN ‘ALEL-’ERA’IKI MUTTEKI’UNE
LEHUM FIHA FAKIHETUN WE LEHUM MA JEDDA’UNE
SELAMUN KAWLÆN MIN RABBIN REHIMIN
WE EMTAZUL-JEWME ‘EJJUHAL-MUXHRIMUNE
‘ELEM ‘A’HED ‘ILEJKUM JA BENI ‘ADEME ‘EN LA TA’BUDU ESH-SHEJTANE ‘INNEHU LEKUM ‘ADUWUN MUBINUN
WE ‘ENI A’BUDUNI HADHA SIRATUN MUSTEKIMUN
WE LEKAD ‘EDELLE MINKUM XHIBILLÆN KETHIRÆN ‘EFELEM TEKUNU TA’KILUNE
HEDHIHI XHEHENNEMU ELLETI KUNTUM TU’ADUNE
ESLEWHAL-JEWME BIMA KUNTUM TEKFURUNE
EL-JEWME NEHTIMU ‘ALA ‘EFWAHIHIM WE TUKELLIMUNA ‘EJDIHIM WE TESH/HEDU ‘ERXHULUHUM BIMA KANU JEKSIBUNE
WE LEW NESHA’U LETEMESNA ‘ALA ‘A’JUNIHIM FASTEBEKU ES-SIRATE FE’ENNA JUBSIRUNE
WE LEW NESHA’U LEMESEHNAHUM ‘ALA MEKANETIHIM FEMA ESTETA’U MUDIJÆN WE LA JERXHI’UNE
WE MEN NU’AMMIRHU NUNEKKIS/HU FIL-HALKI ‘EFELA JA’KILUNE
WE MA ‘ALLEMNAHU ESH-SHI’RE WE MA JENBEGI LEHU ‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA DHIKRUN WE KUR’ANUN MUBINUN
LIJUNDHIRE MEN KANE HEJJÆN WE JEHIKKAL-KAWLU ‘ALEL-KAFIRINE
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNA HALEKNA LEHUM MIMMA ‘AMILET ‘EJDINA ‘EN’AMÆN FEHUM LEHA MALIKUNE
WE DHELLELNAHA LEHUM FEMINHA REKUBUHUM WE MINHA JE’KULUNE
WE LEHUM FIHA MENAFI’U WE MESHARIBU ‘EFELA JESHKURUNE
WE ETTEHADHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘ALIHETEN LE’ALLEHUM JUNSERUNE
LA JESTETI’UNE NESREHUM WE HUM LEHUM XHUNDUN MUHDERUNE
FELA JEHZUNKE KAWLUHUM ‘INNA NA’LEMU MA JUSIRRUNE WE MA JU’LINUNE
‘EWELEM JEREL-’INSANU ‘ENNA HALEKNAHU MIN NUTFETIN FE’IDHA HUWE HASIMUN MUBINUN
WE DEREBE LENA METHELÆN WE NESIJE HALKAHU KALE MEN JUHJIL-’IDHAME WE HIJE REMIMUN
KUL JUHJIHAL-LEDHI ‘ENSHE’EHA ‘EWWELE MERRETIN WE HUWE BIKULLI HALKIN ‘ALIMUN
EL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUM MINE ESH-SHEXHERIL-’EHDERI NARÆN FE’IDHA ‘ENTUM MINHU TUKIDUNE
‘EWELEJSEL-LEDHI HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BIKADIRIN ‘ALA ‘EN JEHLUKA MITHLEHUM BELA WE HUWEL-HALLAKUL-’ALIMU
‘INNEMA ‘EMRUHU ‘IDHA ‘ERADE SHEJ’ÆN ‘EN JEKULE LEHU KUN FEJEKUNU
FESUBHANEL-LEDHI BIJEDIHI MELEKUTU KULLI SHEJ’IN WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
WE ES-SAFFATI SEFFÆN
FALZZAXHIRATI ZEXHRÆN
FALTTALIJATI DHIKRÆN
‘INNE ‘ILEHEKUM LEWAHIDUN
REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMA WE REBBUL-MESHARIKI
‘INNA ZEJJENNA ES-SEMA’E ED-DUNJA BIZINETINL-KEWAKIB
WE HIFDHÆN MIN KULLI SHEJTANIN MARIDIN
LA JESSEMMA’UNE ‘ILAL-MELE’IL-’A’LA WE JUKDHEFUNE MIN KULLI XHANIBIN
DUHURÆN WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN WE ESIBUN
‘ILLA MEN HATIFEL-HATFETE FE’ETBE’AHU SHIHABUN THAKIBUNA
FASTEFTIHIM ‘EHUM ‘ESHEDDU HALKÆN ‘EM MEN HALEKNA ‘INNA HALEKNAHUM MIN TININ LAZIBIN
BEL ‘AXHIBTE WE JESHARUNE
WE ‘IDHA DHUKKIRU LA JEDHKURUNE
WE ‘IDHA RE’EW ‘AJETEN JESTESHIRUNE
WE KALU ‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA SIHRUN MUBINUN
‘E’IDHA MITNA WE KUNNA TURABÆN WE ‘IDHAMÆN ‘E’INNA LEMEB’UTHUNE
‘EWE’ABA’UUNAL-’EWWELUNE
KUL NE’AM WE ‘ENTUM DAHIRUNE
FE’INNEMA HIJE ZEXHRETUN WAHIDETUN FE’IDHA HUM JENDHURUNE
WE KALU JA WEJLENA HADHA JEWMU ED-DINI
HADHA JEWMUL-FESLIL-LEDHI KUNTUM BIHI TUKEDHDHIBUNE
EHSHURUL-LEDHINE DHELEMU WE ‘EZWAXHEHUM WE MA KANU JA’BUDUNE
MIN DUNI ELLAHI FAHDUHUM ‘ILA SIRATIL-XHEHIMI
WE KIFUHUM ‘INNEHUM MES’ULUNE
MA LEKUM LA TENASERUNE
BEL HUMUL-JEWME MUSTESLIMUNE
WE ‘EKBELE BA’DUHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN JETESA’ELUNE
KALU ‘INNEKUM KUNTUM TE’TUNENA ‘ANIL-JEMINI
KALU BEL LEM TEKUNU MU’UMININE
WE MA KANE LENA ‘ALEJKUM MIN SULTANIN BEL KUNTUM KAWMÆN TAGINE
FEHEKKA ‘ALEJNA KAWLU RABBINA ‘INNA LEDHA’IKUNE
FE’EGWEJNAKUM ‘INNA KUNNA GAWINE
FE’INNEHUM JEWME’IDHIN FIL-’ADHABI MUSHTERIKUNE
‘INNA KEDHALIKE NEF’ALU BIL-MUXHRIMINE
‘INNEHUM KANU ‘IDHA KILE LEHUM LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLALLAHU JESTEKBIRUNE
WE JEKULUNE ‘E’INNA LETARIKU ‘ALIHETINA LISHA’IRIN MEXHNUNIN
BEL XHA’E BIL-HEKKI WE SEDDEKAL-MURSELINE
‘INNEKUM LEDHA’IKUL-’ADHABIL-’ELIMI
WE MA TUXHZEWNE ‘ILLA MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
‘ILLA ‘IBADEL-LAHIL-MUHLESINE
‘ULA’IKE LEHUM RIZKUN MA’LUMUN
FEWAKIHU WE HUM MUKREMUNE
FI XHENNATI EN-NA’IMI
‘ALA SURURIN MUTEKABILINE
JUTAFU ‘ALEJHIM BIKE’SIN MIN MA’ININ
BEJDA’E LEDHDHETIN LILSHSHARIBINE
LA FIHA GAWLUN WE LA HUM ‘ANHA JUNZEFUNE
WE ‘INDEHUM KASIRATUT-TERFI ‘INUN
KE’ENNEHUNNE BEJDUN MEKNUNUN
FE’EKBELE BA’DUHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN JETESA’ELUNE
KALE KA’ILUN MINHUM ‘INNI KANE LI KARINUN
JEKULU ‘E’INNEKE LEMINEL-MUSEDDIKINE
‘E’IDHA MITNA WE KUNNA TURABÆN WE ‘IDHAMÆN ‘E’INNA LEMEDINUNE
KALE HEL ‘ENTUM MUTTELI’UNE
FATTELE’A FERE’AHU FI SEWA’IL-XHEHIMI
KALE TE-ELLAHI ‘IN KIDTE LETURDINI
WE LEWLA NI’METU RABBI LEKUNTU MINEL-MUHDERINE
‘EFEMA NEHNU BIMEJJITINE
‘ILLA MEWTETENAL-’ULA WE MA NEHNU BIMU’ADHDHEBINE
‘INNE HADHA LEHUWEL-FEWZUL-’ADHIMU
LIMITHLI HADHA FELJA’MELIL-’AMILUNE
‘EDHELIKE HAJRUN NUZULÆN ‘EM SHEXHERETU EZ-ZEKKUMI
‘INNA XHE’ALNAHA FITNETEN LILDHDHALIMINE
‘INNEHA SHEXHERETUN TEHRUXHU FI ‘ESLIL-XHEHIMI
TEL’UHA KE’ENNEHU RU’USU ESH-SHEJATINI
FE’INNEHUM LE’AKILUNE MINHA FEMALI’UNE MINHAL-BUTUNE
THUMME ‘INNE LEHUM ‘ALEJHA LESHEWBÆN MIN HEMIMIN
THUMME ‘INNE MERXHI’AHUM LE’ILAL-XHEHIMI
‘INNEHUM ‘ELFEW ‘ABA’EHUM DALLINE
FEHUM ‘ALA ‘ATHARIHIM JUHRA’UNE
WE LEKAD DELLE KABLEHUM ‘EKTHERUL-’EWWELINE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA FIHIM MUNDHIRINE
FANDHUR KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-MUNDHERINE
‘ILLA ‘IBADEL-LAHIL-MUHLESINE
WE LEKAD NADANA NUHUN FELENI’MEL-MUXHIBUNE
WE NEXHXHEJNAHU WE ‘EHLEHU MINEL-KERBIL-’ADHIMI
WE XHE’ALNA DHURRIJETEHU HUMUL-BAKINE
WE TEREKNA ‘ALEJHI FIL-’AHIRINE
SELAMUN ‘ALA NUHIN FIL-’ALEMINE
‘INNA KEDHALIKE NEXHZIL-MUHSININE
‘INNEHU MIN ‘IBADINAL-MU’UMININE
THUMME ‘EGREKNAL-’AHARINE
WE ‘INNE MIN SHI’ATIHI LE’IBRAHIME
‘IDH XHA’E REBBEHU BIKALBIN SELIMIN
‘IDH KALE LI’EBIHI WE KAWMIHI MADHA TA’BUDUNE
‘E’IFKÆN ‘ALIHETEN DUNEL-LAHI TURIDUNE
FEMA DHENNUKUM BIREBBIL-’ALEMINE
FENEDHERE NEDHRETEN FI EN-NUXHUMI
FEKALE ‘INNI SEKIMUN
FETEWELLEW ‘ANHU MUDBIRINE
FERAGA ‘ILA ‘ALIHETIHIM FEKALE ‘ELA TE’KULUNE
MA LEKUM LA TENTIKUNE
FERAGA ‘ALEJHIM DERBÆN BIL-JEMINI
FE’EKBELU ‘ILEJHI JEZIFFUNE
KALE ‘ETA’BUDUNE MA TENHITUNE
WEL-LAHU HALEKAKUM WE MA TA’MELUNE
KALU EBNU LEHU BUNJANÆN FE’ELKUHU FIL-XHEHIMI
FE’ERADU BIHI KEJDÆN FEXHE’ALNAHUMUL-’ESFELINE
WE KALE ‘INNI DHAHIBUN ‘ILA RABBI SEJEHDINI
REBBI HEB LI MINE ES-SALIHINE
FEBESHSHERNAHU BIGULAMIN HELIMIN
FELEMMA BELEGA ME’AHU ES-SA’JE KALE JA BUNEJJE ‘INNI ‘ERA FIL-MENAMI ‘ENNI ‘EDHBEHUKE FANDHUR MADHA TERA KALE JA ‘EBETI EF’AL MA TU’UMERU SETEXHIDUNI ‘IN SHA’EL-LAHU MINE ES-SABIRINE
FELEMMA ‘ESLEMA WE TELLEHU LILXHEBINI
WE NADEJNAHU ‘EN JA ‘IBRAHIMU
KAD SEDDEKTE ER-RU’UJA ‘INNA KEDHALIKE NEXHZIL-MUHSININE
‘INNE HADHA LEHUWEL-BELA’UL-MUBINU
WE FEDEJNAHU BIDHIBHIN ‘ADHIMIN
WE TEREKNA ‘ALEJHI FIL-’AHIRINE
SELAMUN ‘ALA ‘IBRAHIME
KEDHALIKE NEXHZIL-MUHSININE
‘INNEHU MIN ‘IBADINAL-MU’UMININE
WE BESHSHERNAHU BI’ISHAKA NEBIJÆN MINE ES-SALIHINE
WE BAREKNA ‘ALEJHI WE ‘ALA ‘ISHAKA WE MIN DHURRIJETIHIMA MUHSINUN WE DHALIMUN LINEFSIHI MUBINUN
WE LEKAD MENENNA ‘ALA MUSA WE HARUNE
WE NEXHXHEJNAHUMA WE KAWMEHUMA MINEL-KERBIL-’ADHIMI
WE NESERNAHUM FEKANU HUMUL-GALIBINE
WE ‘ATEJNAHUMAL-KITABEL-MUSTEBINE
WE HEDEJNAHUMA ES-SIRATEL-MUSTEKIME
WE TEREKNA ‘ALEJHIMA FIL-’AHIRINE
SELAMUN ‘ALA MUSA WE HARUNE
‘INNA KEDHALIKE NEXHZIL-MUHSININE
‘INNEHUMA MIN ‘IBADINAL-MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE ‘ILJASE LEMINEL-MURSELINE
‘IDH KALE LIKAWMIHI ‘ELA TETTEKUNE
‘ETED’UNE BA’LÆN WE TEDHERUNE ‘EHSENEL-HALIKINE
ELLAHE REBBEKUM WE REBBE ‘ABA’IKUMUL-’EWWELINE
FEKEDHDHEBUHU FE’INNEHUM LEMUHDERUNE
‘ILLA ‘IBADEL-LAHIL-MUHLESINE
WE TEREKNA ‘ALEJHI FIL-’AHIRINE
SELAMUN ‘ALA ‘IL JA -SIN
‘INNA KEDHALIKE NEXHZIL-MUHSININE
‘INNEHU MIN ‘IBADINAL-MU’UMININE
WE ‘INNE LUTÆN LEMINEL-MURSELINE
‘IDH NEXHXHEJNAHU WE ‘EHLEHU ‘EXHMA’INE
‘ILLA ‘AXHUZÆN FIL-GABIRINE
THUMME DEMMERNAL-’AHARINE
WE ‘INNEKUM LETEMURRUNE ‘ALEJHIM MUSBIHINE
WE BIL-LEJLI ‘EFELA TA’KILUNE
WE ‘INNE JUNIS LEMINEL-MURSELINE
‘IDH ‘EBEKA ‘ILAL-FULKIL-MESHHUNI
FESAHEME FEKANE MINEL-MUDHEDINE
FALTEKAMEHUL-HUTU WE HUWE MULIMUN
FELEWLA ‘ENNEHU KANE MINEL-MUSEBBIHINE
LELEBITHE FI BETNIHI ‘ILA JEWMI JUB’ATHUNE
FENEBEDHNAHU BIL-’ARA’I WE HUWE SEKIMUN
WE ‘ENBETNA ‘ALEJHI SHEXHERETEN MIN JEKTININ
WE ‘ERSELNAHU ‘ILA MIA’ETI ‘ELFIN ‘EW JEZIDUNE
FE’AMENU FEMETTA’NAHUM ‘ILA HININ
FASTEFTIHIM ‘ELIREBBIKEL-BENATU WE LEHUMUL-BENUNE
‘EM HALEKNAL-MELA’IKETE ‘INATHÆN WE HUM SHAHIDUNE
‘ELA ‘INNEHUM MIN ‘IFKIHIM LEJEKULUNE
WELEDEL-LAHU WE ‘INNEHUM LEKADHIBUNE
‘ASTEFAL-BENATI ‘ALEL-BENINE
MA LEKUM KEJFE TEHKUMUNE
‘EFELA TEDHEKKERUN
‘EM LEKUM SULTANUN MUBINUN
FE’TU BIKITABIKUM ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
WE XHE’ALU BEJNEHU WE BEJNEL-XHINNETI NESEBÆN WE LEKAD ‘ALIMETIL-XHINNETU ‘INNEHUM LEMUHDERUNE
SUBHANEL-LAHI ‘AMMA JESIFUNE
‘ILLA ‘IBADEL-LAHIL-MUHLESINE
FE’INNEKUM WE MA TA’BUDUNE
MA ‘ENTUM ‘ALEJHI BIFATININE
‘ILLA MEN HUWE SALIL-XHEHIMI
WE MA MINNA ‘ILLA LEHU MEKAMUN MA’LUMUN
WE ‘INNA LENEHNU ES-SAFFUNE
WE ‘INNA LENEHNUL-MUSEBBIHUNE
WE ‘IN KANU LEJEKULUNE
LEW ‘ENNE ‘INDENA DHIKRÆN MINEL-’EWWELINE
LEKUNNA ‘IBADEL-LAHIL-MUHLESINE
FEKEFERU BIHI FESEWFE JA’LEMUNE
WE LEKAD SEBEKAT KELIMETUNA LI’IBADINAL-MURSELIN
‘INNEHUM LEHUMUL-MENSURUNE
WE ‘INNE XHUNDENA LEHUMUL-GALIBUNE
FETEWELLE ‘ANHUM HETTA HININ
WE ‘EBSIRHUM FESEWFE JUBSIRUNE
‘EFEBI’ADHABINA JESTA’XHILUNE
FE’IDHA NEZELE BISAHETIHIM FESA’E SEBAHUL-MUNDHERINE
WE TEWELLE ‘ANHUM HETTA HININ
WE ‘EBSIR FESEWFE JUBSIRUNE
SUBHANE RABBIKE RABBIL-’IZZETI ‘AMMA JESIFUNE
WE SELAMUN ‘ALEL-MURSELINE
WEL-HEMDU LILLAHI RABBIL-’ALEMINE
SAD WEL-KUR’ANI DHI EDH-DHIKRI
BELIL-LEDHINE KEFERU FI ‘IZZETIN WE SHIKAKIN
KEM ‘EHLEKNA MIN KABLIHIM MIN KARNIN FENADEW WELATE HINE MENASIN
WE ‘AXHIBU ‘EN XHA’EHUM MUNDHIRUN MINHUM WE KALEL-KAFIRUNE HADHA SAHIRUN KEDHDHABUN
‘EXHE’ALEL-’ALIHETE ‘ILEHÆN WAHIDÆN ‘INNE HADHA LESHEJ’UN ‘UXHABUN
WE ENTELEKAL-MELE’U MINHUM ‘ENI EMSHU WE ESBIRU ‘ALA ‘ALIHETIKUM ‘INNE HADHA LESHEJ’UN JURADU
MA SEMI’NA BIHEDHA FIL-MILLETIL-’AHIRETI ‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA EHTILAKUN
‘E’UUNZILE ‘ALEJHI EDH-DHIKRU MIN BEJNINA BEL HUM FI SHEKKIN MIN DHIKRI BEL LEMMA JEDHUKU ‘ADHABI
‘EM ‘INDEHUM HAZA’INU REHMETI RABBIKEL-’AZIZIL-WEHHABI
‘EM LEHUM MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMA FELJERTEKU FIL-’ESBABI
XHUNDUN MA HUNALIKE MEHZUMUN MINEL-’EHZABI
KEDHDHEBET KABLEHUM KAWMU NUHIN WE ‘ADUN WE FIR’AWNU DHUL-’EWTADI
WE THEMUDU WE KAWMU LUTIN WE ‘ESHABUL-’EJKETI ‘ULA’IKEL-’EHZABU
‘IN KULLUN ‘ILLA KEDHDHEBE ER-RUSULE FEHEKKA ‘IKABI
WE MA JENDHURU HA’UULA’ ‘ILLA SEJHETEN WAHIDETEN MA LEHA MIN FEWAKIN
WE KALU REBBENA ‘AXHXHIL LENA KITTENA KABLE JEWMIL-HISABI
ESBIR ‘ALA MA JEKULUNE WE EDHKUR ‘ABDENA DAWUDE DHAL-’EJDI ‘INNEHU ‘EWWABUN
‘INNA SEHHARNAL-XHIBALE ME’AHU JUSEBBIHNE BIL-’ASHIJI WEL-’ISHRAKI
WET-TEJRE MEHSHURETEN KULLUN LEHU ‘EWWABUN
WE SHEDEDNA MULKEHU WE ‘ATEJNAHUL-HIKMETE WE FESLEL-HITABI
WE HEL ‘ETAKE NEBE’UL-HASMI ‘IDH TESEWWERUL-MIHRABE
‘IDH DEHALU ‘ALA DAWUDE FEFEZI’A MINHUM KALU LA TEHAF HASMANI BEGA BA’DUNA ‘ALA BA’DIN FAHKUM BEJNENA BIL-HEKKI WE LA TUSHTIT WE EHDINA ‘ILA SEWA’I ES-SIRATI
‘INNE HADHA ‘EHI LEHU TIS’UN WE TIS’UNE NA’XHETEN WE LIJE NA’XHETUN WAHIDETUN FEKALE ‘EKFILNIHA WE ‘AZZENI FIL-HITABI
KALE LEKAD DHELEMEKE BISU’UALI NA’XHETIKE ‘ILA NI’AXHIHI WE ‘INNE KETHIRÆN MINEL-HULETA’I LEJEBGI BA’DUHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN ‘ILLAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI WE KALILUN MA HUM WE DHENNE DAWUDU ‘ENNEMA FETENNAHU FASTEGFERE REBBEHU WE HARRE RAKI’ÆN WE 
FEGAFERNA LEHU DHALIKE WE ‘INNE LEHU ‘INDENA LEZULFA WE HUSNE ME’ABIN
JA DAWUDU ‘INNA XHE’ALNAKE HALIFETEN FIL-’ERDI FAHKUM BEJNE EN-NASI BIL-HEKKI WE LA TETTEBI’IL-HEWA FEJUDILLEKE ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI ‘INNEL-LEDHINE JEDILLUNE ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI LEHUM ‘ADHABUN SHEDIDUN BIMA NESU JEWMEL-HISABI
WE MA HALEKNA ES-SEMA’E WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA BATILÆN DHALIKE DHENNUL-LEDHINE KEFERU FEWEJLUN LILLEDHINE KEFERU MINE EN-NARI
‘EM NEXH’ALUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI KALMUFSIDINE FIL-’ERDI ‘EM NEXH’ALUL-MUTTEKINE KALFUXHXHARI
KITABUN ‘ENZELNAHU ‘ILEJKE MUBAREKUN LIJEDDEBBERU ‘AJATIHI WE LIJETEDHEKKERE ‘ULUL-’ELBABI
WE WEHEBNA LIDAWUDE SULEJMANE NI’MEL-’ABDU ‘INNEHU ‘EWWABUN
‘IDH ‘URIDE ‘ALEJHI BIL-’ASHIJI ES-SAFINATUL-XHIJADU
FEKALE ‘INNI ‘EHBEBTU HUBBEL-HAJRI ‘AN DHIKRI RABBI HETTA TEWARET BIL-HIXHABI
RUDDUHA ‘ALEJJE FETEFIKA MESHÆN BIS-SUKI WEL-’A’NAKI
WE LEKAD FETENNA SULEJMANE WE ‘ELKAJNA ‘ALA KURSIJIHI XHESEDÆN THUMME ‘ENABE
KALE RABBI EGFIR LI WE HEB LI MULKÆN LA JENBEGI LI’HEDIN MIN BA’DI ‘INNEKE ‘ENTEL-WEHHABU
FESEHHARNA LEHU ER-RIHE TEXHRI BI’EMRIHI RUHA’EN HEJTHU ‘ESABE
WE ESH-SHEJATINE KULLE BENNA’IN WE GAWWASIN
WE ‘AHARINE MUKARRENINE FIL-’ESFADI
HADHA ‘ATA’UUNA FAMNUN ‘EW ‘EMSIK BIGAJRI HISABIN
WE ‘INNE LEHU ‘INDENA LEZULFA WE HUSNE ME’ABIN
WE EDHKUR ‘ABDENA ‘EJJUBE ‘IDH NADA REBBEHU ‘ENNI MESSENI ESH-SHEJTANU BINUSBIN WE ‘ADHABIN
ERKUD BIRIXHLIKE HADHA MUGTESELUN BARIDUN WE SHERABUN
WE WEHEBNA LEHU ‘EHLEHU WE MITHLEHUM ME’AHUM REHMETEN MINNA WE DHIKRA LI’WLIL-’ELBABI
WE HUDH BIJEDIKE DIGTHÆN FADRIB BIHI WE LA TEHNETH ‘INNA WE XHEDNAHU SABIRÆN NI’MEL-’ABDU ‘INNEHU ‘EWWABUN
WE EDHKUR ‘IBADENA ‘IBRAHIME WE ‘ISHAKA WE JA’KUBE ‘ULIL-’EJDI WEL-’EBSARI
‘INNA ‘EHLESNAHUM BIHALISETIN DHIKRA ED-DARI
WE ‘INNEHUM ‘INDENA LEMINEL-MUSTEFEJNEL-’EHJARI
WE EDHKUR ‘ISMA’ILE WEL-JESE’A WE DHAL-KIFLI WE KULLUN MINEL-’EHJARI
HADHA DHIKRUN WE ‘INNE LILMUTTEKINE LEHUSNE ME’ABIN
XHENNATI ‘ADNIN MUFETTEHETEN LEHUMUL-’EBWABU
MUTTEKI’INE FIHA JED’UNE FIHA BIFAKIHETIN KETHIRETIN WE SHERABIN
WE ‘INDEHUM KASIRATUT-TERFI ‘ETRABUN
HADHA MA TU’ADUNE LIJEWMIL-HISABI
‘INNE HADHA LERIZKUNA MA LEHU MIN NEFADIN
HADHA WE ‘INNE LILTTAGINE LESHERRE ME’ABIN
XHEHENNEME JESLEWNEHA FEBI’SEL-MIHADU
HADHA FELJEDHUKUHU HEMIMUN WE GASSAKUN
WE ‘AHARU MIN SHEKLIHI ‘EZWAXHUN
HADHA FEWXHUN MUKTEHIMUN ME’AKUM LA MERHEBÆN BIHIM ‘INNEHUM SALU EN-NARI
KALU BEL ‘ENTUM LA MERHEBÆN BIKUM ‘ENTUM KADDEMTUMUHU LENA FEBI’SEL-KARARU
KALU REBBENA MEN KADDEME LENA HADHA FEZID/HU ‘ADHABÆN DI’FÆN FI EN-NARI
WE KALU MA LENA LA NERA RIXHALÆN KUNNA NA’UDDUHUM MINEL-’ESHRAR
‘ATTEHADHNAHUM SIHRIJÆN ‘EM ZAGAT ‘ANHUMUL-’EBSARU
‘INNE DHALIKE LEHEKKUN TEHASUMU ‘EHLI EN-NARI
KUL ‘INNEMA ‘ENA MUNDHIRUN WE MA MIN ‘ILEHIN ‘ILLALLAHUL-WAHIDUL-KAHHARU
REBBU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMAL-’AZIZUL-GAFFARU
KUL HUWE NEBE’UN ‘ADHIMUN
‘ENTUM ‘ANHU MU’RIDUNE
MA KANE LIJE MIN ‘ILMIN BIL-MELE’IL-’A’LA ‘IDH JEHTESIMUNE
‘IN JUHA ‘ILEJJE ‘ILLA ‘ENNEMA ‘ENA NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
‘IDH KALE REBBUKE LILMELA’IKETI ‘INNI HALIKUN BESHERÆN MIN TININ
FE’IDHA SEWWEJTUHU WE NEFEHTU FIHI MIN RUHI FEKA’U LEHU SAXHIDINE
FESEXHEDEL-MELA’IKETU KULLUHUM ‘EXHMA’UNE
‘ILLA ‘IBLISE ESTEKBERE WE KANE MINEL-KAFIRINE
KALE JA ‘IBLISU MA MENE’AKE ‘EN TESXHUDE LIMA HALEKTU BIJEDEJJE ‘ASTEKBERTE ‘EM KUNTE MINEL-’ALINE
KALE ‘ENA HAJRUN MINHU HALEKTENI MIN NARIN WE HALEKTEHU MIN TININ
KALE FAHRUXH MINHA FE’INNEKE REXHIMUN
WE ‘INNE ‘ALEJKE LA’NETI ‘ILA JEWMI ED-DINI
KALE RABBI FE’ENDHIRNI ‘ILA JEWMI JUB’ATHUNE
KALE FE’INNEKE MINEL-MUNDHERINE
‘ILA JEWMIL-WEKTIL-MA’LUMI
KALE FEBI’IZZETIKE LE’UGWIJENNEHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
‘ILLA ‘IBADEKE MINHUMUL-MUHLESINE
KALE FALHEKKU WEL-HEKKA ‘EKULU
LE’EMLE’ENNE XHEHENNEME MINKE WE MIMMEN TEBI’AKE MINHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
KUL MA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI MIN ‘EXHRIN WE MA ‘ENA MINEL-MUTEKELLIFINE
‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA DHIKRUN LIL’ALEMINE
WE LETA’LEMUNNE NEBE’EHU BA’DE HININ
TENZILUL-KITABI MINEL-LAHIL-’AZIZIL-HEKIMI
‘INNA ‘ENZELNA ‘ILEJKEL-KITABE BIL-HEKKI FA’BUDI ELLAHE MUHLISÆN LEHU ED-DINE
‘ELA LILLAHI ED-DINUL-HALISU WEL-LEDHINE ETTEHADHU MIN DUNIHI ‘EWLIJA’E MA NA’BUDUHUM ‘ILLA LIJUKARRIBUNA ‘ILA ELLAHI ZULFA ‘INNALL-LLAHE JEHKUMU BEJNEHUM FI MA HUM FIHI JEHTELIFUNE ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JEHDI MEN HUWE KADHIBUN KEFFARUN
LEW ‘ERADEL-LAHU ‘EN JETTEHIDHE WELEDÆN LASTEFA MIMMA JEHLUKU MA JESHA’U SUBHANEHU HUWEL-LAHUL-WAHIDUL-KAHHARU
HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BIL-HEKKI JUKEWWIRUL-LEJLE ‘ALA EN-NEHARI WE JUKEWWIRU EN-NEHARE ‘ALEL-LEJLI WE SEHHARE ESH-SHEMSE WEL-KAMERE KULLUN JEXHRI LI’XHELIN MUSEMMEN ‘ELA HUWEL-’AZIZUL-GAFFARU
HALEKAKUM MIN NEFSIN WAHIDETIN THUMME XHE’ALE MINHA ZEWXHEHA WE ‘ENZELE LEKUM MINEL-’EN’AM THEMANIJETE ‘EZWAXHIN JEHLUKUKUM FI BUTUNI ‘UMMEHATIKUM HALKÆN MIN BA’DI HALKIN FI DHULUMATIN THELATHIN DHELIKUMU ELLAHU REBBUKUM LEHUL-MULKU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE F
‘IN TEKFURU FE’INNALL-LLAHE GANIJUN ‘ANKUM WE LA JERDA LI’IBADIHIL-KUFRE WE ‘IN TESHKURU JERDEHU LEKUM WE LA TEZIRU WAZIRETUN WIZRE ‘UHRA THUMME ‘ILA RABBIKUM MERXHI’UKUM FEJUNEBBI’UKUM BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE ‘INNEHU ‘ALIMUN BIDHATI ES-SUDURI
WE ‘IDHA MESSEL-’INSANE DURRUN DA’A REBBEHU MUNIBÆN ‘ILEJHI THUMME ‘IDHA HAWWELEHU NI’METEN MINHU NESIJE MA KANE JED’U ‘ILEJHI MIN KABLU WE XHE’ALE LILLAHI ‘ENDADÆN LIJUDILLE ‘AN SEBILIHI KUL TEMETTA’ BIKUFRIKE KALILÆN ‘INNEKE MIN ‘ESHABI EN-NARI
‘EMMEN HUWE KANITUN ‘ANA’EL-LEJLI SAXHIDÆN WE KA’IMÆN JEHDHERUL-’AHIRETE WE JERXHU REHMETE RABBIHI KUL HEL JESTEWIL-LEDHINE JA’LEMUNE WEL-LEDHINE LA JA’LEMUNE ‘INNEMA JETEDHEKKERU ‘ULUL-’ELBABI
KUL JA ‘IBADIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ETTEKU REBBEKUM LILLEDHINE ‘EHSENU FI HEDHIHI ED-DUNJA HESENETUN WE ‘ERDU ELLAHI WASI’ATUN ‘INNEMA JUWEFFA ES-SABIRUNE ‘EXHREHUM BIGAJRI HISABIN
KUL ‘INNI ‘UMIRTU ‘EN ‘A’BUDEL-LAHE MUHLISÆN LEHU ED-DINE
WE ‘UMIRTU LI’N ‘EKUNE ‘EWWELEL-MUSLIMINE
KUL ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘IN ‘ASEJTU RABBI ‘ADHABE JEWMIN ‘ADHIMIN
KULI ELLAHE ‘A’BUDU MUHLISÆN LEHU DINI
FA’BUDU MA SHI’TUM MIN DUNIHI KUL ‘INNEL-HASIRINEL-LEDHINE HASIRU ‘ENFUSEHUM WE ‘EHLIHIM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘ELA DHALIKE HUWEL-HUSRANUL-MUBINU
LEHUM MIN FEWKIHIM DHULELUN MINE EN-NARI WE MIN TEHTIHIM DHULELUN DHALIKE JUHAWWIFU ELLAHU BIHI ‘IBADEHU JA ‘IBADI FE ETTEKUNI
WEL-LEDHINE EXHTENEBUT-TAGUTE ‘EN JA’BUDUHA WE ‘ENABU ‘ILA ELLAHI LEHUMUL-BUSHRA FEBESHSHIR ‘IBADI
EL-LEDHINE JESTEMI’UNEL-KAWLE FEJETTEBI’UNE ‘EHSENEHU ‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE HEDAHUMU ELLAHU WE ‘ULA’IKE HUM ‘ULUL-’ELBABI
‘EFEMEN HEKKA ‘ALEJHI KELIMETUL-’ADHABI ‘EFE’ENTE TUNKIDHU MEN FI EN-NARI
LEKINIL-LEDHINE ETTEKAW REBBEHUM LEHUM GUREFUN MIN FEWKIHA GUREFUN MEBNIJETUN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU WA’DEL-LAHI LA JUHLIFU ELLAHUL-MI’AD
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE ‘ENZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN FESELEKEHU JENABI’A FIL-’ERDI THUMME JUHRIXHU BIHI ZER’ÆN MUHTELIFÆN ‘ELWANUHU THUMME JEHIXHU FETERAHU MUSFERRÆN THUMME JEXH’ALUHU HUTAMÆN ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LEDHIKRA LI’WLIL-’ELBABI
‘EFEMEN SHEREHEL-LAHU SEDREHU LIL’ISLAMI FEHUWE ‘ALA NURIN MIN RABBIHI FEWEJLUN LILKASIJETI KULUBUHUM MIN DHIKRI ELLAHI ‘ULA’IKE FI DELALIN MUBININ
ELLAHU NEZZELE ‘EHSENEL-HEDITHI KITABÆN MUTESHABIHÆN METHANIJE TEKSHA’IRRU MINHU XHULUDUL-LEDHINE JEHSHEWNE REBBEHUM THUMME TELINU XHULUDUHUM WE KULUBUHUM ‘ILA DHIKRI ELLAHI DHALIKE HUDA ELLAHI JEHDI BIHI MEN JESHA’U WE MEN JUDLILI ELLAHU FEMA LEHU MIN HA
‘EFEMEN JETTEKI BIWEXHHIHI SU’EL-’ADHABI JEWMEL-KIJAMETI WE KILE LILDHDHALIMINE DHUKU MA KUNTUM TEKSIBUNE
KEDHDHEBEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM FE’ETAHUMUL-’ADHABU MIN HEJTHU LA JESH’URUNE
FE’EDHAKAHUMU ELLAHUL-HIZJE FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE LE’ADHABUL-’AHIRETI ‘EKBERU LEW KANU JA’LEMUNE
WE LEKAD DEREBNA LILNNASI FI HADHAL-KUR’ANI MIN KULLI METHELIN LE’ALLEHUM JETEDHEKKERUNE
KUR’ANÆN ‘AREBIJÆN GAJRE DHI ‘IWEXHIN LE’ALLEHUM JETTEKUNE
