DEREBEL-LAHU METHELÆN REXHULÆN FIHI SHUREKA’U MUTESHAKISUNE WE REXHULÆN SELEMÆN LIREXHULIN HEL JESTEWIJANI METHELÆNL-HEMDU LILLAHI BEL ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
‘INNEKE MEJJITUN WE ‘INNEHUM MEJJITUNE
THUMME ‘INNEKUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘INDE RABBIKUM TEHTESIMUNE
FEMEN ‘EDHLEMU MIMMEN KEDHEBE ‘ALA ELLAHI WE KEDHDHEBE BIS-SIDKI ‘IDH XHA’EHU ‘ELEJSE FI XHEHENNEME METHWEN LILKAFIRINE
WEL-LEDHI XHA’E BIS-SIDKI WE SEDDEKA BIHI ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUTTEKUNE
LEHUM MA JESHA’UNE ‘INDE RABBIHIM DHALIKE XHEZA’UL-MUHSININE
LIJUKEFFIREL-LAHU ‘ANHUM ‘ESWE’EL-LEDHI ‘AMILU WE JEXHZIJEHUM ‘EXHREHUM BI’EHSENIL-LEDHI KANU JA’MELUNE
‘ELEJSEL-LAHU BIKAFIN ‘ABDEHU WE JUHAWWIFUNEKE BIEL-LEDHINE MIN DUNIHI WE MEN JUDLILI ELLAHU FEMA LEHU MIN HADIN
WE MEN JEHDI ELLAHU FEMA LEHU MIN MUDILLIN ‘ELEJSEL-LAHU BI’AZIZIN DHI ENTIKAMIN
WE LE’IN SE’ELTEHUM MEN HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE LEJEKULUNNEL-LAHU KUL ‘EFERE’EJTUM MA TED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘IN ‘ERADENIJEL-LAHU BIDURRIN HEL HUNNE KASHIFATU DURRIHI ‘EW ‘ERADENI BIREHMETIN HEL HUNNE MUMSIKATU REHMETIHI KUL HESBIJEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHI JE
KUL JA KAWMI A’MELU ‘ALA MEKANETIKUM ‘INNI ‘AMILUN FESEWFE TA’LEMUNE
MEN JE’TIHI ‘ADHABUN JUHZIHI WE JEHILLU ‘ALEJHI ‘ADHABUN MUKIMUN
‘INNA ‘ENZELNA ‘ALEJKEL-KITABE LILNNASI BIL-HEKKI FEMENI EHTEDA FELINEFSIHI WE MEN DELLE FE’INNEMA JEDILLU ‘ALEJHA WE MA ‘ENTE ‘ALEJHIM BIWEKILIN
ELLAHU JETEWEFFAL-’ENFUSE HINE MEWTIHA WE E-ETI LEM TEMUT FI MENAMIHA FEJUMSIKU ELLETI KADA ‘ALEJHAL-MEWTE WE JURSILUL-’UHRA ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JETEFEKKERUNE
‘EMI ETTEHADHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI SHUFA’A’E KUL ‘EWELEW KANU LA JEMLIKUNE SHEJ’ÆN WE LA JA’KILUNE
KUL LILLAHI ESH-SHEFA’ATU XHEMI’ÆN LEHU MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI THUMME ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
WE ‘IDHA DHUKIREL-LAHU WEHDEHU ESHME’EZZET KULUBUL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI WE ‘IDHA DHUKIREL-LEDHINE MIN DUNIHI ‘IDHA HUM JESTEBSHIRUNE
KULIL-LEHUMME FATIRE ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘ALIMEL-GAJBI WE ESH-SHEHADETI ‘ENTE TEHKUMU BEJNE ‘IBADIKE FI MA KANU FIHI JEHTELIFUNE
WE LEW ‘ENNE LILLEDHINE DHELEMU MA FIL-’ERDI XHEMI’ÆN WE MITHLEHU ME’AHU LAFTEDEW BIHI MIN SU’IL-’ADHABI JEWMEL-KIJAMETI WE BEDA LEHUM MINEL-LAHI MA LEM JEKUNU JEHTESIBUNE
WE BEDA LEHUM SEJJI’ATU MA KESEBU WE HAKA BIHIM MA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
FE’IDHA MESSEL-’INSANE DURRUN DA’ANA THUMME ‘IDHA HAWWELNAHU NI’METEN MINNA KALE ‘INNEMA ‘UTITUHU ‘ALA ‘ILMIN BEL HIJE FITNETUN WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHEREHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
KAD KALEHAL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM FEMA ‘EGNA ‘ANHUM MA KANU JEKSIBUNE
FE’ESABEHUM SEJJI’ATU MA KESEBU WEL-LEDHINE DHELEMU MIN HA’UULA’ SEJUSIBUHUM SEJJI’ATU MA KESEBU WE MA HUM BIMU’XHIZINE
‘EWELEM JA’LEMU ‘ENNEL-LAHE JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U WE JEKDIRU ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JU’UMINUNE
KUL JA ‘IBADIL-LEDHINE ‘ESREFU ‘ALA ‘ENFUSIHIM LA TEKNETU MIN REHMETI ELLAHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE JEGFIRU EDH-DHUNUBE XHEMI’ÆN ‘INNEHU HUWEL-GAFURU ER-REHIMU
WE ‘ENIBU ‘ILA RABBIKUM WE ‘ESLIMU LEHU MIN KABLI ‘EN JE’TIJEKUMUL-’ADHABU THUMME LA TUNSERUNE
WE ETTEBI’U ‘EHSENE MA ‘UNZILE ‘ILEJKUM MIN RABBIKUM MIN KABLI ‘EN JE’TIJEKUMUL-’ADHABU BEGTETEN WE ‘ENTUM LA TESH’URUNE
‘EN TEKULE NEFSUN JA HESRETA ‘ALA MA FERRETTU FI XHENBI ELLAHI WE ‘IN KUNTU LEMINE ES-SAHIRINE
‘EW TEKULE LEW ‘ENNEL-LAHE HEDANI LEKUNTU MINEL-MUTTEKINE
‘EW TEKULE HINE TERAL-’ADHABE LEW ‘ENNE LI KERRETEN FE’EKUNE MINEL-MUHSININE
BELA KAD XHA’ETKE ‘AJATI FEKEDHDHEBTE BIHA WE ESTEKBERTE WE KUNTE MINEL-KAFIRINE
WE JEWMEL-KIJAMETI TERAL-LEDHINE KEDHEBU ‘ALA ELLAHI WUXHUHUHUM MUSWEDDETUN ‘ELEJSE FI XHEHENNEME METHWEN LILMUTEKEBBIRINE
WE JUNEXHXHI ELLAHUL-LEDHINE ETTEKAW BIMEFAZETIHIM LA JEMESSUHUMU ES-SU’U WE LA HUM JEHZENUNE
ELLAHU HALIKU KULLI SHEJ’IN WE HUWE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN WE KILUN
LEHU MEKALIDU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BI’AJATI ELLAHI ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-HASIRUNE
KUL ‘EFEGAJREL-LAHI TE’MURUNNI ‘A’BUDU ‘EJJUHAL-XHAHILUNE
WE LEKAD ‘UHIJE ‘ILEJKE WE ‘ILAL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIKE LE’IN ‘ESHREKTE LEJEHBETENNE ‘AMELUKE WE LETEKUNENNE MINEL-HASIRINE
BELI ELLAHE FA’BUD WE KUN MINE ESH-SHAKIRINE
WE MA KADERU ELLAHE HEKKA KADRIHI WEL-’ERDU XHEMI’ÆN KABDETUHU JEWMEL-KIJAMETI WE ES-SEMAWATU METWIJATUN BIJEMINIHI SUBHANEHU WE TA’ALA ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
WE NUFIHA FI ES-SURI FESA’IKA MEN FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MEN FIL-’ERDI ‘ILLA MEN SHA’EL-LAHU THUMME NUFIHA FIHI ‘UHRA FE’IDHA HUM KIJAMUN JENDHURUNE
WE ‘ESHREKATIL-’ERDU BINURI RABBIHA WE WUDI’AL-KITABU WE XHI’E BIN-NEBIJINE WE ESH-SHUHEDA’I WE KUDIJE BEJNEHUM BIL-HEKKI WE HUM LA JUDHLEMUNE
WE WUFFIJET KULLU NEFSIN MA ‘AMILET WE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMA JEF’ALUNE
WE SIKAL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘ILA XHEHENNEME ZUMERÆN HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’UHA FUTIHET ‘EBWABUHA WE KALE LEHUM HAZENETUHA ‘ELEM JE’TIKUM RUSULUN MINKUM JETLUNE ‘ALEJKUM ‘AJATI RABBIKUM WE JUNDHIRUNEKUM LIKA’E JEWMIKUM HADHA KALU BELA WE LEKIN HEKKAT KELIMETUL-’ADHAB
KILE EDHULU ‘EBWABE XHEHENNEME HALIDINE FIHA FEBI’SE METHWAL-MUTEKEBBIRINE
WE SIKAL-LEDHINE ETTEKAW REBBEHUM ‘ILAL-XHENNETI ZUMERÆN HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’UHA WE FUTIHET ‘EBWABUHA WE KALE LEHUM HAZENETUHA SELAMUN ‘ALEJKUM TIBTUM FADHULUHA HALIDINE
WE KALUL-HEMDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI SEDEKANA WA’DEHU WE ‘EWRETHENAL-’ERDE NETEBEWWE’U MINEL-XHENNETI HEJTHU NESHA’U FENI’ME ‘EXHRUL-’AMILINE
WE TERAL-MELA’IKETE HAFFINE MIN HEWLIL-’ARSHI JUSEBBIHUNE BIHEMDI RABBIHIM WE KUDIJE BEJNEHUM BIL-HEKKI WE KILEL-HEMDU LILLAHI RABBIL-’ALEMINE
HA-MIM
TENZILUL-KITABI MINEL-LAHIL-’AZIZIL-’ALIMI
GAFIRI EDH-DHENBI WE KABILIT-TEWBI SHEDIDIL-’IKABI DHIT-TEWLI LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE ‘ILEJHIL-MESIRU
MA JUXHADILU FI ‘AJATI ELLAHI ‘ILLAL-LEDHINE KEFERU FELA JEGRURKE TEKALLUBUHUM FIL-BILADI
KEDHDHEBET KABLEHUM KAWMU NUHIN WEL-’EHZABU MIN BA’DIHIM WE HEMMET KULLU ‘UMMETIN BIRESULIHIM LIJE’HUDHUHU WE XHADELU BIL-BATILI LIJUDHIDU BIHIL-HEKKA FE’EHADHTUHUM FEKEJFE KANE ‘IKABI
WE KEDHELIKE HEKKAT KELIMETU RABBIKE ‘ALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘ENNEHUM ‘ESHABU EN-NARI
EL-LEDHINE JEHMILUNEL-’ARSHE WE MEN HEWLEHU JUSEBBIHUNE BIHEMDI RABBIHIM WE JU’UMINUNE BIHI WE JESTEGFIRUNE LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU REBBENA WESI’TE KULLE SHEJ’IN REHMETEN WE ‘ILMÆN FAGFIR LILLEDHINE TABU WE ETTEBA’U SEBILEKE WE KIHIM ‘ADHABEL-XHEHIMI
REBBENA WE ‘EDHILHUM XHENNATI ‘ADNIN ELLETI WE’ADTEHUM WE MEN SELEHE MIN ‘ABA’IHIM WE ‘EZWAXHIHIM WE DHURRIJATIHIM ‘INNEKE ‘ENTEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
WE KIHIMU ES-SEJJI’ATI WE MEN TEKI ES-SEJJI’ATI JEWME’IDHIN FEKAD REHIMTEHU WE DHELIKE HUWEL-FEWZUL-’ADHIMU
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU JUNADEWNE LEMEKTU ELLAHI ‘EKBERU MIN MEKTIKUM ‘ENFUSEKUM ‘IDH TUD’AWNE ‘ILAL-’IMANI FETEKFURUNE
KALU REBBENA ‘EMETTENA ETHNETEJNI WE ‘EHJEJTENA ETHNETEJNI FA’TEREFNA BIDHUNUBINA FEHEL ‘ILA HURUXHIN MIN SEBILIN
DHALIKUM BI’ENNEHU ‘IDHA DU’IJEL-LAHU WEHDEHU KEFERTUM WE ‘IN JUSHREK BIHI TU’UMINU FALHUKMU LILLAHIL-’ALIJIL-KEBIRI
HUWEL-LEDHI JURIKUM ‘AJATIHI WE JUNEZZILU LEKUM MINE ES-SEMA’I RIZKÆN WE MA JETEDHEKKERU ‘ILLA MEN JUNIBU
FAD’U ELLAHE MUHLISINE LEHU ED-DINE WE LEW KERIHEL-KAFIRUNE
REFI’U ED-DEREXHATI DHUL-’ARSHI JULKI ER-RUHE MIN ‘EMRIHI ‘ALA MEN JESHA’U MIN ‘IBADIHI LIJUNDHIRE JEWMET-TELAKI
JEWME HUM BARIZUNE LA JEHFA ‘ALA ELLAHI MINHUM SHEJ’UN LIMENIL-MULKUL-JEWME LILLAHIL-WAHIDIL-KAHHARI
EL-JEWME TUXHZA KULLU NEFSIN BIMA KESEBET LA DHULMEL-JEWME ‘INNALL-LLAHE SERI’UL-HISABI
WE ‘ENDHIRHUM JEWMEL-’AZIFETI ‘IDHIL-KULUBU LEDAL-HENAXHIRI KADHIMINE MA LILDHDHALIMINE MIN HEMIMIN WE LA SHEFI’IN JUTA’U
JA’LEMU HA’INETEL-’A’JUNI WE MA TUHFI ES-SUDURU
WEL-LAHU JEKDI BIL-HEKKI WEL-LEDHINE JED’UNE MIN DUNIHI LA JEKDUNE BISHEJ’IN ‘INNALL-LLAHE HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-BESIRU
‘EWE LEM JESIRU FIL-’ERDI FEJENDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-LEDHINE KANU MIN KABLIHIM KANU HUM ‘ESHEDDE MINHUM KUWETEN WE ‘ATHARÆN FIL-’ERDI FE’EHADHEHUMU ELLAHU BIDHUNUBIHIM WE MA KANE LEHUM MINI ELLAHI MIN WAKIN
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUM KANET TE’TIHIM RUSULUHUM BIL-BEJJINATI FEKEFERU FE’EHADHEHUMU ELLAHU ‘INNEHU KAWIJUN SHEDIDUL-’IKABI
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA MUSA BI’AJATINA WE SULTANIN MUBININ
‘ILA FIR’AWNE WE HAMANE WE KARUNE FEKALU SAHIRUN KEDHDHABUN
FELEMMA XHA’EHUM BIL-HEKKI MIN ‘INDINA KALU EKTULU ‘EBNA’EL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ME’AHU WE ESTEHJU NISA’EHUM WE MA KEJDUL-KAFIRINE ‘ILLA FI DELALIN
WE KALE FIR’AWNU DHERUNI ‘EKTUL MUSA WE LIED’U REBBEHU ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘EN JUBEDDILE DINEKUM ‘EW ‘EN JUDHHIRE FIL-’ERDIL-FESADE
WE KALE MUSA ‘INNI ‘UDHTU BIREBBI WE RABBIKUM MIN KULLI MUTEKEBBIRIN LA JU’UMINU BIJEWMIL-HISABI
WE KALE REXHULUN MU’UMINUN MIN ‘ALI FIR’AWNE JEKTUMU ‘IMANEHU ‘ETEKTULUNE REXHULÆN ‘EN JEKULE RABBIJEL-LAHU WE KAD XHA’EKUM BIL-BEJJINATI MIN RABBIKUM WE ‘IN JEKU KADHIBÆN FE’ALEJHI KEDHIBUHU WE ‘IN JEKU SADIKÆN JUSIBKUM BA’DUL-LEDHI JA’IDUKUM ‘INNALL-LLA
JA KAWMI LEKUMUL-MULKUL-JEWME DHAHIRINE FIL-’ERDI FEMEN JENSURUNA MIN BE’SI ELLAHI ‘IN XHA’ENA KALE FIR’AWNU MA ‘URIKUM ‘ILLA MA ‘ERA WE MA ‘EHDIKUM ‘ILLA SEBILE ER-RESHADI
WE KALEL-LEDHI ‘AMENE JA KAWMI ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘ALEJKUM MITHLE JEWMIL-’EHZABI
MITHLE DE’BI KAWMI NUHIN WE ‘ADIN WE THEMUDE WEL-LEDHINE MIN BA’DIHIM WE MALLAHU JURIDU DHULMÆN LIL’IBADI
WE JAKAWMI ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘ALEJKUM JEWMET-TENADI
JEWME TUWELLUNE MUDBIRINE MA LEKUM MINEL-LAHI MIN ‘ASIMIN WE MEN JUDLILI ELLAHU FEMA LEHU MIN HADIN
WE LEKAD XHA’EKUM JUSUFU MIN KABLU BIL-BEJJINATI FEMA ZILTUM FI SHEKKIN MIMMA XHA’EKUM BIHI HETTA ‘IDHA HELEKE KULTUM LEN JEB’ATHEL-LAHU MIN BA’DIHI RESULÆN KEDHALIKE JUDILLU ELLAHU MEN HUWE MUSRIFUN MURTABUN
EL-LEDHINE JUXHADILUNE FI ‘AJATI ELLAHI BIGAJRI SULTANIN ‘ETAHUM KEBURE MEKTÆN ‘INDEL-LAHI WE ‘INDEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU KEDHALIKE JETBA’U ELLAHU ‘ALA KULLI KALBI MUTEKEBBIRIN XHEBBARIN
WE KALE FIR’AWNU JA HAMANU EBNI LI SERHÆN LE’ALLI ‘EBLUGUL-’ESBABE
‘ESBABE ES-SEMAWATI FE’ETTELI’A ‘ILA ‘ILEHI MUSA WE ‘INNI LE’EDHUNNUHU KADHIBÆN WE KEDHELIKE ZUJJINE LIFIR’AWNE SU’U ‘AMELIHI WE SUDDE ‘ANI ES-SEBILI WE MA KEJDU FIR’AWNE ‘ILLA FI TEBABIN
WE KALEL-LEDHI ‘AMENE JA KAWMI ETTEBI’UNI ‘EHDIKUM SEBILE ER-RESHADI
JA KAWMI ‘INNEMA HEDHIHIL-HEJA ETU ED-DUNJA META’UN WE ‘INNEL-’AHIRETE HIJE DARUL-KARARI
MEN ‘AMILE SEJJI’ETEN FELA JUXHZA ‘ILLA MITHLEHA WE MEN ‘AMILE SALIHÆN MIN DHEKERIN ‘EW ‘UNTHA WE HUWE MU’UMINUN FE’ULA’IKE JEDHULUNEL-XHENNETE JURZEKUNE FIHA BIGAJRI HISABIN
WE JAKAWMI MA LI ‘ED’UKUM ‘ILA EN-NEXHÆTI WE TED’UNENI ‘ILA EN-NARI
TED’UNENI LI’KFURE BILLAHI WE ‘USHRIKE BIHI MA LEJSE LI BIHI ‘ILMUN WE ‘ENA ‘ED’UKUM ‘ILAL-’AZIZIL-GAFFARI
LA XHEREME ‘ENNEMA TED’UNENI ‘ILEJHI LEJSE LEHU DA’WETUN FI ED-DUNJA WE LA FIL-’AHIRETI WE ‘ENNE MEREDDENA ‘ILA ELLAHI WE ‘ENNEL-MUSRIFINE HUM ‘ESHABU EN-NARI
FESETEDHKURUNE MA ‘EKULU LEKUM WE ‘UFEWWIDU ‘EMRI ‘ILA ELLAHI ‘INNALL-LLAHE BESIRUN BIL-’IBADI
FEWEKAHU ELLAHU SEJJI’ATI MA MEKERU WE HAKA BI’ALI FIR’AWNE SU’UL-’ADHABI
EN-NARU JU’REDUNE ‘ALEJHA GUDUWÆN WE ‘ASHIJÆN WE JEWME TEKUMU ES-SA’ATU ‘EDHILU ‘ALE FIR’AWNE ‘ESHEDDEL-’ADHABI
WE ‘IDH JETEHAXHXHUNE FI EN-NARI FEJEKULU ED-DU’AFA’U LILLEDHINE ESTEKBERU ‘INNA KUNNA LEKUM TEBA’ÆN FEHEL ‘ENTUM MUGNUNE ‘ANNA NESIBÆN MINE EN-NARI
KALEL-LEDHINE ESTEKBERU ‘INNA KULLUN FIHA ‘INNALL-LLAHE KAD HEKEME BEJNEL-’IBADI
WE KALEL-LEDHINE FI EN-NARI LIHAZENETI XHEHENNEME ED’U REBBEKUM JUHAFFIF ‘ANNA JEWMÆN MINEL-’ADHABI
KALU ‘EWE LEM TEKU TE’TIKUM RUSULUKUM BIL-BEJJINATI KALU BELA KALU FAD’U WE MA DU’A’UL-KAFIRINE ‘ILLA FI DELALIN
‘INNA LENENSURU RUSULENA WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE JEWME JEKUMUL-’ESH/HADU
JEWME LA JENFA’U EDH-DHALIMINE MA’DHIRETUHUM WE LEHUMUL-LA’NETU WE LEHUM SU’U ED-DARI
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-HUDA WE ‘EWRETHNA BENI ‘ISRA’ILEL-KITABE
HUDEN WE DHIKRA LI’WLIL-’ELBABI
FASBIR ‘INNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN WE ESTEGFIR LIDHENBIKE WE SEBBIH BIHEMDI RABBIKE BIL-’ASHIJI WEL-’IBKARI
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JUXHADILUNE FI ‘AJATI ELLAHI BIGAJRI SULTANIN ‘ETAHUM ‘IN FI SUDURIHIM ‘ILLA KIBRUN MA HUM BIBALIGIHI FASTA’IDH BILLAHI ‘INNEHU HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-BESIRU
LEHALKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI ‘EKBERU MIN HALKI EN-NASI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
WE MA JESTEWIL-’A’MA WEL-BESIRU WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI WE LAL-MUSI’U KALILÆN MA TETEDHEKKERUNE
‘INNE ES-SA’ATE LE’ATIJETUN LA REJBE FIHA WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JU’UMINUNE
WE KALE REBBUKUM ED’UNI ‘ESTEXHIB LEKUM ‘INNEL-LEDHINE JESTEKBIRUNE ‘AN ‘IBADETI SEJEDHULUNE XHEHENNEME DAHIRINE
ELLAHUL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-LEJLE LITESKUNU FIHI WE EN-NEHARE MUBSIRÆN ‘INNALL-LLAHE LEDHU FEDLIN ‘ALA EN-NASI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JESHKURUNE
DHELIKUMU ELLAHU REBBUKUM HALIKU KULLI SHEJ’IN LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE FE’ENNA TU’UFEKUNE
KEDHALIKE JU’UFEKUL-LEDHINE KANU BI’AJATI ELLAHI JEXHHEDUNE
ELLAHUL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-’ERDE KARARÆN WE ES-SEMA’E BINA’EN WE SEWWEREKUM FE’EHSENE SUWEREKUM WE REZEKAKUM MINET-TEJJIBATI DHELIKUMU ELLAHU REBBUKUM FETEBAREKEL-LAHU REBBUL-’ALEMINE
HUWEL-HEJJU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE FAD’UHU MUHLISINE LEHU ED-DINEL-HEMDU LILLAHI RABBIL-’ALEMINE
KUL ‘INNI NUHITU ‘EN ‘A’BUDEL-LEDHINE TED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI LEMMA XHA’ENIJEL-BEJJINATU MIN RABBI WE ‘UMIRTU ‘EN ‘USLIME LIREBBIL-’ALEMINE
HUWEL-LEDHI HALEKAKUM MIN TURABIN THUMME MIN NUTFETIN THUMME MIN ‘ALEKATIN THUMME JUHRIXHUKUM TIFLÆN THUMME LITEBLUGU ‘ESHUDDEKUM THUMME LITEKUNU SHUJUHÆN WE MINKUM MEN JUTEWEFFA MIN KABLU WE LITEBLUGU ‘EXHELÆN MUSEMMEN WE LE’ALLEKUM TA’KILUNE
HUWEL-LEDHI JUHJI WE JUMITU FE’IDHA KADA ‘EMRÆN FE’INNEMA JEKULU LEHU KUN FEJEKUNU
‘ELEM TERA ‘ILAL-LEDHINE JUXHADILUNE FI ‘AJATI ELLAHI ‘ENNA JUSREFUNE
EL-LEDHINE KEDHDHEBU BIL-KITABI WE BIMA ‘ERSELNA BIHI RUSULENA FESEWFE JA’LEMUNE
‘IDHIL-’EGLALU FI ‘A’NAKIHIM WE ES-SELASILU JUSHEBUNE
FIL-HEMIMI THUMME FI EN-NARI JUSXHERUNE
THUMME KILE LEHUM ‘EJNE MA KUNTUM TUSHRIKUNE
MIN DUNI ELLAHI KALU DELLU ‘ANNA BEL LEM NEKUN NED’U MIN KABLU SHEJ’ÆN KEDHALIKE JUDILLU ELLAHUL-KAFIRINE
DHALIKUM BIMA KUNTUM TEFREHUNE FIL-’ERDI BIGAJRIL-HEKKI WE BIMA KUNTUM TEMREHUNE
EDHULU ‘EBWABE XHEHENNEME HALIDINE FIHA FEBI’SE METHWAL-MUTEKEBBIRINE
FASBIR ‘INNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN FE’IMMA NURIJENNEKE BA’DEL-LEDHI NA’IDUHUM ‘EW NETEWEFFEJENNEKE FE’ILEJNA JURXHA’UNE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA RUSULÆN MIN KABLIKE MINHUM MEN KASESNA ‘ALEJKE WE MINHUM MEN LEM NEKSUS ‘ALEJKE WE MA KANE LIRESULIN ‘EN JE’TIJE BI’AJETIN ‘ILLA BI’IDHNI ELLAHI FE’IDHA XHA’E ‘EMRU ELLAHI KUDIJE BIL-HEKKI WE HASIRE HUNALIKEL-MUBTILUNE
ELLAHUL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-’EN’AM LITERKEBU MINHA WE MINHA TE’KULUNE
WE LEKUM FIHA MENAFI’U WE LITEBLUGU ‘ALEJHA HAXHETEN FI SUDURIKUM WE ‘ALEJHA WE ‘ALEL-FULKI TUHMELUNE
WE JURIKUM ‘AJATIHI FE’EJJE ‘AJATI ELLAHI TUNKIRUNE
‘EFELEM JESIRU FIL-’ERDI FEJENDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM KANU ‘EKTHERE MINHUM WE ‘ESHEDDE KUWETEN WE ‘ATHARÆN FIL-’ERDI FEMA ‘EGNA ‘ANHUM MA KANU JEKSIBUNE
FELEMMA XHA’ET/HUM RUSULUHUM BIL-BEJJINATI FERIHU BIMA ‘INDEHUM MINEL-’ILMI WE HAKA BIHIM MA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
FELEMMA RE’EW BE’SENA KALU ‘AMENNA BILLAHI WEHDEHU WE KEFERNA BIMA KUNNA BIHI MUSHRIKINE
FELEM JEKU JENFA’UHUM ‘IMANUHUM LEMMA RE’EW BE’SENA SUNNETEL-LAHI ELLETI KAD HALET FI ‘IBADIHI WE HASIRE HUNALIKEL-KAFIRUNE
HA-MIM
TENZILUN MINE ER-REHMANI ER-REHIMI
KITABUN FUSSILET ‘AJATUHU KUR’ANÆN ‘AREBIJÆN LIKAWMIN JA’LEMUNE
BESHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN FE’A’REDE ‘EKTHERUHUM FEHUM LA JESMA’UNE
WE KALU KULUBUNA FI ‘EKINNETIN MIMMA TED’UNA ‘ILEJHI WE FI ‘ADHANINA WEKRUN WE MIN BEJNINA WE BEJNIKE HIXHABUN FA’MEL ‘INNENA ‘AMILUNE
KUL ‘INNEMA ‘ENA BESHERUN MITHLUKUM JUHA ‘ILEJJE ‘ENNEMA ‘ILEHUKUM ‘ILEHUN WAHIDUN FASTEKIMU ‘ILEJHI WE ESTEGFIRUHU WE WEJLUN LILMUSHRIKINE
EL-LEDHINE LA JU’UTUNE EZ-ZEKÆTE WE HUM BIL-’AHIRETI HUM KAFIRUNE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LEHUM ‘EXHRUN GAJRU MEMNUNIN
KUL ‘E’INNEKUM LETEKFURUNE BIEL-LEDHI HALEKAL-’ERDE FI JEWMEJNI WE TEXH’ALUNE LEHU ‘ENDADÆN DHALIKE REBBUL-’ALEMINE
WE XHE’ALE FIHA REWASIJE MIN FEWKIHA WE BAREKE FIHA WE KADDERE FIHA ‘EKWATEHA FI ‘ERBE’ATI ‘EJJAMIN SEWA’EN LILSSA’ILINE
THUMME ESTEWA ‘ILA ES-SEMA’I WE HIJE DUHANUN FEKALE LEHA WE LIL’ERDI EI’TIJA TEW’ÆN ‘EW KERHÆN KALETA ‘ETEJNA TA’I’INE
FEKADAHUNNE SEB’A SEMAWATIN FI JEWMEJNI WE ‘EWHA FI KULLI SEMA’IN ‘EMREHA WE ZEJJENNA ES-SEMA’E ED-DUNJA BIMESABIHE WE HIFDHÆN DHALIKE TEKDIRUL-’AZIZIL-’ALIMI
FE’IN ‘A’REDU FEKUL ‘ENDHERTUKUM SA’IKATEN MITHLE SA’IKATI ‘ADIN WE THEMUDE
‘IDH XHA’ET/HUMU ER-RUSULU MIN BEJNI ‘EJDIHIM WE MIN HALFIHIM ‘ELLA TA’BUDU ‘ILLALLAHE KALU LEW SHA’E REBBUNA LE’ENZELE MELA’IKETEN FE’INNA BIMA ‘URSILTUM BIHI KAFIRUNE
FE’EMMA ‘ADUN FASTEKBERU FIL-’ERDI BIGAJRIL-HEKKI WE KALU MEN ‘ESHEDDU MINNA KUWETEN ‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNEL-LAHEL-LEDHI HALEKAHUM HUWE ‘ESHEDDU MINHUM KUWETEN WE KANU BI’AJATINA JEXHHEDUNE
FE’ERSELNA ‘ALEJHIM RIHÆN SERSERÆN FI ‘EJJAMIN NEHISATIN LINUDHIKAHUM ‘ADHABEL-HIZJI FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE LE’ADHABUL-’AHIRETI ‘EHZA WE HUM LA JUNSERUNE
WE ‘EMMA THEMUDU FEHEDEJNAHUM FASTEHEBBUL-’AMA ‘ALEL-HUDA FE’EHADHET/HUM SA’IKATUL-’ADHABIL-HUNI BIMA KANU JEKSIBUNE
WE NEXHXHEJNAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE KANU JETTEKUNE
WE JEWME JUHSHERU ‘A’DA’U ELLAHI ‘ILA EN-NARI FEHUM JUZA’UNE
HETTA ‘IDHA MA XHA’UHA SHEHIDE ‘ALEJHIM SEM’UHUM WE ‘EBSARUHUM WE XHULUDUHUM BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
WE KALU LIXHULUDIHIM LIME SHEHIDTUM ‘ALEJNA KALU ‘ENTEKANALLAHUL-LEDHI ‘ENTEKA KULLE SHEJ’IN WE HUWE HALEKAKUM ‘EWWELE MERRETIN WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
WE MA KUNTUM TESTETIRUNE ‘EN JESH/HEDE ‘ALEJKUM SEM’UKUM WE LA ‘EBSARUKUM WE LA XHULUDUKUM WE LEKIN DHENENTUM ‘ENNEL-LAHE LA JA’LEMU KETHIRÆN MIMMA TA’MELUNE
WE DHELIKUM DHENNUKUMUL-LEDHI DHENENTUM BIREBBIKUM ‘ERDAKUM FE’ESBEHTUM MINEL-HASIRINE
FE’IN JESBIRU FALNNARU METHWEN LEHUM WE ‘IN JESTA’TIBU FEMA HUM MINEL-MU’TEBINE
WE KAJJEDNA LEHUM KURENA’E FEZEJJENU LEHUM MA BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE MA HALFEHUM WE HEKKA ‘ALEJHIMUL-KAWLU FI ‘UMEMIN KAD HALET MIN KABLIHIM MINEL-XHINNI WEL-’INSI ‘INNEHUM KANU HASIRINE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LA TESMA’U LIHEDHAL-KUR’ANI WEL-GAW FIHI LE’ALLEKUM TEGLIBUNE
FELENUDHIKANNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘ADHABÆN SHEDIDÆN WE LENEXHZIJENNEHUM ‘ESWE’EL-LEDHI KANU JA’MELUNE
DHALIKE XHEZA’U ‘A’DA’I ELLAHI EN-NARU LEHUM FIHA DARUL-HULDI XHEZA’EN BIMA KANU BI’AJATINA JEXHHEDUNE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU REBBENA ‘ERINAL-LEDHEJNI ‘EDELLANA MINEL-XHINNI WEL-’INSI NEXH’ALHUMA TEHTE ‘EKDAMINA LIJEKUNA MINEL-’ESFELINE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KALU REBBUNALLAHU THUMME ESTEKAMU TETENEZZELU ‘ALEJHIMUL-MELA’IKETU ‘ELLA TEHAFU WE LA TEHZENU WE ‘EBSHIRU BIL-XHENNETI ELLETI KUNTUM TU’ADUNE
NEHNU ‘EWLIJA’UUKUM FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE FIL-’AHIRETI WE LEKUM FIHA MA TESHTEHI ‘ENFUSUKUM WE LEKUM FIHA MA TEDDA’UNE
NUZULÆN MIN GAFURIN REHIMIN
WE MEN ‘EHSENU KAWLÆN MIMMEN DA’A ‘ILA ELLAHI WE ‘AMILE SALIHÆN WE KALE ‘INNENI MINEL-MUSLIMINE
WE LA TESTEWIL-HESENETU WE LA ES-SEJJI’ETU EDFA’ BI-ETI HIJE ‘EHSENU FE’IDHAL-LEDHI BEJNEKE WE BEJNEHU ‘ADAWETUN KE’ENNEHU WE LIJUN HEMIMUN
WE MA JULEKKAHA ‘ILLAL-LEDHINE SEBERU WE MA JULEKKAHA ‘ILLA DHU HEDHDHIN ‘ADHIMIN
WE ‘IMMA JENZEGANNEKE MINE ESH-SHEJTANI NEZGUN FASTA’IDH BILLAHI ‘INNEHU HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-’ALIMU
WE MIN ‘AJATIHIL-LEJLU WE EN-NEHARU WE ESH-SHEMSU WEL-KAMERU LA TESXHUDU LILSHSHEMSI WE LA LILKAMERI WE ESXHUDU LILLAHIL-LEDHI HALEKAHUNNE ‘IN KUNTUM ‘IJAHU TA’BUDUNE
FE’INI ESTEKBERU FE-EL-LEDHINE ‘INDE RABBIKE JUSEBBIHUNE LEHU BIL-LEJLI WE EN-NEHARI WE HUM LA JES’EMUNE
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI ‘ENNEKE TERAL-’ERDE HASHI’ATEN FE’IDHA ‘ENZELNA ‘ALEJHAL-MA’E EHTEZZET WE REBET ‘INNEL-LEDHI ‘EHJAHA LEMUHJIL-MEWTA ‘INNEHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JULHIDUNE FI ‘AJATINA LA JEHFEWNE ‘ALEJNA ‘EFEMEN JULKA FI EN-NARI HAJRUN ‘EM MEN JE’TI ‘AMINÆN JEWMEL-KIJAMETI A’MELU MA SHI’TUM ‘INNEHU BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BIDH-DHIKRI LEMMA XHA’EHUM WE ‘INNEHU LEKITABUN ‘AZIZUN
LA JE’TIHIL-BATILU MIN BEJNI JEDEJHI WE LA MIN HALFIHI TENZILUN MIN HEKIMIN HEMIDIN
MA JUKALU LEKE ‘ILLA MA KAD KILE LILRRUSULI MIN KABLIKE ‘INNE REBBEKE LEDHU MEGFIRETIN WE DHU ‘IKABIN ‘ELIMIN
WE LEW XHE’ALNAHU KUR’ANÆN ‘A’XHEMIJÆN LEKALU LEWLA FUSSILET ‘AJATUHU ‘E’A’XHEMIJUN WE ‘AREBIJUN KUL HUWE LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU HUDEN WE SHIFA’UN WEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE FI ‘ADHANIHIM WEKRUN WE HUWE ‘ALEJHIM ‘AMEN ‘ULA’IKE JUNADEWNE MIN MEKANIN BA’IDIN
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA MUSAL-KITABE FAHTULIFE FIHI WE LEWLA KELIMETUN SEBEKAT MIN RABBIKE LEKUDIJE BEJNEHUM WE ‘INNEHUM LEFI SHEKKIN MINHU MURIBIN
MEN ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FELINEFSIHI WE MEN ‘ESA’E FE’ALEJHA WE MA REBBUKE BIDHELLAMIN LIL’ABIDI
‘ILEJHI JUREDDU ‘ILMU ES-SA’ATI WE MA TEHRUXHU MIN THEMERATIN MIN ‘EKMAMIHA WE MA TEHMILU MIN ‘UNTHA WE LA TEDA’U ‘ILLA BI’ILMIHI WE JEWME JUNADIHIM ‘EJNE SHUREKA’I KALU ‘ADHENNAKE MA MINNA MIN SHEHIDIN
WE DELLE ‘ANHUM MA KANU JED’UNE MIN KABLU WE DHENNU MA LEHUM MIN MEHISIN
LA JES’EMUL-’INSANU MIN DU’A’IL-HAJRI WE ‘IN MESSEHU ESH-SHERRU FEJE’USUN KANUTUN
WE LE’IN ‘EDHEKNAHU REHMETEN MINNA MIN BA’DI DERRA’E MESSET/HU LEJEKULENNE HADHA LI WE MA ‘EDHUNNU ES-SA’ATE KA’IMETEN WE LE’IN RUXHI’TU ‘ILA RABBI ‘INNE LI ‘INDEHU LELHUSNA FELENUNEBBI’ENNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BIMA ‘AMILU WE LENUDHIKANNEHUM MIN ‘ADHABIN GALI
WE ‘IDHA ‘EN’AMNA ‘ALEL-’INSANI ‘A’REDE WE NE’A BIXHANIBIHI WE ‘IDHA MESSEHU ESH-SHERRU FEDHU DU’A’IN ‘ARIDIN
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN KANE MIN ‘INDI ELLAHI THUMME KEFERTUM BIHI MEN ‘EDELLU MIMMEN HUWE FI SHIKAKIN BA’IDIN
SENURIHIM ‘AJATINA FIL-’AFAKI WE FI ‘ENFUSIHIM HETTA JETEBEJJENE LEHUM ‘ENNEHUL-HEKKU ‘EWELEM JEKFI BIREBBIKE ‘ENNEHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN SHEHIDUN
‘ELA ‘INNEHUM FI MIRJETIN MIN LIKA’I RABBIHIM ‘ELA ‘INNEHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN MUHITUN
HA-MIM
‘SK
KEDHALIKE JUHI ‘ILEJKE WE ‘ILAL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIKEL-LAHUL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE HUWEL-’ALIJUL-’ADHIMU
TEKADU ES-SEMAWATU JETEFETTERNE MIN FEWKIHINNE WEL-MELA’IKETU JUSEBBIHUNE BIHEMDI RABBIHIM WE JESTEGFIRUNE LIMEN FIL-’ERDI ‘ELA ‘INNALL-LLAHE HUWEL-GAFURU ER-REHIMU
WEL-LEDHINE ETTEHADHU MIN DUNIHI ‘EWLIJA’EL-LAHU HEFIDHUN ‘ALEJHIM WE MA ‘ENTE ‘ALEJHIM BIWEKILIN
WE KEDHELIKE ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE KUR’ANÆN ‘AREBIJÆN LITUNDHIRE ‘UMMEL-KURA WE MEN HEWLEHA WE TUNDHIRE JEWMEL-XHEM’I LA REJBE FIHI FERIKUN FIL-XHENNETI WE FERIKUN FI ES-SA’IRI
WE LEW SHA’EL-LAHU LEXHE’ALEHUM ‘UMMETEN WAHIDETEN WE LEKIN JUDHILU MEN JESHA’U FI REHMETIHI WE EDH-DHALIMUNE MA LEHUM MIN WE LIJIN WE LA NESIRIN
‘EM ETTEHADHU MIN DUNIHI ‘EWLIJA’E FE-ELLAHU HUWEL-WELIJU WE HUWE JUHJIL-MEWTA WE HUWE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
WE MA EHTELEFTUM FIHI MIN SHEJ’IN FEHUKMUHU ‘ILA ELLAHI DHELIKUMU ELLAHU RABBI ‘ALEJHI TEWEKKELTU WE ‘ILEJHI ‘UNIBU
FATIRU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI XHE’ALE LEKUM MIN ‘ENFUSIKUM ‘EZWAXHÆN WE MINEL-’EN’AM ‘EZWAXHÆN JEDHRE’UUKUM FIHI LEJSE KEMITHLIHI SHEJ’UN WE HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-BESIRU
LEHU MEKALIDU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI JEBSUTU ER-RIZKA LIMEN JESHA’U WE JEKDIRU ‘INNEHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMUN
SHERE’A LEKUM MINE ED-DINI MA WESSA BIHI NUHÆN WEL-LEDHI ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE WE MA WESSEJNA BIHI ‘IBRAHIME WE MUSA WE ‘ISA ‘EN ‘EKIMU ED-DINE WE LA TETEFERREKU FIHI KEBURE ‘ALEL-MUSHRIKINE MA TED’UHUM ‘ILEJHI ELLAHU JEXHTEBI ‘ILEJHI MEN JESHA’U WE JEHDI ‘ILE
WE MA TEFERREKU ‘ILLA MIN BA’DI MA XHA’EHUMUL-’ILMU BEGJÆN BEJNEHUM WE LEWLA KELIMETUN SEBEKAT MIN RABBIKE ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN LEKUDIJE BEJNEHUM WE ‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘URITHUL-KITABE MIN BA’DIHIM LEFI SHEKKIN MINHU MURIBIN
FELIDHELIKE FAD’U WE ESTEKIM KEMA ‘UMIRTE WE LA TETTEBI’ ‘EHWA’EHUM WE KUL ‘AMENTU BIMA ‘ENZELEL-LAHU MIN KITABIN WE ‘UMIRTU LI’’DILE BEJNEKUMU ELLAHU REBBUNA WE REBBUKUM LENA ‘A’MALUNA WE LEKUM ‘A’MALUKUM LA HUXHXHETE BEJNENA WE BEJNEKUMU ELLAHU JEXHMA’U
WEL-LEDHINE JUHAXHXHUNE FI ELLAHI MIN BA’DI MA ESTUXHIBE LEHU HUXHXHETUHUM DAHIDETUN ‘INDE RABBIHIM WE ‘ALEJHIM GADEBUN WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN SHEDIDUN
ELLAHUL-LEDHI ‘ENZELEL-KITABE BIL-HEKKI WEL-MIZANE WE MA JUDRIKE LE’ALLE ES-SA’ATE KARIBUN
JESTA’XHILU BIHAL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIHA WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU MUSHFIKUNE MINHA WE JA’LEMUNE ‘ENNEHAL-HEKKU ‘ELA ‘INNEL-LEDHINE JUMARUNE FI ES-SA’ATI LEFI DELALIN BA’IDIN
ELLAHU LETIFUN BI’IBADIHI JERZUKU MEN JESHA’U WE HUWEL-KAWIJUL-’AZIZU
MEN KANE JURIDU HERTHEL-’AHIRETI NEZID LEHU FI HERTHIHI WE MEN KANE JURIDU HERTHE ED-DUNJA NU’UTIHI MINHA WE MA LEHU FIL-’AHIRETI MIN NESIBIN
‘EM LEHUM SHUREKA’U SHERA’U LEHUM MINE ED-DINI MA LEM JE’DHEN BIHI ELLAHU WE LEWLA KELIMETUL-FESLI LEKUDIJE BEJNEHUM WE ‘INNE EDH-DHALIMINE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
TERA EDH-DHALIMINE MUSHFIKINE MIMMA KESEBU WE HUWE WAKI’UN BIHIM WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI FI REWDATIL-XHENNATI LEHUM MA JESHA’UNE ‘INDE RABBIHIM DHALIKE HUWEL-FEDLUL-KEBIRU
DHALIKEL-LEDHI JUBESHSHIRU ELLAHU ‘IBADEHUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI KUL LA ‘ES’ELUKUM ‘ALEJHI ‘EXHRÆN ‘ILLAL-MEWEDDETE FIL-KURBA WE MEN JEKTERIF HESENETEN NEZID LEHU FIHA HUSNÆN ‘INNALL-LLAHE GAFURUN SHEKURUN
‘EM JEKULUNE EFTERA ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN FE’IN JESHE’I ELLAHU JEHTIM ‘ALA KALBIKE WE JEMHU ELLAHUL-BATILE WE JUHIKKUL-HEKKA BIKELIMATIHI ‘INNEHU ‘ALIMUN BIDHATI ES-SUDURI
WE HUWEL-LEDHI JEKBELUT-TEWBET ‘AN ‘IBADIHI WE JA’FU ‘ANI ES-SEJJI’ATI WE JA’LEMU MA TEF’ALUNE
WE JESTEXHIBUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI WE JEZIDUHUM MIN FEDLIHI WEL-KAFIRUNE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN SHEDIDUN
WE LEW BESETEL-LAHU ER-RIZKA LI’IBADIHI LEBEGAW FIL-’ERDI WE LEKIN JUNEZZILU BIKADERIN MA JESHA’U ‘INNEHU BI’IBADIHI HABIRUN BESIRUN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI JUNEZZILUL-GAJTHE MIN BA’DI MA KANETU WE JENSHURU REHMETEHU WE HUWEL-WELIJUL-HEMIDU
WE MIN ‘AJATIHI HALKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BETHTHE FIHIMA MIN DABBETIN WE HUWE ‘ALA XHEM’IHIM ‘IDHA JESHA’U KADIRUN
WE MA ‘ESABEKUM MIN MUSIBETIN FEBIMA KESEBET ‘EJDIKUM WE JA’FU ‘AN KETHIRIN
WE MA ‘ENTUM BIMU’XHIZINE FIL-’ERDI WE MA LEKUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI MIN WE LIJIN WE LA NESIRIN
WE MIN ‘AJATIHIL-XHEWARI FIL-BEHRI KAL’A’LAMI
‘IN JESHE’ JUSKINI ER-RIHE FEJEDHLELNE REWAKIDE ‘ALA DHEHRIHI ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKULLI SEBBARIN SHEKURIN
‘EW JUBIKHUNNE BIMA KESEBU WE JA’FU ‘AN KETHIRIN
WE JA’LEMEL-LEDHINE JUXHADILUNE FI ‘AJATINA MA LEHUM MIN MEHISIN
FEMA ‘UTITUM MIN SHEJ’IN FEMETA’UL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE MA ‘INDEL-LAHI HAJRUN WE ‘EBKA LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘ALA RABBIHIM JETEWEKKELUNE
WEL-LEDHINE JEXHTENIBUNE KEBA’IREL-’ITHMI WEL-FEWAHISHE WE ‘IDHA MA GADIBU HUM JEGFIRUNE
WEL-LEDHINE ESTEXHABU LIREBBIHIM WE ‘EKAMU ES-SELÆTE WE ‘EMRUHUM SHURA BEJNEHUM WE MIMMA REZEKNAHUM JUNFIKUNE
WEL-LEDHINE ‘IDHA ‘ESABEHUMUL-BEGJU HUM JENTESIRUNE
WE XHEZA’U SEJJI’ETIN SEJJI’ETUN MITHLUHA FEMEN ‘AFA WE ‘ESLEHE FE’EXHRUHU ‘ALA ELLAHI ‘INNEHU LA JUHIBBU EDH-DHALIMINE
WE LEMENI ENTESERE BA’DE DHULMIHI FE’ULA’IKE MA ‘ALEJHIM MIN SEBILIN
‘INNEMA ES-SEBILU ‘ALEL-LEDHINE JEDHLIMUNE EN-NASE WE JEBGUNE FIL-’ERDI BIGAJRIL-HEKKI ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
WE LEMEN SEBERE WE GAFERE ‘INNE DHALIKE LEMIN ‘AZMIL-’UMURI
WE MEN JUDLILI ELLAHU FEMA LEHU MIN WE LIJIN MIN BA’DIHI WE TERA EDH-DHALIMINE LEMMA RE’EWL-’ADHABE JEKULUNE HEL ‘ILA MEREDDIN MIN SEBILIN
WE TERAHUM JU’REDUNE ‘ALEJHA HASHI’INE MINE EDH-DHULLI JENDHURUNE MIN TERFIN HAFIJIN WE KALEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘INNEL-HASIRINEL-LEDHINE HASIRU ‘ENFUSEHUM WE ‘EHLIHIM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI ‘ELA ‘INNE EDH-DHALIMINE FI ‘ADHABIN MUKIMIN
WE MA KANE LEHUM MIN ‘EWLIJA’E JENSURUNEHUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI WE MEN JUDLILI ELLAHU FEMA LEHU MIN SEBILIN
ESTEXHIBU LIREBBIKUM MIN KABLI ‘EN JE’TIJE JEWMUN LA MEREDDE LEHU MINEL-LAHI MA LEKUM MIN MELXHE’IIN JEWME’IDHIN WE MA LEKUM MIN NEKIRIN
FE’IN ‘A’REDU FEMA ‘ERSELNAKE ‘ALEJHIM HEFIDHÆN ‘IN ‘ALEJKE ‘ILLAL-BELAGU WE ‘INNA ‘IDHA ‘EDHEKNAL-’INSANE MINNA REHMETEN FERIHE BIHA WE ‘IN TUSIBHUM SEJJI’ETUN BIMA KADDEMET ‘EJDIHIM FE’INNEL-’INSANE KEFURUN
LILLAHI MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI JEHLUKU MA JESHA’U JEHEBU LIMEN JESHA’U ‘INATHÆN WE JEHEBU LIMEN JESHA’U EDH-DHUKURE
‘EW JUZEWWIXHUHUM DHUKRANÆN WE ‘INATHÆN WE JEXH’ALU MEN JESHA’U ‘AKIMÆN ‘INNEHU ‘ALIMUN KADIRUN
WE MA KANE LIBESHERIN ‘EN JUKELLIMEHU ELLAHU ‘ILLA WEHJÆN ‘EW MIN WERA’I HIXHABIN ‘EW JURSILE RESULÆN FEJUHIJE BI’IDHNIHI MA JESHA’U ‘INNEHU ‘ALIJUN HEKIMUN
WE KEDHELIKE ‘EWHEJNA ‘ILEJKE RUHÆN MIN ‘EMRINA MA KUNTE TEDRI MAL-KITABU WE LAL-’IMANU WE LEKIN XHE’ALNAHU NURÆN NEHDI BIHI MEN NESHA’U MIN ‘IBADINA WE ‘INNEKE LETEHDI ‘ILA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
SIRATI ELLAHIL-LEDHI LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI ‘ELA ‘ILA ELLAHI TESIRUL-’UMURU
HA-MIM
WEL-KITABIL-MUBINI
‘INNA XHE’ALNAHU KUR’ANÆN ‘AREBIJÆN LE’ALLEKUM TA’KILUNE
WE ‘INNEHU FI ‘UMMIL-KITABI LEDEJNA LE’ALIJUN HEKIMUN
‘EFENEDRIBU ‘ANKUMU EDH-DHIKRE SEFHÆN ‘EN KUNTUM KAWMÆN MUSRIFINE
WE KEM ‘ERSELNA MIN NEBIJIN FIL-’EWWELINE
WE MA JE’TIHIM MIN NEBIJIN ‘ILLA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
FE’EHLEKNA ‘ESHEDDE MINHUM BETSHÆN WE MEDA METHELUL-’EWWELINE
WE LE’IN SE’ELTEHUM MEN HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE LEJEKULUNNE HALEKAHUNNEL-’AZIZUL-’ALIMU
EL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-’ERDE MEHDÆN WE XHE’ALE LEKUM FIHA SUBULÆN LE’ALLEKUM TEHTEDUNE
WEL-LEDHI NEZZELE MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN BIKADERIN FE’ENSHERNA BIHI BELDETEN MEJTÆN KEDHALIKE TUHREXHUNE
WEL-LEDHI HALEKAL-’EZWAXHE KULLEHA WE XHE’ALE LEKUM MINEL-FULKI WEL-’EN’AM MA TERKEBUNE
LITESTEWU ‘ALA DHUHURIHI THUMME TEDHKURU NI’METE RABBIKUM ‘IDHA ESTEWEJTUM ‘ALEJHI WE TEKULU SUBHANEL-LEDHI SEHHARE LENA HADHA WE MA KUNNA LEHU MUKRININE
WE ‘INNA ‘ILA RABBINA LEMUNKALIBUNE
WE XHE’ALU LEHU MIN ‘IBADIHI XHUZ’ÆN ‘INNEL-’INSANE LEKEFURUN MUBINUN
‘EM ETTEHADHE MIMMA JEHLUKU BENATIN WE ‘ESFAKUM BIL-BENINE
WE ‘IDHA BUSHSHIRE ‘EHEDUHUM BIMA DEREBE LILRREHMENI METHELÆN DHELLE WEXHHUHU MUSWEDDÆN WE HUWE KEDHIMUN
‘EWEMEN JUNESHSHE’U FIL-HILJETI WE HUWE FIL-HISAMI GAJRU MUBININ
WE XHE’ALUL-MELA’IKETEL-LEDHINE HUM ‘IBADU ER-REHMANI ‘INATHÆN ‘ESHEHIDU HALKAHUM SETUKTEBU SHEHADETUHUM WE JUS’ELUNE
WE KALU LEW SHA’E ER-REHMANU MA ‘ABEDNAHUM MA LEHUM BIDHALIKE MIN ‘ILMIN ‘IN HUM ‘ILLA JEHRUSUNE
‘EM ‘ATEJNAHUM KITABÆN MIN KABLIHI FEHUM BIHI MUSTEMSIKUNE
BEL KALU ‘INNA WEXHEDNA ‘ABA’ENA ‘ALA ‘UMMETIN WE ‘INNA ‘ALA ‘ATHARIHIM MUHTEDUNE
WE KEDHELIKE MA ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE FI KARJETIN MIN NEDHIRIN ‘ILLA KALE MUTREFUHA ‘INNA WEXHEDNA ‘ABA’ENA ‘ALA ‘UMMETIN WE ‘INNA ‘ALA ‘ATHARIHIM MUKTEDUNE
KALE ‘EWELEW XHI’TUKUM BI’EHDA MIMMA WEXHEDTUM ‘ALEJHI ‘ABA’EKUM KALU ‘INNA BIMA ‘URSILTUM BIHI KAFIRUNE
FANTEKAMNA MINHUM FANDHUR KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-MUKEDHDHIBINE
WE ‘IDH KALE ‘IBRAHIMU LI’EBIHI WE KAWMIHI ‘INNENI BERA’UN MIMMA TA’BUDUNE
‘ILLAL-LEDHI FETERENI FE’INNEHU SEJEHDINI
WE XHE’ALEHA KELIMETEN BAKIJETEN FI ‘AKIBIHI LE’ALLEHUM JERXHI’UNE
BEL METTA’TU HA’UULA’ WE ‘ABA’EHUM HETTA XHA’EHUMUL-HEKKU WE RESULUN MUBINUN
WE LEMMA XHA’EHUMUL-HEKKU KALU HADHA SIHRUN WE ‘INNA BIHI KAFIRUNE
WE KALU LEWLA NUZZILE HADHAL-KUR’ANU ‘ALA REXHULIN MINEL-KARJETEJNI ‘ADHIMIN
‘EHUM JEKSIMUNE REHMETE RABBIKE NEHNU KASEMNA BEJNEHUM MA’ISHETEHUM FIL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WE REFA’NA BA’DEHUM FEWKA BA’DIN DEREXHATIN LIJETTEHIDHE BA’DUHUM BA’DÆN SUHRIJÆN WE REHMETU RABBIKE HAJRUN MIMMA JEXHMA’UNE
WE LEWLA ‘EN JEKUNE EN-NASU ‘UMMETEN WAHIDETEN LEXHE’ALNA LIMEN JEKFURU BIR-REHMENI LIBUJUTIHIM SUKUFÆN MIN FEDDETIN WE MA’ARIXHE ‘ALEJHA JEDHHERUNE
WE LIBUJUTIHIM ‘EBWABÆN WE SURURÆN ‘ALEJHA JETTEKI’UNE
WE ZUHRUFÆN WE ‘IN KULLU DHALIKE LEMMA META’UL-HEJÆTI ED-DUNJA WEL-’AHIRETU ‘INDE RABBIKE LILMUTTEKINE
WE MEN JA’SHU ‘AN DHIKRI ER-REHMANI NUKAJJID LEHU SHEJTANÆN FEHUWE LEHU KARINUN
WE ‘INNEHUM LEJESUDDUNEHUM ‘ANI ES-SEBILI WE JEHSEBUNE ‘ENNEHUM MUHTEDUNE
HETTA ‘IDHA XHA’ENA KALE JA LEJTE BEJNI WE BEJNEKE BU’DEL-MESHRIKAJNI FEBI’SEL-KARINU
WE LEN JENFE’AKUMUL-JEWME ‘IDH DHELEMTUM ‘ENNEKUM FIL-’ADHABI MUSHTERIKUNE
‘EFE’ENTE TUSMI’U ES-SUMME ‘EW TEHDIL-’UMJE WE MEN KANE FI DELALIN MUBININ
FE’IMMA NEDH/HEBENNE BIKE FE’INNA MINHUM MUNTEKIMUNE
‘EW NURIJENNEKEL-LEDHI WE’ADNAHUM FE’INNA ‘ALEJHIM MUKTEDIRUNE
FASTEMSIK BIEL-LEDHI ‘UHIJE ‘ILEJKE ‘INNEKE ‘ALA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
WE ‘INNEHU LEDHIKRUN LEKE WE LIKAWMIKE WE SEWFE TUS’ELUNE
WE ES’EL MEN ‘ERSELNA MIN KABLIKE MIN RUSULINA ‘EXHE’ALNA MIN DUNI ER-REHMANI ‘ALIHETEN JU’BEDUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA MUSA BI’AJATINA ‘ILA FIR’AWNE WE MELE’IHI FEKALE ‘INNI RESULU RABBIL-’ALEMINE
FELEMMA XHA’EHUM BI’AJATINA ‘IDHA HUM MINHA JEDHEKUNE
WE MA NURIHIM MIN ‘AJETIN ‘ILLA HIJE ‘EKBERU MIN ‘UHTIHA WE ‘EHADHNAHUM BIL-’ADHABI LE’ALLEHUM JERXHI’UNE
WE KALU JA ‘EJJUHA ES-SAHIRU ED’U LENA REBBEKE BIMA ‘AHIDE ‘INDEKE ‘INNENA LEMUHTEDUN
FELEMMA KESHEFNA ‘ANHUMUL-’ADHABE ‘IDHA HUM JENKUTHUNE
WE NADA FIR’AWNU FI KAWMIHI KALE JA KAWMI ‘ELEJSE LI MULKU MISRE WE HEDHIHIL-’ENHARU TEXHRI MIN TEHTI ‘EFELA TUBSIRUNE
‘EM ‘ENA HAJRUN MIN HADHAL-LEDHI HUWE MEHINUN WE LA JEKADU JUBINU
FELEWLA ‘ULKIJE ‘ALEJHI ‘ESWIRETUN MIN DHEHEBIN ‘EW XHA’E ME’AHUL-MELA’IKETU MUKTERININE
FASTEHAFFE KAWMEHU FE’ETA’UHU ‘INNEHUM KANU KAWMÆN FASIKINE
FELEMMA ‘ASEFUNA ENTEKAMNA MINHUM FE’EGREKNAHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
FEXHE’ALNAHUM SELEFÆN WE METHELÆN LIL’AHIRINE
WE LEMMA DURIBE EBNU MERJEME METHELÆN ‘IDHA KAWMUKE MINHU JESIDDUNE
WE KALU ‘E’ALIHETUNA HAJRUN ‘EM HUWE MA DEREBUHU LEKE ‘ILLA XHEDELÆN BEL HUM KAWMUN HASIMUNE
‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA ‘ABDUN ‘EN’AMNA ‘ALEJHI WE XHE’ALNAHU METHELÆN LIBENI ‘ISRA’ILE
WE LEW NESHA’U LEXHE’ALNA MINKUM MELA’IKETEN FIL-’ERDI JEHLUFUNE
WE ‘INNEHU LA’ILMUN LILSSA’ATI FELA TEMTERUNNE BIHA WE ETTEBI’UNI HADHA SIRATUN MUSTEKIMUN
WE LA JESUDDENNEKUMU ESH-SHEJTANU ‘INNEHU LEKUM ‘ADUWUN MUBINUN
WE LEMMA XHA’E ‘ISA BIL-BEJJINATI KALE KAD XHI’TUKUM BIL-HIKMETI WE LI’EBEJJINE LEKUM BA’DEL-LEDHI TEHTELIFUNE FIHI FE ETTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’UNI
‘INNALL-LLAHE HUWE RABBI WE REBBUKUM FA’BUDUHU HADHA SIRATUN MUSTEKIMUN
FAHTELEFEL-’EHZABU MIN BEJNIHIM FEWEJLUN LILLEDHINE DHELEMU MIN ‘ADHABI JEWMIN ‘ELIMIN
HEL JENDHURUNE ‘ILLA ES-SA’ATE ‘EN TE’TIJEHUM BEGTETEN WE HUM LA JESH’URUNE
EL-’EHILLA’U JEWME’IDHIN BA’DUHUM LIBA’DIN ‘ADUWUN ‘ILLAL-MUTTEKINE
JA ‘IBADI LA HAWFUN ‘ALEJKUMUL-JEWME WE LA ‘ENTUM TEHZENUNE
EL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU BI’AJATINA WE KANU MUSLIMINE
EDHULUL-XHENNETE ‘ENTUM WE ‘EZWAXHUKUM TUHBERUNE
JUTAFU ‘ALEJHIM BISIHAFIN MIN DHEHEBIN WE ‘EKWABIN WE FIHA MA TESHTEHIHIL-’ENFUSU WE TELEDHDHUL-’A’JUNU WE ‘ENTUM FIHA HALIDUNE
WE TILKEL-XHENNETU ELLETI ‘URITHTUMUHA BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
LEKUM FIHA FAKIHETUN KETHIRETUN MINHA TE’KULUNE
‘INNEL-MUXHRIMINE FI ‘ADHABI XHEHENNEME HALIDUN
LA JUFETTERU ‘ANHUM WE HUM FIHI MUBLISUNE
WE MA DHELEMNAHUM WE LEKIN KANU HUMU EDH-DHALIMINE
WE NADEW JA MALIKU LIJEKDI ‘ALEJNA REBBUKE KALE ‘INNEKUM MAKITHUNE
LEKAD XHI’NAKUM BIL-HEKKI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHEREKUM LILHEKKI KARIHUNE
‘EM ‘EBREMU ‘EMRÆN FE’INNA MUBRIMUNE
‘EM JEHSEBUNE ‘ENNA LA NESMA’U SIRREHUM WE NEXHWAHUM BELA WE RUSULUNA LEDEJHIM JEKTUBUNE
KUL ‘IN KANE LILRREHMENI WELEDUN FE’ENA ‘EWWELUL-’ABIDINE
SUBHANE RABBI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI RABBIL-’ARSHI ‘AMMA JESIFUNE
FEDHERHUM JEHUDU WE JEL’ABU HETTA JULAKU JEWMEHUMUL-LEDHI JU’ADUNE
WE HUWEL-LEDHI FI ES-SEMA’I ‘ILEHUN WE FIL-’ERDI ‘ILEHUN WE HUWEL-HEKIMUL-’ALIMU
WE TEBAREKEL-LEDHI LEHU MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMA WE ‘INDEHU ‘ILMU ES-SA’ATI WE ‘ILEJHI TURXHA’UNE
WE LA JEMLIKUL-LEDHINE JED’UNE MIN DUNIHI ESH-SHEFA’ATE ‘ILLA MEN SHEHIDE BIL-HEKKI WE HUM JA’LEMUNE
WE LE’IN SE’ELTEHUM MEN HALEKAHUM LEJEKULUNNEL-LAHU FE’ENNA JU’UFEKUNE
WE KILIHI JA RABBI ‘INNE HA’UULA’ KAWMUN LA JU’UMINUNE
FASFEH ‘ANHUM WE KUL SELAMUN FESEWFE JA’LEMUNE
HA-MIM
WEL-KITABIL-MUBINI
‘INNA ‘ENZELNAHU FI LEJLETIN MUBAREKETIN ‘INNA KUNNA MUNDHIRINE
FIHA JUFREKU KULLU ‘EMRIN HEKIMIN
‘EMRÆN MIN ‘INDINA ‘INNA KUNNA MURSILINE
REHMETEN MIN RABBIKE ‘INNEHU HUWE ES-SEMI’UL-’ALIMU
REBBI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE MA BEJNEHUMA ‘IN KUNTUM MUKININE
LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE JUHJI WE JUMITU REBBUKUM WE REBBU ‘ABA’IKUMUL-’EWWELINE
BEL HUM FI SHEKKIN JEL’ABUNE
FARTEKIB JEWME TE’TI ES-SEMA’U BIDUHANIN MUBININ
JEGSHA EN-NASE HADHA ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
REBBENA EKSHIF ‘ANNAL-’ADHABE ‘INNA MU’UMINUNE
‘ENNA LEHUMU EDH-DHIKRA WE KAD XHA’EHUM RESULUN MUBINUN
THUMME TEWELLEW ‘ANHU WE KALU MU’ALLEMUN MEXHNUNUN
‘INNA KASHIFUL-’ADHABI KALILÆN ‘INNEKUM ‘A’IDUNE
JEWME NEBTISHUL-BETSHETEL-KUBRA ‘INNA MUNTEKIMUNE
WE LEKAD FETENNA KABLEHUM KAWME FIR’AWNE WE XHA’EHUM RESULUN KERIMUN
‘EN ‘EDDU ‘ILEJJE ‘IBADEL-LAHI ‘INNI LEKUM RESULUN ‘EMINUN
WE ‘EN LA TA’LU ‘ALA ELLAHI ‘INNI ‘ATIKUM BISULTANIN MUBININ
WE ‘INNI ‘UDHTU BIREBBI WE RABBIKUM ‘EN TERXHUMUNI
WE ‘IN LEM TU’UMINU LI FA’TEZILUNI
FEDA’A REBBEHU ‘ENNE HA’UULA’ KAWMUN MUXHRIMUNE
FE’ESRI BI’IBADI LEJLÆN ‘INNEKUM MUTTEBA’UNE
WE ETRUKIL-BEHRE REHWEN ‘INNEHUM XHUNDUN MUGREKUNE
KEM TEREKU MIN XHENNATIN WE ‘UJUNIN
WE ZURU’IN WE MEKAMIN KERIMIN
WE NA’METIN KANU FIHA FAKIHINE
KEDHALIKE WE ‘EWRETHNAHA KAWMÆN ‘AHARINE
FEMA BEKET ‘ALEJHIMU ES-SEMA’U WEL-’ERDU WE MA KANU MUNDHERINE
WE LEKAD NEXHXHEJNA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE MINEL-’ADHABIL-MUHINI
MIN FIR’AWNE ‘INNEHU KANE ‘ALIÆN MINEL-MUSRIFINE
WE LEKADI EHTERNAHUM ‘ALA ‘ILMIN ‘ALEL-’ALEMINE
WE ‘ATEJNAHUM MINEL-’AJATI MA FIHI BELA’UN MUBINUN
‘INNE HA’UULA’ LEJEKULUNE
‘IN HIJE ‘ILLA MEWTETUNAL-’ULA WE MA NEHNU BIMUNSHERINE
FE’TU BI’ABA’INA ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
‘EHUM HAJRUN ‘EM KAWMU TUBBA’IN WEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM ‘EHLEKNAHUM ‘INNEHUM KANU MUXHRIMINE
WE MA HALEKNA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA LA’IBINE
MA HALEKNAHUMA ‘ILLA BIL-HEKKI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHEREHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
‘INNE JEWMEL-FESLI MIKATUHUM ‘EXHMA’INE
JEWME LA JUGNI MEWLEN ‘AN MEWLEN SHEJ’ÆN WE LA HUM JUNSERUNE
‘ILLA MEN REHIMEL-LAHU ‘INNEHU HUWEL-’AZIZU ER-REHIMU
‘INNE SHEXHERETE EZ-ZEKKUMI
TA’AMUL-’ETHIMI
KALMUHLI JEGLI FIL-BUTUNI
KEGALJIL-HEMIMI
HUDHUHU FA’TILUHU ‘ILA SEWA’IL-XHEHIMI
THUMME SUBBU FEWKA RE’SIHI MIN ‘ADHABIL-HEMIMI
DHUK ‘INNEKE ‘ENTEL-’AZIZUL-KERIMU
‘INNE HADHA MA KUNTUM BIHI TEMTERUNE
‘INNEL-MUTTEKINE FI MEKAMIN ‘EMININ
FI XHENNATIN WE ‘UJUNIN
JELBESUNE MIN SUNDUSIN WE ‘ISTEBREKIN MUTEKABILINE
KEDHALIKE WE ZEWWEXHNAHUM BIHURIN ‘ININ
JED’UNE FIHA BIKULLI FAKIHETIN ‘AMININE
LA JEDHUKUNE FIHAL-MEWTE ‘ILLAL-MEWTETEL-’ULA WE WEKAHUM ‘ADHABEL-XHEHIMI
FEDLÆN MIN RABBIKE DHALIKE HUWEL-FEWZUL-’ADHIMU
FE’INNEMA JESSERNAHU BILISANIKE LE’ALLEHUM JETEDHEKKERUNE
FARTEKIB ‘INNEHUM MURTEKIBUNE
HA-MIM
TENZILUL-KITABI MINEL-LAHIL-’AZIZIL-HEKIMI
‘INNE FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI LE’AJATIN LILMU’UMININE
WE FI HALKIKUM WE MA JEBUTHTHU MIN DABBETIN ‘AJATUN LIKAWMIN JUKINUNE
WE EHTILAFIL-LEJLI WE EN-NEHARI WE MA ‘ENZELEL-LAHU MINE ES-SEMA’I MIN RIZKIN FE’EHJA BIHIL-’ERDE BA’DE MEWTIHA WE TESRIFI ER-RIJAHI ‘AJATUN LIKAWMIN JA’KILUNE
TILKE ‘AJATU ELLAHI NETLUHA ‘ALEJKE BIL-HEKKI FEBI’EJJI HEDITHIN BA’DEL-LAHI WE ‘AJATIHI JU’UMINUNE
WEJLUN LIKULLI ‘EFFAKIN ‘ETHIMIN
JESMA’U ‘AJATI ELLAHI TUTLA ‘ALEJHI THUMME JUSIRRU MUSTEKBIRÆN KE’EN LEM JESMA’HA FEBESHSHIRHU BI’ADHABIN ‘ELIMIN
WE ‘IDHA ‘ALIME MIN ‘AJATINA SHEJ’ÆN ETTEHADHEHA HUZUEN ‘ULA’IKE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN MUHINUN
MIN WERA’IHIM XHEHENNEMU WE LA JUGNI ‘ANHUM MA KESEBU SHEJ’ÆN WE LA MA ETTEHADHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘EWLIJA’E WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ADHIMUN
HADHA HUDEN WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BI’AJATI RABBIHIM LEHUM ‘ADHABUN MIN RIXHZIN ‘ELIMUN
ELLAHUL-LEDHI SEHHARE LEKUMUL-BEHRE LITEXHRIJEL-FULKU FIHI BI’EMRIHI WE LITEBTEGU MIN FEDLIHI WE LE’ALLEKUM TESHKURUNE
WE SEHHARE LEKUM MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI XHEMI’ÆN MINHU ‘INNE FI DHALIKE LE’AJATIN LIKAWMIN JETEFEKKERUNE
KUL LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU JEGFIRU LILLEDHINE LA JERXHUNE ‘EJJAMEL-LAHI LIJEXHZIJE KAWMÆN BIMA KANU JEKSIBUNE
MEN ‘AMILE SALIHÆN FELINEFSIHI WE MEN ‘ESA’E FE’ALEJHA THUMME ‘ILA RABBIKUM TURXHA’UNE
WE LEKAD ‘ATEJNA BENI ‘ISRA’ILEL-KITABE WEL-HUKME WE EN-NUBUWETE WE REZEKNAHUM MINET-TEJJIBATI WE FEDDELNAHUM ‘ALEL-’ALEMINE
WE ‘ATEJNAHUM BEJJINATIN MINEL-’EMRI FEMA EHTELEFU ‘ILLA MIN BA’DI MA XHA’EHUMUL-’ILMU BEGJÆN BEJNEHUM ‘INNE REBBEKE JEKDI BEJNEHUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI FIMA KANU FIHI JEHTELIFUNE
THUMME XHE’ALNAKE ‘ALA SHERI’ATIN MINEL-’EMRI FE ETTEBI’HA WE LA TETTEBI’ ‘EHWA’EL-LEDHINE LA JA’LEMUNE
‘INNEHUM LEN JUGNU ‘ANKE MINEL-LAHI SHEJ’ÆN WE ‘INNE EDH-DHALIMINE BA’DUHUM ‘EWLIJA’U BA’DIN WEL-LAHU WE LIJUL-MUTTEKINE
HADHA BESA’IRU LILNNASI WE HUDEN WE REHMETUN LIKAWMIN JUKINUNE
‘EM HESIBEL-LEDHINE EXHTEREHU ES-SEJJI’ATI ‘EN NEXH’ALEHUM KALLEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI SEWA’EN MEHJAHUM WE MEMATUHUM SA’E MA JEHKUMUNE
WE HALEKAL-LAHU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BIL-HEKKI WE LITUXHZA KULLU NEFSIN BIMA KESEBET WE HUM LA JUDHLEMUNE
‘EFERE’EJTE MENI ETTEHADHE ‘ILEHEHU HEWAHU WE ‘EDELLEHU ELLAHU ‘ALA ‘ILMIN WE HATEME ‘ALA SEM’IHI WE KALBIHI WE XHE’ALE ‘ALA BESERIHI GISHAWETEN FEMEN JEHDIHI MIN BA’DI ELLAHI ‘EFELA TEDHEKKERUNE
WE KALU MA HIJE ‘ILLA HEJATUNA ED-DUNJA NEMUTU WE NEHJA WE MA JUHLIKUNA ‘ILLA ED-DEHRU WE MA LEHUM BIDHALIKE MIN ‘ILMIN ‘IN HUM ‘ILLA JEDHUNNUNE
WE ‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATUNA BEJJINATIN MA KANE HUXHXHETEHUM ‘ILLA ‘EN KALU E’TU BI’ABA’INA ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
KULI ELLAHU JUHJIKUM THUMME JUMITUKUM THUMME JEXHMA’UKUM ‘ILA JEWMIL-KIJAMETI LA REJBE FIHI WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHERE EN-NASI LA JA’LEMUNE
WE LILLEHI MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE JEWME TEKUMU ES-SA’ATU JEWME’IDHIN JEHSERUL-MUBTILUNE
WE TERA KULLE ‘UMMETIN XHATHIJETEN KULLU ‘UMMETIN TUD’A ‘ILA KITABIHAL-JEWME TUXHZEWNE MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
HADHA KITABUNA JENTIKU ‘ALEJKUM BIL-HEKKI ‘INNA KUNNA NESTENSIHU MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
FE’EMMAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI FEJUDHILUHUM REBBUHUM FI REHMETIHI DHALIKE HUWEL-FEWZUL-MUBINU
WE ‘EMMAL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘EFELEM TEKUN ‘AJATI TUTLA ‘ALEJKUM FASTEKBERTUM WE KUNTUM KAWMÆN MUXHRIMINE
WE ‘IDHA KILE ‘INNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN WE ES-SA’ATU LA REJBE FIHA KULTUM MA NEDRI MA ES-SA’ATU ‘IN NEDHUNNU ‘ILLA DHENNÆN WE MA NEHNU BIMUSTEJKININE
WE BEDA LEHUM SEJJI’ATU MA ‘AMILU WE HAKA BIHIM MA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
WE KILEL-JEWME NENSAKUM KEMA NESITUM LIKA’E JEWMIKUM HADHA WE ME’WAKUMU EN-NARU WE MA LEKUM MIN NASIRINE
DHALIKUM BI’ENNEKUM ETTEHADHTUM ‘AJATI ELLAHI HUZUEN WE GARRETKUMUL-HEJÆTU ED-DUNJA FALJEWME LA JUHREXHUNE MINHA WE LA HUM JUSTA’TEBUNE
FELILLAHIL-HEMDU RABBI ES-SEMAWATI WE RABBIL-’ERDI RABBIL-’ALEMINE
WE LEHUL-KIBRIJA’U FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
HA-MIM
TENZILUL-KITABI MINEL-LAHIL-’AZIZIL-HEKIMI
MA HALEKNA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA ‘ILLA BIL-HEKKI WE ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘AMMA ‘UNDHIRU MU’RIDUNE
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM MA TED’UNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘ERUNI MADHA HALEKU MINEL-’ERDI ‘EM LEHUM SHIRKUN FI ES-SEMAWATI EI’TUNI BIKITABIN MIN KABLI HADHA ‘EW ‘ETHARETIN MIN ‘ILMIN ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
WE MEN ‘EDELLU MIMMEN JED’U MIN DUNI ELLAHI MEN LA JESTEXHIBU LEHU ‘ILA JEWMIL-KIJAMETI WE HUM ‘AN DU’A’IHIM GAFILUNE
WE ‘IDHA HUSHIRE EN-NASU KANU LEHUM ‘A’DA’EN WE KANU BI’IBADETIHIM KAFIRINE
WE ‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATUNA BEJJINATIN KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LILHEKKI LEMMA XHA’EHUM HADHA SIHRUN MUBINUN
‘EM JEKULUNE EFTERAHU KUL ‘INI EFTEREJTUHU FELA TEMLIKUNE LI MINEL-LAHI SHEJ’ÆN HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMA TUFIDUNE FIHI KEFA BIHI SHEHIDÆN BEJNI WE BEJNEKUM WE HUWEL-GAFURU ER-REHIMU
KUL MA KUNTU BID’ÆN MINE ER-RUSULI WE MA ‘EDRI MA JUF’ALU BI WE LA BIKUM ‘IN ‘ETTEBI’U ‘ILLA MA JUHA ‘ILEJJE WE MA ‘ENA ‘ILLA NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN KANE MIN ‘INDI ELLAHI WE KEFERTUM BIHI WE SHEHIDE SHAHIDUN MIN BENI ‘ISRA’ILE ‘ALA MITHLIHI FE’AMENE WE ESTEKBERTUM ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JEHDIL-KAWME EDH-DHALIMINE
WE KALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU LEW KANE HAJRÆN MA SEBEKUNA ‘ILEJHI WE ‘IDH LEM JEHTEDU BIHI FESEJEKULUNE HADHA ‘IFKUN KADIMUN
WE MIN KABLIHI KITABU MUSA ‘IMAMÆN WE REHMETEN WE HEDHA KITABUN MUSEDDIKUN LISANÆN ‘AREBIJÆN LIJUNDHIREL-LEDHINE DHELEMU WE BUSHRA LILMUHSININE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KALU REBBUNALLAHU THUMME ESTEKAMU FELA HAWFUN ‘ALEJHIM WE LA HUM JEHZENUNE
‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABUL-XHENNETI HALIDINE FIHA XHEZA’EN BIMA KANU JA’MELUNE
WE WESSEJNAL-’INSANE BIWALIDEJHI ‘IHSANÆN HEMELET/HU ‘UMMUHU KURHÆN WE WEDE’AT/HU KURHÆN WE HEMLUHU WE FISALUHU THELATHUNE SHEHRÆN HETTA ‘IDHA BELEGA ‘ESHUDDEHU WE BELEGA ‘ERBA’INE SENETEN KALE RABBI ‘EWZI’NI ‘EN ‘ESHKURE NI’METEKEL-LETI ‘EN’AMTE ‘ALEJJE 
‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE NETEKABBELU ‘ANHUM ‘EHSENE MA ‘AMILU WE NETEXHAWEZU ‘AN SEJJI’ATIHIM FI ‘ESHABIL-XHENNETI WA’DE ES-SIDKIL-LEDHI KANU JU’ADUNE
WEL-LEDHI KALE LIWALIDEJHI ‘UFFIN LEKUMA ‘ETA’IDANINI ‘EN ‘UHREXHE WE KAD HALETIL-KURUNU MIN KABLI WE HUMA JESTEGITHANI ELLAHE WEJLEKE ‘AMIN ‘INNE WA’DEL-LAHI HEKKUN FEJEKULU MA HADHA ‘ILLA ‘ESATIRUL-’EWWELINE
‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE HEKKA ‘ALEJHIMUL-KAWLU FI ‘UMEMIN KAD HALET MIN KABLIHIM MINEL-XHINNI WEL-’INSI ‘INNEHUM KANU HASIRINE
WE LIKULLIN DEREXHATUN MIMMA ‘AMILU WE LIJUWEFFIJEHUM ‘A’MALEHUM WE HUM LA JUDHLEMUNE
WE JEWME JU’REDUL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘ALA EN-NARI ‘EDH/HEBTUM TEJJIBATIKUM FI HEJATIKUMU ED-DUNJA WE ESTEMTA’TUM BIHA FALJEWME TUXHZEWNE ‘ADHABEL-HUNI BIMA KUNTUM TESTEKBIRUNE FIL-’ERDI BIGAJRIL-HEKKI WE BIMA KUNTUM TEFSUKUNE
WE EDHKUR ‘EHA ‘ADIN ‘IDH ‘ENDHERE KAWMEHU BIL-’EHKAFI WE KAD HALETI EN-NUDHURU MIN BEJNI JEDEJHI WE MIN HALFIHI ‘ELLA TA’BUDU ‘ILLALLAHE ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ‘ALEJKUM ‘ADHABE JEWMIN ‘ADHIMIN
KALU ‘EXHI’TENA LITE’FIKENA ‘AN ‘ALIHETINA FE’TINA BIMA TA’IDUNA ‘IN KUNTE MINE ES-SADIKINE
KALE ‘INNEMAL-’ILMU ‘INDEL-LAHI WE ‘UBELLIGUKUM MA ‘URSILTU BIHI WE LEKINNI ‘ERAKUM KAWMÆN TEXHHELUNE
FELEMMA RE’EWHU ‘ARIDÆN MUSTEKBILE ‘EWDIJETIHIM KALU HADHA ‘ARIDUN MUMTIRUNA BEL HUWE MA ESTA’XHELTUM BIHI RIHUN FIHA ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
TUDEMMIRU KULLE SHEJ’IN BI’EMRI RABBIHA FE’ESBEHU LA JURA ‘ILLA MESAKINUHUM KEDHALIKE NEXHZIL-KAWMEL-MUXHRIMINE
WE LEKAD MEKKENNAHUM FIMA ‘IN MEKKENNAKUM FIHI WE XHE’ALNA LEHUM SEM’ÆN WE ‘EBSARÆN WE ‘EF’IDETEN FEMA ‘EGNA ‘ANHUM SEM’UHUM WE LA ‘EBSARUHUM WE LA ‘EF’IDETUHUM MIN SHEJ’IN ‘IDH KANU JEXHHEDUNE BI’AJATI ELLAHI WE HAKA BIHIM MA KANU BIHI JESTEHZI’UN
WE LEKAD ‘EHLEKNA MA HEWLEKUM MINEL-KURA WE SERREFNAL-’AJATI LE’ALLEHUM JERXHI’UNE
FELEWLA NESEREHUMUL-LEDHINE ETTEHADHU MIN DUNI ELLAHI KURBANÆN ‘ALIHETEN BEL DELLU ‘ANHUM WE DHELIKE ‘IFKUHUM WE MA KANU JEFTERUNE
WE ‘IDH SEREFNA ‘ILEJKE NEFERÆN MINEL-XHINNI JESTEMI’UNEL-KUR’ANE FELEMMA HEDERUHU KALU ‘ENSITU FELEMMA KUDIJE WE LLEW ‘ILA KAWMIHIM MUNDHIRINE
KALU JA KAWMENA ‘INNA SEMI’NA KITABÆN ‘UNZILE MIN BA’DI MUSA MUSEDDIKÆN LIMA BEJNE JEDEJHI JEHDI ‘ILAL-HEKKI WE ‘ILA TERIKIN MUSTEKIMIN
JA KAWMENA ‘EXHIBU DA’IJEL-LAHI WE ‘AMINU BIHI JEGFIR LEKUM MIN DHUNUBIKUM WE JUXHIRKUM MIN ‘ADHABIN ‘ELIMIN
WE MEN LA JUXHIB DA’IJEL-LAHI FELEJSE BIMU’XHIZIN FIL-’ERDI WE LEJSE LEHU MIN DUNIHI ‘EWLIJA’U ‘ULA’IKE FI DELALIN MUBININ
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ENNEL-LAHEL-LEDHI HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE LEM JA’JE BIHALKIHINNE BIKADIRIN ‘ALA ‘EN JUHJIJEL-MEWTA BELA ‘INNEHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
WE JEWME JU’REDUL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘ALA EN-NARI ‘ELEJSE HADHA BIL-HEKKI KALU BELA WE RABBINA KALE FEDHUKUL-’ADHABE BIMA KUNTUM TEKFURUNE
FASBIR KEMA SEBERE ‘ULUL-’AZMI MINE ER-RUSULI WE LA TESTA’XHIL LEHUM KE’ENNEHUM JEWME JEREWNE MA JU’ADUNE LEM JELBETHU ‘ILLA SA’ATEN MIN NEHARIN BELAGUN FEHEL JUHLEKU ‘ILLAL-KAWMUL-FASIKUNE
EL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE SEDDU ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI ‘EDELLE ‘A’MALEHUM
WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI WE ‘AMENU BIMA NUZZILE ‘ALA MUHEMMEDIN WE HUWEL-HEKKU MIN RABBIHIM KEFFERE ‘ANHUM SEJJI’ATIHIM WE ‘ESLEHE BALEHUM
DHALIKE BI’ENNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ETTEBA’UL-BATILE WE ‘ENNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ETTEBA’UL-HEKKA MIN RABBIHIM KEDHALIKE JEDRIBU ELLAHU LILNNASI ‘EMTHALEHUM
FE’IDHA LEKITUMUL-LEDHINE KEFERU FEDERBE ER-RIKABI HETTA ‘IDHA ‘ETHHANTUMUHUM FESHUDDUL-WETHAKA FE’IMMA MENNÆN BA’DU WE ‘IMMA FIDA’EN HETTA TEDE’AL-HERBU ‘EWZAREHA DHALIKE WE LEW JESHA’U ELLAHU LANTESERE MINHUM WE LEKIN LIJEBLUWE BA’DEKUM BIBA’DIN WEL-LED
SEJEHDIHIM WE JUSLIHU BALEHUM
WE JUDHILUHUMUL-XHENNETE ‘ARREFEHA LEHUM
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IN TENSURU ELLAHE JENSURKUM WE JUTHEBBIT ‘EKDAMEKUM
WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU FETA’SÆN LEHUM WE ‘EDELLE ‘A’MALEHUM
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUM KERIHU MA ‘ENZELEL-LAHU FE’EHBETE ‘A’MALEHUM
‘EFELEM JESIRU FIL-’ERDI FEJENDHURU KEJFE KANE ‘AKIBETUL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM DEMMEREL-LAHU ‘ALEJHIM WE LILKAFIRINE ‘EMTHALUHA
DHALIKE BI’ENNEL-LAHE MEWLAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘ENNEL-KAFIRINE LA MEWLA LEHUM
‘INNALL-LLAHE JUDHILUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU JETEMETTA’UNE WE JE’KULUNE KEMA TE’KULUL-’EN’AM WE EN-NARU METHWEN LEHUM
WE KE’EJJIN MIN KARJETIN HIJE ‘ESHEDDU KUWETEN MIN KARJETIKEL-LETI ‘EHREXHETKE ‘EHLEKNAHUM FELA NASIRE LEHUM
‘EFEMEN KANE ‘ALA BEJJINETIN MIN RABBIHI KEMEN ZUJJINE LEHU SU’U ‘AMELIHI WE ETTEBA’U ‘EHWA’EHUM
METHELUL-XHENNETI ELLETI WU’IDEL-MUTTEKUNE FIHA ‘ENHARUN MIN MA’IN GAJRI ‘ASININ WE ‘ENHARUN MIN LEBENIN LEM JETEGAJJER TA’MUHU WE ‘ENHARUN MIN HAMRIN LEDHDHETIN LILSHSHARIBINE WE ‘ENHARUN MIN ‘ASELIN MUSEFFEN WE LEHUM FIHA MIN KULLI ETH-THEMERATI WE MEGF
WE MINHUM MEN JESTEMI’U ‘ILEJKE HETTA ‘IDHA HAREXHU MIN ‘INDIKE KALU LILLEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME MADHA KALE ‘ANIFÆN ‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE TEBE’ALLAHU ‘ALA KULUBIHIM WE ETTEBA’U ‘EHWA’EHUM
WEL-LEDHINE EHTEDEW ZADEHUM HUDEN WE ‘ATAHUM TEKWHUM
FEHEL JENDHURUNE ‘ILLA ES-SA’ATE ‘EN TE’TIJEHUM BEGTETEN FEKAD XHA’E ‘ESHRATUHA FE’ENNA LEHUM ‘IDHA XHA’ET/HUM DHIKRAHUM
FA’LEM ‘ENNEHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLALLAHU WE ESTEGFIR LIDHENBIKE WE LILMU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU MUTEKALLEBEKUM WE METHWAKUM
WE JEKULUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LEWLA NUZZILET SURETUN FE’IDHA ‘UNZILET SURETUN MUHKEMETUN WE DHUKIRE FIHAL-KITALU RE’EJTEL-LEDHINE FI KULUBIHIM MEREDUN JENDHURUNE ‘ILEJKE NEDHEREL-MEGSHIJI ‘ALEJHI MINEL-MEWTI FE’EWLA LEHUM
TA’ATUN WE KAWLUN MA’RUFUN FE’IDHA ‘AZEMEL-’EMRU FELEW SEDEKU ELLAHE LEKANE HAJRÆN LEHUM
FEHEL ‘ASEJTUM ‘IN TEWELLEJTUM ‘EN TUFSIDU FIL-’ERDI WE TUKATTI’U ‘ERHAMEKUM
‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE LE’ANEHUMU ELLAHU FE’ESEMMEHUM WE ‘A’MA ‘EBSAREHUM
‘EFELA JETEDEBBERUNEL-KUR’ANE ‘EM ‘ALA KULUBIN ‘EKFALUHA
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ERTEDDU ‘ALA ‘EDBARIHIM MIN BA’DI MA TEBEJJENE LEHUMUL-HUDA ESH-SHEJTANU SEWWELE LEHUM WE ‘EMLA LEHUM
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUM KALU LILLEDHINE KERIHU MA NEZZELEL-LAHU SENUTI’UKUM FI BA’DIL-’EMRI WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU ‘ISRAREHUM
FEKEJFE ‘IDHA TEWEFFET/HUMUL-MELA’IKETU JEDRIBUNE WUXHUHEHUM WE ‘EDBAREHUM
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUMU ETTEBA’U MA ‘ESHATEL-LAHE WE KERIHU RIDWANEHU FE’EHBETE ‘A’MALEHUM
‘EM HESIBEL-LEDHINE FI KULUBIHIM MEREDUN ‘EN LEN JUHRIXHEL-LAHU ‘EDGANEHUM
WE LEW NESHA’U LE’EREJNAKEHUM FELE’AREFTEHUM BISIMAHUM WE LETA’RIFENNEHUM FI LEHNIL-KAWLI WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU ‘A’MALEKUM
WE LENEBLUWENNEKUM HETTA NA’LEMEL-MUXHAHIDINE MINKUM WE ES-SABIRINE WE NEBLUWE ‘EHBAREKUM
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE SEDDU ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI WE SHAKKU ER-RESULE MIN BA’DI MA TEBEJJENE LEHUMUL-HUDA LEN JEDURRU ELLAHE SHEJ’ÆN WE SEJUHBITU ‘A’MALEHUM
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘ETI’U ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’U ER-RESULE WE LA TUBTILU ‘A’MALEKUM
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE SEDDU ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI THUMME MATU WE HUM KUFFARUN FELEN JEGFIREL-LAHU LEHUM
FELA TEHINU WE TED’U ‘ILA ES-SELMI WE ‘ENTUMUL-’A’LEWNE WEL-LAHU ME’AKUM WE LEN JETIREKUM ‘A’MALEKUM
‘INNEMAL-HEJÆTU ED-DUNJA LA’IBUN WE LEHWUN WE ‘IN TU’UMINU WE TETTEKU JU’UTIKUM ‘UXHUREKUM WE LA JES’ELKUM ‘EMWALEKUM
‘IN JES’ELKUMUHA FEJUHFIKUM TEBHALU WE JUHRIXH ‘EDGANEKUM
HA’ENTUM HA’UULA’ TUD’AWNE LITUNFIKU FI SEBILI ELLAHI FEMINKUM MEN JEBHALU WE MEN JEBHAL FE’INNEMA JEBHALU ‘AN NEFSIHI WEL-LAHUL-GANIJU WE ‘ENTUMUL-FUKARA’U WE ‘IN TETEWELLEW JESTEBDIL KAWMÆN GAJREKUM THUMME LA JEKUNU ‘EMTHALEKUM
‘INNA FETEHNA LEKE FETHÆN MUBINÆN
LIJEGFIRE LEKEL-LAHU MA TEKADDEME MIN DHENBIKE WE MA TE’EHHARE WE JUTIMME NI’METEHU ‘ALEJKE WE JEHDIJEKE SIRATÆN MUSTEKIMÆN
WE JENSUREKEL-LAHU NESRÆN ‘AZIZÆN
HUWEL-LEDHI ‘ENZELE ES-SEKINETE FI KULUBIL-MU’UMININE LIJEZDADU ‘IMANÆN ME’A ‘IMANIHIM WE LILLEHI XHUNUDU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE KANEL-LAHU ‘ALIMÆN HEKIMÆN
LIJUDHILEL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA WE JUKEFFIRE ‘ANHUM SEJJI’ATIHIM WE KANE DHALIKE ‘INDEL-LAHI FEWZÆN ‘ADHIMÆN
WE JU’ADHDHIBEL-MUNAFIKINE WEL-MUNAFIKATI WEL-MUSHRIKINE WEL-MUSHRIKATI EDH-DHANNINE BILLAHI DHENNE ES-SEW’I ‘ALEJHIM DA’IRETU ES-SEW’I WE GADIBEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHIM WE LE’ANEHUM WE ‘E’ADDE LEHUM XHEHENNEME WE SA’ET MESIRÆN
WE LILLEHI XHUNUDU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE KANEL-LAHU ‘AZIZÆN HEKIMÆN
‘INNA ‘ERSELNAKE SHAHIDÆN WE MUBESHSHIRÆN WE NEDHIRÆN
LITU’UMINU BILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE TU’AZZIRUHU WE TUWEKKIRUHU WE TUSEBBIHUHU BUKRETEN WE ‘ESILÆN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JUBAJI’UNEKE ‘INNEMA JUBAJI’UNEL-LAHE JEDU ELLAHI FEWKA ‘EJDIHIM FEMEN NEKETHE FE’INNEMA JENKUTHU ‘ALA NEFSIHI WE MEN ‘EWFA BIMA ‘AHEDE ‘ALEJHU ELLAHE FESEJU’UTIHI ‘EXHRÆN ‘ADHIMÆN
SEJEKULU LEKEL-MUHALLEFUNE MINEL-’A’RABI SHEGALETNA ‘EMWALUNA WE ‘EHLUNA FASTEGFIR LENA JEKULUNE BI’ELSINETIHIM MA LEJSE FI KULUBIHIM KUL FEMEN JEMLIKU LEKUM MINEL-LAHI SHEJ’ÆN ‘IN ‘ERADE BIKUM DERRÆN ‘EW ‘ERADE BIKUM NEF’ÆN BEL KANEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE 
BEL DHENENTUM ‘EN LEN JENKALIBE ER-RESULU WEL-MU’UMINUNE ‘ILA ‘EHLIHIM ‘EBEDÆN WE ZUJJINE DHALIKE FI KULUBIKUM WE DHENENTUM DHENNE ES-SEW’I WE KUNTUM KAWMÆN BURÆN
WE MEN LEM JU’UMIN BILLAHI WE RESULIHI FE’INNA ‘A’TEDNA LILKAFIRINE SA’IRÆN
WE LILLEHI MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI JEGFIRU LIMEN JESHA’U WE JU’ADHDHIBU MEN JESHA’U WE KANEL-LAHU GAFURÆN REHIMÆN
SEJEKULUL-MUHALLEFUNE ‘IDHA ENTELEKTUM ‘ILA MEGANIME LITE’HUDHUHA DHERUNA NETTEBI’KUM JURIDUNE ‘EN JUBEDDILU KELAMEL-LAHI KUL LEN TETTEBI’UNA KEDHALIKUM KALEL-LAHU MIN KABLU FESEJEKULUNE BEL TEHSUDUNENA BEL KANU LA JEFKAHUNE ‘ILLA KALILÆN
KUL LILMUHALLEFINE MINEL-’A’RABI SETUD’AWNE ‘ILA KAWMIN ‘ULI BE’SIN SHEDIDIN TUKATILUNEHUM ‘EW JUSLIMUNE FE’IN TUTI’U JU’UTIKUMU ELLAHU ‘EXHRÆN HESENÆN WE ‘IN TETEWELLEW KEMA TEWELLEJTUM MIN KABLU JU’ADHDHIBKUM ‘ADHABÆN ‘ELIMÆN
LEJSE ‘ALEL-’A’MA HEREXHUN WE LA ‘ALEL-’A’REXHI HEREXHUN WE LA ‘ALEL-MERIDI HEREXHUN WE MEN JUTI’I ELLAHE WE RESULEHU JUDHILHU XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU WE MEN JETEWELLE JU’ADHDHIBHU ‘ADHABÆN ‘ELIMÆN
LEKAD REDIJEL-LAHU ‘ANIL-MU’UMININE ‘IDH JUBAJI’UNEKE TEHTE ESH-SHEXHERETI FE’ALIME MA FI KULUBIHIM FE’ENZELE ES-SEKINETE ‘ALEJHIM WE ‘ETHABEHUM FETHÆN KARIBÆN
WE MEGANIME KETHIRETEN JE’HUDHUNEHA WE KANEL-LAHU ‘AZIZÆN HEKIMÆN
WE’ADEKUMU ELLAHU MEGANIME KETHIRETEN TE’HUDHUNEHA FE’AXHXHELE LEKUM HEDHIHI WE KEFFE ‘EJDIJE EN-NASI ‘ANKUM WE LITEKUNE ‘AJETEN LILMU’UMININE WE JEHDIJEKUM SIRATÆN MUSTEKIMÆN
WE ‘UHRA LEM TEKDIRU ‘ALEJHA KAD ‘EHATEL-LAHU BIHA WE KANEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRÆN
WE LEW KATELEKUMUL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEWELLEWL-’EDBARE THUMME LA JEXHIDUNE WELIJÆN WE LA NESIRÆN
SUNNETEL-LAHI ELLETI KAD HALET MIN KABLU WE LEN TEXHIDE LISUNNETI ELLAHI TEBDILÆN
WE HUWEL-LEDHI KEFFE ‘EJDIJEHUM ‘ANKUM WE ‘EJDIJEKUM ‘ANHUM BIBETNI MEKKETE MIN BA’DI ‘EN ‘EDHFEREKUM ‘ALEJHIM WE KANEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRÆN
HUMUL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE SEDDUKUM ‘ANIL-MESXHIDIL-HERAMI WEL-HEDJE MA’KUFÆN ‘EN JEBLUGA MEHILLEHU WE LEWLA RIXHALUN MU’UMINUNE WE NISA’UN MU’UMINATUN LEM TA’LEMUHUM ‘EN TETE’UHUM FETUSIBEKUM MINHUM ME’ARRETUN BIGAJRI ‘ILMIN LIJUDHILEL-LAHU FI REHMETIHI MEN
‘IDH XHE’ALEL-LEDHINE KEFERU FI KULUBIHIMUL-HEMIJETE HEMIJETEL-XHAHILIJETI FE’ENZELEL-LAHU SEKINETEHU ‘ALA RESULIHI WE ‘ALEL-MU’UMININE WE ‘ELZEMEHUM KELIMETET-TEKWA WE KANU ‘EHEKKA BIHA WE ‘EHLEHA WE KANEL-LAHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMÆN
LEKAD SEDEKAL-LAHU RESULEHU ER-RU’UJA BIL-HEKKI LETEDHULUNNEL-MESXHIDEL-HERAME ‘IN SHA’EL-LAHU ‘AMININE MUHELLIKINE RU’USEKUM WE MUKASSIRINE LA TEHAFUNE FE’ALIME MA LEM TA’LEMU FEXHE’ALE MIN DUNI DHALIKE FETHÆN KARIBÆN
HUWEL-LEDHI ‘ERSELE RESULEHU BIL-HUDA WE DINIL-HEKKI LIJUDHHIREHU ‘ALA ED-DINI KULLIHI WE KEFA BILLAHI SHEHIDÆN
MUHEMMEDUN RESULU ELLAHI WEL-LEDHINE ME’AHU ‘ESHIDDA’U ‘ALEL-KUFFARI RUHEMA’U BEJNEHUM TERAHUM RUKKA’ÆN SUXHXHEDÆN JEBTEGUNE FEDLÆN MINEL-LAHI WE RIDWANÆN SIMAHUM FI WUXHUHIHIM MIN ‘ETHERI ES-SUXHUDI DHALIKE METHELUHUM FIT-TEWRÆTI WE METHELUHUM FIL-’INXHI
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TUKADDIMU BEJNE JEDEJI ELLAHI WE RESULIHI WE ETTEKU ELLAHE ‘INNALL-LLAHE SEMI’UN ‘ALIMUN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TERFA’U ‘ESWATEKUM FEWKA SEWTI EN-NEBIJI WE LA TEXHHERU LEHU BIL-KAWLI KEXHEHRI BA’DIKUM LIBA’DIN ‘EN TEHBETE ‘A’MALUKUM WE ‘ENTUM LA TESH’URUNE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JEGUDDUNE ‘ESWATEHUM ‘INDE RESULI ELLAHI ‘ULA’IKEL-LEDHINE EMTEHENEL-LAHU KULUBEHUM LILTTEKWA LEHUM MEGFIRETUN WE ‘EXHRUN ‘ADHIMUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JUNADUNEKE MIN WERA’IL-HUXHURATI ‘EKTHERUHUM LA JA’KILUNE
WE LEW ‘ENNEHUM SEBERU HETTA TEHRUXHE ‘ILEJHIM LEKANE HAJRÆN LEHUM WEL-LAHU GAFURUN REHIMUN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IN XHA’EKUM FASIKUN BINEBE’IIN FETEBEJJENU ‘EN TUSIBU KAWMÆN BIXHEHALETIN FETUSBIHU ‘ALA MA FE’ALTUM NADIMINE
WE A’LEMU ‘ENNE FIKUM RESULEL-LAHI LEW JUTI’UKUM FI KETHIRIN MINEL-’EMRI LE’ANITTUM WE LEKINNALL-LLAHE HEBBEBE ‘ILEJKUMUL-’IMANE WE ZEJJENEHU FI KULUBIKUM WE KERREHE ‘ILEJKUMUL-KUFRE WEL-FUSUKA WEL-’ISJANE ‘ULA’IKE HUMU ER-RASHIDUNE
FEDLÆN MINEL-LAHI WE NI’METEN WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN HEKIMUN
WE ‘IN TA’IFETANI MINEL-MU’UMININE EKTETELU FE’ESLIHU BEJNEHUMA FE’IN BEGAT ‘IHDAHUMA ‘ALEL-’UHRA FEKATILU ELLETI TEBGI HETTA TEFI’E ‘ILA ‘EMRI ELLAHI FE’IN FA’ET FE’ESLIHU BEJNEHUMA BIL-’ADLI WE ‘EKSITU ‘INNALL-LLAHE JUHIBBUL-MUKSITINE
‘INNEMAL-MU’UMINUNE ‘IHWETUN FE’ESLIHU BEJNE ‘EHAWEJKUM WE ETTEKU ELLAHE LE’ALLEKUM TURHEMUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA JESHAR KAWMUN MIN KAWMIN ‘ASA ‘EN JEKUNU HAJRÆN MINHUM WE LA NISA’UN MIN NISA’IN ‘ASA ‘EN JEKUNNE HAJRÆN MINHUNNE WE LA TELMIZU ‘ENFUSEKUM WE LA TENABEZU BIL-’ELKABI BI’SEL-EISMUL-FUSUKU BA’DEL-’IMANI WE MEN LEM JETUB FE’ULA’
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU EXHTENIBU KETHIRÆN MINE EDH-DHENNI ‘INNE BA’DE EDH-DHENNI ‘ITHMUN WE LA TEXHESSESU WE LA JEGTEB BA’DUKUM BA’DÆN ‘EJUHIBBU ‘EHEDUKUM ‘EN JE’KULE LEHME ‘EHIHI MEJTÆN FEKERIHTUMUHU WE ETTEKU ELLAHE ‘INNALL-LLAHE TEWWABUN REHIMUN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NASU ‘INNA HALEKNAKUM MIN DHEKERIN WE ‘UNTHA WE XHE’ALNAKUM SHU’UBÆN WE KABA’ILE LITA’AREFU ‘INNE ‘EKREMEKUM ‘INDEL-LAHI ‘ETKAKUM ‘INNALL-LLAHE ‘ALIMUN HABIRUN
KALETIL-’A’RABU ‘AMENNA KUL LEM TU’UMINU WE LEKIN KULU ‘ESLEMNA WE LEMMA JEDHULIL-’IMANU FI KULUBIKUM WE ‘IN TUTI’U ELLAHE WE RESULEHU LA JELITKUM MIN ‘A’MALIKUM SHEJ’ÆN ‘INNALL-LLAHE GAFURUN REHIMUN
‘INNEMAL-MU’UMINUNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU BILLAHI WE RESULIHI THUMME LEM JERTABU WE XHAHEDU BI’EMWALIHIM WE ‘ENFUSIHIM FI SEBILI ELLAHI ‘ULA’IKE HUMU ES-SADIKUNE
KUL ‘ETU’ALLIMUNEL-LAHE BIDINIKUM WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WEL-LAHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMUN
JEMUNNUNE ‘ALEJKE ‘EN ‘ESLEMU KUL LA TEMUNNU ‘ALEJJE ‘ISLAMEKUM BELI ELLAHU JEMUNNU ‘ALEJKUM ‘EN HEDAKUM LIL’IMANI ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
‘INNALL-LLAHE JA’LEMU GAJBE ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WEL-LAHU BESIRUN BIMA TA’MELUNE
KAF WEL-KUR’ANIL-MEXHIDI
BEL ‘AXHIBU ‘EN XHA’EHUM MUNDHIRUN MINHUM FEKALEL-KAFIRUNE HADHA SHEJ’UN ‘AXHIBUN
‘E’IDHA MITNA WE KUNNA TURABÆN DHALIKE REXH’UN BA’IDUN
KAD ‘ALIMNA MA TENKUSUL-’ERDU MINHUM WE ‘INDENA KITABUN HEFIDHUN
BEL KEDHDHEBU BIL-HEKKI LEMMA XHA’EHUM FEHUM FI ‘EMRIN MERIXHIN
‘EFELEM JENDHURU ‘ILA ES-SEMA’I FEWKAHUM KEJFE BENEJNAHA WE ZEJJENNAHA WE MA LEHA MIN FURUXHIN
WEL-’ERDE MEDEDNAHA WE ‘ELKAJNA FIHA REWASIJE WE ‘ENBETNA FIHA MIN KULLI ZEWXHIN BEHIXHIN
TEBSIRETEN WE DHIKRA LIKULLI ‘ABDIN MUNIBIN
WE NEZZELNA MINE ES-SEMA’I MA’EN MUBAREKÆN FE’ENBETNA BIHI XHENNATIN WE HEBBEL-HESIDI
WE EN-NEHLE BASIKATIN LEHA TEL’UN NEDIDUN
RIZKÆN LIL’IBADI WE ‘EHJEJNA BIHI BELDETEN MEJTÆN KEDHALIKEL-HURUXHU
KEDHDHEBET KABLEHUM KAWMU NUHIN WE ‘ESHABU ER-RESSI WE THEMUDU
WE ‘ADUN WE FIR’AWNU WE ‘IHWANU LUTIN
WE ‘ESHABUL-’EJKETI WE KAWMU TUBBA’IN KULLUN KEDHDHEBE ER-RUSULE FEHEKKA WA’IDI
‘EFE’AJINA BIL-HALKIL-’EWWELI BEL HUM FI LEBSIN MIN HALKIN XHEDIDIN
WE LEKAD HALEKNAL-’INSANE WE NA’LEMU MA TUWESWISU BIHI NEFSUHU WE NEHNU ‘EKREBU ‘ILEJHI MIN HEBLIL-WERIDI
‘IDH JETELEKKAL-MUTELEKKIJANI ‘ANIL-JEMINI WE ‘ANI ESH-SHIMALI KA’IDUN
MA JELFIDHU MIN KAWLIN ‘ILLA LEDEJHI REKIBUN ‘ATIDUN
WE XHA’ET SEKRETUL-MEWTI BIL-HEKKI DHALIKE MA KUNTE MINHU TEHIDU
WE NUFIHA FI ES-SURI DHALIKE JEWMUL-WA’IDI
WE XHA’ET KULLU NEFSIN ME’AHA SA’IKUN WE SHEHIDUN
LEKAD KUNTE FI GAFLETIN MIN HADHA FEKESHEFNA ‘ANKE GITA’EKE FEBESERUKEL-JEWME HEDIDUN
WE KALE KARINUHU HADHA MA LEDEJJE ‘ATIDUN
‘ELKIJA FI XHEHENNEME KULLE KEFFARIN ‘ANIDIN
MENNA’IN LILHAJRI MU’TEDIN MURIBIN
EL-LEDHI XHE’ALE ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE FE’ELKIJAHU FIL-’ADHABI ESH-SHEDIDI
KALE KARINUHU REBBENA MA ‘ETGAJTUHU WE LEKIN KANE FI DELALIN BA’IDIN
KALE LA TEHTESIMU LEDEJJE WE KAD KADDEMTU ‘ILEJKUM BIL-WA’IDI
MA JUBEDDELUL-KAWLU LEDEJJE WE MA ‘ENA BIDHELLAMIN LIL’ABIDI
JEWME NEKULU LIXHEHENNEME HEL EMTELE’TI WE TEKULU HEL MIN MEZIDIN
WE ‘UZLIFETIL-XHENNETU LILMUTTEKINE GAJRE BA’IDIN
HADHA MA TU’ADUNE LIKULLI ‘EWWABIN HEFIDHIN
MEN HASHIJE ER-REHMENE BIL-GAJBI WE XHA’E BIKALBIN MUNIBIN
EDHULUHA BISELAMIN DHALIKE JEWMUL-HULUDI
LEHUM MA JESHA’UNE FIHA WE LEDEJNA MEZIDUN
WE KEM ‘EHLEKNA KABLEHUM MIN KARNIN HUM ‘ESHEDDU MINHUM BETSHÆN FENEKKABU FIL-BILADI HEL MIN MEHISIN
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LEDHIKRA LIMEN KANE LEHU KALBUN ‘EW ‘ELKA ES-SEM’A WE HUWE SHEHIDUN
WE LEKAD HALEKNA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE WE MA BEJNEHUMA FI SITTETI ‘EJJAMIN WE MA MESSENA MIN LUGUBIN
FASBIR ‘ALA MA JEKULUNE WE SEBBIH BIHEMDI RABBIKE KABLE TULU’I ESH-SHEMSI WE KABLEL-GURUBI
WE MINEL-LEJLI FESEBBIHHU WE ‘EDBARE ES-SUXHUDI
WE ESTEMI’ JEWME JUNADIL-MUNADI MIN MEKANIN KARIBIN
JEWME JESMA’UNE ES-SEJHETE BIL-HEKKI DHALIKE JEWMUL-HURUXHI
‘INNA NEHNU NUHJI WE NUMITU WE ‘ILEJNAL-MESIRU
JEWME TESHEKKAKUL-’ERDU ‘ANHUM SIRA’ÆN DHALIKE HESHRUN ‘ALEJNA JESIRUN
NEHNU ‘A’LEMU BIMA JEKULUNE WE MA ‘ENTE ‘ALEJHIM BIXHEBBARIN FEDHEKKIR BIL-KUR’ANI MEN JEHAFU WA’IDI
WE EDH-DHARIJATI DHERWEN
FALHAMILATI WIKRÆN
FALXHARIJATI JUSRÆN
FALMUKASSIMATI ‘EMRÆN
‘INNEMA TU’ADUNE LESADIKUN
WE ‘INNE ED-DINE LEWAKI’UN
WE ES-SEMA’I DHATIL-HUBUKI
‘INNEKUM LEFI KAWLIN MUHTELIFIN
JU’UFEKU ‘ANHU MEN ‘UFIKE
KUTILEL-HARRASUNE
EL-LEDHINE HUM FI GAMRETIN SAHUNE
JES’ELUNE ‘EJJANE JEWMU ED-DINI
JEWME HUM ‘ALA EN-NARI JUFTENUNE
DHUKU FITNETEKUM HADHAL-LEDHI KUNTUM BIHI TESTA’XHILUNE
‘INNEL-MUTTEKINE FI XHENNATIN WE ‘UJUNIN
‘AHIDHINE MA ‘ATAHUM REBBUHUM ‘INNEHUM KANU KABLE DHALIKE MUHSININE
KANU KALILÆN MINEL-LEJLI MA JEHXHA’UNE
WE BIL-’ESHARI HUM JESTEGFIRUNE
WE FI ‘EMWALIHIM HEKKUN LILSSA’ILI WEL-MEHRUMI
WE FIL-’ERDI ‘AJATUN LILMUKININE
WE FI ‘ENFUSIKUM ‘EFELA TUBSIRUNE
WE FI ES-SEMA’I RIZKUKUM WE MA TU’ADUNE
FEWEREBBI ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI ‘INNEHU LEHEKKUN MITHLE MA ‘ENNEKUM TENTIKUNE
HEL ‘ETAKE HEDITHU DEJFI ‘IBRAHIMEL-MUKREMINE
‘IDH DEHALU ‘ALEJHI FEKALU SELAMÆN KALE SELAMUN KAWMUN MUNKERUNE
FERAGA ‘ILA ‘EHLIHI FEXHA’E BI’IXHLIN SEMININ
FEKARREBEHU ‘ILEJHIM KALE ‘ELA TE’KULUNE
FE’EWXHESE MINHUM HIFETEN KALU LA TEHAF WE BESHSHERUHU BIGULAMIN ‘ALIMIN
FE’EKBELETI EMRE’ETUHU FI SERRETIN FESEKKET WEXHHEHA WE KALET ‘AXHUZUN ‘AKIMUN
KALU KEDHALIKI KALE REBBUKI ‘INNEHU HUWEL-HEKIMUL-’ALIMU
KALE FEMA HATBUKUM ‘EJJUHAL-MURSELUNE
KALU ‘INNA ‘URSILNA ‘ILA KAWMIN MUXHRIMINE
LINURSILE ‘ALEJHIM HIXHARETEN MIN TININ
MUSEWWEMETEN ‘INDE RABBIKE LILMUSRIFINE
FE’EHREXHNA MEN KANE FIHA MINEL-MU’UMININE
FEMA WEXHEDNA FIHA GAJRE BEJTIN MINEL-MUSLIMINE
WE TEREKNA FIHA ‘AJETEN LILLEDHINE JEHAFUNEL-’ADHABEL-’ELIME
WE FI MUSA ‘IDH ‘ERSELNAHU ‘ILA FIR’AWNE BISULTANIN MUBININ
FETEWELLA BIRUKNIHI WE KALE SAHIRUN ‘EW MEXHNUNUN
FE’EHADHNAHU WE XHUNUDEHU FENEBEDHNAHUM FIL-JEMMI WE HUWE MULIMUN
WE FI ‘ADIN ‘IDH ‘ERSELNA ‘ALEJHIMU ER-RIHEL-’AKIME
MA TEDHERU MIN SHEJ’IN ‘ETET ‘ALEJHI ‘ILLA XHE’ALET/HU KALRREMIMI
WE FI THEMUDE ‘IDH KILE LEHUM TEMETTA’U HETTA HININ
FE’ATEW ‘AN ‘EMRI RABBIHIM FE’EHADHET/HUMU ES-SA’IKATU WE HUM JENDHURUNE
FEMA ESTETA’U MIN KIJAMIN WE MA KANU MUNTESIRINE
WE KAWME NUHIN MIN KABLU ‘INNEHUM KANU KAWMÆN FASIKINE
WE ES-SEMA’E BENEJNAHA BI’EJJDIN WE ‘INNA LEMUSI’UNE
WEL-’ERDE FERESHNAHA FENI’MEL-MAHIDUNE
WE MIN KULLI SHEJ’IN HALEKNA ZEWXHEJNI LE’ALLEKUM TEDHEKKERUNE
FEFIRRU ‘ILA ELLAHI ‘INNI LEKUM MINHU NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
WE LA TEXH’ALU ME’A ELLAHI ‘ILEHÆN ‘AHARE ‘INNI LEKUM MINHU NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
KEDHALIKE MA ‘ETAL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM MIN RESULIN ‘ILLA KALU SAHIRUN ‘EW MEXHNUNUN
‘ETEWASEW BIHI BEL HUM KAWMUN TAGUNE
FETEWELLE ‘ANHUM FEMA ‘ENTE BIMELUMIN
WE DHEKKIR FE’INNE EDH-DHIKRA TENFA’UL-MU’UMININE
WE MA HALEKTUL-XHINNE WEL-’INSE ‘ILLA LIJA’BUDUNI
MA ‘URIDU MINHUM MIN RIZKIN WE MA ‘URIDU ‘EN JUT’IMUNI
‘INNALL-LLAHE HUWE ER-REZZAKU DHUL-KUWETIL-METINU
FE’INNE LILLEDHINE DHELEMU DHENUBÆN MITHLE DHENUBI ‘ESHABIHIM FELA JESTA’XHILUNI
FEWEJLUN LILLEDHINE KEFERU MIN JEWMIHIMUL-LEDHI JU’ADUNE
WET-TURI
WE KITABIN MESTURIN
FI REKKIN MENSHURIN
WEL-BEJTIL-MA’MURI
WE ES-SEKFIL-MERFU’I
WEL-BEHRIL-MESXHURI
‘INNE ‘ADHABE RABBIKE LEWAKI’UN
MA LEHU MIN DAFI’IN
JEWME TEMURU ES-SEMA’U MEWRÆN
WE TESIRUL-XHIBALU SEJRÆN
FEWEJLUN JEWME’IDHIN LILMUKEDHDHIBINE
EL-LEDHINE HUM FI HAWDIN JEL’ABUNE
JEWME JUDA’’UNE ‘ILA NARI XHEHENNEME DA’’ÆN
HEDHIHI EN-NARU ELLETI KUNTUM BIHA TUKEDHDHIBUNE
‘EFESIHRUN HADHA ‘EM ‘ENTUM LA TUBSIRUNE
ESLEWHA FASBIRU ‘EW LA TESBIRU SEWA’UN ‘ALEJKUM ‘INNEMA TUXHZEWNE MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
‘INNEL-MUTTEKINE FI XHENNATIN WE NA’IMIN
FAKIHINE BIMA ‘ATAHUM REBBUHUM WE WEKAHUM REBBUHUM ‘ADHABEL-XHEHIMI
KULU WE ESHREBU HENI’ÆN BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
MUTTEKI’INE ‘ALA SURURIN MESFUFETIN WE ZEWWEXHNAHUM BIHURIN ‘ININ
WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ETTEBE’AT/HUM DHURRIJETUHUM BI’IMANIN ‘ELHEKNA BIHIM DHURRIJETEHUM WE MA ‘ELETNAHUM MIN ‘AMELIHIM MIN SHEJ’IN KULLU EMRI’IN BIMA KESEBE REHINUN
WE ‘EMDEDNAHUM BIFAKIHETIN WE LEHMIN MIMMA JESHTEHUNE
JETENAZA’UNE FIHA KE’SÆN LA LEGWUN FIHA WE LA TE’THIMUN
WE JETUFU ‘ALEJHIM GILMANUN LEHUM KE’ENNEHUM LU’ULU’UUN MEKNUNUN
WE ‘EKBELE BA’DUHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN JETESA’ELUNE
KALU ‘INNA KUNNA KABLU FI ‘EHLINA MUSHFIKINE
FEMENNEL-LAHU ‘ALEJNA WE WEKANA ‘ADHABE ES-SEMUMI
‘INNA KUNNA MIN KABLU NED’UHU ‘INNEHU HUWEL-BERRU ER-REHIMU
FEDHEKKIR FEMA ‘ENTE BINI’METI RABBIKE BIKAHININ WE LA MEXHNUNIN
‘EM JEKULUNE SHA’IRUN NETEREBBESU BIHI REJBEL-MENUNI
KUL TEREBBESU FE’INNI ME’AKUM MINEL-MUTEREBBISINE
‘EM TE’MURUHUM ‘EHLAMUHUM BIHEDHA ‘EM HUM KAWMUN TAGUNE
‘EM JEKULUNE TEKAWWELEHU BEL LA JU’UMINUNE
FELJE’TU BIHEDITHIN MITHLIHI ‘IN KANU SADIKINE
‘EM HULIKU MIN GAJRI SHEJ’IN ‘EM HUMUL-HALIKUNE
‘EM HALEKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BEL LA JUKINUNE
‘EM ‘INDEHUM HAZA’INU RABBIKE ‘EM HUMUL-MUSEJTIRUNE
‘EM LEHUM SULLEMUN JESTEMI’UNE FIHI FELJE’TI MUSTEMI’UHUM BISULTANIN MUBININ
‘EM LEHUL-BENATU WE LEKUMUL-BENUNE
‘EM TES’ELUHUM ‘EXHRÆN FEHUM MIN MEGREMIN MUTHKALUNE
‘EM ‘INDEHUMUL-GAJBU FEHUM JEKTUBUNE
‘EM JURIDUNE KEJDÆN FE-EL-LEDHINE KEFERU HUMUL-MEKIDUNE
‘EM LEHUM ‘ILEHUN GAJRU ELLAHI SUBHANEL-LAHI ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
WE ‘IN JEREW KISFÆN MINE ES-SEMA’I SAKITÆN JEKULU SEHABUN MERKUMUN
FEDHERHUM HETTA JULAKU JEWMEHUMUL-LEDHI FIHI JUS’AKUNE
JEWME LA JUGNI ‘ANHUM KEJDUHUM SHEJ’ÆN WE LA HUM JUNSERUNE
WE ‘INNE LILLEDHINE DHELEMU ‘ADHABÆN DUNE DHALIKE WE LEKINNE ‘EKTHEREHUM LA JA’LEMUNE
WE ESBIR LIHUKMI RABBIKE FE’INNEKE BI’A’JUNINA WE SEBBIH BIHEMDI RABBIKE HINE TEKUMU
WE MINEL-LEJLI FESEBBIHHU WE ‘IDBARE EN-NUXHUMI
WE EN-NEXHMI ‘IDHA HEWA
MA DELLE SAHIBUKUM WE MA GAWA
WE MA JENTIKU ‘ANIL-HEWA
‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA WEHJUN JUHA
‘ALLEMEHU SHEDIDUL-KUWA
DHU MIRRETIN FASTEWA
WE HUWE BIL-’UFUKIL-’A’LA
THUMME DENA FETEDELLA
FEKANE KABE KAWSEJNI ‘EW ‘EDNA
FE’EWHA ‘ILA ‘ABDIHI MA ‘EWHA
MA KEDHEBEL-FU’UADU MA RE’A
‘EFETUMARUNEHU ‘ALA MA JERA
WE LEKAD RE’AHU NEZLETEN ‘UHRA
‘INDE SIDRETIL-MUNTEHA
‘INDEHA XHENNETUL-ME’WA
‘IDH JEGSHA ES-SIDRETE MA JEGSHA
MA ZAGAL-BESERU WE MA TEGA
LEKAD RE’A MIN ‘AJATI RABBIHIL-KUBRA
‘EFERE’EJTUMUL-LATE WEL-’UZZA
WE MENÆTE ETH-THALITHETEL-’UHRA
‘ELEKUMU EDH-DHEKERU WE LEHUL-’UNTHA
TILKE ‘IDHÆN KISMETUN DIZA
‘IN HIJE ‘ILLA ‘ESMA’UN SEMMEJTUMUHA ‘ENTUM WE ‘ABA’UUKUM MA ‘ENZELEL-LAHU BIHA MIN SULTANIN ‘IN JETTEBI’UNE ‘ILLA EDH-DHENNE WE MA TEHWAL-’ENFUSU WE LEKAD XHA’EHUM MIN RABBIHIMUL-HUDA
‘EM LIL’INSANI MA TEMENNA
FELILLAHIL-’AHIRETU WEL-’ULA
WE KEM MIN MELEKIN FI ES-SEMAWATI LA TUGNI SHEFA’ATUHUM SHEJ’ÆN ‘ILLA MIN BA’DI ‘EN JE’DHENEL-LAHU LIMEN JESHA’U WE JERDA
‘INNEL-LEDHINE LA JU’UMINUNE BIL-’AHIRETI LEJUSEMMUNEL-MELA’IKETE TESMIJETEL-’UNTHA
WE MA LEHUM BIHI MIN ‘ILMIN ‘IN JETTEBI’UNE ‘ILLA EDH-DHENNE WE ‘INNE EDH-DHENNE LA JUGNI MINEL-HEKKI SHEJ’ÆN
FE’A’RID ‘AN MEN TEWELLA ‘AN DHIKRINA WE LEM JURID ‘ILLAL-HEJÆTE ED-DUNJA
DHALIKE MEBLEGUHUM MINEL-’ILMI ‘INNE REBBEKE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMEN DELLE ‘AN SEBILIHI WE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMENI EHTEDA
WE LILLEHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI LIJEXHZIJEL-LEDHINE ‘ESA’U BIMA ‘AMILU WE JEXHZIJEL-LEDHINE ‘EHSENU BIL-HUSNA
EL-LEDHINE JEXHTENIBUNE KEBA’IREL-’ITHMI WEL-FEWAHISHE ‘ILLAL-LEMEME ‘INNE REBBEKE WASI’UL-MEGFIRETI HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIKUM ‘IDH ‘ENSHE’EKUM MINEL-’ERDI WE ‘IDH ‘ENTUM ‘EXHINNETUN FI BUTUNI ‘UMMEHATIKUM FELA TUZEKKU ‘ENFUSEKUM HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMENI ETTEKA
‘EFERE’EJTEL-LEDHI TEWELLA
WE ‘A’TA KALILÆN WE ‘EKDA
‘A’INDEHU ‘ILMUL-GAJBI FEHUWE JERA

‘INNEHUM KANU KABLE DHALIKE MUTREFINE

‘EWE ‘ABA’UUNAL-’EWWELUNE
KUL ‘INNEL-’EWWELINE WEL-’AHIRINE
LEMEXHMU’UNE ‘ILA MIKATI JEWMIN MA’LUMIN
