LE’AKILUNE MIN SHEXHERIN MIN ZEKKUMIN
FEMALI’UNE MINHAL-BUTUNE
FESHARIBUNE ‘ALEJHI MINEL-HEMIMI
FESHARIBUNE SHURBEL-HIMI
HADHA NUZULUHUM JEWME ED-DINI
NEHNU HALEKNAKUM FELEWLA TUSEDDIKUNE
‘EFERE’EJTUM MA TUMNUNE
‘E’ENTUM TEHLUKUNEHU ‘EM NEHNUL-HALIKUNE
NEHNU KADDERNA BEJNEKUMUL-MEWTE WE MA NEHNU BIMESBUKINE
‘ALA ‘EN NUBEDDILE ‘EMTHALEKUM WE NUNSHI’EKUM FI MA LA TA’LEMUNE
WE LEKAD ‘ALIMTUMU EN-NESH’ETEL-’ULA FELEWLA TEDHKKERUNE
‘EFERE’EJTUM MA TEHRUTHUNE
‘E’ENTUM TEZRA’UNEHU ‘EM NEHNU EZ-ZARI’UNE
LEW NESHA’U LEXHE’ALNAHU HUTAMÆN FEDHELELTUM TEFEKKEHUNE
‘INNA LEMUGREMUNE
BEL NEHNU MEHRUMUNE
‘EFERE’EJTUMUL-MA’EL-LEDHI TESHREBUNE
‘E’ENTUM ‘ENZELTUMUHU MINEL-MUZNI ‘EM NEHNUL-MUNZILUNE
LEW NESHA’U XHE’ALNAHU ‘UXHAXHÆN FELEWLA TESHKURUNE
‘EFERE’EJTUMU EN-NAREL-LETI TURUNE
‘E’ENTUM ‘ENSHE’TUM SHEXHERETEHA ‘EM NEHNUL-MUNSHI’UNE
NEHNU XHE’ALNAHA TEDHKIRETEN WE META’ÆN LILMUKWINE
FESEBBIH BIASMI RABBIKEL-’ADHIMI
FELA ‘UKSIMU BIMEWAKI’I EN-NUXHUMI
WE ‘INNEHU LEKASEMUN LEW TA’LEMUNE ‘ADHIMUN
‘INNEHU LEKUR’ANUN KERIMUN
FI KITABIN MEKNUNIN
LA JEMESSUHU ‘ILLAL-MUTEHHERUNE
TENZILUN MIN RABBIL-’ALEMINE
‘EFEBIHEDHAL-HEDITHI ‘ENTUM MUD/HINUNE
WE TEXH’ALUNE RIZKAKUM ‘ENNEKUM TUKEDHDHIBUNE
FELEWLA ‘IDHA BELEGATIL-HULKUME
WE ‘ENTUM HINE’IDHIN TENDHURUNE
WE NEHNU ‘EKREBU ‘ILEJHI MINKUM WE LEKIN LA TUBSIRUNE
FELEWLA ‘IN KUNTUM GAJRE MEDININE
TERXHI’UNEHA ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
FE’EMMA ‘IN KANE MINEL-MUKARREBINE
FEREWHUN WE REJHANUN WE XHENNETU NA’IMIN
WE ‘EMMA ‘IN KANE MIN ‘ESHABIL-JEMINI
FESELAMUN LEKE MIN ‘ESHABIL-JEMINI
WE ‘EMMA ‘IN KANE MINEL-MUKEDHDHIBINE ED-DALLINE
FENUZULUN MIN HEMIMIN
WE TESLIJETU XHEHIMIN
‘INNE HADHA LEHUWE HEKKUL-JEKINI
FESEBBIH BIASMI RABBIKEL-’ADHIMI
SEBBEHE LILLAHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
LEHU MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI JUHJI WE JUMITU WE HUWE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
HUWEL-’EWWELU WEL-’AHIRU WE EDH-DHAHIRU WEL-BATINU WE HUWE BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMUN
HUWEL-LEDHI HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE FI SITTETI ‘EJJAMIN THUMME ESTEWA ‘ALEL-’ARSHI JA’LEMU MA JELIXHU FIL-’ERDI WE MA JEHRUXHU MINHA WE MA JENZILU MINE ES-SEMA’I WE MA JA’RUXHU FIHA WE HUWE ME’AKUM ‘EJNE MA KUNTUM WEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRUN
LEHU MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE ‘ILA ELLAHI TURXHA’UL-’UMURU
JULIXHUL-LEJLE FI EN-NEHARI WE JULIXHU EN-NEHARE FIL-LEJLI WE HUWE ‘ALIMUN BIDHATI ES-SUDURI
‘AMINU BILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE ‘ENFIKU MIMMA XHE’ALEKUM MUSTEHLEFINE FIHI FE-EL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU MINKUM WE ‘ENFEKU LEHUM ‘EXHRUN KEBIRUN
WE MA LEKUM LA TU’UMINUNE BILLAHI WE ER-RESULU JED’UKUM LITU’UMINU BIREBBIKUM WE KAD ‘EHADHE MITHAKAKUM ‘IN KUNTUM MU’UMININE
HUWEL-LEDHI JUNEZZILU ‘ALA ‘ABDIHI ‘AJATIN BEJJINATIN LIJUHRIXHEKUM MINE EDH-DHULUMATI ‘ILA EN-NURI WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE BIKUM LERE’UFUN REHIMUN
WE MA LEKUM ‘ELLA TUNFIKU FI SEBILI ELLAHI WE LILLEHI MIRATHU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI LA JESTEWI MINKUM MEN ‘ENFEKA MIN KABLIL-FETHI WE KATELE ‘ULA’IKE ‘A’DHEMU DEREXHETEN MINEL-LEDHINE ‘ENFEKU MIN BA’DU WE KATELU WE KULLÆN WE’ADEL-LAHUL-HUSNA WEL-LAHU BIMA
MEN DHAL-LEDHI JUKRIDU ELLAHE KARDÆN HESENÆN FEJUDA’IFEHU LEHU WE LEHU ‘EXHRUN KERIMUN
JEWME TERAL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI JES’A NURUHUM BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE BI’EJMANIHIM BUSHRAKUMUL-JEWME XHENNATUN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA DHALIKE HUWEL-FEWZUL-’ADHIMU
JEWME JEKULUL-MUNAFIKUNE WEL-MUNAFIKATU LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU ENDHURUNA NEKTEBIS MIN NURIKUM KILE ERXHI’U WERA’EKUM FALTEMISU NURÆN FEDURIBE BEJNEHUM BISURIN LEHU BABUN BATINUHU FIHI ER-REHMETU WE DHAHIRUHU MIN KIBELIHIL-’ADHABU
JUNADUNEHUM ‘ELEM NEKUN ME’AKUM KALU BELA WE LEKINNEKUM FETENTUM ‘ENFUSEKUM WE TEREBBESTUM WE ERTEBTUM WE GARRETKUMUL-’EMANIJU HETTA XHA’E ‘EMRU ELLAHI WE GARREKUM BILLAHIL-GARURU
FALJEWME LA JU’UHADHU MINKUM FIDJETUN WE LA MINEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ME’WAKUMU EN-NARU HIJE MEWLAKUM WE BI’SEL-MESIRU
‘ELEM JE’NI LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘EN TEHSHE’A KULUBUHUM LIDHIKRI ELLAHI WE MA NEZELE MINEL-HEKKI WE LA JEKUNU KALLEDHINE ‘UTUL-KITABE MIN KABLU FETALE ‘ALEJHIMUL-’EMEDU FEKASET KULUBUHUM WE KETHIRUN MINHUM FASIKUNE
A’LEMU ‘ENNEL-LAHE JUHJIL-’ERDE BA’DE MEWTIHA KAD BEJJENNA LEKUMUL-’AJATI LE’ALLEKUM TA’KILUNE
‘INNEL-MUSSEDDIKINE WEL-MUSSEDDIKATI WE ‘EKREDU ELLAHE KARDÆN HESENÆN JUDA’AFU LEHUM WE LEHUM ‘EXHRUN KERIMUN
WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU BILLAHI WE RUSULIHI ‘ULA’IKE HUMU ES-SIDDIKUNE WE ESH-SHUHEDA’U ‘INDE RABBIHIM LEHUM ‘EXHRUHUM WE NURUHUM WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATINA ‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABUL-XHEHIMI
A’LEMU ‘ENNEMAL-HEJÆTU ED-DUNJA LA’IBUN WE LEHWUN WE ZINETUN WE TEFAHURUN BEJNEKUM WE TEKATHURUN FIL-’EMWLI WEL-’EWLADI KEMETHELI GAJTHIN ‘A’XHEBEL-KUFFARE NEBATUHU THUMME JEHIXHU FETERAHU MUSFERRÆN THUMME JEKUNU HUTAMÆN WE FIL-’AHIRETI ‘ADHABUN SHEDIDUN 
SABIKU ‘ILA MEGFIRETIN MIN RABBIKUM WE XHENNETIN ‘ARDUHA KE’ARDI ES-SEMA’I WEL-’ERDI ‘U’IDDET LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU BILLAHI WE RUSULIHI DHALIKE FEDLU ELLAHI JU’UTIHI MEN JESHA’U WEL-LAHU DHUL-FEDLIL-’ADHIMI
MA ‘ESABE MIN MUSIBETIN FIL-’ERDI WE LA FI ‘ENFUSIKUM ‘ILLA FI KITABIN MIN KABLI ‘EN NEBRE’EHA ‘INNE DHALIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI JESIRUN
LIKEJLA TE’SEW ‘ALA MA FATEKUM WE LA TEFREHU BIMA ‘ATAKUM WEL-LAHU LA JUHIBBU KULLE MUHTALIN FEHURIN
EL-LEDHINE JEBHALUNE WE JE’MURUNE EN-NASE BIL-BUHLI WE MEN JETEWELLE FE’INNALL-LLAHE HUWEL-GANIJUL-HEMIDU
LEKAD ‘ERSELNA RUSULENA BIL-BEJJINATI WE ‘ENZELNA ME’AHUMUL-KITABE WEL-MIZANE LIJEKUME EN-NASU BIL-KISTI WE ‘ENZELNAL-HEDIDE FIHI BE’SUN SHEDIDUN WE MENAFI’U LILNNASI WE LIJA’LEMEL-LAHU MEN JENSURUHU WE RUSULEHU BIL-GAJBI ‘INNALL-LLAHE KAWIJUN ‘AZIZUN
WE LEKAD ‘ERSELNA NUHÆN WE ‘IBRAHIME WE XHE’ALNA FI DHURRIJETIHIMA EN-NUBUWETE WEL-KITABE FEMINHUM MUHTEDIN WE KETHIRUN MINHUM FASIKUNE
THUMME KAFFEJNA ‘ALA ‘ATHARIHIM BIRUSULINA WE KAFFEJNA BI’ISA EBNI MERJEME WE ‘ATEJNAHUL-’INXHILE WE XHE’ALNA FI KULUBIL-LEDHINE ETTEBA’UHU RE’FETEN WE REHMETEN WE REHBANIJETEN EBTEDA’UHA MA KETEBNAHA ‘ALEJHIM ‘ILLA EBTIGA’E RIDWANI ELLAHI FEMA RE’AWHA HE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ETTEKU ELLAHE WE ‘AMINU BIRESULIHI JU’UTIKUM KIFLEJNI MIN REHMETIHI WE JEXH’AL LEKUM NURÆN TEMSHUNE BIHI WE JEGFIR LEKUM WEL-LAHU GAFURUN REHIMUN
LI’ELLA JA’LEME ‘EHLUL-KITABI ‘ELLA JEKDIRUNE ‘ALA SHEJ’IN MIN FEDLI ELLAHI WE ‘ENNEL-FEDLE BIJEDI ELLAHI JU’UTIHI MEN JESHA’U WEL-LAHU DHUL-FEDLIL-’ADHIMI
KAD SEMI’ALLAHU KAWLEL-LETI TUXHADILUKE FI ZEWXHIHA WE TESHTEKI ‘ILA ELLAHI WEL-LAHU JESMA’U TEHAWUREKUMA ‘INNALL-LLAHE SEMI’UN BESIRUN
EL-LEDHINE JUDHAHIRUNE MINKUM MIN NISA’IHIM MA HUNNE ‘UMMEHATIHIM ‘IN ‘UMMEHATUHUM ‘ILLAL-LA’I WELEDNEHUM WE ‘INNEHUM LEJEKULUNE MUNKERÆN MINEL-KAWLI WE ZURÆN WE ‘INNALL-LLAHE LE’AFUWUN GAFURUN
WEL-LEDHINE JUDHAHIRUNE MIN NISA’IHIM THUMME JA’UDUNE LIMA KALU FETEHRIRU REKABETIN MIN KABLI ‘EN JETEMASSA DHALIKUM TU’ADHUNE BIHI WEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE HABIRUN
FEMEN LEM JEXHID FESIJAMU SHEHREJNI MUTETABI’AJNI MIN KABLI ‘EN JETEMASSA FEMEN LEM JESTETI’ FE’IT’AMU SITTINE MISKINÆN DHALIKE LITU’UMINU BILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE TILKE HUDUDU ELLAHI WE LILKAFIRINE ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JUHADDUNEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU KUBITU KEMA KUBITEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM WE KAD ‘ENZELNA ‘AJATIN BEJJINATIN WE LILKAFIRINE ‘ADHABUN MUHINUN
JEWME JEB’ATHUHUMU ELLAHU XHEMI’ÆN FEJUNEBBI’UHUM BIMA ‘AMILU ‘EHSAHU ELLAHU WE NESUHU WEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN SHEHIDUN
‘ELEM TERA ‘ENNEL-LAHE JA’LEMU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI MA JEKUNU MIN NEXHWA THELATHETIN ‘ILLA HUWE RABI’UHUM WE LA HAMSETIN ‘ILLA HUWE SADISUHUM WE LA ‘EDNA MIN DHALIKE WE LA ‘EKTHERE ‘ILLA HUWE ME’AHUM ‘EJNE MA KANU THUMME JUNEBBI’UHUM BIMA ‘AM
‘ELEM TERA ‘ILAL-LEDHINE NUHU ‘ANI EN-NEXHWA THUMME JA’UDUNE LIMA NUHU ‘ANHU WE JETENAXHEWNE BIL-’ITHMI WEL-’UDWANI WE MA’SIJETI ER-RESULI WE ‘IDHA XHA’UKE HEJJEWKE BIMA LEM JUHEJJIKE BIHI ELLAHU WE JEKULUNE FI ‘ENFUSIHIM LEWLA JU’ADHDHIBUNALLAHU BIMA NEK
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IDHA TENAXHEJTUM FELA TETENAXHEW BIL-’ITHMI WEL-’UDWANI WE MA’SIJETI ER-RESULI WE TENAXHEW BIL-BIRRI WET-TEKWA WE ETTEKU ELLAHEL-LEDHI ‘ILEJHI TUHSHERUNE
‘INNEMA EN-NEXHWA MINE ESH-SHEJTANI LIJEHZUNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE LEJSE BIDARRIHIM SHEJ’ÆN ‘ILLA BI’IDHNI ELLAHI WE ‘ALA ELLAHI FELJETEWEKKELIL-MU’UMINUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IDHA KILE LEKUM TEFESSEHU FIL-MEXHALISI FAFSEHU JEFSEHI ELLAHU LEKUM WE ‘IDHA KILE ENSHUZU FANSHUZU JERFA’I ELLAHUL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU MINKUM WEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-’ILME DEREXHATIN WEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE HABIRUN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IDHA NAXHEJTUMU ER-RESULE FEKADDIMU BEJNE JEDEJ NEXHWAKUM SEDEKATEN DHALIKE HAJRUN LEKUM WE ‘ETHERU FE’IN LEM TEXHIDU FE’INNALL-LLAHE GAFURUN REHIMUN
‘E’ESHFEKTUM ‘EN TUKADDIMU BEJNE JEDEJ NEXHWAKUM SEDEKATIN FE’IDH LEM TEF’ALU WE TABEL-LAHU ‘ALEJKUM FE’EKIMU ES-SELÆTE WE ‘ATU EZ-ZEKÆTE WE ‘ETI’U ELLAHE WE RESULEHU WEL-LAHU HABIRUN BIMA TA’MELUNE
‘ELEM TERA ‘ILAL-LEDHINE TEWELLEW KAWMÆN GADIBEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHIM MA HUM MINKUM WE LA MINHUM WE JEHLIFUNE ‘ALEL-KEDHIBI WE HUM JA’LEMUNE
‘E’ADDEL-LAHU LEHUM ‘ADHABÆN SHEDIDÆN ‘INNEHUM SA’E MA KANU JA’MELUNE
ETTEHADHU ‘EJMANEHUM XHUNNETEN FESEDDU ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI FELEHUM ‘ADHABUN MUHINUN
LEN TUGNIJE ‘ANHUM ‘EMWALUHUM WE LA ‘EWLADUHUM MINEL-LAHI SHEJ’ÆN ‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABU EN-NARI HUM FIHA HALIDUNE
JEWME JEB’ATHUHUMU ELLAHU XHEMI’ÆN FEJEHLIFUNE LEHU KEMA JEHLIFUNE LEKUM WE JEHSEBUNE ‘ENNEHUM ‘ALA SHEJ’IN ‘ELA ‘INNEHUM HUMUL-KADHIBUNE
ESTEHWEDHE ‘ALEJHIMU ESH-SHEJTANU FE’ENSAHUM DHIKREL-LAHI ‘ULA’IKE HIZBU ESH-SHEJTANI ‘ELA ‘INNE HIZBE ESH-SHEJTANI HUMUL-HASIRUNE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JUHADDUNEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU ‘ULA’IKE FIL-’EDHELLINE
KETEBEL-LAHU LE’EGLIBENNE ‘ENA WE RUSULI ‘INNALL-LLAHE KAWIJUN ‘AZIZUN
LA TEXHIDU KAWMÆN JU’UMINUNE BILLAHI WEL-JEWMIL-’AHIRI JUWADDUNE MEN HADDEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU WE LEW KANU ‘ABA’EHUM ‘EW ‘EBNA’EHUM ‘EW ‘IHWANEHUM ‘EW ‘ASHIRETEHUM ‘ULA’IKE KETEBE FI KULUBIHIMUL-’IMANE WE ‘EJJEDEHUM BIRUHIN MINHU WE JUDHILUHUM XHENNATIN TEX
SEBBEHE LILLAHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
HUWEL-LEDHI ‘EHREXHEL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN ‘EHLIL-KITABI MIN DIJARIHIM LI’WWELIL-HESHRI MA DHENENTUM ‘EN JEHRUXHU WE DHENNU ‘ENNEHUM MANI’ATUHUM HUSUNUHUM MINEL-LAHI FE’ETAHUMU ELLAHU MIN HEJTHU LEM JEHTESIBU WE KADHEFE FI KULUBIHIMU ER-RU’BE JUHRIBUNE BUJU
WE LEWLA ‘EN KETEBEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHIMUL-XHELA’E LE’ADHDHEBEHUM FI ED-DUNJA WE LEHUM FIL-’AHIRETI ‘ADHABU EN-NARI
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUM SHAKKU ELLAHE WE RESULEHU WE MEN JUSHAKKI ELLAHE FE’INNALL-LLAHE SHEDIDUL-’IKABI
MA KATA’TUM MIN LINETIN ‘EW TEREKTUMUHA KA’IMETEN ‘ALA ‘USULIHA FEBI’IDHNI ELLAHI WE LIJUHZIJEL-FASIKINE
WE MA ‘EFA’EL-LAHU ‘ALA RESULIHI MINHUM FEMA ‘EWXHEFTUM ‘ALEJHI MIN HAJLIN WE LA RIKABIN WE LEKINNALL-LLAHE JUSELLITU RUSULEHU ‘ALA MEN JESHA’U WEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
MA ‘EFA’EL-LAHU ‘ALA RESULIHI MIN ‘EHLIL-KURA FELILLAHI WE LILRRESULI WE LIDHIL-KURBA WEL-JETAMA WEL-MESAKINI WE EBNI ES-SEBILI KEJ LA JEKUNE DULETEN BEJNEL-’EGNIJA’I MINKUM WE MA ‘ATAKUMU ER-RESULU FEHUDHUHU WE MA NEHAKUM ‘ANHU FANTEHU WE ETTEKU ELLAHE ‘
LILFUKARA’IL-MUHAXHIRINEL-LEDHINE ‘UHRIXHU MIN DIARIHIM WE ‘EMWALIHIM JEBTEGUNE FEDLÆN MINEL-LAHI WE RIDWANÆN WE JENSURUNEL-LAHE WE RESULEHU ‘ULA’IKE HUMU ES-SADIKUNE
WEL-LEDHINE TEBEWWE’U ED-DARE WEL-’IMANE MIN KABLIHIM JUHIBBUNE MEN HAXHERE ‘ILEJHIM WE LA JEXHIDUNE FI SUDURIHIM HAXHETEN MIMMA ‘UTU WE JU’UTHIRUNE ‘ALA ‘ENFUSIHIM WE LEW KANE BIHIM HASASETUN WE MEN JUKA SHUHHE NEFSIHI FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUFLIHUNE
WEL-LEDHINE XHA’U MIN BA’DIHIM JEKULUNE REBBENA EGFIR LENA WE LI’EHWANINAL-LEDHINE SEBEKUNA BIL-’IMANI WE LA TEXH’AL FI KULUBINA GILLÆN LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU REBBENA ‘INNEKE RE’UFUN REHIMUN
‘ELEM TERA ‘ILAL-LEDHINE NAFEKU JEKULUNE LI’HWANIHIMUL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN ‘EHLIL-KITABI LE’IN ‘UHRIXHTUM LENEHRUXHENNE ME’AKUM WE LA NUTI’U FIKUM ‘EHEDÆN ‘EBEDÆN WE ‘IN KUTILTUM LENENSURENNEKUM WEL-LAHU JESH/HEDU ‘INNEHUM LEKADHIBUNE
LE’IN ‘UHRIXHU LA JEHRUXHUNE ME’AHUM WE LE’IN KUTILU LA JENSURUNEHUM WE LE’IN NESERUHUM LEJUWELLUNNEL-’EDBARE THUMME LA JUNSERUNE
LE’ENTUM ‘ESHEDDU REHBETEN FI SUDURIHIM MINEL-LAHI DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUM KAWMUN LA JEFKAHUNE
LA JUKATILUNEKUM XHEMI’ÆN ‘ILLA FI KUREN MUHESSENETIN ‘EW MIN WERA’I XHUDURIN BE’SUHUM BEJNEHUM SHEDIDUN TEHSEBUHUM XHEMI’ÆN WE KULUBUHUM SHETTA DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUM KAWMUN LA JA’KILUNE
KEMETHELIL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM KARIBÆN DHAKU WEBALE ‘EMRIHIM WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
KEMETHELI ESH-SHEJTANI ‘IDH KALE LIL’INSANI EKFUR FELEMMA KEFERE KALE ‘INNI BERI’UN MINKE ‘INNI ‘EHAFU ELLAHE REBBEL-’ALEMINE
FEKANE ‘AKIBETEHUMA ‘ENNEHUMA FI EN-NARI HALIDEJNI FIHA WE DHELIKE XHEZA’U EDH-DHALIMINE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ETTEKU ELLAHE WE LTENDHUR NEFSUN MA KADDEMET LIGADIN WE ETTEKU ELLAHE ‘INNALL-LLAHE HABIRUN BIMA TA’MELUNE
WE LA TEKUNU KALLEDHINE NESU ELLAHE FE’ENSAHUM ‘ENFUSEHUM ‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-FASIKUNE
LA JESTEWI ‘ESHABU EN-NARI WE ‘ESHABUL-XHENNETI ‘ESHABUL-XHENNETI HUMUL-FA’IZUNE
LEW ‘ENZELNA HADHAL-KUR’ANE ‘ALA XHEBELIN LERE’EJTEHU HASHI’ÆN MUTESEDDI’ÆN MIN HASHJETI ELLAHI WE TILKEL-’EMTHALU NEDRIBUHA LILNNASI LE’ALLEHUM JETEFEKKERUNE
HUWEL-LAHUL-LEDHI LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE ‘ALIMUL-GAJBI WE ESH-SHEHADETI HUWE ER-REHMANU ER-REHIMU
HUWEL-LAHUL-LEDHI LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWEL-MELIKUL-KUDDUSU ES-SELAMUL-MU’UMINUL-MUHEJMINUL-’AZIZUL-XHEBBARUL-MUTEKEBBIRU SUBHANEL-LAHI ‘AMMA JUSHRIKUNE
HUWEL-LAHUL-HALIKUL-BARI’UL-MUSEWWIRU LEHUL-’ESMA’UL-HUSNA JUSEBBIHU LEHU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TETTEHIDHU ‘ADUWI WE ‘ADUWEKUM ‘EWLIJA’E TULKUNE ‘ILEJHIM BIL-MEWEDDETI WE KAD KEFERU BIMA XHA’EKUM MINEL-HEKKI JUHRIXHUNE ER-RESULE WE ‘IJAKUM ‘EN TU’UMINU BILLAHI RABBIKUM ‘IN KUNTUM HAREXHTUM XHIHADÆN FI SEBILI WE EBTIGA’E
‘IN JETHKAFUKUM JEKUNU LEKUM ‘A’DA’EN WE JEBSUTU ‘ILEJKUM ‘EJDIJEHUM WE ‘ELSINETEHUM BIS-SU’I WE WEDDU LEW TEKFURUNE
LEN TENFE’AKUM ‘ERHAMUKUM WE LA ‘EWLADUKUM JEWMEL-KIJAMETI JEFSILU BEJNEKUM WEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRUN
KAD KANET LEKUM ‘USWETUN HESENETUN FI ‘IBRAHIME WEL-LEDHINE ME’AHU ‘IDH KALU LIKAWMIHIM ‘INNA BURE’A’U MINKUM WE MIMMA TA’BUDUNE MIN DUNI ELLAHI KEFERNA BIKUM WE BEDA BEJNENA WE BEJNEKUMUL-’ADAWETU WEL-BEGDA’U ‘EBEDÆN HETTA TU’UMINU BILLAHI WEHDEHU ‘ILLA 
REBBENA LA TEXH’ALNA FITNETEN LILLEDHINE KEFERU WE EGFIR LENA REBBENA ‘INNEKE ‘ENTEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
LEKAD KANE LEKUM FIHIM ‘USWETUN HESENETUN LIMEN KANE JERXHU ELLAHE WEL-JEWMEL-’AHIRE WE MEN JETEWELLE FE’INNALL-LLAHE HUWEL-GANIJUL-HEMIDU
‘ASALLAHU ‘EN JEXH’ALE BEJNEKUM WE BEJNEL-LEDHINE ‘ADEJTUM MINHUM MEWEDDETEN WEL-LAHU KADIRUN WEL-LAHU GAFURUN REHIMUN
LA JENHAKUMU ELLAHU ‘ANIL-LEDHINE LEM JUKATILUKUM FI ED-DINI WE LEM JUHRIXHUKUM MIN DIJARIKUM ‘EN TEBERRUHUM WE TUKSITU ‘ILEJHIM ‘INNALL-LLAHE JUHIBBUL-MUKSITINE
‘INNEMA JENHAKUMU ELLAHU ‘ANIL-LEDHINE KATELUKUM FI ED-DINI WE ‘EHREXHUKUM MIN DIJARIKUM WE DHAHERU ‘ALA ‘IHRAXHIKUM ‘EN TEWELLEWHUM WE MEN JETEWELLEHUM FE’ULA’IKE HUMU EDH-DHALIMUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IDHA XHA’EKUMUL-MU’UMINATU MUHAXHIRATIN FAMTEHINUHUNNEL-LAHU ‘A’LEMU BI’IMANIHINNE FE’IN ‘ALIMTUMUHUNNE MU’UMINATIN FELA TERXHI’UHUNNE ‘ILAL-KUFFARI LA HUNNE HILLUN LEHUM WE LA HUM JEHILLUNE LEHUNNE WE ‘ATUHUM MA ‘ENFEKU WE LA 
WE ‘IN FATEKUM SHEJ’UN MIN ‘EZWAXHIKUM ‘ILAL-KUFFARI FA’AKABTUM FE’ATUL-LEDHINE DHEHEBET ‘EZWAXHUHUM MITHLE MA ‘ENFEKU WE ETTEKU ELLAHEL-LEDHI ‘ENTUM BIHI MU’UMINUNE
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU ‘IDHA XHA’EKEL-MU’UMINATU JUBAJI’NEKE ‘ALA ‘EN LA JUSHRIKNE BILLAHI SHEJ’ÆN WE LA JESRIKNE WE LA JEZNINE WE LA JEKTULNE ‘EWLADEHUNNE WE LA JE’TINE BIBUHTANIN JEFTERINEHU BEJNE ‘EJDIHINNE WE ‘ERXHULIHINNE WE LA JA’SINEKE FI MA’RUFIN FE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TETEWELLEW KAWMÆN GADIBEL-LAHU ‘ALEJHIM KAD JE’ISU MINEL-’AHIRETI KEMA JE’ISEL-KUFFARU MIN ‘ESHABIL-KUBURI
SEBBEHE LILLAHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘ÆMENU LIME TEKULUNE MA LA TEF’ALUNE
KEBURE MEKTÆN ‘INDEL-LAHI ‘EN TEKULU MA LA TEF’ALUNE
‘INNALL-LLAHE JUHIBBUL-LEDHINE JUKATILUNE FI SEBILIHI SEFFÆN KE’ENNEHUM BUNJANUN MERSUSUN
WE ‘IDH KALE MUSA LIKAWMIHI JA KAWMI LIME TU’UDHUNENI WE KAD TA’LEMUNE ‘ENNI RESULU ELLAHI ‘ILEJKUM FELEMMA ZAGU ‘EZAGALLAHU KULUBEHUM WEL-LAHU LA JEHDIL-KAWMEL-FASIKINE
WE ‘IDH KALE ‘ISA EBNU MERJEME JA BENI ‘ISRA’ILE ‘INNI RESULU ELLAHI ‘ILEJKUM MUSEDDIKÆN LIMA BEJNE JEDEJJE MINET-TEWRÆTI WE MUBESHSHIRÆN BIRESULIN JE’TI MIN BA’DI ESMUHU ‘EHMEDU FELEMMA XHA’EHUM BIL-BEJJINATI KALU HADHA SIHRUN MUBINUN
WE MEN ‘EDHLEMU MIMMENI EFTERA ‘ALA ELLAHIL-KEDHIBE WE HUWE JUD’A ‘ILAL-’ISLAMI WEL-LAHU LA JEHDIL-KAWME EDH-DHALIMINE
JURIDUNE LIJUTFI’U NUREL-LAHI BI’EFWAHIHIM WEL-LAHU MUTIMMU NURIHI WE LEW KERIHEL-KAFIRUNE
HUWEL-LEDHI ‘ERSELE RESULEHU BIL-HUDA WE DINIL-HEKKI LIJUDHHIREHU ‘ALA ED-DINI KULLIHI WE LEW KERIHEL-MUSHRIKUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘ÆMENU HEL ‘EDULLUKUM ‘ALA TIXHARETIN TUNXHIKUM MIN ‘ADHABIN ‘ELIMIN
TU’UMINUNE BILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE TUXHAHIDUNE FI SEBILI ELLAHI BI’EMWALIKUM WE ‘ENFUSIKUM DHALIKUM HAJRUN LEKUM ‘IN KUNTUM TA’LEMUNE
JEGFIR LEKUM DHUNUBEKUM WE JUDHILKUM XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU WE MESAKINE TEJJIBETEN FI XHENNATI ‘ADNIN DHALIKEL-FEWZUL-’ADHIMU
WE ‘UHRA TUHIBBUNEHA NESRUN MINEL-LAHI WE FETHUN KARIBUN WE BESHSHIRIL-MU’UMININE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘ÆMENU KUNW ‘ENSAREL-LAHI KEMA KALE ‘ISA EBNU MERJEME LILHEWARIJINE MEN ‘ENSARI ‘ILA ELLAHI KALEL-HEWARIJUNE NEHNU ‘ENSARU ELLAHI FE’ÆMENET TA’IFETUN MIN BENI ‘ISRA’ILE WE KEFERET TA’IFETUN FE’EJJEDNAL-LEDHINE ‘ÆMENU ‘ALA ‘ADUWIHIM FE’
JUSEBBIHU LILLAHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDIL-MELIKIL-KUDDUSIL-’AZIZIL-HEKIMI
HUWEL-LEDHI BE’ATHE FIL-’UMMIJINE RESULÆN MINHUM JETLU ‘ALEJHIM ‘AJATIHI WE JUZEKKIHIM WE JU’ALLIMUHUMUL-KITABE WEL-HIKMETE WE ‘IN KANU MIN KABLU LEFI DELALIN MUBININ
WE ‘AHARINE MINHUM LEMMA JELHEKU BIHIM WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
DHALIKE FEDLU ELLAHI JU’UTIHI MEN JESHA’U WEL-LAHU DHUL-FEDLIL-’ADHIMI
METHELUL-LEDHINE HUMMILUT-TEWRÆTE THUMME LEM JEHMILUHA KEMETHELIL-HIMARI JEHMILU ‘ESFARÆN BI’SE METHELUL-KAWMIL-LEDHINE KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATI ELLAHI WEL-LAHU LA JEHDIL-KAWME EDH-DHALIMINE
KUL JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE HADU ‘IN ZE’AMTUM ‘ENNEKUM ‘EWLIJA ‘U LILLAHI MIN DUNI EN-NASI FETEMENNEWL-MEWTE ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
WE LA JETEMENNEWNEHU ‘EBEDÆN BIMA KADDEMET ‘EJDIHIM WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN BIDH-DHALIMINE
KUL ‘INNEL-MEWTEL-LEDHI TEFIRRUNE MINHU FE’INNEHU MULAKIKUM THUMME TUREDDUNE ‘ILA ‘ALIMIL-GAJBI WE ESH-SHEHADETI FEJUNEBBI’UKUM BIMA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IDHA NUDI LILSSELÆTI MIN JEWMIL-XHUMU’ATI FAS’AW ‘ILA DHIKRI ELLAHI WE DHERUL-BEJ’A DHALIKUM HAJRUN LEKUM ‘IN KUNTUM TA’LEMUNE
FE’IDHA KUDIJETI ES-SELÆTU FANTESHIRU FIL-’ERDI WE EBTEGU MIN FEDLI ELLAHI WE EDHKURU ELLAHE KETHIRÆN LE’ALLEKUM TUFLIHUNE
WE ‘IDHA RE’EW TIXHARETEN ‘EW LEHWEN ENFEDDU ‘ILEJHA WE TEREKUKE KA’IMÆN KUL MA ‘INDEL-LAHI HAJRUN MINEL-LEHWI WE MINET-TIXHARETI WEL-LAHU HAJRU ER-RAZIKINE
‘IDHA XHA’EKEL-MUNAFIKUNE KALU NESH/HEDU ‘INNEKE LERESULU ELLAHI WEL-LAHU JA’LEMU ‘INNEKE LERESULUHU WEL-LAHU JESH/HEDU ‘INNEL-MUNAFIKINE LEKADHIBUNE
ETTEHADHU ‘EJMANEHUM XHUNNETEN FESEDDU ‘AN SEBILI ELLAHI ‘INNEHUM SA’E MA KANU JA’MELUNE
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHUM ‘AMENU THUMME KEFERU FETUBI’A ‘ALA KULUBIHIM FEHUM LA JEFKAHUNE
WE ‘IDHA RE’EJTEHUM TU’XHIBUKE ‘EXHSAMUHUM WE ‘IN JEKULU TESMA’ LIKAWLIHIM KE’ENNEHUM HUSHUBUN MUSENNEDETUN JEHSEBUNE KULLE SEJHETIN ‘ALEJHIM HUMUL-’ADUWU FAHDHERHUM KATELEHUMU ELLAHU ‘ENNA JU’UFEKUNE
WE ‘IDHA KILE LEHUM TA’ALEW JESTEGFIR LEKUM RESULU ELLAHI LEWWEW RU’USEHUM WE RE’EJTEHUM JESUDDUNE WE HUM MUSTEKBIRUNE
SEWA’UN ‘ALEJHIM ‘ASTEGFERTE LEHUM ‘EM LEM TESTEGFIR LEHUM LEN JEGFIREL-LAHU LEHUM ‘INNALL-LLAHE LA JEHDIL-KAWMEL-FASIKINE
HUMUL-LEDHINE JEKULUNE LA TUNFIKU ‘ALA MEN ‘INDE RESULI ELLAHI HETTA JENFEDDU WE LILLEHI HAZA’INU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE LEKINNEL-MUNAFIKINE LA JEFKAHUNE
JEKULUNE LE’IN REXHA’NA ‘ILAL-MEDINETI LEJUHRIXHENNEL-’E’AZZU MINHAL-’EDHELLE WE LILLEHIL-’IZZETU WE LIRESULIHI WE LILMU’UMININE WE LEKINNEL-MUNAFIKINE LA JA’LEMUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU LA TULHIKUM ‘EMWALUKUM WE LA ‘EWLADUKUM ‘AN DHIKRI ELLAHI WE MEN JEF’AL DHALIKE FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-HASIRUNE
WE ‘ENFIKU MIN MA REZEKNAKUM MIN KABLI ‘EN JE’TIJE ‘EHEDEKUMUL-MEWTU FEJEKULE RABBI LEWLA ‘EHHARTENI ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN KARIBIN FE’ESSEDDEKA WE ‘EKUN MINE ES-SALIHINE
WE LEN JU’UEHHIREL-LAHU NEFSÆN ‘IDHA XHA’E ‘EXHELUHA WEL-LAHU HABIRUN BIMA TA’MELUNE
JUSEBBIHU LILLAHI MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WE MA FIL-’ERDI LEHUL-MULKU WE LEHUL-HEMDU WE HUWE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
HUWEL-LEDHI HALEKAKUM FEMINKUM KAFIRUN WE MINKUM MU’UMINUN WEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE BESIRUN
HALEKA ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDE BIL-HEKKI WE SEWWEREKUM FE’EHSENE SUWEREKUM WE ‘ILEJHIL-MESIRU
JA’LEMU MA FI ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WE JA’LEMU MA TUSIRRUNE WE MA TU’LINUNE WEL-LAHU ‘ALIMUN BIDHATI ES-SUDURI
‘ELEM JE’TIKUM NEBE’UL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN KABLU FEDHAKU WEBALE ‘EMRIHIM WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
DHALIKE BI’ENNEHU KANET TE’TIHIM RUSULUHUM BIL-BEJJINATI FEKALU ‘EBESHERUN JEHDUNENA FEKEFERU WE TEWELLEW WE ESTEGNALLAHU WEL-LAHU GANIJUN HEMIDUN
ZE’AMEL-LEDHINE KEFERU ‘EN LEN JUB’ATHU KUL BELA WE RABBI LETUB’ATHUNNE THUMME LETUNEBBE’UUNNE BIMA ‘AMILTUM WE DHELIKE ‘ALA ELLAHI JESIRUN
FE’AMINU BILLAHI WE RESULIHI WE EN-NURIL-LEDHI ‘ENZELNA WEL-LAHU BIMA TA’MELUNE HABIRUN
JEWME JEXHMA’UKUM LIJEWMIL-XHEM’I DHALIKE JEWMUT-TEGABUNI WE MEN JU’UMIN BILLAHI WE JA’MEL SALIHÆN JUKEFFIR ‘ANHU SEJJI’ATIHI WE JUDHILHU XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA ‘EBEDÆN DHALIKEL-FEWZUL-’ADHIMU
WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE KEDHDHEBU BI’AJATINA ‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABU EN-NARI HALIDINE FIHA WE BI’SEL-MESIRU
MA ‘ESABE MIN MUSIBETIN ‘ILLA BI’IDHNI ELLAHI WE MEN JU’UMIN BILLAHI JEHDI KALBEHU WEL-LAHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ALIMUN
WE ‘ETI’U ELLAHE WE ‘ETI’U ER-RESULE FE’IN TEWELLEJTUM FE’INNEMA ‘ALA RESULINAL-BELAGUL-MUBINU
ELLAHU LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE WE ‘ALA ELLAHI FELJETEWEKKELIL-MU’UMINUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘INNE MIN ‘EZWAXHIKUM WE ‘EWLADIKUM ‘ADUWÆN LEKUM FAHDHERUHUM WE ‘IN TA’FU WE TESFEHU WE TEGFIRU FE’INNALL-LLAHE GAFURUN REHIMUN
‘INNEMA ‘EMWALUKUM WE ‘EWLADUKUM FITNETUN WEL-LAHU ‘INDEHU ‘EXHRUN ‘ADHIMUN
FATTEKU ELLAHE MA ESTETA’TUM WE ESMA’U WE ‘ETI’U WE ‘ENFIKU HAJRÆN LI’NFUSIKUM WE MEN JUKA SHUHHE NEFSIHI FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-MUFLIHUNE
‘IN TUKRIDU ELLAHE KARDÆN HESENÆN JUDA’IFHU LEKUM WE JEGFIR LEKUM WEL-LAHU SHEKURUN HELIMUN
‘ALIMUL-GAJBI WE ESH-SHEHADETIL-’AZIZUL-HEKIMU
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU ‘IDHA TELLEKTUMU EN-NISA’ FETELLIKUHUNNE LI’IDDETIHINNE WE ‘EHSUL-’IDDETE WE ETTEKU ELLAHE REBBEKUM LA TUHRIXHUHUNNE MIN BUJUTIHINNE WE LA JEHRUXHNE ‘ILLA ‘EN JE’TINE BIFAHISHETIN MUBEJJINETIN WE TILKE HUDUDU ELLAHI WE MEN JETE’ADDE H
FE’IDHA BELEGNE ‘EXHELEHUNNE FE’EMSIKUHUNNE BIMA’RUFIN ‘EW FARIKUHUNNE BIMA’RUFIN WE ‘ESH/HIDU DHEWEJ ‘ADLIN MINKUM WE ‘EKIMU ESH-SHEHADETE LILLAHI DHALIKUM JU’ADHU BIHI MEN KANE JU’UMINU BILLAHI WEL-JEWMIL-’AHIRI WE MEN JETTEKI ELLAHE JEXH’AL LEHU MEHREX
WE JERZUKHU MIN HEJTHU LA JEHTESIBU WE MEN JETEWEKKEL ‘ALA ELLAHI FEHUWE HESBUHU ‘INNALL-LLAHE BALIGU ‘EMRIHI KAD XHE’ALEL-LAHU LIKULLI SHEJ’IN KADRÆN
WEL-LA’I JE’ISNE MINEL-MEHIDI MIN NISA’IKUM ‘INI ERTEBTUM FA’IDDETUHUNNE THELATHETU ‘ESH/HURIN WEL-LA’I LEM JEHIDNE WE ‘ULATUL-’EHMALI ‘EXHELUHUNNE ‘EN JEDA’NE HEMLEHUNNE WE MEN JETTEKI ELLAHE JEXH’AL LEHU MIN ‘EMRIHI JUSRÆN
DHALIKE ‘EMRU ELLAHI ‘ENZELEHU ‘ILEJKUM WE MEN JETTEKI ELLAHE JUKEFFIR ‘ANHU SEJJI’ATIHI WE JU’DHIM LEHU ‘EXHRÆN
‘ESKINUHUNNE MIN HEJTHU SEKENTUM MIN WUXHDIKUM WE LA TUDARRUHUNNE LITUDEJJIKU ‘ALEJHINNE WE ‘IN KUNNE ‘ULATI HEMLIN FE’ENFIKU ‘ALEJHINNE HETTA JEDA’NE HEMLEHUNNE FE’IN ‘ERDA’NE LEKUM FE’ATUHUNNE ‘UXHUREHUNNE WE ‘TEMIRU BEJNEKUM BIMA’RUFIN WE ‘IN TA’ASERTU
LIJUNFIK DHU SE’ATIN MIN SE’ATIHI WE MEN KUDIRE ‘ALEJHI RIZKUHU FELJUNFIK MIMMA ‘ATAHU ELLAHU LA JUKELLIFU ELLAHU NEFSÆN ‘ILLA MA ‘ATAHA SEJEXH’ALU ELLAHU BA’DE ‘USRIN JUSRÆN
WE KE’EJJIN MIN KARJETIN ‘ATET ‘AN ‘EMRI RABBIHA WE RUSULIHI FEHASEBNAHA HISABÆN SHEDIDÆN WE ‘ADHDHEBNAHA ‘ADHABÆN NUKRÆN
FEDHAKAT WEBALE ‘EMRIHA WE KANE ‘AKIBETU ‘EMRIHA HUSRÆN
‘E’ADDEL-LAHU LEHUM ‘ADHABÆN SHEDIDÆN FE ETTEKU ELLAHE JA ‘ULIL-’ELBABIL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU KAD ‘ENZELEL-LAHU ‘ILEJKUM DHIKRÆN
RESULÆN JETLU ‘ALEJKUM ‘AJATI ELLAHI MUBEJJINATIN LIJUHRIXHEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI MINE EDH-DHULUMATI ‘ILA EN-NURI WE MEN JU’UMIN BILLAHI WE JA’MEL SALIHÆN JUDHILHU XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA ‘EBEDÆN KAD ‘EHSENEL-L
ELLAHUL-LEDHI HALEKA SEB’A SEMAWATIN WE MINEL-’ERDI MITHLEHUNNE JETENEZZELUL-’EMRU BEJNEHUNNE LITA’LEMU ‘ENNEL-LAHE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN WE ‘ENNEL-LAHE KAD ‘EHATE BIKULLI SHEJ’IN ‘ILMÆN
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU LIME TUHERRIMU MA ‘EHELLEL-LAHU LEKE TEBTEGI MERDÆTE ‘EZWAXHIKE WEL-LAHU GAFURUN REHIMUN
KAD FEREDEL-LAHU LEKUM TEHILLETE ‘EJMANIKUM WEL-LAHU MEWLAKUM WE HUWEL-’ALIMUL-HEKIMU
WE ‘IDH ‘ESERRE EN-NEBIJU ‘ILA BA’DI ‘EZWAXHIHI HEDITHÆN FELEMMA NEBBE’ET BIHI WE ‘EDHHEREHU ELLAHU ‘ALEJHI ‘ARREFE BA’DEHU WE ‘A’REDE ‘AN BA’DIN FELEMMA NEBBE’EHA BIHI KALET MEN ‘ENBE’EKE HADHA KALE NEBBE’ENIJEL-’ALIMUL-HABIRU
‘IN TETUBA ‘ILA ELLAHI FEKAD SEGAT KULUBUKUMA WE ‘IN TEDHAHERA ‘ALEJHI FE’INNALL-LLAHE HUWE MEWLAHU WE XHIBRILU WE SALIHUL-MU’UMININE WEL-MELA’IKETU BA’DE DHALIKE DHEHIRUN
‘ASA REBBUHU ‘IN TELLEKAKUNNE ‘EN JUBDILEHU ‘EZWAXHÆN HAJRÆN MINKUNNE MUSLIMATIN MU’UMINATIN KANITATIN TA’IBATIN ‘ABIDATIN SA’IHATIN THEJJIBATIN WE ‘EBKARÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU KU ‘ENFUSEKUM WE ‘EHLIKUM NARÆN WEKUDUHA EN-NASU WEL-HIXHARETU ‘ALEJHA MELA’IKETUN GILADHUN SHIDADUN LA JA’SUNEL-LAHE MA ‘EMEREHUM WE JEF’ALUNE MA JU’UMERUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE KEFERU LA TA’TEDHIRUL-JEWME ‘INNEMA TUXHZEWNE MA KUNTUM TA’MELUNE
JA ‘EJJUHAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU TUBU ‘ILA ELLAHI TEWBETEN NESUHÆN ‘ASA REBBUKUM ‘EN JUKEFFIRE ‘ANKUM SEJJI’ATIKUM WE JUDHILEKUM XHENNATIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU JEWME LA JUHZI ELLAHU EN-NEBIJE WEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ME’AHU NURUHUM JES’A BEJNE ‘EJDIHIM WE BI’E
JA ‘EJJUHA EN-NEBIJU XHAHIDIL-KUFFARE WEL-MUNAFIKINE WE EGLUDH ‘ALEJHIM WE ME’WAHUM XHEHENNEMU WE BI’SEL-MESIRU
DEREBEL-LAHU METHELÆN LILLEDHINE KEFERU EIMRE’ETE NUHIN WE EIMRE’ETE LUTIN KANETA TEHTE ‘ABDEJNI MIN ‘IBADINA SALIHEJNI FEHANETAHUMA FELEM JUGNIJA ‘ANHUMA MINEL-LAHI SHEJ’ÆN WE KILE EDHULA EN-NARE ME’A ED-DAHILINE
WE DEREBEL-LAHU METHELÆN LILLEDHINE ‘AMENU EIMRE’ETE FIR’AWNE ‘IDH KALET RABBI EBNI LI ‘INDEKE BEJTÆN FIL-XHENNETI WE NEXHXHINI MIN FIR’AWNE WE ‘AMELIHI WE NEXHXHINI MINEL-KAWMI EDH-DHALIMINE
WE MERJEME EBNETE ‘IMRANEL-LETI ‘EHSENET FERXHEHA FENEFEHNA FIHI MIN RUHINA WE SEDDEKAT BIKELIMATI RABBIHA WE KUTUBIHI WE KANET MINEL-KANITINE
TEBAREKEL-LEDHI BIJEDIHIL-MULKU WE HUWE ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN KADIRUN
EL-LEDHI HALEKAL-MEWTE WEL-HEJÆTE LIJEBLUWEKUM ‘EJJUKUM ‘EHSENU ‘AMELÆN WE HUWEL-’AZIZUL-GAFURU
EL-LEDHI HALEKA SEB’A SEMAWATIN TIBAKÆN MA TERA FI HALKI ER-REHMANI MIN TEFAWUTIN FARXHI’IL-BESERE HEL TERA MIN FUTURIN
THUMME ERXHI’IL-BESERE KERRETEJNI JENKALIB ‘ILEJKEL-BESERU HASI’ÆN WE HUWE HESIRUN
WE LEKAD ZEJJENNA ES-SEMA’E ED-DUNJA BIMESABIHE WE XHE’ALNAHA RUXHUMÆN LILSHSHEJATINI WE ‘A’TEDNA LEHUM ‘ADHABE ES-SA’IRI
WE LILLEDHINE KEFERU BIREBBIHIM ‘ADHABU XHEHENNEME WE BI’SEL-MESIRU
‘IDHA ‘ULKU FIHA SEMI’U LEHA SHEHIKÆN WE HIJE TEFURU
TEKADU TEMEJJEZU MINEL-GAJDHI KULLEMA ‘ULKIJE FIHA FEWXHUN SE’ELEHUM HAZENETUHA ‘ELEM JE’TIKUM NEDHIRUN
KALU BELA KAD XHA’ENA NEDHIRUN FEKEDHDHEBNA WE KULNA MA NEZZELEL-LAHU MIN SHEJ’IN ‘IN ‘ENTUM ‘ILLA FI DELALIN KEBIRIN
WE KALU LEW KUNNA NESMA’U ‘EW NA’KILU MA KUNNA FI ‘ESHABI ES-SA’IRI
FA’TEREFU BIDHENBIHIM FESUHKÆN LI’SHABI ES-SA’IRI
‘INNEL-LEDHINE JEHSHEWNE REBBEHUM BIL-GAJBI LEHUM MEGFIRETUN WE ‘EXHRUN KEBIRUN
WE ‘ESIRRU KAWLEKUM ‘EW EXHHERU BIHI ‘INNEHU ‘ALIMUN BIDHATI ES-SUDURI
‘ELA JA’LEMU MEN HALEKA WE HUWEL-LETIFUL-HABIRU
HUWEL-LEDHI XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-’ERDE DHELULÆN FAMSHU FI MENAKIBIHA WE KULU MIN RIZKIHI WE ‘ILEJHI EN-NUSHURU
‘E’EMINTUM MEN FI ES-SEMA’I ‘EN JEHSIFE BIKUMUL-’ERDE FE’IDHA HIJE TEMURU
‘EM ‘EMINTUM MEN FI ES-SEMA’I ‘EN JURSILE ‘ALEJKUM HASIBÆN FESETA’LEMUNE KEJFE NEDHIRI
WE LEKAD KEDHDHEBEL-LEDHINE MIN KABLIHIM FEKEJFE KANE NEKIRI
‘EWELEM JEREW ‘ILAT-TEJRI FEWKAHUM SAFFATIN WE JEKBIDNE MA JUMSIKUHUNNE ‘ILLA ER-REHMANU ‘INNEHU BIKULLI SHEJ’IN BESIRUN
‘EMMEN HADHAL-LEDHI HUWE XHUNDUN LEKUM JENSURUKUM MIN DUNI ER-REHMANI ‘INIL-KAFIRUNE ‘ILLA FI GURURIN
‘EMMEN HADHAL-LEDHI JERZUKUKUM ‘IN ‘EMSEKE RIZKAHU BEL LEXHXHU FI ‘UTUWIN WE NUFURIN
‘EFEMEN JEMSHI MUKIBBÆN ‘ALA WEXHHIHI ‘EHDA ‘EMMEN JEMSHI SEWIJÆN ‘ALA SIRATIN MUSTEKIMIN
KUL HUWEL-LEDHI ‘ENSHE’EKUM WE XHE’ALE LEKUMU ES-SEM’A WEL-’EBSARE WEL-’EF’IDETE KALILÆN MA TESHKURUNE
KUL HUWEL-LEDHI DHERE’EKUM FIL-’ERDI WE ‘ILEJHI TUHSHERUNE
WE JEKULUNE META HADHAL-WA’DU ‘IN KUNTUM SADIKINE
KUL ‘INNEMAL-’ILMU ‘INDEL-LAHI WE ‘INNEMA ‘ENA NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
FELEMMA RE’EWHU ZULFETEN SI’ET WUXHUHUL-LEDHINE KEFERU WE KILE HADHAL-LEDHI KUNTUM BIHI TEDDA’UNE
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN ‘EHLEKENIJEL-LAHU WE MEN MA’I ‘EW REHIMENA FEMEN JUXHIRUL-KAFIRINE MIN ‘ADHABIN ‘ELIMIN
KUL HUWE ER-REHMANU ‘AMENNA BIHI WE ‘ALEJHI TEWEKKELNA FESETA’LEMUNE MEN HUWE FI DELALIN MUBININ
KUL ‘ERE’EJTUM ‘IN ‘ESBEHE MA’UUKUM GAWRÆN FEMEN JE’TIKUM BIMA’IN MA’ININ
NUN WEL-KALEMI WE MA JESTURUNE
MA ‘ENTE BINI’METI RABBIKE BIMEXHNUNIN
WE ‘INNE LEKE LE’EXHRÆN GAJRE MEMNUNIN
WE ‘INNEKE LE’ALA HULUKIN ‘ADHIMIN
FESETUBSIRU WE JUBSIRUNE
BI’EJJJIKUMUL-MEFTUNU
‘INNE REBBEKE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIMEN DELLE ‘AN SEBILIHI WE HUWE ‘A’LEMU BIL-MUHTEDINE
FELA TUTI’IL-MUKEDHDHIBINE
WE DDU LEW TUD/HINU FEJUD/HINUNE
WE LA TUTI’ KULLE HELLAFIN MEHININ
HEMMAZIN MESHSHA’IN BINEMIMIN
MENNA’IN LILHAJRI MU’TEDIN ‘ETHIMIN
‘UTULLIN BA’DE DHALIKE ZENIMIN
‘EN KANE DHA MALIN WE BENINE
‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHI ‘AJATUNA KALE ‘ESATIRUL-’EWWELINE
SENESIMUHU ‘ALEL-HURTUMI
‘INNA BELEWNAHUM KEMA BELEWNA ‘ESHABEL-XHENNETI ‘IDH ‘EKSEMU LEJESRIMUNNEHA MUSBIHINE
WE LA JESTETHNUNE
FETAFE ‘ALEJHA TA’IFUN MIN RABBIKE WE HUM NA’IMUNE
FE’ESBEHET KALSSERIMI
FETENADEW MUSBIHINE
‘ENI EGDU ‘ALA HERTHIKUM ‘IN KUNTUM SARIMINE
FANTELEKU WE HUM JETEHAFETUNE
‘EN LA JEDHULENNEHAL-JEWME ‘ALEJKUM MISKINUN
WEGADEW ‘ALA HERDIN KADIRINE
FELEMMA RE’EWHA KALU ‘INNA LEDALLUNE
BEL NEHNU MEHRUMUNE
KALE ‘EWSETUHUM ‘ELEM ‘EKUL LEKUM LEWLA TUSEBBIHUNE
KALU SUBHANE RABBINA ‘INNA KUNNA DHALIMINE
FE’EKBELE BA’DUHUM ‘ALA BA’DIN JETELAWEMUNE
KALU JA WEJLENA ‘INNA KUNNA TAGINE
‘ASA REBBUNA ‘EN JUBDILENA HAJRÆN MINHA ‘INNA ‘ILA RABBINA RAGIBUNE
KEDHALIKEL-’ADHABU WE LE’ADHABUL-’AHIRETI ‘EKBERU LEW KANU JA’LEMUNE
‘INNE LILMUTTEKINE ‘INDE RABBIHIM XHENNATI EN-NA’IMI
‘EFENEXH’ALUL-MUSLIMINE KALMUXHRIMINE
MA LEKUM KEJFE TEHKUMUNE
‘EM LEKUM KITABUN FIHI TEDRUSUNE
‘INNE LEKUM FIHI LEMA TEHAJJERUNE
‘EM LEKUM ‘EJMANUN ‘ALEJNA BALIGATUN ‘ILA JEWMIL-KIJAMETI ‘INNE LEKUM LEMA TEHKUMUNE
SELHUM ‘EJJUHUM BIDHALIKE ZA’IMUN
‘EM LEHUM SHUREKA’U FELJE’TU BISHUREKA’IHIM ‘IN KANU SADIKINE
JEWME JUKSHEFU ‘AN SAKIN WE JUD’AWNE ‘ILA ES-SUXHUDI FELA JESTETI’UNE
HASHI’ATEN ‘EBSARUHUM TERHEKUHUM DHILLETUN WE KAD KANU JUD’AWNE ‘ILA ES-SUXHUDI WE HUM SALIMUNE
FEDHERNI WE MEN JUKEDHDHIBU BIHEDHAL-HEDITHI SENESTEDRIXHUHUM MIN HEJTHU LA JA’LEMUNE
WE ‘UMLI LEHUM ‘INNE KEJDI METINUN
‘EM TES’ELUHUM ‘EXHRÆN FEHUM MIN MEGREMIN MUTHKALUNE
‘EM ‘INDEHUMUL-GAJBU FEHUM JEKTUBUNE
FASBIR LIHUKMI RABBIKE WE LA TEKUN KESAHIBIL-HUTI ‘IDH NADA WE HUWE MEKDHUMUN
LEWLA ‘EN TEDAREKEHU NI’METUN MIN RABBIHI LENUBIDHE BIL-’ARA’I WE HUWE MEDHMUMUN
FAXHTEBAHU REBBUHU FEXHE’ALEHU MINE ES-SALIHINE
WE ‘IN JEKADUL-LEDHINE KEFERU LEJUZLIKUNEKE BI’EBSARIHIM LEMMA SEMI’U EDH-DHIKRE WE JEKULUNE ‘INNEHU LEMEXHNUNUN
WE MA HUWE ‘ILLA DHIKRUN LIL’ALEMINE
EL-HAKKATU
MAL-HAKKATU
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MAL-HAKKATU
KEDHDHEBET THEMUDU WE ‘ADUN BIL-KARI’ATI
FE’EMMA THEMUDU FE’UHLIKU BIT-TAGIJETI
WE ‘EMMA ‘ADUN FE’UHLIKU BIRIHIN SERSERIN ‘ATIJETIN
SEHHAREHA ‘ALEJHIM SEB’A LEJALIN WE THEMANIJETE ‘EJJAMIN HUSUMÆN FETERAL-KAWME FIHA SER’A KE’ENNEHUM ‘A’XHAZU NEHLIN HAWIJETIN
FEHEL TERA LEHUM MIN BAKIJETIN
WE XHA’E FIR’AWNU WE MEN KABLEHU WEL-MU’UTEFIKATU BIL-HATI’ETI
FE’ASEW RESULE RABBIHIM FE’EHADHEHUM ‘EHDHETEN RABIJETEN
‘INNA LEMMA TEGAL-MA’U HEMELNAKUM FIL-XHARIJETI
LINEXH’ALEHA LEKUM TEDHKIRETEN WE TA’IJEHA ‘UDHUNUN WA’IJETUN
FE’IDHA NUFIHA FI ES-SURI NEFHATUN WAHIDETUN
WE HUMILETIL-’ERDU WEL-XHIBALU FEDUKKETA DEKKETEN WAHIDETEN
FEJEWME’IDHIN WEKA’ATIL-WAKI’ATU
WE ENSHEKKATI ES-SEMA’U FEHIJE JEWME’IDHIN WE EHIJETUN
WEL-MELEKU ‘ALA ‘ERXHA’IHA WE JEHMILU ‘ARSHE RABBIKE FEWKAHUM JEWME’IDHIN THEMANIJETUN
JEWME’IDHIN TU’REDUNE LA TEHFA MINKUM HAFIJETUN
FE’EMMA MEN ‘UTIJE KITABEHU BIJEMINIHI FEJEKULU HA’UUM EKRE’U KITABI
‘INNI DHENENTU ‘ENNI MULAKIN HISABIJEH
FEHUWE FI ‘ISHETIN RADIJETIN
FI XHENNETIN ‘ALIJETIN
KUTUFUHA DANIJETUN
KULU WE ESHREBU HENI’ÆN BIMA ‘ESLEFTUM FIL-’EJJAMIL-HALIJETI
WE ‘EMMA MEN ‘UTIJE KITABEHU BISHIMALIHI FEJEKULU JA LEJTENI LEM ‘UTE KITABIH
WE LEM ‘EDRI MA HISABIH
JA LEJTEHA KANETIL-KADIJETE
MA ‘EGNA ‘ANNI MALIH
HELEKE ‘ANNI SULTANIH
HUDHUHU FEGULLUHU
THUMMEL-XHEHIME SELLUHU
THUMME FI SILSILETIN DHER’UHA SEB’UNE DHIRA’ÆN FASLUKUHU
‘INNEHU KANE LA JU’UMINU BILLAHIL-’ADHIMI
WE LA JEHUDDU ‘ALA TA’AMIL-MISKINI
FELEJSE LEHUL-JEWME HAHUNA HEMIMUN
WE LA TA’AMUN ‘ILLA MIN GISLININ
LA JE’KULUHU ‘ILLAL-HATI’UNE
FELA ‘UKSIMU BIMA TUBSIRUNE
WE MA LA TUBSIRUNE
‘INNEHU LEKAWLU RESULIN KERIMIN
WE MA HUWE BIKAWLI SHA’IRIN KALILÆN MA TU’UMINUNE
WE LA BIKAWLI KAHININ KALILÆN MA TEDHEKKERUNE
TENZILUN MIN RABBIL-’ALEMINE
WE LEW TEKAWWELE ‘ALEJNA BA’DEL-’EKAWILI
LE’EHADHNA MINHU BIL-JEMINI
THUMME LEKATA’NA MINHUL-WETINE
FEMA MINKUM MIN ‘EHEDIN ‘ANHU HAXHIZINE
WE ‘INNEHU LETEDHKIRETUN LILMUTTEKINE
WE ‘INNA LENA’LEMU ‘ENNE MINKUM MUKEDHDHIBINE
WE ‘INNEHU LEHESRETUN ‘ALEL-KAFIRINE
WE ‘INNEHU LEHEKKUL-JEKINI
FESEBBIH BIASMI RABBIKEL-’ADHIMI
SE’ELE SA’ILUN BI’ADHABIN WAKI’IN
LILKAFIRJNE LEJSE LEHU DAFI’UN
MINEL-LAHI DHIL-MA’ARIXHI
TA’RUXHUL-MELA’IKETU WE ER-RUHU ‘ILEJHI FI JEWMIN KANE MIKDARUHU HAMSINE ‘ELFE SENETIN
FASBIR SEBRÆN XHEMILÆN
‘INNEHUM JEREWNEHU BA’IDÆN
WE NERAHU KARIBÆN
JEWME TEKUNU ES-SEMA’U KALMUHLI
WE TEKUNUL-XHIBALU KAL’IHNI
WE LA JES’ELU HEMIMUN HEMIMÆN
JUBESSERUNEHUM JEWEDDUL-MUXHRIMU LEW JEFTEDI MIN ‘ADHABI JEWMI’IDHIN BIBENIHI
WE SAHIBETIHI WE ‘EHIHI
WE FESILETIHI ELLETI TU’UWJHI
WE MEN FIL-’ERDI XHEMI’ÆN THUMME JUNXHIHI
KELLA ‘INNEHA LEDHA
NEZZA’ATEN LILSHSHEWA
TED’U MEN ‘EDBERE WE TEWELLA
WE XHEME’A FE’EW’A
‘INNEL-’INSANE HULIKA HELU’ÆN
‘IDHA MESSEHU ESH-SHERRU XHEZU’ÆN
WE ‘IDHA MESSEHUL-HAJRU MENU’ÆN
‘ILLAL-MUSELLINE
EL-LEDHINE HUM ‘ALA SELATIHIM DA’IMUNE
WEL-LEDHINE FI ‘EMWALIHIM HEKKUN MA’LUMUN
LILSSA’ILI WEL-MEHRUMI
WEL-LEDHINE JUSEDDIKUNE BIJEWMI ED-DINI
WEL-LEDHINE HUM MIN ‘ADHABI RABBIHIM MUSHFIKUNE
‘INNE ‘ADHABE RABBIHIM GAJRU ME’MUNIN
WEL-LEDHINE HUM LIFURUXHIHIM HAFIDHUNE
‘ILLA ‘ALA ‘EZWAXHIHIM ‘EW MA MELEKET ‘EJMANUHUM FE’INNEHUM GAJRU MELUMINE
FEMENI EBTEGA WERA’E DHALIKE FE’ULA’IKE HUMUL-’ADUNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM LI’MANATIHIM WE ‘AHDIHIM RA’UNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM BISHEHADATIHIM KA’IMUNE
WEL-LEDHINE HUM ‘ALA SELATIHIM JUHAFIDHUNE
‘ULA’IKE FI XHENNATIN MUKREMUNE
FEMALIL-LEDHINE KEFERU KIBELEKE MUHTI’INE
‘ANIL-JEMINI WE ‘ANI ESH-SHIMALI ‘IZINE
‘EJETMA’U KULLU EMRI’IN MINHUM ‘EN JUDHALE XHENNETE NA’IMIN
KELLA ‘INNA HALEKNAHUM MIMMA JA’LEMUNE
FELA ‘UKSIMU BIREBBIL-MESHARIKI WEL-MEGARIBI ‘INNA LEKADIRUNE
‘ALA ‘EN NUBEDDILE HAJRÆN MINHUM WE MA NEHNU BIMESBUKINE
FEDHERHUM JEHUDU WE JEL’ABU HETTA JULAKU JEWMEHUMUL-LEDHI JU’ADUNE
JEWME JEHRUXHUNE MINEL-’EXHDATHI SIRA’ÆN KE’ENNEHUM ‘ILA NUSUBIN JUFIDUNE
HASHI’ATEN ‘EBSARUHUM TERHEKUHUM DHILLETUN DHALIKEL-JEWMUL-LEDHI KANU JU’ADUNE
‘INNA ‘ERSELNA NUHÆN ‘ILA KAWMIHI ‘EN ‘ENDHIR KAWMEKE MIN KABLI ‘EN JE’TIJEHUM ‘ADHABUN ‘ELIMUN
KALE JA KAWMI ‘INNI LEKUM NEDHIRUN MUBINUN
‘ENI A’BUDU ELLAHE WE ETTEKUHU WE ‘ETI’UNI
JEGFIR LEKUM MIN DHUNUBIKUM WE JU’UEHHIRKUM ‘ILA ‘EXHELIN MUSEMMEN ‘INNE ‘EXHELEL-LAHI ‘IDHA XHA’E LA JU’UEHHARU LEW KUNTUM TA’LEMUNE
KALE RABBI ‘INNI DE’AWTU KAWMI LEJLÆN WE NEHARÆN
FELEM JEZID/HUM DU’A’I ‘ILLA FIRARÆN
WE ‘INNI KULLEMA DE’AWTUHUM LITEGFIRE LEHUM XHE’ALU ‘ESABI’AHUM FI ‘ADHANIHIM WE ESTEGSHEW THIJABEHUM WE ‘ESERRU WE ESTEKBERU ESTIKBARÆN
THUMME ‘INNI DE’AWTUHUM XHIHARÆN
THUMME ‘INNI ‘A’LENTU LEHUM WE ‘ESRERTU LEHUM ‘ISRARÆN
FEKULTU ESTEGFIRU REBBEKUM ‘INNEHU KANE GAFFARÆN
JURSILI ES-SEMA’E ‘ALEJKUM MIDRARÆN
WE JUMDIDKUM BI’EMWALIN WE BENINE WE JEXH’AL LEKUM XHENNATIN WE JEXH’AL LEKUM ‘ENHARÆN
MA LEKUM LA TERXHUNE LILLAHI WEKARÆN
WE KAD HALEKAKUM ‘ETWARÆN
‘ELEM TEREW KEJFE HALEKAL-LAHU SEB’A SEMAWATIN TIBAKÆN
WE XHE’ALEL-KAMERE FIHINNE NURÆN WE XHE’ALE ESH-SHEMSE SIRAXHÆN
WEL-LAHU ‘ENBETEKUM MINEL-’ERDI NEBATÆN
THUMME JU’IDUKUM FIHA WE JUHRIXHUKUM ‘IHRAXHÆN
WEL-LAHU XHE’ALE LEKUMUL-’ERDE BISATÆN
LITESLUKU MINHA SUBULÆN FIXHAXHÆN
KALE NUHUN RABBI ‘INNEHUM ‘ASEWNI WE ETTEBA’U MEN LEM JEZID/HU MALUHU WE WELEDUHU ‘ILLA HASARÆN
WE MEKERU MEKRÆN KUBBARÆN
WE KALU LA TEDHERUNNE ‘ALIHETEKUM WE LA TEDHERUNNE WEDDÆN WE LA SUWA’ÆN WE LA JEGUTHE WE JA’UKA WE NESRÆN
WE KAD ‘EDELLU KETHIRÆN WE LA TEZIDI EDH-DHALIMINE ‘ILLA DELALÆN
MIMMA HATI’ATIHIM ‘UGRIKU FE’UDHILU NARÆN FELEM JEXHIDU LEHUM MIN DUNI ELLAHI ‘ENSARÆN
WE KALE NUHUN RABBI LA TEDHER ‘ALEL-’ERDI MINEL-KAFIRINE DEJJARÆN
‘INNEKE ‘IN TEDHERHUM JUDILLU ‘IBADEKE WE LA JELIDU ‘ILLA FAXHIRÆN KEFFARÆN
REBBI EGFIR LI WE LIWALIDEJJE WE LIMEN DEHALE BEJTIJE MU’UMINÆN WE LILMU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI WE LA TEZIDI EDH-DHALIMINE ‘ILLA TEBARÆN
KUL ‘UHIJE ‘ILEJJE ‘ENNEHU ESTEME’A NEFERUN MINEL-XHINNI FEKALU ‘INNA SEMI’NA KUR’ANÆN ‘AXHEBÆN
JEHDI ‘ILA ER-RUSHDI FE’AMENNA BIHI WE LEN NUSHRIKE BIREBBINA ‘EHEDÆN
WE ‘ENNEHU TA’ALA XHEDDU RABBINA MA ETTEHADHE SAHIBETEN WE LA WELEDÆN
WE ‘ENNEHU KANE JEKULU SEFIHUNA ‘ALA ELLAHI SHETETÆN
WE ‘ENNA DHENENNA ‘EN LEN TEKULEL-’INSU WEL-XHINNU ‘ALA ELLAHI KEDHIBÆN
WE ‘ENNEHU KANE RIXHALUN MINEL-’INSI JA’UDHUNE BIRIXHALIN MINEL-XHINNI FEZADUHUM REHEKÆN
WE ‘ENNEHUM DHENNU KEMA DHENENTUM ‘EN LEN JEB’ATHEL-LAHU ‘EHEDÆN
WE ‘ENNA LEMESNA ES-SEMA’E FEWEXHEDNAHA MULI’ET HERESÆN SHEDIDÆN WE SHUHUBÆN
WE ‘ENNA KUNNA NEK’UDU MINHA MEKA’IDE LILSSEM’I FEMEN JESTEMI’IL-’ANE JEXHID LEHU SHIHABÆN RESEDÆN
WE ‘ENNA LA NEDRI ‘ESHERRUN ‘URIDE BIMEN FIL-’ERDI ‘EM ‘ERADE BIHIM REBBUHUM RESHEDÆN
WE ‘ENNA MINNA ES-SALIHUNE WE MINNA DUNE DHALIKE KUNNA TERA’IKA KIDEDÆN
WE ‘ENNA DHENENNA ‘EN LEN NU’XHIZEL-LAHE FIL-’ERDI WE LEN NU’XHIZEHU HEREBÆN
WE ‘ENNA LEMMA SEMI’NAL-HUDA ‘AMENNA BIHI FEMEN JU’UMIN BIREBBIHI FELA JEHAFU BEHSÆN WE LA REHEKÆN
WE ‘ENNA MINNAL-MUSLIMUNE WE MINNAL-KASITUNE FEMEN ‘ESLEME FE’ULA’IKE TEHERREW RESHEDÆN
WE ‘EMMAL-KASITUNE FEKANU LIXHEHENNEME HETEBÆN
WE ‘ELLEWI ESTEKAMU ‘ALAT-TERIKATI L’ESKAJNAHUM MA’EN GADEKÆN
LINEFTINEHUM FIHI WE MEN JU’RID ‘AN DHIKRI RABBIHI JESLUK/HU ‘ADHABÆN SE’ADÆN
WE ‘ENNEL-MESAXHIDE LILLAHI FELA TED’U ME’A ELLAHI ‘EHEDÆN
WE ‘ENNEHU LEMMA KAME ‘ABDU ELLAHI JED’UHU KADU JEKUNUNE ‘ALEJHI LIBEDÆN
KUL ‘INNEMA ‘ED’U RABBI WE LA ‘USHRIKU BIHI ‘EHEDÆN
KUL ‘INNI LA ‘EMLIKU LEKUM DERRÆN WE LA RESHEDÆN
KUL ‘INNI LEN JUXHIRENI MINEL-LAHI ‘EHEDUN WE LEN ‘EXHIDE MIN DUNIHI MULTEHEDÆN
‘ILLA BELAGÆN MINEL-LAHI WE RISALATIHI WE MEN JA’SI ELLAHE WE RESULEHU FE’INNE LEHU NARE XHEHENNEME HALIDINE FIHA ‘EBEDÆN
HETTA ‘IDHA RE’EW MA JU’ADUNE FESEJA’LEMUNE MEN ‘ED’AFU NASIRÆN WE ‘EKALLU ‘ADEDÆN
KUL ‘IN ‘EDRI ‘EKARIBUN MA TU’ADUNE ‘EM JEXH’ALU LEHU RABBI ‘EMEDÆN
‘ALIMUL-GAJBI FELA JUDHHIRU ‘ALA GAJBIHI ‘EHEDÆN
‘ILLA MENI ERTEDA MIN RESULIN FE’INNEHU JESLUKU MIN BEJNI JEDEJHI WE MIN HALFIHI RESEDÆN
LIJA’LEME ‘EN KAD ‘EBLEGU RISALATI RABBIHIM WE ‘EHATE BIMA LEDEJHIM WE ‘EHSA KULLE SHEJ’IN ‘ADEDÆN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-MUZZEMMILU
KUMIL-LEJLE ‘ILLA KALILÆN
NISFEHU ‘EW ENKUS MINHU KALILÆN
‘EW ZID ‘ALEJHI WE RETTILIL-KUR’ANE TERTILÆN
‘INNA SENULKI ‘ALEJKE KAWLÆN THEKILÆN
‘INNE NASHI’ETEL-LEJLI HIJE ‘ESHEDDU WET’ÆN WE ‘EKWEMU KILÆN
‘INNE LEKE FI EELNNEHARI SEBHÆN TEWILÆN
WE EDHKUR ESME RABBIKE WE TEBETTEL ‘ILEJHI TEBTILÆN
REBBUL-MESHRIKI WEL-MEGRIBI LA ‘ILAHE ‘ILLA HUWE FE ETTEHIDH/HU WE KILÆN
WE ESBIR ‘ALA MA JEKULUNE WE EHXHURHUM HEXHRÆN XHEMILÆN
WE DHERNI WEL-MUKEDHDHIBINE ‘ULI EN-NA’METI WE MEHHILHUM KALILÆN
‘INNE LEDEJNA ‘ENKALÆN WE XHEHIMÆN
WE TA’AMÆN DHA GUSSETIN WE ‘ADHABÆN ‘ELIMÆN
JEWME TERXHUFUL-’ERDU WEL-XHIBALU WE KANETIL-XHIBALU KETHIBÆN MEHILÆN
‘INNA ‘ERSELNA ‘ILEJKUM RESULÆN SHAHIDÆN ‘ALEJKUM KEMA ‘ERSELNA ‘ILA FIR’AWNE RESULÆN
FE’ASA FIR’AWNU ER-RESULE FE’EHADHNAHU ‘EHDHÆN WEBILÆN
FEKEJFE TETTEKUNE ‘IN KEFERTUM JEWMÆN JEXH’ALUL-WILDANE SHIBÆN
ES-SEMA’U MUNFETIRUN BIHI KANE WA’DUHU MEF’ULÆN
‘INNE HEDHIHI TEDHKIRETUN FEMEN SHA’E ETTEHADHE ‘ILA RABBIHI SEBILÆN
‘INNE REBBEKE JA’LEMU ‘ENNEKE TEKUMU ‘EDNA MIN THULUTHEJIL-LEJLI WE NISFEHU WE THULUTHEHU WE TA’IFETUN MINEL-LEDHINE ME’AKE WEL-LAHU JUKADDIRUL-LEJLE WE EN-NEHARE ‘ALIME ‘EN LEN TUHSUHU FETABE ‘ALEJKUM FAKRE’U MA TEJESSERE MINEL-KUR’ANI ‘ALIME ‘EN SEJEKUN
JA ‘EJJUHAL-MUDDETHTHIRU
KUM FE’ENDHIR
WE REBBEKE FEKEBBIR
WE THIJABEKE FETEHHIR
WE ER-RUXHZE FAHXHUR
WE LA TEMNUN TESTEKTHIRU
WE LIREBBIKE FASBIR
FE’IDHA NUKIRE FI EN-NAKURI
FEDHALIKE JEWME’IDHIN JEWMUN ‘ASIRUN
‘ALEL-KAFIRINE GAJRU JESIRIN
DHERNI WE MEN HALEKTU WEHIDÆN
WE XHE’ALTU LEHU MALÆN MEMDUDÆN
WE BENINE SHUHUDÆN
WE MEHHEDTU LEHU TEMHIDÆN
THUMME JETMA’U ‘EN ‘EZIDE
KELLA ‘INNEHU KANE LI’JATINA ‘ANIDÆN
SE’URHIKUHU SA’UDÆN
‘INNEHU FEKKERE WE KADDERE
FEKUTILE KEJFE KADDERE
THUMME KUTILE KEJFE KADDERE
THUMME NEDHERE
THUMME ‘ABESE WE BESERE
THUMME ‘EDBERE WE ESTEKBERE
FEKALE ‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA SIHRUN JU’UTHERU
‘IN HADHA ‘ILLA KAWLUL-BESHERI
SE’USLIHI SEKARE
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MA SEKARU
LA TUBKI WE LA TEDHERU
LEWWAHETUN LILBESHERI
‘ALEJHA TIS’ATE ‘ASHERE
WE MA XHE’ALNA ‘ESHABE EN-NARI ‘ILLA MELA’IKETEN WE MA XHE’ALNA ‘IDDETEHUM ‘ILLA FITNETEN LILLEDHINE KEFERU LIJESTEJKINEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-KITABE WE JEZDADEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU ‘IMANÆN WE LA JERTABEL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-KITABE WEL-MU’UMINUNE WE LIJEKULEL-LEDHINE FI KU
KELLA WEL-KAMERI
WEL-LEJLI ‘IDH ‘EDBERE
WE ES-SUBHI ‘IDHA ‘ESFERE
‘INNEHA LE’IHDAL-KUBERI
NEDHIRÆN LILBESHERI
LIMEN SHA’E MINKUM ‘EN JETEKADDEME ‘EW JETE’EHHARE
KULLU NEFSIN BIMA KESEBET REHINETUN
‘ILLA ‘ESHABEL-JEMINI
FI XHENNATIN JETESA’ELUNE
‘ANIL-MUXHRIMINE
MA SELEKEKUM FI SEKARE
KALU LEM NEKU MINEL-MUSELLINE
WE LEM NEKU NUT’IMUL-MISKINE
WE KUNNA NEHUDU ME’AL-HA’IDINE
WE KUNNA NUKEDHDHIBU BIJEWMI ED-DINI
HETTA ‘ETANAL-JEKINU
FEMA TENFA’UHUM SHEFA’ATU ESH-SHAFI’INE
FEMA LEHUM ‘ANIT-TEDHKIRETI MU’RIDINE
KE’ENNEHUM HUMURUN MUSTENFIRETUN
FERRET MIN KASWERETIN
BEL JURIDU KULLU EMRI’IN MINHUM ‘EN JU’UTA SUHUFÆN MUNESHSHERETEN
KELLA BEL LA JEHAFUNEL-’AHIRETE
KELLA ‘INNEHU TEDHKIRETUN
FEMEN SHA’E DHEKEREHU
WE MA JEDHKURUNE ‘ILLA ‘EN JESHA’EL-LAHU HUWE ‘EHLUT-TEKWA WE ‘EHLUL-MEGFIRETI
LA ‘UKSIMU BIJEWMIL-KIJAMETI
WE LA ‘UKSIMU BIN-NEFSIL-LEWWAMETI
‘EJEHSEBUL-’INSANU ‘ELLEN NEXHME’A ‘IDHAMEHU
BELA KADIRINE ‘ALA ‘EN NUSEWWIJE BENANEHU
BEL JURIDUL-’INSANU LIJEFXHURE ‘EMAMEHU
JES’ELU ‘EJJANE JEWMUL-KIJAMETI
FE’IDHA BERIKAL-BESERU
WE HASEFEL-KAMERU
WE XHUMI’A ESH-SHEMSU WEL-KAMERU
JEKULUL-’INSANU JEWME’IDHIN ‘EJNEL-MEFERRU
KELLA LA WEZERE
‘ILA RABBIKE JEWME’IDHINL-MUSTEKARRU
JUNEBBE’UL-’INSANU JEWME’IDHIN BIMA KADDEME WE ‘EHHARE
BELIL-’INSANU ‘ALA NEFSIHI BESIRETUN
WE LEW ‘ELKA MA’ADHIREHU
LA TUHERRIK BIHI LISANEKE LITA’XHELE BIHI
‘INNE ‘ALEJNA XHEM’AHU WE KUR’ANEHU
FE’IDHA KARE’NAHU FE ETTEBI’ KUR’ANEHU
THUMME ‘INNE ‘ALEJNA BEJANEHU
KELLA BEL TUHIBBUNEL-’AXHILETE
WE TEDHERUNEL-’AHIRETE
WUXHUHUN JEWME’IDHIN NADIRETUN
‘ILA RABBIHA NADHIRETUN
WE WUXHUHUN JEWME’IDHIN BASIRETUN
TEDHUNNU ‘EN JUF’ALE BIHA FAKIRETUN
KELLA ‘IDHA BELEGATIT-TERAKI
WE KILE MEN RAKIN
WE DHENNE ‘ENNEHUL-FIRAKU
WET-TEFFETI ES-SAKU BIS-SAKI
‘ILA RABBIKE JEWME’IDHINL-MESAKU
FELA SEDDEKA WE LA SELLA
WE LEKIN KEDHDHEBE WE TEWELLA
THUMME DHEHEBE ‘ILA ‘EHLIHI JETEMETTA
‘EWLA LEKE FE’EWLA
THUMME ‘EWLA LEKE FE’EWLA
‘EJEHSEBUL-’INSANU ‘EN JUTREKE SUDEN
‘ELEM JEKU NUTFETEN MIN MENIJIN JUMNA
THUMME KANE ‘ALEKATEN FEHALEKA FESEWWA
FEXHE’ALE MINHU EZ-ZEWXHEJNI EDH-DHEKERE WEL-’UNTHA
‘ELEJSE DHALIKE BIKADIRIN ‘ALA ‘EN JUHJIJEL-MEWTA
HEL ‘ETA ‘ALEL-’INSANI HINUN MINE ED-DEHRI LEM JEKUN SHEJ’ÆN MEDHKURÆN
‘INNA HALEKNAL-’INSANE MIN NUTFETIN ‘EMSHAXHIN NEBTELIHI FEXHE’ALNAHU SEMI’ÆN BESIRÆN
‘INNA HEDEJNAHU ES-SEBILE ‘IMMA SHAKIRÆN WE ‘IMMA KEFURÆN
‘INNA ‘A’TEDNA LILKAFIRINE SELASILÆN WE ‘EGLALÆN WE SA’IRÆN
‘INNEL-’EBRARE JESHREBUNE MIN KE’SIN KANE MIZAXHUHA KAFURÆN
‘AJNÆN JESHREBU BIHA ‘IBADU ELLAHI JUFEXHXHIRUNEHA TEFXHIRÆN
JUFUNE BIN-NEDHRI WE JEHAFUNE JEWMÆN KANE SHERRUHU MUSTETIRÆN
WE JUT’IMUNET-TA’AME ‘ALA HUBBIHI MISKINÆN WE JETIMÆN WE ‘ESIRÆN
‘INNEMA NUT’IMUKUM LIWEXHHI ELLAHI LA NURIDU MINKUM XHEZA’EN WE LA SHUKURÆN
‘INNA NEHAFU MIN RABBINA JEWMÆN ‘ABUSÆN KAMTERIRÆN
FEWEKAHUMU ELLAHU SHERRE DHALIKEL-JEWMI WE LEKKAHUM NEDRETEN WE SURURÆN
WE XHEZAHUM BIMA SEBERU XHENNETEN WE HERIRÆN
MUTTEKI’INE FIHA ‘ALEL-’ERA’IKI LA JEREWNE FIHA SHEMSÆN WE LA ZEMHERIRÆN
WE DANIJETEN ‘ALEJHIM DHILALUHA WE DHULLILET KUTUFUHA TEDHLILÆN
WE JUTAFU ‘ALEJHIM BI’ANIJETIN MIN FIDDETIN WE ‘EKWABIN KANET KAWARIRE
KAWARIRE MIN FIDDETIN KADDERUHA TEKDIRÆN
WE JUSKAWNE FIHA KE’SÆN KANE MIZAXHUHA ZENXHEBILÆN
‘AJNÆN FIHA TUSEMMA SELSEBILÆN
WE JETUFU ‘ALEJHIM WILDANUN MUHALLEDUNE ‘IDHA RE’EJTEHUM HESIBTEHUM LU’ULU’UÆN MENTHURÆN
WE ‘IDHA RE’EJTE THEMME RE’EJTE NA’IMÆN WE MULKÆN KEBIRÆN
‘ALIJEHUM THIJABU SUNDUSIN HUDRUN WE ‘ISTEBREKUN WE HULLU ‘ESAWIRE MIN FIDDETIN WE SEKAHUM REBBUHUM SHERABÆN TEHURÆN
‘INNE HADHA KANE LEKUM XHEZA’EN WE KANE SA’JUKUM MESHKURÆN
‘INNA NEHNU NEZZELNA ‘ALEJKEL-KUR’ANE TENZILÆN
FASBIR LIHUKMI RABBIKE WE LA TUTI’ MINHUM ‘ATHIMÆN ‘EW KEFURÆN
WE EDHKUR ESME RABBIKE BUKRETEN WE ‘ESILÆN
WE MINEL-LEJLI FASXHUD LEHU WE SEBBIHHU LEJLÆN TEWILÆN
‘INNE HA’UULA’ JUHIBBUNEL-’AXHILETE WE JEDHERUNE WERA’EHUM JEWMÆN THEKILÆN
NEHNU HALEKNAHUM WE SHEDEDNA ‘ESREHUM WE ‘IDHA SHI’NA BEDDELNA ‘EMTHALEHUM TEBDILÆN
‘INNE HEDHIHI TEDHKIRETUN FEMEN SHA’E ETTEHADHE ‘ILA RABBIHI SEBILÆN
WE MA TESHA’UNE ‘ILLA ‘EN JESHA’EL-LAHU ‘INNALL-LLAHE KANE ‘ALIMÆN HEKIMÆN

FAL’ASIFATI ‘ASFÆN
WE EN-NASHIRATI NESHRÆN
FALFARIKATI FERKÆN
FALMULKIJATI DHIKRÆN

‘ILA KADERIN MA’LUMIN

‘ELEM NEXH’ALIL-’ERDE KIFATÆN
‘EHJA’EN WE ‘EMWATÆN

‘INNE LILMUTTEKINE MEFAZÆN

WE KEWA’IBE ‘ETRABÆN
WE KE’SÆN DIHAKÆN

XHEZA’EN MIN RABBIKE ‘ATA’EN HISABÆN

JEWME JEKUMU ER-RUHU WEL-MELA’IKETU SEFFÆN LA JETEKELLEMUNE ‘ILLA MEN ‘EDHINE LEHU ER-REHMANU WE KALE SEWABÆN
DHALIKEL-JEWMUL-HEKKU FEMEN SHA’E ETTEHADHE ‘ILA RABBIHI ME’ABÆN

FEHESHERE FENADA
FEKALE ‘ENA REBBUKUMUL-’A’LA
FE’EHADHEHU ELLAHU NEKALEL-’AHIRETI WEL-’ULA
‘INNE FI DHALIKE LA’IBRETEN LIMEN JEHSHA
‘E’ENTUM ‘ESHEDDU HALKÆN ‘EMI ES-SEMA’U BENAHA
REFE’A SEMKEHA FESEWWAHA
WE ‘EGTESHE LEJLEHA WE ‘EHREXHE DUHAHA
WEL-’ERDE BA’DE DHALIKE DEHAHA
‘EHREXHE MINHA MA’EHA WE MER’AHA
WEL-XHIBALE ‘ERSAHA
META’ÆN LEKUM WE LI’EN’AMIKUM
FE’IDHA XHA’ETIT-TAMMETUL-KUBRA
JEWME JETEDHEKKERUL-’INSANU MA SA’A
WE BURRIZETIL-XHEHIMU LIMEN JERA
FE’EMMA MEN TEGA
WE ‘ATHEREL-HEJÆTE ED-DUNJA
FE’INNEL-XHEHIME HIJEL-ME’WA
WE ‘EMMA MEN HAFE MEKAME RABBIHI WE NEHA EN-NEFSE ‘ANIL-HEWA
FE’INNEL-XHENNETE HIJEL-ME’WA
JES’ELUNEKE ‘ANI ES-SA’ATI ‘EJJANE MURSAHA
FIME ‘ENTE MIN DHIKRAHA
‘ILA RABBIKE MUNTEHAHA
‘INNEMA ‘ENTE MUNDHIRU MEN JEHSHAHA
KE’ENNEHUM JEWME JEREWNEHA LEM JELBETHU ‘ILLA ‘ASHIJETEN ‘EW DUHAHA
‘ABESE WE TEWELLA
‘EN XHA’EHUL-’A’MA
WE MA JUDRIKE LE’ALLEHU JEZZEKKA
‘EW JEDHDHEKKERU FETENFE’AHU EDH-DHIKRA
‘EMMA MENI ESTEGNA
FE’ENTE LEHU TESEDDA
WE MA ‘ALEJKE ‘ELLA JEZZEKKA
WE ‘EMMA MEN XHA’EKE JES’A
WE HUWE JEHSHA
FE’ENTE ‘ANHU TELEHHA
KELLA ‘INNEHA TEDHKIRETUN
FEMEN SHA’E DHEKEREHU
FI SUHUFIN MUKERREMETIN
MERFU’ATIN MUTEHHERETIN
BI’EJDI SEFERETIN
KIRAMIN BERERETIN
KUTILEL-’INSANU MA ‘EKFEREHU
MIN ‘EJJI SHEJ’IN HALEKAHU
MIN NUTFETIN HALEKAHU FEKADDEREHU
THUMME ES-SEBILE JESSEREHU
THUMME ‘EMATEHU FE’EKBEREHU
THUMME ‘IDHA SHA’E ‘ENSHEREHU
KELLA LEMMA JEKDI MA ‘EMEREHU
FELJENDHURIL-’INSANU ‘ILA TA’AMIHI
‘ENNA SEBEBNAL-MA’E SEBBÆN
THUMME SHEKAKNAL-’ERDE SHEKKÆN
FE’ENBETNA FIHA HEBBÆN
WE ‘INEBÆN WE KADBÆN
WE ZEJTUNÆN WE NEHLÆN
WE HEDA’IKA GULBÆN
WE FAKIHETEN WE ‘EBBÆN
META’ÆN LEKUM WE LI’EN’AMIKUM
FE’IDHA XHA’ETI ES-SAHHATU
JEWME JEFIRRUL-MER’U MIN ‘EHIHI
WE ‘UMMIHI WE ‘EBIHI
WE SAHIBETIHI WE BENIHI
LIKULLI EMRI’IN MINHUM JEWME’IDHIN SHE’NUN JUGNIHI
WUXHUHUN JEWME’IDHIN MUSFIRETUN
DAHIKETUN MUSTEBSHIRETUN
WE WUXHUHUN JEWME’IDHIN ‘ALEJHA GABERETUN
TERHEKUHA KATERETUN
‘ULA’IKE HUMUL-KEFERETUL-FEXHERETU
‘IDHA ESH-SHEMSU KUWIRET
WE ‘IDHA EN-NUXHUMU ENKEDERET
WE ‘IDHAL-XHIBALU SUJJIRET
WE ‘IDHAL-’ISHARU ‘UTTILET
WE ‘IDHAL-WUHUSHU HUSHIRET
WE ‘IDHAL-BIHARU SUXHXHIRET
WE ‘IDHA EN-NUFUSU ZUWIXHET
WE ‘IDHAL-MEW’UDETU SU’ILET
BI’EJJI DHENBIN KUTILET
WE ‘IDHA ES-SUHUFU NUSHIRET
WE ‘IDHA ES-SEMA’U KUSHITET
WE ‘IDHAL-XHEHIMU SU’’IRET
WE ‘IDHAL-XHENNETU ‘UZLIFET
‘ALIMET NEFSUN MA ‘EHDERET
FELA ‘UKSIMU BIL-HUNNESI
EL-XHEWARIL-KUNNESI
WEL-LEJLI ‘IDHA ‘AS’ASE
WE ES-SUBHI ‘IDHA TENEFFESE
‘INNEHU LEKAWLU RESULIN KERIMIN
DHI KUWETIN ‘INDE DHIL-’ARSHI MEKININ
MUTA’IN THEMME ‘EMININ
WE MA SAHIBUKUM BIMEXHNUNIN
WE LEKAD RE’AHU BIL-’UFUKIL-MUBINI
WE MA HUWE ‘ALEL-GAJBI BIDENININ
WE MA HUWE BIKAWLI SHEJTANIN REXHIMIN
FE’EJNE TEDH/HEBUNE
‘IN HUWE ‘ILLA DHIKRUN LIL’ALEMINE
LIMEN SHA’E MINKUM ‘EN JESTEKIME
WE MA TESHA’UNE ‘ILLA ‘EN JESHA’EL-LAHU REBBUL-’ALEMINE
‘IDHA ES-SEMA’U ENFETERET
WE ‘IDHAL-KEWAKIBU ENTETHERET
WE ‘IDHAL-BIHARU FUXHXHIRET
WE ‘IDHAL-KUBURU BU’THIRET
‘ALIMET NEFSUN MA KADDEMET WE ‘EHHARET
JA ‘EJJUHAL-’INSANU MA GARREKE BIREBBIKEL-KERIMI
EL-LEDHI HALEKAKE FESEWWAKE FE’ADELEKE
FI ‘EJJI SURETIN MA SHA’E REKKEBEKE
KELLA BEL TUKEDHDHIBUNE BID-DINI
WE ‘INNE ‘ALEJKUM LEHAFIDHINE
KIRAMÆN KATIBINE
JA’LEMUNE MA TEF’ALUNE
‘INNEL-’EBRARE LEFI NA’IMIN
WE ‘INNEL-FUXHXHARE LEFI XHEHIMIN
JESLEWNEHA JEWME ED-DINI
WE MA HUM ‘ANHA BIGA’IBINE
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MA JEWMU ED-DINI
THUMME MA ‘EDRAKE MA JEWMU ED-DINI
JEWME LA TEMLIKU NEFSUN LINEFSIN SHEJ’ÆN WEL-’EMRU JEWME’IDHIN LILLAHI
WEJLUN LILMUTEFFIFINE
EL-LEDHINE ‘IDHA EKTALU ‘ALA EN-NASI JESTEWFUNE
WE ‘IDHA KALUHUM ‘EW WEZENUHUM JUHSIRUNE
‘ELA JEDHUNNU ‘ULE’IKE ‘ENNEHUM MEB’UTHUNE
LIJEWMIN ‘ADHIMIN
JEWME JEKUMU EN-NASU LIREBBIL-’ALEMINE
KELLA ‘INNE KITABEL-FUXHXHARI LEFI SIXHXHININ
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MA SIXHXHINUN
KITABUN MERKUMUN
WEJLUN JEWME’IDHIN LILMUKEDHDHIBINE
EL-LEDHINE JUKEDHDHIBUNE BIJEWMI ED-DINI
WE MA JUKEDHDHIBU BIHI ‘ILLA KULLU MU’TEDIN ‘ETHIMIN
‘IDHA TUTLA ‘ALEJHI ‘AJATUNA KALE ‘ESATIRUL-’EWWELINE
KELLA BEL RANE ‘ALA KULUBIHIM MA KANU JEKSIBUNE
KELLA ‘INNEHUM ‘AN RABBIHIM JEWME’IDHIN LEMEHXHUBUNE
THUMME ‘INNEHUM LESALUL-XHEHIMI
THUMME JUKALU HADHAL-LEDHI KUNTUM BIHI TUKEDHDHIBUNE
KELLA ‘INNE KITABEL-’EBRARI LEFI ‘ILLIJINE
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MA ‘ILLIJUNE
KITABUN MERKUMUN
JESH/HEDUHUL-MUKARREBUNE
‘INNEL-’EBRARE LEFI NA’IMIN
‘ALEL-’ERA’IKI JENDHURUNE
TA’RIFU FI WUXHUHIHIM NEDRETE EN-NA’IMI
JUSKAWNE MIN REHIKIN MEHTUMIN
HITAMUHU MISKUN WE FI DHALIKE FELJETENAFESIL-MUTENAFISUNE
WE MIZAXHUHU MIN TESNIMIN
‘AJNÆN JESHREBU BIHAL-MUKARREBUNE
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘EXHREMU KANU MINEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU JEDHEKUNE
WE ‘IDHA MERRU BIHIM JETEGAMEZUNE
WE ‘IDHA ENKALEBU ‘ILA ‘EHLIHIMU ENKALEBU FEKIHINE
WE ‘IDHA RE’EWHUM KALU ‘INNE HA’UULA’ LEDALLUNE
WE MA ‘URSILU ‘ALEJHIM HAFIDHINE
FALJEWMEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU MINEL-KUFFARI JEDHEKUNE
‘ALEL-’ERA’IKI JENDHURUNE
HEL THUWIBEL-KUFFARU MA KANU JEF’ALUNE
‘IDHA ES-SEMA’U ENSHEKKAT
WE ‘EDHINET LIREBBIHA WE HUKKAT
WE ‘IDHAL-’ERDU MUDDET
WE ‘ELKAT MA FIHA WE TEHALLET
WE ‘EDHINET LIREBBIHA WE HUKKAT
JA ‘EJJUHAL-’INSANU ‘INNEKE KADIHUN ‘ILA RABBIKE KEDHÆN FEMULAKIHI
FE’EMMA MEN ‘UTIJE KITABEHU BIJEMINIHI
FESEWFE JUHASEBU HISABÆN JESIRÆN
WE JENKALIBU ‘ILA ‘EHLIHI MESRURÆN
WE ‘EMMA MEN ‘UTIJE KITABEHU WERA’E DHEHRIHI
FESEWFE JED’U THUBURÆN
WE JESLA SA’IRÆN
‘INNEHU KANE FI ‘EHLIHI MESRURÆN
‘INNEHU DHENNE ‘EN LEN JEHURE
BELA ‘INNE REBBEHU KANE BIHI BESIRÆN
FELA ‘UKSIMU BISH-SHEFEKI
WEL-LEJLI WE MA WESEKA
WEL-KAMERI ‘IDHA ETTESEKA
LETERKEBUNNE TEBEKÆN ‘AN TEBEKIN
FEMA LEHUM LA JU’UMINUNE
WE ‘IDHA KURI’E ‘ALEJHIMUL-KUR’ANU LA JESXHUDUNE
BELIL-LEDHINE KEFERU JUKEDHDHIBUNE
WEL-LAHU ‘A’LEMU BIMA JU’UNE
FEBESHSHIRHUM BI’ADHABIN ‘ELIMIN
‘ILLAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LEHUM ‘EXHRUN GAJRU MEMNUNIN
WE ES-SEMA’I DHATIL-BURUXHI
WEL-JEWMIL-MEW’UDI
WE SHAHIDIN WE MESH/HUDIN
KUTILE ‘ESHABUL-’UHDUDI
EN-NARI DHATIL-WEKUDI
‘IDH HUM ‘ALEJHA KU’UDUN
WE HUM ‘ALA MA JEF’ALUNE BIL-MU’UMININE SHUHUDUN
WE MA NEKAMU MINHUM ‘ILLA ‘EN JU’UMINU BILLAHIL-’AZIZIL-HEMIDI
EL-LEDHI LEHU MULKU ES-SEMAWATI WEL-’ERDI WEL-LAHU ‘ALA KULLI SHEJ’IN SHEHIDUN
‘INNEL-LEDHINE FETENUL-MU’UMININE WEL-MU’UMINATI THUMME LEM JETUBU FELEHUM ‘ADHABU XHEHENNEME WE LEHUM ‘ADHABUL-HERIKI
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI LEHUM XHENNATUN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU DHALIKEL-FEWZUL-KEBIRU
‘INNE BETSHE RABBIKE LESHEDIDUN
‘INNEHU HUWE JUBDI’U WE JU’IDU
WE HUWEL-GAFURUL-WEDUDU
DHUL-’ARSHIL-MEXHIDU
FA’’ALUN LIMA JURIDU
HEL ‘ETAKE HEDITHUL-XHUNUDI
FIR’AWNE WE THEMUDE
BELIL-LEDHINE KEFERU FI TEKDHIBIN
WEL-LAHU MIN WERA’IHIM MUHITUN
BEL HUWE KUR’ANUN MEXHIDUN
FI LEWHIN MEHFUDHIN
WE ES-SEMA’I WET-TARIKI
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MAT-TARIKU
EN-NEXHMU ETH-THAKIBU
‘IN KULLU NEFSIN LEMMA ‘ALEJHA HAFIDHUN
FELJENDHURIL-’INSANU MIMME HULIKA
HULIKA MIN MA’IN DAFIKIN
JEHRUXHU MIN BEJNI ES-SULBI WET-TERA’IBI
‘INNEHU ‘ALA REXH’IHI LEKADIRUN
JEWME TUBLA ES-SERA’IRU
FEMA LEHU MIN KUWETIN WE LA NASIRIN
WE ES-SEMA’I DHATI ER-REXH’I
WEL-’ERDI DHATI ES-SED’I
‘INNEHU LEKAWLUN FESLUN
WE MA HUWE BIL-HEZLI
‘INNEHUM JEKIDUNE KEJDÆN
WE ‘EKIDU KEJDÆN
FEMEHHILIL-KAFIRINE ‘EMHILHUM RUWEJDÆN
SEBBIHI ESME RABBIKEL-’A’LA
EL-LEDHI HALEKA FESEWWA
WEL-LEDHI KADDERE FEHEDA
WEL-LEDHI ‘EHREXHEL-MER’A
FEXHE’ALEHU GUTHA’EN ‘EHWA
SENUKRI’UKE FELA TENSA
‘ILLA MA SHA’EL-LAHU ‘INNEHU JA’LEMUL-XHEHRE WE MA JEHFA
WE NUJESSIRUKE LILJUSRA
FEDHEKKIR ‘IN NEFE’ATI EDH-DHIKRA
SEJEDHDHEKKERU MEN JEHSHA
WE JETEXHENNEBUHAL-’ESHKA
EL-LEDHI JESLA EN-NAREL-KUBRA
THUMME LA JEMUTU FIHA WE LA JEHJA
KAD ‘EFLEHE MEN TEZEKKA
WE DHEKERE ESME RABBIHI FESELLA
BEL TU’UTHIRUNEL-HEJÆTE ED-DUNJA
WEL-’AHIRETU HAJRUN WE ‘EBKA
‘INNE HADHA LEFI ES-SUHUFIL-’ULA
SUHUFI ‘IBRAHIME WE MUSA
HEL ‘ETAKE HEDITHUL-GASHIJETI
WUXHUHUN JEWME’IDHIN HASHI’ATUN
‘AMILETUN NASIBETUN
TESLA NARÆN HAMIJETEN
TUSKA MIN ‘AJNIN ‘ANIJETIN
LEJSE LEHUM TA’AMUN ‘ILLA MIN DERI’IN
LA JUSMINU WE LA JUGNI MIN XHU’IN
WUXHUHUN JEWME’IDHIN NA’IMETUN
LISA’JIHA RADIJETUN
FI XHENNETIN ‘ALIJETIN
LA TESMA’U FIHA LAGIJETEN
FIHA ‘AJNUN XHARIJETUN
FIHA SURURUN MERFU’ATUN
WE ‘EKWABUN MEWDU’ATUN
WE NEMARIKU MESFUFETUN
WE ZERABIJU MEBTHUTHETUN
‘EFELA JENDHURUNE ‘ILAL-’IBILI KEJFE HULIKAT
WE ‘ILA ES-SEMA’I KEJFE RUFI’AT
WE ‘ILAL-XHIBALI KEJFE NUSIBET
WE ‘ILAL-’ERDI KEJFE SUTIHET
FEDHEKKIR ‘INNEMA ‘ENTE MUDHEKKIRUN
LESTE ‘ALEJHIM BIMUSEJTIRIN
‘ILLA MEN TEWELLA WE KEFERE
FEJU’ADHDHIBUHU ELLAHUL-’ADHABEL-’EKBERE
‘INNE ‘ILEJNA ‘IABEHUM
THUMME ‘INNE ‘ALEJNA HISABEHUM
WEL-FEXHRI
WE LEJALIN ‘ASHRIN
WE ESH-SHEF’I WEL-WETRI
WEL-LEJLI ‘IDHA JESRI
HEL FI DHALIKE KASEMUN LIDHI HIXHRIN
‘ELEM TERE KEJFE FE’ALE REBBUKE BI’ADIN
‘IREME DHATIL-’IMADI
ELLETI LEM JUHLEK MITHLUHA FIL-BILADI
WE THEMUDEL-LEDHINE XHABU ES-SEHRE BIL-WADI
WE FIR’AWNE DHIL-’EWTADI
EL-LEDHINE TEGAW FIL-BILADI
FE’EKTHERU FIHAL-FESADE
FESEBBE ‘ALEJHIM REBBUKE SEWTE ‘ADHABIN
‘INNE REBBEKE LEBIALMIRSADI
FE’EMMAL-’INSANU ‘IDHA MA EBTELAHU REBBUHU FE’EKREMEHU WE NA’’AMEHU FEJEKULU RABBI ‘EKREMENI
WE ‘EMMA ‘IDHA MA EBTELAHU FEKADERE ‘ALEJHI RIZKAHU FEJEKULU RABBI ‘EHANENI
KELLA BEL LA TUKRIMUNEL-JETIME
WE LA TEHADDUNE ‘ALA TA’AMIL-MISKINI
WE TE’KULUNET-TURATHE ‘EKLÆN LEMMÆN
WE TUHIBBUNEL-MALE HUBBÆN XHEMMÆN
KELLA ‘IDHA DUKKETIL-’ERDU DEKKÆN DEKKÆN
WE XHA’E REBBUKE WEL-MELEKU SEFFÆN SEFFÆN
WE XHI’E JEWME’IDHIN BIXHEHENNEME JEWME’IDHIN JETEDHEKKERUL-’INSANU WE ‘ENNA LEHU EDH-DHIKRA
JEKULU JA LEJTENI KADDEMTU LIHEJATI
FEJEWME’IDHIN LA JU’ADHDHIBU ‘ADHABEHU ‘EHEDUN
WE LA JUTHIKU WETHAKAHU ‘EHEDUN
JA ‘EJJETUHA EN-NEFSUL-MUTME’INNETU
ERXHI’I ‘ILA RABBIKI RADIJETEN MERDIJETEN
FADHULI FI ‘IBADI
WE EDHULI XHENNETI
LA ‘UKSIMU BIHEDHAL-BELEDI
WE ‘ENTE HILLUN BIHEDHAL-BELEDI
WE WALIDIN WE MA WELEDE
LEKAD HALEKNAL-’INSANE FI KEBEDIN
‘EJEHSEBU ‘EN LEN JEKDIRE ‘ALEJHI ‘EHEDUN
JEKULU ‘EHLEKTU MALÆN LUBEDÆN
‘EJEHSEBU ‘EN LEM JEREHU ‘EHEDUN
‘ELEM NEXH’AL LEHU ‘AJNEJNI
WE LISANÆN WE SHEFETEJNI
WE HEDEJNAHU EN-NEXHDEJNI
FELA EKTEHEMEL-’AKABETE
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MAL-’AKABETU
FEKKU REKABETIN
‘EW ‘IT’AMUN FI JEWMIN DHI MESGABETIN
JETIMÆN DHA MEKREBETIN
‘EW MISKINÆN DHA METREBETIN
THUMME KANE MINEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE TEWASEW BIS-SEBRI WE TEWASEW BIL-MERHEMETI
‘ULA’IKE ‘ESHABUL-MEJMENETI
WEL-LEDHINE KEFERU BI’AJATINA HUM ‘ESHABUL-MESH’EMETI
‘ALEJHIM NARUN MU’USEDETUN
WE ESH-SHEMSI WE DUHAHA
WEL-KAMERI ‘IDHA TELAHA
WE EN-NEHARI ‘IDHA XHELLAHA
WEL-LEJLI ‘IDHA JEGSHAHA
WE ES-SEMA’I WE MA BENAHA
WEL-’ERDI WE MA TEHAHA
WE NEFSIN WE MA SEWWAHA
FE’ELHEMEHA FUXHUREHA WE TEKWAHA
KAD ‘EFLEHE MEN ZEKKAHA
WE KAD HABE MEN DESSAHA
KEDHDHEBET THEMUDU BITEGWAHA
‘IDHI ENBE’ATHE ‘ESHKAHA
FEKALE LEHUM RESULU ELLAHI NAKATEL-LAHI WE SUKJAHA
FEKEDHDHEBUHU FE’AKARUHA FEDEMDEME ‘ALEJHIM REBBUHUM BIDHENBIHIM FESEWWAHA
WE LA JEHAFU ‘UKBAHA
WEL-LEJLI ‘IDHA JEGSHA
WE EN-NEHARI ‘IDHA TEXHELLA
WE MA HALEKA EDH-DHEKERE WEL-’UNTHA
‘INNE SA’JEKUM LESHETTA
FE’EMMA MEN ‘A’TA WE ETTEKA
WE SEDDEKA BIL-HUSNA
FESENUJESSIRUHU LILJUSRA
WE ‘EMMA MEN BEHILE WE ESTEGNA
WE KEDHDHEBE BIL-HUSNA
FESENUJESSIRUHU LIL’USRA
WE MA JUGNI ‘ANHU MALUHU ‘IDHA TEREDDA
‘INNE ‘ALEJNA LELHUDA
WE ‘INNE LENA LEL’AHIRETE WEL-’ULA
FE’ENDHERTUKUM NARÆN TELEDHDHA
LA JESLAHA ‘ILLAL-’ESHKA
EL-LEDHI KEDHDHEBE WE TEWELLA
WE SEJUXHENNEBUHAL-’ETKA
EL-LEDHI JU’UTI MALEHU JETEZEKKA
WE MA LI’HEDIN ‘INDEHU MIN NI’METIN TUXHZA
‘ILLA EBTIGA’E WEXHHI RABBIHIL-’A’LA
WE LESEWFE JERDA
WE ED-DUHA
WEL-LEJLI ‘IDHA SEXHA
MA WEDDE’AKE REBBUKE WE MA KALA
WE LEL’AHIRETU HAJRUN LEKE MINEL-’ULA
WE LESEWFE JU’TIKE REBBUKE FETERDA
‘ELEM JEXHIDKE JETIMÆN FE’AWA
WE WEXHEDEKE DALLÆN FEHEDA
WE WEXHEDEKE ‘A’ILÆN FE’EGNA
FE’EMMAL-JETIME FELA TEKHER
WE ‘EMMA ES-SA’ILE FELA TENHER
WE ‘EMMA BINI’METI RABBIKE FEHEDDITH
‘ELEM NESHREH LEKE SEDREKE
WE WEDA’NA ‘ANKE WIZREKE
EL-LEDHI ‘ENKADE DHEHREKE
WE REFA’NA LEKE DHIKREKE
FE’INNE ME’AL-’USRI JUSRÆN
‘INNE ME’AL-’USRI JUSRÆN
FE’IDHA FEREGTE FANSEB
WE ‘ILA RABBIKE FARGAB
WET-TINI WE EZ-ZEJTUNI
WE TURI SININE
WE HEDHAL-BELEDIL-’EMINI
LEKAD HALEKNAL-’INSANE FI ‘EHSENI TEKWIMIN
THUMME REDEDNAHU ‘ESFELE SAFILINE
‘ILLAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI FELEHUM ‘EXHRUN GAJRU MEMNUNIN
FEMA JUKEDHDHIBUKE BA’DU BID-DINI
‘ELEJSEL-LAHU BI’EHKEMIL-HAKIMINE
EKRE’ BIASMI RABBIKEL-LEDHI HALEKA
HALEKAL-’INSANE MIN ‘ALEKIN
EKRE’ WE REBBUKEL-’EKREMU
EL-LEDHI ‘ALLEME BIL-KALEMI
‘ALLEMEL-’INSANE MA LEM JA’LEM
KELLA ‘INNEL-’INSANE LEJETGA
‘EN RE’AHU ESTEGNA
‘INNE ‘ILA RABBIKE ER-RUXH’A
‘ERE’EJTEL-LEDHI JENHA
‘ABDÆN ‘IDHA SELLA
‘ERE’EJTE ‘IN KANE ‘ALEL-HUDA
‘EW ‘EMERE BIT-TEKWA
‘ERE’EJTE ‘IN KEDHDHEBE WE TEWELLA
‘ELEM JA’LEM BI’ENNEL-LAHE JERA
KELLA LE’IN LEM JENTEHI LENESFA’A BIN-NASIJETI
NASIJETIN KADHIBETIN HATI’ETIN
FELJED’U NADIJEH
SENED’U EZ-ZEBANIJETE
KELLA LA TUTI’HU WE ESXHUD WAKTERIB
‘INNA ‘ENZELNAHU FI LEJLETIL-KADRI
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MA LEJLETUL-KADRI
LEJLETUL-KADRI HAJRUN MIN ‘ELFI SHEHRIN
TENEZZELUL-MELA’IKETU WE ER-RUHU FIHA BI’IDHNI RABBIHIM MIN KULLI ‘EMRIN
SELAMUN HIJE HETTA METLA’IL-FEXHRI
LEM JEKUNIL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN ‘EHLIL-KITABI WEL-MUSHRIKINE MUNFEKKINE HETTA TE’TIJEHUMUL-BEJJINETU
RESULUN MINEL-LAHI JETLU SUHUFÆN MUTEHHERETEN
FIHA KUTUBUN KAJJIMETUN
WE MA TEFERREKAL-LEDHINE ‘UTUL-KITABE ‘ILLA MIN BA’DI MA XHA’ET/HUMUL-BEJJINETU
WE MA ‘UMIRU ‘ILLA LIJA’BUDU ELLAHE MUHLISINE LEHU ED-DINE HUNEFA’E WE JUKIMU ES-SELÆTE WE JU’UTU EZ-ZEKÆTE WE DHELIKE DINUL-KAJJIMETI
‘INNEL-LEDHINE KEFERU MIN ‘EHLIL-KITABI WEL-MUSHRIKINE FI NARI XHEHENNEME HALIDINE FIHA ‘ULA’IKE HUM SHERRUL-BERIJETI
‘INNEL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI ‘ULA’IKE HUM HAJRUL-BERIJETI
XHEZA’UUHUM ‘INDE RABBIHIM XHENNATU ‘ADNIN TEXHRI MIN TEHTIHAL-’ENHARU HALIDINE FIHA ‘EBEDÆN REDIJEL-LAHU ‘ANHUM WE REDU ‘ANHU DHALIKE LIMEN HASHIJE REBBEHU
‘IDHA ZULZILETIL-’ERDU ZILZALEHA
WE ‘EHREXHETIL-’ERDU ‘ETHKALEHA
WE KALEL-’INSANU MA LEHA
JEWME’IDHIN TUHEDDITHU ‘EHBAREHA
BI’ENNE REBBEKE ‘EWHA LEHA
JEWME’IDHIN JESDURU EN-NASU ‘ESHTATÆN LIJUREW ‘A’MALEHUM
FEMEN JA’MEL MITHKALE DHERRETIN HAJRÆN JEREHU
WE MEN JA’MEL MITHKALE DHERRETIN SHERRÆN JEREHU
WEL-’ADIJATI DEBHÆN
FALMURIJATI KADHÆN
FALMUGIRATI SUBHÆN
FE’ETHERNE BIHI NEK’ÆN
FEWESETNE BIHI XHEM’ÆN
‘INNEL-’INSANE LIREBBIHI LEKENUDUN
WE ‘INNEHU ‘ALA DHALIKE LESHEHIDUN
WE ‘INNEHU LIHUBBIL-HAJRI LESHEDIDUN
‘EFELA JA’LEMU ‘IDHA BU’THIRE MA FIL-KUBURI
WE HUSSILE MA FI ES-SUDURI
‘INNE REBBEHUM BIHIM JEWME’IDHIN LEHABIRUN
EL-KARI’ATU
MAL-KARI’ATU
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MAL-KARI’ATU
JEWME JEKUNU EN-NASU KALFERASHIL-MEBTHUTHI
WE TEKUNUL-XHIBALU KAL’IHNIL-MENFUSHI
FE’EMMA MEN THEKULET MEWAZINUHU
FEHUWE FI ‘ISHETIN RADIJETIN
WE ‘EMMA MEN HAFFET MEWAZINUHU
FE’UMMUHU HAWIJETUN
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MA HIJEH
NARUN HAMIJETUN
‘ELHAKUMUT-TEKATHURU
HETTA ZURTUMUL-MEKABIRE
KELLA SEWFE TA’LEMUNE
THUMME KELLA SEWFE TA’LEMUNE
KELLA LEW TA’LEMUNE ‘ILMEL-JEKINI
LETEREWUNNEL-XHEHIME
THUMME LETEREWUNNEHA ‘AJNEL-JEKINI
THUMME LETUS’ELUNNE JEWME’IDHIN ‘ANI EN-NA’IMI
WEL-’ASRI
‘INNEL-’INSANE LEFI HUSRIN
‘ILLAL-LEDHINE ‘AMENU WE ‘AMILU ES-SALIHATI WE TEWASEW BIL-HEKKI WE TEWASEW BIS-SEBRI
WEJLUN LIKULLI HUMEZETIN LUMEZETIN
EL-LEDHI XHEME’A MALÆN WE ‘ADDEDEHU
JEHSEBU ‘ENNE MALEHU ‘EHLEDEHU
KELLA LEJUNBEDHENNE FIL-HUTEMETI
WE MA ‘EDRAKE MAL-HUTEMETU
NARU ELLAHIL-MUKADETU
ELLETI TETTELI’U ‘ALEL-’EF’IDETI
‘INNEHA ‘ALEJHIM MU’USEDETUN
FI ‘AMEDIN MUMEDDEDETIN
‘ELEM TERA KEJFE FE’ALE REBBUKE BI’ESHABIL-FIL
‘ELEM JEXH’AL KEJDEHUM FI TEDLILIN
WE ‘ERSELE ‘ALEJHIM TEJRÆN ‘EBABILE
TERMIHIM BIHIXHARETIN MIN SIXHXHILIN
FEXHE’ALEHUM KE’ASFIN ME’KULIN
LI’ILAFI KUREJSHIN
‘ILAFIHIM RIHLETE ESH-SHITA’I WE ES-SEJFI
FELJA’BUDU REBBE HADHAL-BEJTI
EL-LEDHI ‘ET’AMEHUM MIN XHU’IN WE ‘AMENEHUM MIN HAWFIN
‘ERE’EJTEL-LEDHI JUKEDHDHIBU BID-DINI
FEDHALIKEL-LEDHI JEDU’’UL-JETIME
WE LA JEHUDDU ‘ALA TA’AMIL-MISKINI
FEWEJLUN LILMUSELLINE
EL-LEDHINE HUM ‘AN SELATIHIM SAHUNE
EL-LEDHINE HUM JURA’UNE
WE JEMNA’UNEL-MA’UNE
‘INNA ‘A’TEJNAKEL-KEWTHERE
FESELLI LIREBBIKE WE ENHER
‘INNE SHANI’EKE HUWEL-’EBTERU
KUL JA ‘EJJUHAL-KAFIRUNE
LA ‘A’BUDU MA TA’BUDUNE
WE LA ‘ENTUM ‘ABIDUNE MA ‘A’BUDU
WE LA ‘ENA ‘ABIDUN MA ‘ABEDTTUM
WE LA ‘ENTUM ‘ABIDUNE MA ‘A’BUDU
LEKUM DINUKUM WE LIJE DINI
‘IDHA XHA’E NESRU ELLAHI WEL-FETHU
WE RE’EJTE EN-NASE JEDHULUNE FI DINI ELLAHI ‘EFWAXHÆN
FESEBBIH BIHEMDI RABBIKE WE ESTEGFIRHU ‘INNEHU KANE TEWWABÆN
TEBBET JEDA ‘EBI LEHEBIN WE TEBBE
MA ‘EGNA ‘ANHU MALUHU WE MA KESEBE
SEJESLA NARÆN DHATE LEHEBIN
WE EMRE’ETUHU HEMMALETEL-HETEBI
FI XHIDIHA HEBLUN MIN MESEDIN
KUL HUWEL-LAHU ‘EHEDUN
ELLAHU ES-SEMEDU
LEM JELID WE LEM JULED
WELEM JEKUN LEHU KUFUEN ‘EHEDUN
KUL ‘A’UDHU BIREBBIL-FELEKI
MIN SHERRI MA HALEKA
WE MIN SHERRI GASIKIN ‘IDHA WEKABE
WE MIN SHERRI EN-NEFFATHATI FIL-’UKADI
WE MIN SHERRI HASIDIN ‘IDHA HESEDE
KUL ‘A’UDHU BIREBBI EN-NASI
MELIKI EN-NASI
‘ILEHI EN-NASI
MIN SHERRIL-WESWASIL-HANNASI
EL-LEDHI JUWESWISU FI SUDURI EN-NASI
MINEL-XHINNETI WE EN-NASI
